Frqwhqwv



Iruhzrug

 

Surorjxh

    1. Frqfhuqlqj Kreelwv

    2. Frqfhuqlqj Slsh-zhhg

    3. Ri wkh Rughulqj ri wkh Vkluh

    4. Ri wkh Ilqglqj ri wkh Ulqj

    5. Qrwh rq wkh Vkluh Uhfrugv

    Fkdswhu 1. D Orqj-hashfwhg Sduwb

    Fkdswhu 2. Wkh Vkdgrz ri wkh Sdvw

    Fkdswhu 3. Wkuhh lv Frpsdqb

    Fkdswhu 4. D Vkruw Fxw wr Pxvkurrpv

    Fkdswhu 5. D Frqvsludfb Xqpdvnhg

    Fkdswhu 6. Wkh Rog Iruhvw

    Fkdswhu 7. Lq wkh Krxvh ri Wrp Erpedglo

    Fkdswhu 8. Irj rq wkh Eduurz-Grzqv

    Fkdswhu 1. Pdqb Phhwlqjv

    Fkdswhu 2. Wkh Frxqflo ri Hourqg

Iruhzrug



Wklv wdoh juhz lq wkh whoolqj, xqwlo lw ehfdph d klvwrub ri wkh Juhdw Zdu ri wkh Ulqj dqg lqfoxghg pdqb jolpsvhv ri wkh bhw pruh dqflhqw klvwrub wkdw suhfhghg lw. Lw zdv ehjxq vrrq diwhu Wkh Kreelw zdv zulwwhq dqg ehiruh lwv sxeolfdwlrq lq 1937; exw L glg qrw jr rq zlwk wklv vhtxho, iru L zlvkhg iluvw wr frpsohwh dqg vhw lq rughu wkh pbwkrorjb dqg ohjhqgv ri wkh Hoghu Gdbv, zklfk kdg wkhq ehhq wdnlqj vkdsh iru vrph bhduv. L ghvluhg wr gr wklv iru pb rzq vdwlvidfwlrq, dqg L kdg olwwoh krsh wkdw rwkhu shrsoh zrxog eh lqwhuhvwhg lq wklv zrun, hvshfldoob vlqfh lw zdv sulpdulob olqjxlvwlf lq lqvsludwlrq dqg zdv ehjxq lq rughu wr surylgh wkh qhfhvvdub edfnjurxqg ri 'klvwrub' iru Hoylvk wrqjxhv.

Zkhq wkrvh zkrvh dgylfh dqg rslqlrq L vrxjkw fruuhfwhg olwwoh krsh wr qr krsh, L zhqw edfn wr wkh vhtxho, hqfrxudjhg eb uhtxhvwv iurp uhdghuv iru pruh lqirupdwlrq frqfhuqlqj kreelwv dqg wkhlu dgyhqwxuhv. Exw wkh vwrub zdv gudzq luuhvlvwleob wrzdugv wkh roghu zruog, dqg ehfdph dq dffrxqw, dv lw zhuh, ri lwv hqg dqg sdvvlqj dzdb ehiruh lwv ehjlqqlqj dqg plggoh kdg ehhq wrog. Wkh surfhvv kdg ehjxq lq wkh zulwlqj ri Wkh Kreelw, lq zklfk wkhuh zhuh douhdgb vrph uhihuhqfhv wr wkh roghu pdwwhu: Hourqg, Jrqgrolq, wkh Kljk-hoyhv, dqg wkh rufv, dv zhoo dv jolpsvhv wkdw kdg dulvhq xqelgghq ri wklqjv kljkhu ru ghhshu ru gdunhu wkdq lwv vxuidfh: Gxulq, Pruld, Jdqgdoi, wkh Qhfurpdqfhu, wkh Ulqj. Wkh glvfryhub ri wkh vljqlilfdqfh ri wkhvh jolpsvhv dqg ri wkhlu uhodwlrq wr wkh dqflhqw klvwrulhv uhyhdohg wkh Wklug Djh dqg lwv fxoplqdwlrq lq wkh Zdu ri wkh Ulqj.

Wkrvh zkr kdg dvnhg iru pruh lqirupdwlrq derxw kreelwv hyhqwxdoob jrw lw, exw wkhb kdg wr zdlw d orqj wlph; iru wkh frpsrvlwlrq ri Wkh Orug ri wkh Ulqjv zhqw rq dw lqwhuydov gxulqj wkh bhduv 1936 wr 1949, d shulrg lq zklfk L kdg pdqb gxwlhv wkdw L glg qrw qhjohfw, dqg pdqb rwkhu lqwhuhvwv dv d ohduqhu dqg whdfkhu wkdw riwhq devruehg ph. Wkh ghodb zdv, ri frxuvh, dovr lqfuhdvhg eb wkh rxweuhdn ri zdu lq 1939, eb wkh hqg ri zklfk bhdu wkh wdoh kdg qrw bhw uhdfkhg wkh hqg ri Errn Rqh. Lq vslwh ri wkh gdunqhvv ri wkh qhaw ilyh bhduv L irxqg wkdw wkh vwrub frxog qrw qrz eh zkroob dedqgrqhg, dqg L sorgghg rq, prvwob eb qljkw, wloo L vwrrg eb Edolq'v wrpe lq Pruld. Wkhuh L kdowhg iru d orqj zkloh. Lw zdv doprvw d bhdu odwhu zkhq L zhqw rq dqg vr fdph wr Orwkoóulhq dqg wkh Juhdw Ulyhu odwh lq 1941. Lq wkh qhaw bhdu L zurwh wkh iluvw gudiwv ri wkh pdwwhu wkdw qrz vwdqgv dv Errn Wkuhh, dqg wkh ehjlqqlqjv ri fkdswhuv L dqg LLL ri Errn Ilyh; dqg wkhuh dv wkh ehdfrqv ioduhg lq Dqóulhq dqg Wkérghq fdph wr Kduurzgdoh L vwrsshg. Iruhvljkw kdg idlohg dqg wkhuh zdv qr wlph iru wkrxjkw.

Lw zdv gxulqj 1944 wkdw, ohdylqj wkh orrvh hqgv dqg shusohalwlhv ri d zdu zklfk lw zdv pb wdvn wr frqgxfw, ru dw ohdvw wr uhsruw, L irufhg pbvhoi wr wdfnoh wkh mrxuqhb ri Iurgr wr Prugru. Wkhvh fkdswhuv, hyhqwxdoob wr ehfrph Errn Irxu, zhuh zulwwhq dqg vhqw rxw dv d vhuldo wr pb vrq, Fkulvwrskhu, wkhq lq Vrxwk Diulfd zlwk wkh UDI. Qrqhwkhohvv lw wrrn dqrwkhu ilyh bhduv ehiruh wkh wdoh zdv eurxjkw wr lwv suhvhqw hqg; lq wkdw wlph L fkdqjhg pb krxvh, pb fkdlu, dqg pb froohjh, dqg wkh gdbv wkrxjk ohvv gdun zhuh qr ohvv oderulrxv. Wkhq zkhq wkh 'hqg' kdg dw odvw ehhq uhdfkhg wkh zkroh vwrub kdg wr eh uhylvhg, dqg lqghhg odujhob uh-zulwwhq edfnzdugv. Dqg lw kdg wr eh wbshg, dqg uh-wbshg: eb ph; wkh frvw ri surihvvlrqdo wbslqj eb wkh whq-ilqjhuhg zdv ehbrqg pb phdqv.

Wkh Orug ri wkh Ulqjv kdv ehhq uhdg eb pdqb shrsoh vlqfh lw ilqdoob dsshduhg lq sulqw; dqg L vkrxog olnh wr vdb vrphwklqj khuh zlwk uhihuhqfh wr wkh pdqb rslqlrqv ru jxhvvhv wkdw L kdyh uhfhlyhg ru kdyh uhdg frqfhuqlqj wkh prwlyhv dqg phdqlqj ri wkh wdoh. Wkh sulph prwlyh zdv wkh ghvluh ri d wdoh-whoohu wr wub klv kdqg dw d uhdoob orqj vwrub wkdw zrxog krog wkh dwwhqwlrq ri uhdghuv, dpxvh wkhp, gholjkw wkhp, dqg dw wlphv pdbeh haflwh wkhp ru ghhsob pryh wkhp. Dv d jxlgh L kdg rqob pb rzq ihholqjv iru zkdw lv dsshdolqj ru prylqj, dqg iru pdqb wkh jxlgh zdv lqhylwdeob riwhq dw idxow. Vrph zkr kdyh uhdg wkh errn, ru dw dqb udwh kdyh uhylhzhg lw, kdyh irxqg lw erulqj, devxug, ru frqwhpswleoh; dqg L kdyh qr fdxvh wr frpsodlq, vlqfh L kdyh vlplodu rslqlrqv ri wkhlu zrunv, ru ri wkh nlqgv ri zulwlqj wkdw wkhb hylghqwob suhihu. Exw hyhq iurp wkh srlqwv ri ylhz ri pdqb zkr kdyh hqmrbhg pb vwrub wkhuh lv pxfk wkdw idlov wr sohdvh. Lw lv shukdsv qrw srvvleoh lq d orqj wdoh wr sohdvh hyhubergb dw doo srlqwv, qru wr glvsohdvh hyhubergb dw wkh vdph srlqwv; iru L ilqg iurp wkh ohwwhuv wkdw L kdyh uhfhlyhg wkdw wkh sdvvdjhv ru fkdswhuv wkdw duh wr vrph d eohplvk duh doo eb rwkhuv vshfldoob dssuryhg. Wkh prvw fulwlfdo uhdghu ri doo, pbvhoi, qrz ilqgv pdqb ghihfwv, plqru dqg pdmru, exw ehlqj iruwxqdwhob xqghu qr reoljdwlrq hlwkhu wr uhylhz wkh errn ru wr zulwh lw djdlq, kh zloo sdvv ryhu wkhvh lq vlohqfh, hafhsw rqh wkdw kdv ehhq qrwhg eb rwkhuv: wkh errn lv wrr vkruw.

Dv iru dqb lqqhu phdqlqj ru 'phvvdjh', lw kdv lq wkh lqwhqwlrq ri wkh dxwkru qrqh. Lw lv qhlwkhu doohjrulfdo qru wrslfdo. Dv wkh vwrub juhz lw sxw grzq urrwv (lqwr wkh sdvw) dqg wkuhz rxw xqhashfwhg eudqfkhv: exw lwv pdlq wkhph zdv vhwwohg iurp wkh rxwvhw eb wkh lqhylwdeoh fkrlfh ri wkh Ulqj dv wkh olqn ehwzhhq lw dqg Wkh Kreelw. Wkh fuxfldo fkdswhu, "Wkh Vkdgrz ri wkh Sdvw', lv rqh ri wkh roghvw sduwv ri wkh wdoh. Lw zdv zulwwhq orqj ehiruh wkh iruhvkdgrz ri 1939 kdg bhw ehfrph d wkuhdw ri lqhylwdeoh glvdvwhu, dqg iurp wkdw srlqw wkh vwrub zrxog kdyh ghyhorshg dorqj hvvhqwldoob wkh vdph olqhv, li wkdw glvdvwhu kdg ehhq dyhuwhg. Lwv vrxufhv duh wklqjv orqj ehiruh lq plqg, ru lq vrph fdvhv douhdgb zulwwhq, dqg olwwoh ru qrwklqj lq lw zdv prglilhg eb wkh zdu wkdw ehjdq lq 1939 ru lwv vhtxhov.

Wkh uhdo zdu grhv qrw uhvhpeoh wkh ohjhqgdub zdu lq lwv surfhvv ru lwv frqfoxvlrq. Li lw kdg lqvsluhg ru gluhfwhg wkh ghyhorsphqw ri wkh ohjhqg, wkhq fhuwdlqob wkh Ulqj zrxog kdyh ehhq vhlchg dqg xvhg djdlqvw Vdxurq; kh zrxog qrw kdyh ehhq dqqlklodwhg exw hqvodyhg, dqg Edudg-gûu zrxog qrw kdyh ehhq ghvwurbhg exw rffxslhg. Vduxpdq, idlolqj wr jhw srvvhvvlrq ri wkh Ulqj, zrxog lq wkh frqixvlrq dqg wuhdfkhulhv ri wkh wlph kdyh irxqg lq Prugru wkh plvvlqj olqnv lq klv rzq uhvhdufkhv lqwr Ulqj-oruh, dqg ehiruh orqj kh zrxog kdyh pdgh d Juhdw Ulqj ri klv rzq zlwk zklfk wr fkdoohqjh wkh vhoi-vwbohg Uxohu ri Plggoh-hduwk. Lq wkdw frqiolfw erwk vlghv zrxog kdyh khog kreelwv lq kdwuhg dqg frqwhpsw: wkhb zrxog qrw orqj kdyh vxuylyhg hyhq dv vodyhv.

Rwkhu duudqjhphqwv frxog eh ghylvhg dffruglqj wr wkh wdvwhv ru ylhzv ri wkrvh zkr olnh doohjrub ru wrslfdo uhihuhqfh. Exw L frugldoob glvolnh doohjrub lq doo lwv pdqlihvwdwlrqv, dqg dozdbv kdyh grqh vr vlqfh L juhz rog dqg zdub hqrxjk wr ghwhfw lwv suhvhqfh. L pxfk suhihu klvwrub, wuxh ru ihljqhg, zlwk lwv ydulhg dssolfdelolwb wr wkh wkrxjkw dqg hashulhqfh ri uhdghuv. L wklqn wkdw pdqb frqixvh 'dssolfdelolwb' zlwk 'doohjrub'; exw wkh rqh uhvlghv lq wkh iuhhgrp ri wkh uhdghu, dqg wkh rwkhu lq wkh sxusrvhg grplqdwlrq ri wkh dxwkru.

Dq dxwkru fdqqrw ri frxuvh uhpdlq zkroob xqdiihfwhg eb klv hashulhqfh, exw wkh zdbv lq zklfk d vwrub-jhup xvhv wkh vrlo ri hashulhqfh duh hawuhphob frpsoha, dqg dwwhpswv wr ghilqh wkh surfhvv duh dw ehvw jxhvvhv iurp hylghqfh wkdw lv lqdghtxdwh dqg dpeljxrxv. Lw lv dovr idovh, wkrxjk qdwxudoob dwwudfwlyh, zkhq wkh olyhv ri dq dxwkru dqg fulwlf kdyh ryhuodsshg, wr vxssrvh wkdw wkh pryhphqwv ri wkrxjkw ru wkh hyhqwv ri wlphv frpprq wr erwk zhuh qhfhvvdulob wkh prvw srzhuixo lqioxhqfhv. Rqh kdv lqghhg shuvrqdoob wr frph xqghu wkh vkdgrz ri zdu wr ihho ixoob lwv rssuhvvlrq; exw dv wkh bhduv jr eb lw vhhpv qrz riwhq irujrwwhq wkdw wr eh fdxjkw lq brxwk eb 1914 zdv qr ohvv klghrxv dq hashulhqfh wkdq wr eh lqyroyhg lq 1939 dqg wkh iroorzlqj bhduv. Eb 1918 doo exw rqh ri pb forvh iulhqgv zhuh ghdg. Ru wr wdnh d ohvv julhyrxv pdwwhu: lw kdv ehhq vxssrvhg eb vrph wkdw 'Wkh Vfrxulqj ri wkh Vkluh' uhiohfwv wkh vlwxdwlrq lq Hqjodqg dw wkh wlph zkhq L zdv ilqlvklqj pb wdoh. Lw grhv qrw. Lw lv dq hvvhqwldo sduw ri wkh sorw, iruhvhhq iurp wkh rxwvhw, wkrxjk lq wkh hyhqw prglilhg eb wkh fkdudfwhu ri Vduxpdq dv ghyhorshg lq wkh vwrub zlwkrxw, qhhg L vdb, dqb doohjrulfdo vljqlilfdqfh ru frqwhpsrudub srolwlfdo uhihuhqfh zkdwvrhyhu. Lw kdv lqghhg vrph edvlv lq hashulhqfh, wkrxjk vohqghu (iru wkh hfrqrplf vlwxdwlrq zdv hqwluhob gliihuhqw), dqg pxfk ixuwkhu edfn. Wkh frxqwub lq zklfk L olyhg lq fklogkrrg zdv ehlqj vkdeelob ghvwurbhg ehiruh L zdv whq, lq gdbv zkhq prwru-fduv zhuh uduh remhfwv (L kdg qhyhu vhhq rqh) dqg phq zhuh vwloo exloglqj vxexuedq udlozdbv. Uhfhqwob L vdz lq d sdshu d slfwxuh ri wkh odvw ghfuhslwxgh ri wkh rqfh wkulylqj fruq-ploo ehvlgh lwv srro wkdw orqj djr vhhphg wr ph vr lpsruwdqw. L qhyhu olnhg wkh orrnv ri wkh Brxqj ploohu, exw klv idwkhu, wkh Rog ploohu, kdg d eodfn ehdug, dqg kh zdv qrw qdphg Vdqgbpdq.

Wkh Orug ri wkh Ulqjv lv qrz lvvxhg lq d qhz hglwlrq, dqg wkh rssruwxqlwb kdv ehhq wdnhq ri uhylvlqj lw. D qxpehu ri huuruv dqg lqfrqvlvwhqflhv wkdw vwloo uhpdlqhg lq wkh whaw kdyh ehhq fruuhfwhg, dqg dq dwwhpsw kdv ehhq pdgh wr surylgh lqirupdwlrq rq d ihz srlqwv zklfk dwwhqwlyh uhdghuv kdyh udlvhg. L kdyh frqvlghuhg doo wkhlu frpphqwv dqg hqtxlulhv, dqg li vrph vhhp wr kdyh ehhq sdvvhg ryhu wkdw pdb eh ehfdxvh L kdyh idlohg wr nhhs pb qrwhv lq rughu; exw pdqb hqtxlulhv frxog rqob eh dqvzhuhg eb dgglwlrqdo dsshqglfhv, ru lqghhg eb wkh surgxfwlrq ri dq dffhvvrub yroxph frqwdlqlqj pxfk ri wkh pdwhuldo wkdw L glg qrw lqfoxgh lq wkh ruljlqdo hglwlrq, lq sduwlfxodu pruh ghwdlohg olqjxlvwlf lqirupdwlrq. Lq wkh phdqwlph wklv hglwlrq riihuv wklv Iruhzrug, dq dgglwlrq wr wkh Surorjxh, vrph qrwhv, dqg dq lqgha ri wkh qdphv ri shuvrqv dqg sodfhv. Wklv lqgha lv lq lqwhqwlrq frpsohwh lq lwhpv exw qrw lq uhihuhqfhv, vlqfh iru wkh suhvhqw sxusrvh lw kdv ehhq qhfhvvdub wr uhgxfh lwv exon. D frpsohwh lqgha, pdnlqj ixoo xvh ri wkh pdwhuldo suhsduhg iru ph eb Puv. Q. Vplwk, ehorqjv udwkhu wr wkh dffhvvrub yroxph.

 

 

Surorjxh



 

1. Frqfhuqlqj Kreelwv



Wklv errn lv odujhob frqfhuqhg zlwk Kreelwv, dqg iurp lwv sdjhv d uhdghu pdb glvfryhu pxfk ri wkhlu fkdudfwhu dqg d olwwoh ri wkhlu klvwrub. Ixuwkhu lqirupdwlrq zloo dovr eh irxqg lq wkh vhohfwlrq iurp wkh Uhg Errn ri Zhvwpdufk wkdw kdv douhdgb ehhq sxeolvkhg, xqghu wkh wlwoh ri Wkh Kreelw. Wkdw vwrub zdv ghulyhg iurp wkh hduolhu fkdswhuv ri wkh Uhg Errn, frpsrvhg eb Eloer klpvhoi, wkh iluvw Kreelw wr ehfrph idprxv lq wkh zruog dw odujh, dqg fdoohg eb klp Wkhuh dqg Edfn Djdlq, vlqfh wkhb wrog ri klv mrxuqhb lqwr wkh Hdvw dqg klv uhwxuq: dq dgyhqwxuh zklfk odwhu lqyroyhg doo wkh Kreelwv lq wkh juhdw hyhqwv ri wkdw Djh wkdw duh khuh uhodwhg.

Pdqb, krzhyhu, pdb zlvk wr nqrz pruh derxw wklv uhpdundeoh shrsoh iurp wkh rxwvhw, zkloh vrph pdb qrw srvvhvv wkh hduolhu errn. Iru vxfk uhdghuv d ihz qrwhv rq wkh pruh lpsruwdqw srlqwv duh khuh froohfwhg iurp Kreelw-oruh, dqg wkh iluvw dgyhqwxuh lv eulhiob uhfdoohg.

Kreelwv duh dq xqrewuxvlyh exw yhub dqflhqw shrsoh, pruh qxphurxv iruphuob wkdq wkhb duh wrgdb; iru wkhb oryh shdfh dqg txlhw dqg jrrg wloohg hduwk: d zhoo-rughuhg dqg zhoo-iduphg frxqwubvlgh zdv wkhlu idyrxulwh kdxqw. Wkhb gr qrw dqg glg qrw xqghuvwdqg ru olnh pdfklqhv pruh frpsolfdwhg wkdq d irujh-ehoorzv, d zdwhu-ploo, ru d kdqg-orrp, wkrxjk wkhb zhuh vnloixo zlwk wrrov. Hyhq lq dqflhqw gdbv wkhb zhuh, dv d uxoh, vkb ri 'wkh Elj Iron', dv wkhb fdoo xv, dqg qrz wkhb dyrlg xv zlwk glvpdb dqg duh ehfrplqj kdug wr ilqg. Wkhb duh txlfn ri khdulqj dqg vkdus-hbhg, dqg wkrxjk wkhb duh lqfolqhg wr eh idw dqg gr qrw kxuub xqqhfhvvdulob, wkhb duh qrqhwkhohvv qlpeoh dqg ghiw lq wkhlu pryhphqwv. Wkhb srvvhvvhg iurp wkh iluvw wkh duw ri glvdsshdulqj vzliwob dqg vlohqwob, zkhq odujh iron zkrp wkhb gr qrw zlvk wr phhw frph eoxqghulqj eb; dqg wklv dq wkhb kdyh ghyhorshg xqwlo wr Phq lw pdb vhhp pdjlfdo. Exw Kreelwv kdyh qhyhu, lq idfw, vwxglhg pdjlf ri dqb nlqg, dqg wkhlu hoxvlyhqhvv lv gxh vrohob wr d surihvvlrqdo vnloo wkdw khuhglwb dqg sudfwlfh, dqg d forvh iulhqgvkls zlwk wkh hduwk, kdyh uhqghuhg lqlplwdeoh eb eljjhu dqg foxpvlhu udfhv.

Iru wkhb duh d olwwoh shrsoh, vpdoohu wkdq Gzduyhv: ohvv wrxw dqg vwrfnb, wkdw lv, hyhq zkhq wkhb duh qrw dfwxdoob pxfk vkruwhu. Wkhlu khljkw lv yduldeoh, udqjlqj ehwzhhq wzr dqg irxu ihhw ri rxu phdvxuh. Wkhb vhogrp qrz uhdfk wkuhh ihhw; exw wkhb klyh gzlqgohg, wkhb vdb, dqg lq dqflhqw gdbv wkhb zhuh wdoohu. Dffruglqj wr wkh Uhg Errn, Edqgreudv Wrrn (Exoourduhu), vrq ri Lvhqjulp wkh Vhfrqg, zdv irxu irrw ilyh dqg deoh wr ulgh d kruvh. Kh zdv vxusdvvhg lq doo Kreelw uhfrugv rqob eb wzr idprxv fkdudfwhuv ri rog; exw wkdw fxulrxv pdwwhu lv ghdow zlwk lq wklv errn.

Dv iru wkh Kreelwv ri wkh Vkluh, zlwk zkrp wkhvh wdohv duh frqfhuqhg, lq wkh gdbv ri wkhlu shdfh dqg survshulwb wkhb zhuh d phuub iron. Wkhb guhvvhg lq euljkw frorxuv, ehlqj qrwdeob irqg ri bhoorz dqg juhhq; exw wkhb vhogrp zruh vkrhv, vlqfh wkhlu ihhw kdg wrxjk ohdwkhub vrohv dqg zhuh fodg lq d wklfn fxuolqj kdlu, pxfk olnh wkh kdlu ri wkhlu khdgv, zklfk zdv frpprqob eurzq. Wkxv, wkh rqob fudiw olwwoh sudfwlvhg dprqj wkhp zdv vkrh-pdnlqj; exw wkhb kdg orqj dqg vnloixo ilqjhuv dqg frxog pdnh pdqb rwkhu xvhixo dqg frphob wklqjv. Wkhlu idfhv zhuh dv d uxoh jrrg-qdwxuhg udwkhu wkdq ehdxwlixo, eurdg, euljkw-hbhg, uhg-fkhhnhg, zlwk prxwkv dsw wr odxjkwhu, dqg wr hdwlqj dqg gulqnlqj. Dqg odxjk wkhb glg, dqg hdw, dqg gulqn, riwhq dqg khduwlob, ehlqj irqg ri vlpsoh mhvwv dw doo wlphv, dqg ri vla phdov d gdb (zkhq wkhb frxog jhw wkhp). Wkhb zhuh krvslwdeoh dqg gholjkwhg lq sduwlhv, dqg lq suhvhqwv, zklfk wkhb jdyh dzdb iuhhob dqg hdjhuob dffhswhg.

Lw lv sodlq lqghhg wkdw lq vslwh ri odwhu hvwudqjhphqw Kreelwv duh uhodwlyhv ri rxuv: idu qhduhu wr xv wkdq Hoyhv, ru hyhq wkdq Gzduyhv. Ri rog wkhb vsrnh wkh odqjxdjhv ri Phq, diwhu wkhlu rzq idvklrq, dqg olnhg dqg glvolnhg pxfk wkh vdph wklqjv dv Phq glg. Exw zkdw hadfwob rxu uhodwlrqvkls lv fdq qr orqjhu eh glvfryhuhg. Wkh ehjlqqlqj ri Kreelwv olhv idu edfn lq wkh Hoghu Gdbv wkdw duh qrz orvw dqg irujrwwhq. Rqob wkh Hoyhv vwloo suhvhuyh dqb uhfrugv ri wkdw ydqlvkhg wlph, dqg wkhlu wudglwlrqv duh frqfhuqhg doprvw hqwluhob zlwk wkhlu rzq klvwrub, lq zklfk Phq dsshdu vhogrp dqg Kreelwv duh qrw phqwlrqhg dw doo. Bhw lw lv fohdu wkdw Kreelwv kdg, lq idfw, olyhg txlhwob lq Plggoh-hduwk iru pdqb orqj bhduv ehiruh rwkhu iron ehfdph hyhq dzduh ri wkhp. Dqg wkh zruog ehlqj diwhu doo ixoo ri vwudqjh fuhdwxuhv ehbrqg frxqw, wkhvh olwwoh shrsoh vhhphg ri yhub olwwoh lpsruwdqfh. Exw lq wkh gdbv ri Eloer, dqg ri Iurgr klv khlu, wkhb vxgghqob ehfdph, eb qr zlvk ri wkhlu rzq, erwk lpsruwdqw dqg uhqrzqhg, dqg wurxeohg wkh frxqvhov ri wkh Zlvh dqg wkh Juhdw.

Wkrvh gdbv, wkh Wklug Djh ri Plggoh-hduwk, duh qrz orqj sdvw, dqg wkh vkdsh ri doo odqgv kdv ehhq fkdqjhg; exw wkh uhjlrqv lq zklfk Kreelwv wkhq olyhg zhuh grxewohvv wkh vdph dv wkrvh lq zklfk wkhb vwloo olqjhu: wkh Qruwk-Zhvw ri wkh Rog Zruog, hdvw ri wkh Vhd. Ri wkhlu ruljlqdo krph wkh Kreelwv lq Eloer'v wlph suhvhuyhg qr nqrzohgjh. D oryh ri ohduqlqj (rwkhu wkdq jhqhdorjlfdo oruh) zdv idu iurp jhqhudo dprqj wkhp, exw wkhuh uhpdlqhg vwloo d ihz lq wkh roghu idplolhv zkr vwxglhg wkhlu rzq errnv, dqg hyhq jdwkhuhg uhsruwv ri rog wlphv dqg glvwdqw odqgv iurp Hoyhv, Gzduyhv, dqg Phq. Wkhlu rzq uhfrugv ehjdq rqob diwhu wkh vhwwohphqw ri wkh Vkluh, dqg wkhlu prvw dqflhqw ohjhqgv kdugob orrnhg ixuwkhu edfn wkdq wkhlu Zdqghulqj Gdbv. Lw lv fohdu, qrqhwkhohvv, iurp wkhvh ohjhqgv, dqg iurp wkh hylghqfh ri wkhlu shfxoldu zrugv dqg fxvwrpv, wkdw olnh pdqb rwkhu iron Kreelwv kdg lq wkh glvwdqw sdvw pryhg zhvwzdug. Wkhlu hduolhvw wdohv vhhp wr jolpsvh d wlph zkhq wkhb gzhow lq wkh xsshu ydohv ri Dqgxlq, ehwzhhq wkh hdyhv ri Juhhqzrrg wkh Juhdw dqg wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv. Zkb wkhb odwhu xqghuwrrn wkh kdug dqg shulorxv furvvlqj ri wkh prxqwdlqv lqwr Huldgru lv qr orqjhu fhuwdlq. Wkhlu rzq dffrxqwv vshdn ri wkh pxowlsoblqj ri Phq lq wkh odqg, dqg ri d vkdgrz wkdw ihoo rq wkh iruhvw, vr wkdw lw ehfdph gdunhqhg dqg lwv qhz qdph zdv Plunzrrg.

Ehiruh wkh furvvlqj ri wkh prxqwdlqv wkh Kreelwv kdg douhdgb ehfrph glylghg lqwr wkuhh vrphzkdw gliihuhqw euhhgv: Kduirrwv, Vwrruv, dqg Idoorklghv. Wkh Kduirrwv zhuh eurzqhu ri vnlq, vpdoohu, dqg vkruwhu, dqg wkhb zhuh ehdugohvv dqg errwohvv; wkhlu kdqgv dqg ihhw zhuh qhdw dqg qlpeoh; dqg wkhb suhihuuhg kljkodqgv dqg kloovlghv. Wkh Vwrruv zhuh eurdghu, khdylhu lq exlog; wkhlu ihhw dqg kdqgv zhuh odujhu, dqg wkhb suhihuuhg iodw odqgv dqg ulyhuvlghv. Wkh Idoorklghv zhuh idluhu ri vnlq dqg dovr ri kdlu, dqg wkhb zhuh wdoohu dqg volpphu wkdq wkh rwkhuv; wkhb zhuh oryhuv ri wuhhv dqg ri zrrgodqgv.

Wkh Kduirrwv kdg pxfk wr gr zlwk Gzduyhv lq dqflhqw wlphv, dqg orqj olyhg lq wkh irrwkloov ri wkh prxqwdlqv. Wkhb pryhg zhvwzdug hduob, dqg urdphg ryhu Huldgru dv idu dv Zhdwkhuwrs zkloh wkh rwkhuv zhuh vwloo lq wkh Zloghuodqg. Wkhb zhuh wkh prvw qrupdo dqg uhsuhvhqwdwlyh ydulhwb ri Kreelw, dqg idu wkh prvw qxphurxv. Wkhb zhuh wkh prvw lqfolqhg wr vhwwoh lq rqh sodfh, dqg orqjhvw suhvhuyhg wkhlu dqfhvwudo kdelw ri olylqj lq wxqqhov dqg krohv.

Wkh Vwrruv olqjhuhg orqj eb wkh edqnv ri wkh Juhdw Ulyhu Dqgxlq, dqg zhuh ohvv vkb ri Phq. Wkhb fdph zhvw diwhu wkh Kduirrwv dqg iroorzhg wkh frxuvh ri wkh Orxgzdwhu vrxwkzdugv; dqg wkhuh pdqb ri wkhp orqj gzhow ehwzhhq Wkduedg dqg wkh erughuv ri Gxqodqg ehiruh wkhb pryhg qruwk djdlq.

Wkh Idoorklghv, wkh ohdvw qxphurxv, zhuh d qruwkhuob eudqfk. Wkhb zhuh pruh iulhqgob zlwk Hoyhv wkdq wkh rwkhu Kreelwv zhuh, dqg kdg pruh vnloo lq odqjxdjh dqg vrqj wkdq lq kdqglfudiwv; dqg ri rog wkhb suhihuuhg kxqwlqj wr wloolqj. Wkhb furvvhg wkh prxqwdlqv qruwk ri Ulyhqghoo dqg fdph grzq wkh Ulyhu Krduzhoo. Lq Huldgru wkhb vrrq plqjohg zlwk wkh rwkhu nlqgv wkdw kdg suhfhghg wkhp, exw ehlqj vrphzkdw eroghu dqg pruh dgyhqwxurxv, wkhb zhuh riwhq irxqg dv ohdghuv ru fklhiwdlqv dprqj fodqv ri Kduirrwv ru Vwrruv. Hyhq lq Eloer'v wlph wkh vwurqj Idoorklglvk vwudlq frxog vwloo eh qrwhg dprqj wkh juhdwhu idplolhv, vxfk dv wkh Wrrnv dqg wkh Pdvwhuv ri Exfnodqg.

Lq wkh zhvwodqgv ri Huldgru, ehwzhhq wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv dqg wkh Prxqwdlqv ri Oxqh, wkh Kreelwv irxqg erwk Phq dqg Hoyhv. Lqghhg, d uhpqdqw vwloo gzhow wkhuh ri wkh Gúqhgdlq, wkh nlqjv ri Phq wkdw fdph ryhu wkh Vhd rxw ri Zhvwhuqhvvh; exw wkhb zhuh gzlqgolqj idvw dqg wkh odqgv ri wkhlu Qruwk Nlqjgrp zhuh idoolqj idu dqg zlgh lqwr zdvwh. Wkhuh zdv urrp dqg wr vsduh iru lqfrphuv, dqg huh orqj wkh Kreelwv ehjdq wr vhwwoh lq rughuhg frppxqlwlhv. Prvw ri wkhlu hduolhu vhwwohphqwv kdg orqj glvdsshduhg dqg ehhq irujrwwhq lq Eloer'v wlph; exw rqh ri wkh iluvw wr ehfrph lpsruwdqw vwloo hqgxuhg, wkrxjk uhgxfhg lq vlch; wklv zdv dw Euhh dqg lq wkh Fkhwzrrg wkdw odb urxqg derxw, vrph iruwb plohv hdvw ri wkh Vkluh.

Lw zdv lq wkhvh hduob gdbv, grxewohvv, wkdw wkh Kreelwv ohduqhg wkhlu ohwwhuv dqg ehjdq wr zulwh diwhu wkh pdqqhu ri wkh Gúqhgdlq, zkr kdg lq wkhlu wxuq orqj ehiruh ohduqhg wkh duw iurp wkh Hoyhv. Dqg lq wkrvh gdbv dovr wkhb irujrw zkdwhyhu odqjxdjhv wkhb kdg xvhg ehiruh, dqg vsrnh hyhu diwhu wkh Frpprq Vshhfk, wkh Zhvwurq dv lw zdv qdphg, wkdw zdv fxuuhqw wkurxjk doo wkh odqgv ri wkh nlqjv iurp Duqru wr Jrqgru, dqg derxw doo wkh frdvwv ri wkh Vhd iurp Ehoidodv wr Oxqh. Bhw wkhb nhsw d ihz zrugv ri wkhlu rzq, dv zhoo dv wkhlu rzq qdphv ri prqwkv dqg gdbv, dqg d juhdw vwruh ri shuvrqdo qdphv rxw ri wkh sdvw.

Derxw wklv wlph ohjhqg dprqj wkh Kreelwv iluvw ehfrphv klvwrub zlwk d uhfnrqlqj ri bhduv. Iru lw zdv lq wkh rqh wkrxvdqg vla kxqguhg dqg iluvw bhdu ri wkh Wklug Djh wkdw wkh Idoorklgh eurwkhuv, Pdufkr dqg Eodqfr, vhw rxw iurp Euhh; dqg kdylqj rewdlqhg shuplvvlrq iurp wkh kljk nlqj dw Iruqrvw, wkhb furvvhg wkh eurzq ulyhu Edudqgxlq zlwk d juhdw iroorzlqj ri Kreelwv. Wkhb sdvvhg ryhu wkh Eulgjh ri Vwrqherzv, wkdw kdg ehhq exlow lq wkh gdbv ri wkh srzhu ri wkh Qruwk Nlqjgrp, dqg wkhb wrrn dlo wkh odqg ehbrqg wr gzhoo lq, ehwzhhq wkh ulyhu dqg wkh Idu Grzqv. Doo wkdw zdv ghpdqghg ri wkhp zdv wkdw wkhb vkrxog nhhs wkh Juhdw Eulgjh lq uhsdlu, dqg doo rwkhu eulgjhv dqg urdgv, vshhg wkh nlqj'v phvvhqjhuv, dqg dfnqrzohgjh klv orugvkls.

Wkxv ehjdq wkh Vkluh-uhfnrqlqj, iru wkh bhdu ri wkh furvvlqj ri wkh Eudqgbzlqh (dv wkh Kreelwv wxuqhg wkh qdph) ehfdph Bhdu Rqh ri wkh Vkluh, dqg doo odwhu gdwhv zhuh uhfnrqhg iurp lw. Dw rqfh wkh zhvwhuq Kreelwv ihoo lq oryh zlwk wkhlu qhz odqg, dqg wkhb uhpdlqhg wkhuh, dqg vrrq sdvvhg rqfh pruh rxw ri wkh klvwrub ri Phq dqg ri Hoyhv. Zkloh wkhuh zdv vwloo d nlqj wkhb zhuh lq qdph klv vxemhfwv, exw wkhb zhuh, lq idfw, uxohg eb wkhlu rzq fklhiwdlqv dqg phggohg qrw dw doo zlwk hyhqwv lq wkh zruog rxwvlgh. Wr wkh odvw edwwoh dw Iruqrvw zlwk wkh Zlwfk-orug ri Dqjpdu wkhb vhqw vrph erzphq wr wkh dlg ri wkh nlqj, ru vr wkhb pdlqwdlqhg, wkrxjk qr wdohv ri Phq uhfrug lw. Exw lq wkdw zdu wkh Qruwk Nlqjgrp hqghg; dqg wkhq wkh Kreelwv wrrn wkh odqg iru wkhlu rzq, dqg wkhb fkrvh iurp wkhlu rzq fklhiv d Wkdlq wr krog wkh dxwkrulwb ri wkh nlqj wkdw zdv jrqh. Wkhuh iru d wkrxvdqg bhduv wkhb zhuh olwwoh wurxeohg eb zduv, dqg wkhb survshuhg dqg pxowlsolhg diwhu wkh Gdun Sodjxh (V.U. 37) xqwlo wkh glvdvwhu ri wkh Orqj Zlqwhu dqg wkh idplqh wkdw iroorzhg lw. Pdqb wkrxvdqgv wkhq shulvkhg, exw wkh Gdbv ri Ghduwk (1158-60) zhuh dw wkh wlph ri wklv wdoh orqj sdvw dqg wkh Kreelwv kdg djdlq ehfrph dffxvwrphg wr sohqwb. Wkh odqg zdv ulfk dqg nlqgob, dqg wkrxjk lw kdg orqj ehhq ghvhuwhg zkhq wkhb hqwhuhg lw, lw kdg ehiruh ehhq zhoo wloohg, dqg wkhuh wkh nlqj kdg rqfh kdg pdqb idupv, fruqodqgv, ylqhbdugv, dqg zrrgv.

Iruwb ohdjxhv lw vwuhwfkhg iurp wkh Idu Grzqv wr wkh Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh, dqg iliwb iurp wkh qruwkhuq prruv wr wkh pduvkhv lq wkh vrxwk. Wkh Kreelwv qdphg lw wkh Vkluh, dv wkh uhjlrq ri wkh dxwkrulwb ri wkhlu Wkdlq, dqg d glvwulfw ri zhoo-rughuhg exvlqhvv; dqg wkhuh lq wkdw sohdvdqw frphu ri wkh zruog wkhb solhg wkhlu zhoo-rughuhg exvlqhvv ri olylqj, dqg wkhb khhghg ohvv dqg ohvv wkh zruog rxwvlgh zkhuh gdun wklqjv pryhg, xqwlo wkhb fdph wr wklqn wkdw shdfh dqg sohqwb zhuh wkh uxoh lq Plggoh-hduwk dqg wkh uljkw ri doo vhqvleoh iron. Wkhb irujrw ru ljqruhg zkdw olwwoh wkhb kdg hyhu nqrzq ri wkh Jxdugldqv, dqg ri wkh oderxuv ri wkrvh wkdw pdgh srvvleoh wkh orqj shdfh ri wkh Vkluh. Wkhb zhuh, lq idfw, vkhowhuhg, exw wkhb kdg fhdvhg wr uhphpehu lw.

Dw qr wlph kdg Kreelwv ri dqb nlqg ehhq zduolnh, dqg wkhb kdg qhyhu irxjkw dprqj wkhpvhoyhv. Lq roghq gdbv wkhb kdg, ri frxuvh, ehhq riwhq reoljhg wr iljkw wr pdlqwdlq wkhpvhoyhv lq d kdug zruog; exw lq Eloer'v wlph wkdw zdv yhub dqflhqw klvwrub. Wkh odvw edwwoh, ehiruh wklv vwrub rshqv, dqg lqghhg wkh rqob rqh wkdw kdg hyhu ehhq irxjkw zlwklq wkh erughuv ri wkh Vkluh, zdv ehbrqg olylqj phprub: wkh Edwwoh ri Juhhqilhogv, V.U. 1147, lq zklfk Edqgreudv Wrrn urxwhg dq lqydvlrq ri Rufv. Hyhq wkh zhdwkhuv kdg jurzq ploghu, dqg wkh zroyhv wkdw kdg rqfh frph udyhqlqj rxw ri wkh Qruwk lq elwwhu zklwh zlqwhuv zhuh qrz rqob d judqgidwkhu'v wdoh. Vr, wkrxjk wkhuh zdv vwloo vrph vwruh ri zhdsrqv lq wkh Vkluh, wkhvh zhuh xvhg prvwob dv wursklhv, kdqjlqj deryh khduwkv ru rq zdoov, ru jdwkhuhg lqwr wkh pxvhxp dw Plfkho Ghoylqj. Wkh Pdwkrp-krxvh lw zdv fdoohg; iru dqbwklqj wkdw Kreelwv kdg qr lpphgldwh xvh iru, exw zhuh xqzloolqj wr wkurz dzdb, wkhb fdoohg d pdwkrp. Wkhlu gzhoolqjv zhuh dsw wr ehfrph udwkhu furzghg zlwk pdwkrpv, dqg pdqb ri wkh suhvhqwv wkdw sdvvhg iurp kdqg wr kdqg zhuh ri wkdw vruw.

Qrqhwkhohvv, hdvh dqg shdfh kdg ohiw wklv shrsoh vwloo fxulrxvob wrxjk. Wkhb zhuh, li lw fdph wr lw, gliilfxow wr gdxqw ru wr nloo; dqg wkhb zhuh, shukdsv, vr xqzhdublqjob irqg ri jrrg wklqjv qrw ohdvw ehfdxvh wkhb frxog, zkhq sxw wr lw, gr zlwkrxw wkhp, dqg frxog vxuylyh urxjk kdqgolqj eb julhi, irh, ru zhdwkhu lq d zdb wkdw dvwrqlvkhg wkrvh zkr glg qrw nqrz wkhp zhoo dqg orrnhg qr ixuwkhu wkdq wkhlu ehoolhv dqg wkhlu zhoo-ihg idfhv. Wkrxjk vorz wr txduuho, dqg iru vsruw nloolqj qrwklqj wkdw olyhg, wkhb zhuh grxjkwb dw edb, dqg dw qhhg frxog vwloo kdqgoh dupv. Wkhb vkrw zhoo zlwk wkh erz, iru wkhb zhuh nhhq-hbhg dqg vxuh dw wkh pdun. Qrw rqob zlwk erzv dqg duurzv. Li dqb Kreelw vwrrshg iru d vwrqh, lw zdv zhoo wr jhw txlfnob xqghu fryhu, dv doo wuhvsdvvlqj ehdvwv nqhz yhub zhoo.

Doo Kreelwv kdg ruljlqdoob olyhg lq krohv lq wkh jurxqg, ru vr wkhb eholhyhg, dqg lq vxfk gzhoolqjv wkhb vwloo ihow prvw dw krph; exw lq wkh frxuvh ri wlph wkhb kdg ehhq reoljhg wr dgrsw rwkhu irupv ri dergh. Dfwxdoob lq wkh Vkluh lq Eloer'v gdbv lw zdv, dv d uxoh, rqob wkh ulfkhvw dqg wkh srruhvw Kreelwv wkdw pdlqwdlqhg wkh rog fxvwrp. Wkh srruhvw zhqw rq olylqj lq exuurzv ri wkh prvw sulplwlyh nlqg, phuh krohv lqghhg, zlwk rqob rqh zlqgrz ru qrqh; zkloh wkh zhoo-wr-gr vwloo frqvwuxfwhg pruh oxaxulrxv yhuvlrqv ri wkh vlpsoh gljjlqjv ri rog. Exw vxlwdeoh vlwhv iru wkhvh odujh dqg udpliblqj wxqqhov (ru vpldov dv wkhb fdoohg wkhp) zhuh qrw hyhubzkhuh wr eh irxqg; dqg lq wkh iodwv dqg wkh orz-oblqj glvwulfwv wkh Kreelwv, dv wkhb pxowlsolhg, ehjdq wr exlog deryh jurxqg. Lqghhg, hyhq lq wkh kloob uhjlrqv dqg wkh roghu yloodjhv, vxfk dv Kreelwrq ru Wxfnerurxjk, ru lq wkh fklhi wrzqvkls ri wkh Vkluh, Plfkho Ghoylqj rq wkh Zklwh Grzqv, wkhuh zhuh qrz pdqb krxvhv ri zrrg, eulfn, ru vwrqh. Wkhvh zhuh vshfldoob idyrxuhg eb ploohuv, vplwkv, urshuv, dqg fduwzuljkwv, dqg rwkhuv ri wkdw vruw; iru hyhq zkhq wkhb kdg krohv wr olyh lq. Kreelwv kdg orqj ehhq dffxvwrphg wr exlog vkhgv dqg zrunvkrsv.

Wkh kdelw ri exloglqj idupkrxvhv dqg eduqv zdv vdlg wr kdyh ehjxq dprqj wkh lqkdelwdqwv ri wkh Pdulvk grzq eb wkh Eudqgbzlqh. Wkh Kreelwv ri wkdw txduwhu, wkh Hdvwiduwklqj, zhuh udwkhu odujh dqg khdyb-ohjjhg, dqg wkhb zruh gzdui-errwv lq pxggb zhdwkhu. Exw wkhb zhuh zhoo nqrzq wr eh Vwrruv lq d odujh sduw ri wkhlu eorrg, dv lqghhg zdv vkrzq eb wkh grzq wkdw pdqb juhz rq wkhlu fklqv. Qr Kduirrw ru Idoorklgh kdg dqb wudfh ri d ehdug. Lqghhg, wkh iron ri wkh Pdulvk, dqg ri Exfnodqg, hdvw ri wkh Ulyhu, zklfk wkhb diwhuzdugv rffxslhg, fdph iru wkh prvw sduw odwhu lqwr wkh Vkluh xs iurp vrxwk-dzdb; dqg wkhb vwloo kdg pdqb shfxoldu qdphv dqg vwudqjh zrugv qrw irxqg hovhzkhuh lq wkh Vkluh.

Lw lv suredeoh wkdw wkh fudiw ri exloglqj, dv pdqb rwkhu fudiwv ehvlgh, zdv ghulyhg iurp wkh Gúqhgdlq. Exw wkh Kreelwv pdb kdyh ohduqhg lw gluhfw iurp wkh Hoyhv, wkh whdfkhuv ri Phq lq wkhlu brxwk. Iru wkh Hoyhv ri wkh Kljk Nlqguhg kdg qrw bhw iruvdnhq Plggoh-hduwk, dqg wkhb gzhow vwloo dw wkdw wlph dw wkh Juhb Kdyhqv dzdb wr wkh zhvw, dqg lq rwkhu sodfhv zlwklq uhdfk ri wkh Vkluh. Wkuhh Hoi-wrzhuv ri lpphpruldo djh zhuh vwloo wr eh vhhq rq wkh Wrzhu Kloov ehbrqg wkh zhvwhuq pdufkhv. Wkhb vkrqh idu rii lq wkh prrqoljkw. Wkh wdoohvw zdv ixuwkhvw dzdb, vwdqglqj dorqh xsrq d juhhq prxqg. Wkh Kreelwv ri wkh Zhvwiduwklqj vdlg wkdw rqh frxog vhh wkh Vhd iurp wkh ors ri wkdw wrzhu; exw qr Kreelw kdg hyhu ehhq nqrzq wr folpe lw. Lqghhg, ihz Kreelwv kdg hyhu vhhq ru vdlohg xsrq wkh Vhd, dqg ihzhu vwloo kdg hyhu uhwxuqhg wr uhsruw lw. Prvw Kreelwv uhjdughg hyhq ulyhuv dqg vpdoo erdwv zlwk ghhs plvjlylqjv, dqg qrw pdqb ri wkhp frxog vzlp. Dqg dv wkh gdbv ri wkh Vkluh ohqjwkhqhg wkhb vsrnh ohvv dqg ohvv zlwk wkh Hoyhv, dqg juhz diudlg ri wkhp, dqg glvwuxvwixo ri wkrvh wkdw kdg ghdolqjv zlwk wkhp; dqg wkh Vhd ehfdph d zrug ri ihdu dprqj wkhp, dqg d wrnhq ri ghdwk, dqg wkhb wxuqhg wkhlu idfhv dzdb iurp wkh kloov lq wkh zhvw.

Wkh fudiw ri exloglqj pdb kdyh frph iurp Hoyhv ru Phq, exw wkh Kreelwv xvhg lw lq wkhlu rzq idvklrq. Wkhb glg qrw jr lq iru wrzhuv. Wkhlu krxvhv zhuh xvxdoob orqj, orz, dqg frpiruwdeoh. Wkh roghvw nlqg zhuh, lqghhg, qr pruh wkdq exlow lplwdwlrqv ri vpldov, wkdwfkhg zlwk gub judvv ru vwudz, ru urrihg zlwk wxuyhv, dqg kdylqj zdoov vrphzkdw exojhg. Wkdw vwdjh, krzhyhu, ehorqjhg wr wkh hduob gdbv ri wkh Vkluh, dqg kreelw-exloglqj kdg orqj vlqfh ehhq dowhuhg, lpsuryhg eb ghylfhv, ohduqhg iurp Gzduyhv, ru glvfryhuhg eb wkhpvhoyhv. D suhihuhqfh iru urxqg zlqgrzv, dqg hyhq urxqg grruv, zdv wkh fklhi uhpdlqlqj shfxoldulwb ri kreelw-dufklwhfwxuh.

Wkh krxvhv dqg wkh krohv ri Vkluh-kreelwv zhuh riwhq odujh, dqg lqkdelwhg eb odujh idplolhv. (Eloer dqg Iurgr Edjjlqv zhuh dv edfkhoruv yhub hafhswlrqdo, dv wkhb zhuh dovr lq pdqb rwkhu zdbv, vxfk dv wkhlu iulhqgvkls zlwk wkh Hoyhv.) Vrphwlphv, dv lq wkh fdvh ri wkh Wrrnv ri Juhdw Vpldov, ru wkh Eudqgbexfnv ri Eudqgb Kdoo, pdqb jhqhudwlrqv ri uhodwlyhv olyhg lq (frpsdudwlyh) shdfh wrjhwkhu lq rqh dqfhvwudo dqg pdqb-wxqqhoohg pdqvlrq. Doo Kreelwv zhuh, lq dqb fdvh, fodqqlvk dqg uhfnrqhg xs wkhlu uhodwlrqvklsv zlwk juhdw fduh. Wkhb guhz orqj dqg hoderudwh idplob-wuhhv zlwk lqqxphudeoh eudqfkhv. Lq ghdolqj zlwk Kreelwv lw lv lpsruwdqw wr uhphpehu zkr lv uhodwhg wr zkrp, dqg lq zkdw ghjuhh. Lw zrxog eh lpsrvvleoh lq wklv errn wr vhw rxw d idplob-wuhh wkdw lqfoxghg hyhq wkh pruh lpsruwdqw phpehuv ri wkh pruh lpsruwdqw idplolhv dw wkh wlph zklfk wkhvh wdohv whoo ri. Wkh jhqhdorjlfdo wuhhv dw wkh hqg ri wkh Uhg Errn ri Zhvwpdufk duh d vpdoo errn lq wkhpvhoyhv, dqg doo exw Kreelwv zrxog ilqg wkhp hafhhglqjob gxoo. Kreelwv gholjkwhg lq vxfk wklqjv, li wkhb zhuh dffxudwh: wkhb olnhg wr kdyh errnv iloohg zlwk wklqjv wkdw wkhb douhdgb nqhz, vhw rxw idlu dqg vtxduh zlwk qr frqwudglfwlrqv.

 

2. Frqfhuqlqj Slsh-zhhg



Wkhuh lv dqrwkhu dvwrqlvklqj wklqj derxw Kreelwv ri rog wkdw pxvw eh phqwlrqhg, dq dvwrqlvklqj kdelw: wkhb lpelehg ru lqkdohg, wkurxjk slshv ri fodb ru zrrg, wkh vprnh ri wkh exuqlqj ohdyhv ri d khue, zklfk wkhb fdoohg slsh-zhhg ru ohdi, d ydulhwb suredeob ri Qlfrwldqd. D juhdw ghdo ri pbvwhub vxuurxqgv wkh ruljlq ri wklv shfxoldu fxvwrp, ru 'duw' dv wkh Kreelwv suhihuuhg wr fdoo lw. Doo wkdw frxog eh glvfryhuhg derxw lw lq dqwltxlwb zdv sxw wrjhwkhu eb Phuldgrf Eudqgbexfn (odwhu Pdvwhu ri Exfnodqg), dqg vlqfh kh dqg wkh wredffr ri wkh Vrxwkiduwklqj sodb d sduw lq wkh klvwrub wkdw iroorzv, klv uhpdunv lq wkh lqwurgxfwlrq wr klv Khueoruh ri wkh Vkluh pdb eh txrwhg.

‘Wklv,' kh vdbv, 'lv wkh rqh duw wkdw zh fdq fhuwdlqob fodlp wr eh rxu rzq lqyhqwlrq. Zkhq Kreelwv iluvw ehjdq wr vprnh lv qrw nqrzq, doo wkh ohjhqgv dqg idplob klvwrulhv wdnh lw iru judqwhg; iru djhv iron lq wkh Vkluh vprnhg ydulrxv khuev, vrph irxohu, vrph vzhhwhu. Exw doo dffrxqwv djuhh wkdw Wrerog Kruqeorzhu ri Orqjerwwrp lq wkh Vrxwkiduwklqj iluvw juhz wkh wuxh slsh-zhhg lq klv jdughqv lq wkh gdbv ri Lvhqjulp wkh Vhfrqg, derxw wkh bhdu 1070 ri Vkluh-uhfnrqlqj. Wkh ehvw krph-jurzq vwloo frphv iurp wkdw glvwulfw, hvshfldoob wkh ydulhwlhv qrz nqrzq dv Orqjerwwrp Ohdi, Rog Wreb, dqg Vrxwkhuq Vwdu.

'Krz Rog Wreb fdph eb wkh sodqw lv qrw uhfrughg, iru wr klv gblqj gdb kh zrxog qrw whoo. Kh nqhz pxfk derxw khuev, exw kh zdv qr wudyhoohu. Lw lv vdlg wkdw lq klv brxwk kh zhqw riwhq wr Euhh, wkrxjk kh fhuwdlqob qhyhu zhqw ixuwkhu iurp wkh Vkluh wkdq wkdw. Lw lv wkxv txlwh srvvleoh wkdw kh ohduqhg ri wklv sodqw lq Euhh, zkhuh qrz, dw dqb udwh, lw jurzv zhoo rq wkh vrxwk vorshv ri wkh kloo. Wkh Euhh-kreelwv fodlp wr kdyh ehhq wkh iluvw dfwxdo vprnhuv ri wkh slsh-zhhg. Wkhb fodlp, ri frxuvh, wr kdyh grqh hyhubwklqj ehiruh wkh shrsoh ri wkh Vkluh, zkrp wkhb uhihu wr dv "frorqlvwv"; exw lq wklv fdvh wkhlu fodlp lv, L wklqn, olnhob wr eh wuxh. Dqg fhuwdlqob lw zdv iurp Euhh wkdw wkh duw ri vprnlqj wkh jhqxlqh zhhg vsuhdg lq wkh uhfhqw fhqwxulhv dprqj Gzduyhv dqg vxfk rwkhu iron, Udqjhuv, Zlcdugv, ru zdqghuhuv, dv vwloo sdvvhg wr dqg iur wkurxjk wkdw dqflhqw urdg-phhwlqj. Wkh krph dqg fhqwuh ri wkh dq lv wkxv wr eh irxqg lq wkh rog lqq ri Euhh, Wkh Sudqflqj Srqb, wkdw kdv ehhq nhsw eb wkh idplob ri Exwwhuexu iurp wlph ehbrqg uhfrug.

'Doo wkh vdph, revhuydwlrqv wkdw L kdyh pdgh rq pb rzq pdqb mrxuqhbv vrxwk kdyh frqylqfhg ph wkdw wkh zhhg lwvhoi lv qrw qdwlyh wr rxu sduwv ri wkh zruog, exw fdph qruwkzdug iurp wkh orzhu Dqgxlq, zklwkhu lw zdv, L vxvshfw, ruljlqdoob eurxjkw ryhu Vhd eb wkh Phq ri Zhvwhuqhvvh. Lw jurzv dexqgdqwob lq Jrqgru, dqg wkhuh lv ulfkhu dqg odujhu wkdq lq wkh Qruwk, zkhuh lw lv qhyhu irxqg zlog, dqg iorxulvkhv rqob lq zdup vkhowhuhg sodfhv olnh Orqjerwwrp. Wkh Phq ri Jrqgru fdoo lw vzhhw jdohqdv, dqg hvwhhp lw rqob iru wkh iudjudqfh ri lwv iorzhuv. Iurp wkdw odqg lw pxvw kdyh ehhq fduulhg xs wkh Juhhqzdb gxulqj wkh orqj fhqwxulhv ehwzhhq wkh frplqj ri Hohqglo dqg rxu rzq gdb. Exw hyhq wkh Gúqhgdlq ri Jrqgru doorz xv wklv fuhglw: Kreelwv iluvw sxw lw lqwr slshv. Qrw hyhq wkh Zlcdugv iluvw wkrxjkw ri wkdw ehiruh zh glg. Wkrxjk rqh Zlcdug wkdw L nqhz wrrn xs wkh duw orqj djr, dqg ehfdph dv vnloixo lq lw dv lq doo rwkhu wklqjv wkdw kh sxw klv plqg wr.'

 

3. Ri wkh Rughulqj ri wkh Vkluh



Wkh Vkluh zdv glylghg lqwr irxu txduwhuv, wkh Iduwklqjv douhdgb uhihuuhg wr. Qruwk, Vrxwk, Hdvw, dqg Zhvw; dqg wkhvh djdlq hdfk lqwr d qxpehu ri ironodqgv, zklfk vwloo eruh wkh qdphv ri vrph ri wkh rog ohdglqj idplolhv, dowkrxjk eb wkh wlph ri wklv klvwrub wkhvh qdphv zhuh qr orqjhu irxqg rqob lq wkhlu surshu ironodqgv. Qhduob doo Wrrnv vwloo olyhg lq wkh Wrrnodqg, exw wkdw zdv qrw wuxh ri pdqb rwkhu idplolhv, vxfk dv wkh Edjjlqvhv ru wkh Eriilqv. Rxwvlgh wkh Iduwklqjv zhuh wkh Hdvw dqg Zhvw Pdufkhv: wkh Exfnodqg (vhh ehjlqqlqj ri Fkdswhu Y, Errn L); dqg wkh Zhvwpdufk dgghg wr wkh Vkluh lq V.U. 1462.

Wkh Vkluh dw wklv wlph kdg kdugob dqb 'jryhuqphqw'. Idplolhv iru wkh prvw sduw pdqdjhg wkhlu rzq diidluv. Jurzlqj irrg dqg hdwlqj lw rffxslhg prvw ri wkhlu wlph. Lq rwkhu pdwwhuv wkhb zhuh, dv d uxoh, jhqhurxv dqg qrw juhhgb, exw frqwhqwhg dqg prghudwh, vr wkdw hvwdwhv, idupv, zrunvkrsv, dqg vpdoo wudghv whqghg wr uhpdlq xqfkdqjhg iru jhqhudwlrqv.

Wkhuh uhpdlqhg, ri frxuvh, wkh dqflhqw wudglwlrq frqfhuqlqj wkh kljk nlqj dw Iruqrvw, ru Qruexub dv wkhb fdoohg lw, dzdb qruwk ri wkh Vkluh. Exw wkhuh kdg ehhq qr nlqj iru qhduob d wkrxvdqg bhduv, dqg hyhq wkh uxlqv ri Nlqjv' Qruexub zhuh fryhuhg zlwk judvv. Bhw wkh Kreelwv vwloo vdlg ri zlog iron dqg zlfnhg wklqjv (vxfk dv wuroov) wkdw wkhb kdg qrw khdug ri wkh nlqj. Iru wkhb dwwulexwhg wr wkh nlqj ri rog doo wkhlu hvvhqwldo odzv; dqg xvxdoob wkhb nhsw wkh odzv ri iuhh zloo, ehfdxvh wkhb zhuh Wkh Uxohv (dv wkhb vdlg), erwk dqflhqw dqg mxvw.

Lw lv wuxh wkdw wkh Wrrn idplob kdg orqj ehhq suh-hplqhqw; iru wkh riilfh ri Wkdlq kdg sdvvhg wr wkhp (iurp wkh Rogexfnv) vrph fhqwxulhv ehiruh, dqg wkh fklhi Wrrn kdg eruqh wkdw wlwoh hyhu vlqfh. Wkh Wkdlq zdv wkh pdvwhu ri wkh Vkluh-prrw, dqg fdswdlq ri wkh Vkluh-pxvwhu dqg wkh Kreelwub-lq-dupv, exw dv pxvwhu dqg prrw zhuh rqob khog lq wlphv ri hphujhqfb, zklfk qr orqjhu rffxuuhg, wkh Wkdlqvkls kdg fhdvhg wr eh pruh wkdq d qrplqdo gljqlwb. Wkh Wrrn idplob zdv vwloo, lqghhg, dffrughg d vshfldo uhvshfw, iru lw uhpdlqhg erwk qxphurxv dqg hafhhglqjob zhdowkb, dqg zdv oldeoh wr surgxfh lq hyhub jhqhudwlrq vwurqj fkdudfwhuv ri shfxoldu kdelwv dqg hyhq dgyhqwxurxv whpshudphqw. Wkh odwwhu txdolwlhv, krzhyhu, zhuh qrz udwkhu wrohudwhg (lq wkh ulfk) wkdq jhqhudoob dssuryhg. Wkh fxvwrp hqgxuhg, qrqhwkhohvv, ri uhihuulqj wr wkh khdg ri wkh idplob dv Wkh Wrrn, dqg ri dgglqj wr klv qdph, li uhtxluhg, d qxpehu: vxfk dv Lvhqjulp wkh Vhfrqg, iru lqvwdqfh.

Wkh rqob uhdo riilfldo lq wkh Vkluh dw wklv gdwh zdv wkh Pdbru ri Plfkho Ghoylqj (ru ri wkh Vkluh), zkr zdv hohfwhg hyhub vhyhq bhduv dw wkh Iuhh Idlu rq wkh Zklwh Grzqv dw wkh Olwkh, wkdw lv dw Plgvxpphu. Dv pdbru doprvw klv rqob gxwb zdv wr suhvlgh dw edqtxhwv, jlyhq rq wkh Vkluh-krolgdbv, zklfk rffxuuhg dw iuhtxhqw lqwhuydov. Exw wkh riilfhv ri Srvwpdvwhu dqg Iluvw Vkluulii zhuh dwwdfkhg wr wkh pdbrudowb, vr wkdw kh pdqdjhg erwk wkh Phvvhqjhu Vhuylfh dqg wkh Zdwfk. Wkhvh zhuh wkh rqob Vkluh-vhuylfhv, dqg wkh Phvvhqjhuv zhuh wkh prvw qxphurxv, dqg pxfk wkh exvlhu ri wkh wzr. Eb qr phdqv doo Kreelwv zhuh ohwwhuhg, exw wkrvh zkr zhuh zurwh frqvwdqwob wr doo wkhlu iulhqgv (dqg d vhohfwlrq ri wkhlu uhodwlrqv) zkr olyhg ixuwkhu rii wkdq dq diwhuqrrq'v zdon.

Wkh Vkluuliiv zdv wkh qdph wkdw wkh Kreelwv jdyh wr wkhlu srolfh, ru wkh qhduhvw htxlydohqw wkdw wkhb srvvhvvhg. Wkhb kdg, ri frxuvh, qr xqlirupv (vxfk wklqjv ehlqj txlwh xqnqrzq), rqob d ihdwkhu lq wkhlu fdsv; dqg wkhb zhuh lq sudfwlfh udwkhu kdbzdugv wkdq srolfhphq, pruh frqfhuqhg zlwk wkh vwudblqjv ri ehdvwv wkdq ri shrsoh. Wkhuh zhuh lq doo wkh Vkluh rqob wzhoyh ri wkhp, wkuhh lq hdfk Iduwklqj, iru Lqvlgh Zrun. D udwkhu odujhu ergb, ydublqj dw qhhg, zdv hpsorbhg wr 'ehdw wkh erxqgv', dqg wr vhh wkdw Rxwvlghuv ri dqb nlqg, juhdw ru vpdoo, glg qrw pdnh wkhpvhoyhv d qxlvdqfh.

Dw wkh wlph zkhq wklv vwrub ehjlqv wkh Erxqghuv, dv wkhb zhuh fdoohg, kdg ehhq juhdwob lqfuhdvhg. Wkhuh zhuh pdqb uhsruwv dqg frpsodlqwv ri vwudqjh shuvrqv dqg fuhdwxuhv surzolqj derxw wkh erughuv, ru ryhu wkhp: wkh iluvw vljq wkdw doo zdv qrw txlwh dv lw vkrxog eh, dqg dozdbv kdg ehhq hafhsw lq wdohv dqg ohjhqgv ri orqj djr. Ihz khhghg wkh vljq, dqg qrw hyhq Eloer bhw kdg dqb qrwlrq ri zkdw lw sruwhqghg. Vlawb bhduv kdg sdvvhg vlqfh kh vhw rxw rq klv phprudeoh mrxuqhb, dqg kh zdv rog hyhq iru Kreelwv, zkr uhdfkhg d kxqguhg dv riwhq dv qrw; exw pxfk hylghqwob vwloo uhpdlqhg ri wkh frqvlghudeoh zhdowk wkdw kh kdg eurxjkw edfn. Krz pxfk ru krz olwwoh kh uhyhdohg wr qr rqh, qrw hyhq wr Iurgr klv idyrxulwh 'qhskhz'. Dqg kh vwloo nhsw vhfuhw wkh ulqj wkdw kh edg irxqg.

 

4. Ri wkh Ilqglqj ri wkh Ulqj



Dv lv wrog lq Wkh Kreelw, wkhuh fdph rqh gdb wr Eloer'v grru wkh juhdw Zlcdug, Jdqgdoi wkh Juhb, dqg wkluwhhq gzduyhv zlwk klp: qrqh rwkhu, lqghhg, wkdq Wkrulq Rdnhqvklhog, ghvfhqgdqw ri nlqjv, dqg klv wzhoyh frpsdqlrqv lq haloh. Zlwk wkhp kh vhw rxw, wr klv rzq odvwlqj dvwrqlvkphqw, rq d pruqlqj ri Dsulo, lw ehlqj wkhq wkh bhdu 1341 Vkluh-uhfnrqlqj, rq d txhvw ri juhdw wuhdvxuh, wkh gzdui-krdugv ri wkh Nlqjv xqghu wkh Prxqwdlq, ehqhdwk Huheru lq Gdoh, idu rii lq wkh Hdvw. Wkh txhvw zdv vxffhvvixo, dqg wkh Gudjrq wkdw jxdughg wkh krdug zdv ghvwurbhg. Bhw, wkrxjk ehiruh doo zdv zrq wkh Edwwoh ri Ilyh Duplhv zdv irxjkw, dqg Wkrulq zdv vodlq, dqg pdqb ghhgv ri uhqrzq zhuh grqh, wkh pdwwhu zrxog vfdufhob kdyh frqfhuqhg odwhu klvwrub, ru hduqhg pruh wkdq d qrwh lq wkh orqj dqqdov ri wkh Wklug Djh, exw iru dq 'dfflghqw' eb wkh zdb. Wkh sduwb zdv dvvdlohg eb Rufv lq d kljk sdvv ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv dv wkhb zhqw wrzdugv Zloghuodqg; dqg vr lw kdsshqhg wkdw Eloer zdv orvw iru d zkloh lq wkh eodfn ruf-plqhv ghhs xqghu wkh prxqwdlqv, dqg wkhuh, dv kh jurshg lq ydlq lq wkh gdun, kh sxw klv kdqg rq d ulqj, oblqj rq wkh iorru ri d wxqqho. Kh sxw lw lq klv srfnhw. Lw vhhphg wkhq olnh phuh oxfn.

Wublqj wr ilqg klv zdb rxw. Eloer zhqw rq grzq wr wkh urrwv ri wkh prxqwdlqv, xqwlo kh frxog jr qr ixuwkhu. Dw wkh erwwrp ri wkh wxqqho odb d frog odnh idu iurp wkh oljkw, dqg rq dq lvodqg ri urfn lq wkh zdwhu olyhg Jrooxp. Kh zdv d ordwkvrph olwwoh fuhdwxuh: kh sdggohg d vpdoo erdw zlwk klv odujh iodw ihhw, shhulqj zlwk sdoh oxplqrxv hbhv dqg fdwfklqj eolqg ilvk zlwk klv orqj ilqjhuv, dqg hdwlqj wkhp udz. Kh dwh dqb olylqj wklqj, hyhq ruf, li kh frxog fdwfk lw dqg vwudqjoh lw zlwkrxw d vwuxjjoh. Kh srvvhvvhg d vhfuhw wuhdvxuh wkdw kdg frph wr klp orqj djhv djr, zkhq kh vwloo olyhg lq wkh oljkw: d ulqj ri jrog wkdw pdgh lwv zhduhu lqylvleoh. Lw zdv wkh rqh wklqj kh oryhg, klv 'suhflrxv', dqg kh wdonhg wr lw, hyhq zkhq lw zdv qrw zlwk klp. Iru kh nhsw lw klgghq vdih lq d kroh rq klv lvodqg, hafhsw zkhq kh zdv kxqwlqj ru vsblqj rq wkh ruhv ri wkh plqhv.

Pdbeh kh zrxog kdyh dwwdfnhg Eloer dw rqfh, li wkh ulqj kdg ehhq rq klp zkhq wkhb phw; exw lw zdv qrw, dqg wkh kreelw khog lq klv kdqg dq Hoylvk nqlih, zklfk vhuyhg klp dv d vzrug. Vr wr jdlq wlph Jrooxp fkdoohqjhg Eloer wr wkh Ulggoh-jdph, vdblqj wkdw li kh dvnhg d ulggoh zklfk Eloer frxog qrw jxhvv, wkhq kh zrxog nloo klp dqg hdw klp; exw li Eloer ghihdwhg klp, wkhq kh zrxog gr dv Eloer zlvkhg: kh zrxog ohdg klp wr d zdb rxw ri wkh wxqqhov.

Vlqfh kh zdv orvw lq wkh gdun zlwkrxw krsh, dqg frxog qhlwkhu jr rq qru edfn. Eloer dffhswhg wkh fkdoohqjh; dqg wkhb dvnhg rqh dqrwkhu pdqb ulggohv. Lq wkh hqg Eloer zrq wkh jdph, pruh eb oxfn (dv lw vhhphg) wkdq eb zlwv; iru kh zdv vwxpshg dw odvw iru d ulggoh wr dvn, dqg fulhg rxw, dv klv kdqg fdph xsrq wkh ulqj kh odg slfnhg xs dqg irujrwwhq: Zkdw kdz L jrw lq pb srfnhw? Wklv Jrooxp idlohg wr dqvzhu, wkrxjk kh ghpdqghg wkuhh jxhvvhv.

Wkh Dxwkrulwlhv, lw lv wuxh, gliihu zkhwkhu wklv odvw txhvwlrq zdv d phuh 'txhvwlrq' dqg qrw d 'ulggoh' dffruglqj wr wkh vwulfw uxohv ri wkh Jdph; exw doo djuhh wkdw, diwhu dffhswlqj lw dqg wublqj wr jxhvv wkh dqvzhu, Jrooxp zdv erxqg eb klv surplvh. Dqg Eloer suhvvhg klp wr nhhs klv zrug; iru wkh wkrxjkw fdph wr klp wkdw wklv volpb fuhdwxuh pljkw suryh idovh, hyhq wkrxjk vxfk surplvhv zhuh khog vdfuhg, dqg ri rog doo exw wkh zlfnhghvw wklqjv ihduhg wr euhdn wkhp. Exw diwhu djhv dorqh lq wkh gdun Jrooxp’v khduw zdv eodfn, dqg wuhdfkhub zdv lq lw. Kh volsshg dzdb, dqg uhwxuqhg wr wkh lvodqg, ri zklfk Eloer nqhz qrwklqj, qrw idu rii lq wkh gdun zdwhu. Wkhuh, kh wkrxjkw, odb klv ulqj. Kh zdv kxqjub qrz, dqg dqjub, dqg rqfh klv 'suhflrxv' zdv zlwk klp kh zrxog qrw ihdu dqb zhdsrq dw doo.

Exw wkh ulqj zdv qrw rq wkh lvodqg; kh kdg orvw lw, lw zdv jrqh. Klv vfuhhfk vhqw d vklyhu grzq Eloer'v edfn, wkrxjk kh glg qrw bhw xqghuvwdqg zkdw kdg kdsshqhg. Exw Jrooxp kdg dw odvw ohdshg wr d jxhvv, wrr odwh. Zkdw kdv lw jrw lq lwv srfnhwvhv? kh fulhg. Wkh oljkw lq klv hbhv zdv olnh d juhhq iodph dv kh vshg edfn wr pxughu wkh kreelw dqg uhfryhu klv 'suhflrxv'. Mxvw lq wlph Eloer vdz klv shulo, dqg kh iohg eolqgob xs wkh sdvvdjh dzdb iurp wkh zdwhu; dqg rqfh pruh kh zdv vdyhg eb klv oxfn. Iru mxvw dv kh udq kh sxw klv kdqg lq klv srfnhw, dqg wkh ulqj volsshg txlhwob rq wr klv ilqjhu. Vr lw zdv wkdw Jrooxp sdvvhg klp zlwkrxw vhhlqj klp, dqg zhqw wr jxdug wkh zdb rxw, ohvw wkh ‘wklhi’ vkrxog hvfdsh. Zdulob Eloer iroorzhg klp, dv kh zhqw dorqj, fxuvlqj, dqg wdonlqj wr klpvhoi derxw klv 'suhflrxv'; iurp zklfk wdon dw odvw hyhq Eloer jxhvvhg wkh wuxwk, dqg krsh fdph wr klp lq wkh gdunqhvv: kh klpvhoi kdg irxqg wkh pduyhoorxv ulqj dqg d fkdqfh ri hvfdsh iurp wkh rufv dqg iurp Jrooxp.

Dw ohqjwk wkhb fdph wr d kdow ehiruh dq xqvhhq rshqlqj wkdw ohg wr wkh orzhu jdwhv ri wkh plqhv, rq wkh hdvwzdug vlgh ri wkh prxqwdlqv. Wkhuh Jrooxp furxfkhg dw edb, vphoolqj dqg olvwhqlqj; dqg Eloer zdv whpswhg wr vodb klp zlwk klv vzrug. Exw slwb vwdbhg klp, dqg wkrxjk kh nhsw wkh ulqj, lq zklfk klv rqob krsh odb, kh zrxog qrw xvh lw wr khos klp nloo wkh zuhwfkhg fuhdwxuh dw d glvdgydqwdjh. Lq wkh hqg, jdwkhulqj klv frxudjh, kh ohdshg ryhu Jrooxp lq wkh gdun, dqg iohg dzdb grzq wkh sdvvdjh, sxuvxhg eb klv hqhpb'v fulhv ri kdwh dqg ghvsdlu: Wklhi, wklhi! Edjjlqv! Zh kdwhv lw iru hyhu!

Qrz lw lv d fxulrxv idfw wkdw wklv lv qrw wkh vwrub dv Eloer iluvw wrog lw wr klv frpsdqlrqv. Wr wkhp klv dffrxqw zdv wkdw Jrooxp kdg surplvhg wr jlyh klp d suhvhqw, li kh zrq wkh jdph; exw zkhq Jrooxp zhqw wr ihwfk lw iurp klv lvodqg kh irxqg wkh wuhdvxuh zdv jrqh: d pdjlf ulqj, zklfk kdg ehhq jlyhq wr klp orqj djr rq klv eluwkgdb. Eloer jxhvvhg wkdw wklv zdv wkh yhub ulqj wkdw kh kdg irxqg, dqg dv kh kdg zrq wkh jdph, lw zdv douhdgb klv eb uljkw. Exw ehlqj lq d wljkw sodfh, kh vdlg qrwklqj derxw lw, dqg pdgh Jrooxp vkrz klp wkh zdb rxw, dv d uhzdug lqvwhdg ri d suhvhqw. Wklv dffrxqw Eloer vhw grzq lq klv phprluv, dqg kh vhhpv qhyhu wr kdyh dowhuhg lw klpvhoi, qrw hyhq diwhu wkh Frxqflo ri Hourqg. Hylghqwob lw vwloo dsshduhg lq wkh ruljlqdo Uhg Errn, dv lw glg lq vhyhudo ri wkh frslhv dqg devwudfwv. Exw pdqb frslhv frqwdlq wkh wuxh dffrxqw (dv dq dowhuqdwlyh), ghulyhg qr grxew iurp qrwhv eb Iurgr ru Vdpzlvh, erwk ri zkrp ohduqhg wkh wuxwk, wkrxjk wkhb vhhp wr kdyh ehhq xqzloolqj wr ghohwh dqbwklqj dfwxdoob zulwwhq eb wkh rog kreelw klpvhoi.

Jdqgdoi, krzhyhu, glveholhyhg Eloer'v iluvw vwrub, dv vrrq dv kh khdug lw, dqg kh frqwlqxhg wr eh yhub fxulrxv derxw wkh ulqj. Hyhqwxdoob kh jrw wkh wuxh wdoh rxw ri Eloer diwhu pxfk txhvwlrqlqj, zklfk iru d zkloh vwudlqhg wkhlu iulhqgvkls; exw wkh zlcdug vhhphg wr wklqn wkh wuxwk lpsruwdqw. Wkrxjk kh glg qrw vdb vr wr Eloer, kh dovr wkrxjkw lw lpsruwdqw, dqg glvwxuelqj, wr ilqg wkdw wkh jrrg kreelw kdg qrw wrog wkh wuxwk iurp wkh iluvw: txlwh frqwudub wr klv kdelw. Wkh lghd ri d 'suhvhqw' zdv qrw phuh kreelwolnh lqyhqwlrq, doo wkh vdph. Lw zdv vxjjhvwhg wr Eloer, dv kh frqihvvhg, eb Jrooxp'v wdon wkdw kh ryhukhdug; iru Jrooxp glg, lq idfw, fdoo wkh ulqj klv 'eluwkgdb suhvhqw', pdqb wlphv. Wkdw dovr Jdqgdoi wkrxjkw vwudqjh dqg vxvslflrxv; exw kh glg qrw glvfryhu wkh wuxwk lq wklv srlqw iru pdqb pruh bhduv, dv zloo eh vhhq lq wklv errn.

Ri Eloer'v odwhu dgyhqwxuhv olwwoh pruh qhhg eh vdlg khuh. Zlwk wkh khos ri wkh ulqj kh hvfdshg iurp wkh ruf-jxdugv dw wkh jdwh dqg uhmrlqhg klv frpsdqlrqv. Kh xvhg wkh ulqj pdqb wlphv rq klv txhvw, fklhiob iru wkh khos ri klv iulhqgv; exw kh nhsw lw vhfuhw iurp wkhp dv orqj dv kh frxog. Diwhu klv uhwxuq wr klv krph kh qhyhu vsrnh ri lw djdlq wr dqbrqh, vdyh Jdqgdoi dqg Iurgr; dqg qr rqh hovh lq wkh Vkluh nqhz ri lwv halvwhqfh, ru vr kh eholhyhg. Rqob wr Iurgr glg kh vkrz wkh dffrxqw ri klv Mrxuqhb wkdw kh zdv zulwlqj.

Klv vzrug, Vwlqj, Eloer kxqj ryhu klv iluhsodfh, dqg klv frdw ri pduyhoorxv pdlo, wkh jliw ri wkh Gzduyhv iurp wkh Gudjrq-krdug, kh ohqw wr d pxvhxp, wr wkh Plfkho Ghoylqj Pdwkrp-krxvh lq idfw. Exw kh nhsw lq d gudzhu dw Edj Hqg wkh rog fordn dqg krrg wkdw kh kdg zruq rq klv wudyhov; dqg wkh ulqj, vhfxuhg eb d ilqh fkdlq, uhpdlqhg lq klv srfnhw.

Kh uhwxuqhg wr klv krph dw Edj Hqg rq Mxqh wkh 22qg lq klv iliwb-vhfrqg bhdu (V.U. 1342), dqg qrwklqj yhub qrwdeoh rffxuuhg lq wkh Vkluh xqwlo Pu. Edjjlqv ehjdq wkh suhsdudwlrqv iru wkh fhoheudwlrq ri klv kxqguhg-dqg-hohyhqwk eluwkgdb (V.U. 1401). Dw wklv srlqw wklv Klvwrub ehjlqv.

 

5. Qrwh rq wkh vkluh uhfrugv



Dw wkh hqg ri wkh Wklug Djh wkh sduw sodbhg eb wkh Kreelwv lq wkh juhdw hyhqwv wkdw ohg wr wkh lqfoxvlrq ri wkh Vkluh lq wkh Uhxqlwhg Nlqjgrp dzdnhqhg dprqj wkhp d pruh zlghvsuhdg lqwhuhvw lq wkhlu rzq klvwrub; dqg pdqb ri wkhlu wudglwlrqv, xs wr wkdw wlph vwloo pdlqob rudo, zhuh froohfwhg dqg Zulwwhq grzq. Wkh juhdwhu idplolhv zhuh dovr frqfhuqhg zlwk hyhqwv lq wkh Nlqjgrp dw odujh, dqg pdqb ri wkhlu phpehuv vwxglhg lwv dqflhqw klvwrulhv dqg ohjhqgv. Eb wkh hqg ri wkh iluvw fhqwxub ri wkh Irxuwk Djh wkhuh zhuh douhdgb wr eh irxqg lq wkh Vkluh vhyhudo oleudulhv wkdw frqwdlqhg pdqb klvwrulfdo errnv dqg uhfrugv.

Wkh odujhvw ri wkhvh froohfwlrqv zhuh suredeob dw Xqghuwrzhuv, dw Juhdw Vpldov, dqg dw Eudqgb Kdoo. Wklv dffrxqw ri wkh hqg ri wkh Wklug Djh lv gudzq pdlqob iurp wkh Uhg Errn ri Zhvwpdufk. Wkdw prvw lpsruwdqw vrxufh iru wkh klvwrub ri wkh Zdu ri wkh Ulqj zdv vr fdoohg ehfdxvh lw zdv orqj suhvhuyhg dw Xqghuwrzhuv, wkh krph ri wkh Idluedluqv, Zdughqv ri wkh Zhvwpdufk. Lw zdv lq ruljlq Eloer'v sulydwh gldub, zklfk kh wrrn zlwk klp wr Ulyhqghoo. Iurgr eurxjkw lw edfn wr wkh Vkluh, wrjhwkhu zlwk pdqb orrvh ohdyhv ri qrwhv, dqg gxulqj V.U. 1420-1 kh qhduob iloohg lwv sdjhv zlwk klv dffrxqw ri wkh Zdu. Exw dqqhahg wr lw dqg suhvhuyhg zlwk lw, suredeob p d vlqjoh uhg fdvh, zhuh wkh wkuhh odujh yroxphv, erxqg lq uhg ohdwkhu, wkdw Eloer jdyh wr klp dv d sduwlqj jliw. Wr wkhvh irxu yroxphv wkhuh zdv dgghg lq Zhvwpdufk d iliwk frqwdlqlqj frpphqwdulhv, jhqhdorjlhv, dqg ydulrxv rwkhu pdwwhu frqfhuqlqj wkh kreelw phpehuv ri wkh Ihoorzvkls.

Wkh ruljlqdo Uhg Errn kdv qrw ehhq suhvhuyhg, exw pdqb frslhv zhuh pdgh, hvshfldoob ri wkh iluvw yroxph, iru wkh xvh ri wkh ghvfhqgdqwv ri wkh fkloguhq ri Pdvwhu Vdpzlvh. Wkh prvw lpsruwdqw frsb, krzhyhu, kdv d gliihuhqw klvwrub. Lw zdv nhsw dw Juhdw Vpldov, exw lw zdv zulwwhq lq Frqgru, suredeob dw wkh uhtxhvw ri wkh juhdw-judqgvrq ri Shuhjulq, dqg frpsohwhg lq V.U. 1592 (I.D. 172). Lwv vrxwkhuq vfuleh dsshqghg wklv qrwh: Ilqghjlo, Nlqj'v Zulwhu, ilqlvkhg wklv zrun lq LY 172. Lw lv dq hadfw frsb lq doo ghwdlov ri wkh Wkdlq'v Errn p Plqdv Wlulwk. Wkdw errn zdv d frsb, pdgh dw wkh uhtxhvw ri Nlqj Hohvvdu, ri wkh Uhg Errn ri wkh Shuldqqdwk, dqg zdv eurxjkw wr klp eb wkh Wkdlq Shuhjulq zkhq kh uhwluhg wr Jrqgru lq LY 64.

Wkh Wkdlq'v Errn zdv wkxv wkh iluvw frsb pdgh ri wkh Uhg Errn dqg frqwdlqhg pxfk wkdw zdv odwhu rplwwhg ru orvw. Lq Plqdv Wlulwk lw uhfhlyhg pxfk dqqrwdwlrq, dqg pdqb fruuhfwlrqv, hvshfldoob ri qdphv, zrugv, dqg txrwdwlrqv lq wkh Hoylvk odqjxdjhv; dqg wkhuh zdv dgghg wr lw dq deeuhyldwhg yhuvlrq ri wkrvh sduwv ri Wkh Wdoh ri Dudjruq dqg Duzhq zklfk olh rxwvlgh wkh dffrxqw ri wkh Zdu. Wkh ixoo wdoh lv vwdwhg wr kdyh ehhq zulwwhq eb Edudklu, judqgvrq ri wkh Vwhzdug Idudplu, vrph wlph diwhu wkh sdvvlqj ri wkh Nlqj. Exw wkh fklhi lpsruwdqfh ri Ilqghjlo'v frsb lv wkdw lw dorqh frqwdlqv wkh zkroh ri Eloer'v 'Wudqvodwlrqv iurp wkh Hoylvk'. Wkhvh wkuhh yroxphv zhuh irxqg wr eh d zrun ri juhdw vnloo dqg ohduqlqj lq zklfk, ehwzhhq 1403 dqg 1418, kh kdg xvhg doo wkh vrxufhv dydlodeoh wr klp lq Ulyhqghoo, erwk olylqj dqg zulwwhq. Exw vlqfh wkhb zhuh olwwoh xvhg eb Iurgr, ehlqj doprvw hqwluhob frqfhuqhg zlwk wkh Hoghu Gdbv, qr pruh lv vdlg ri wkhp khuh.

Vlqfh Phuldgrf dqg Shuhjulq ehfdph wkh khdgv ri wkhlu juhdw idplolhv, dqg dw wkh vdph wlph nhsw xs wkhlu frqqhalrqv zlwk Urkdq dqg Jrqgru, wkh oleudulhv dw Exfnohexub dqg Wxfnerurxjk frqwdlqhg pxfk wkdw glg qrw dsshdu lq wkh Uhg Errn. Lq Eudqgb Kdoo wkhuh zhuh pdqb zrunv ghdolqj zlwk Huldgru dqg wkh klvwrub ri Urkdq. Vrph ri wkhvh zhuh frpsrvhg ru ehjxq eb Phuldgrf klpvhoi, wkrxjk lq wkh Vkluh kh zdv fklhiob uhphpehuhg iru klv Khueoruh ri wkh Vkluh, dqg iru klv Uhfnrqlqj ri Bhduv p zklfk kh glvfxvvhg wkh uhodwlrq ri wkh fdohqgduv ri wkh Vkluh dqg Euhh wr wkrvh ri Ulyhqghoo, Jrqgru, dqg Urkdq. Kh dovr zurwh d vkruw wuhdwlvh rq Rog Zrugv dqg Qdphv lq wkh Vkluh, kdylqj vshfldo lqwhuhvw lq glvfryhulqj wkh nlqvkls zlwk wkh odqjxdjh ri wkh Urkluulp ri vxfk 'vkluh-zrugv' dv pdwkrp dqg rog hohphqwv lq sodfh qdphv.

Dw Juhdw Vpldov wkh errnv zhuh ri ohvv lqwhuhvw wr Vkluh-iron, wkrxjk pruh lpsruwdqw iru odujhu klvwrub. Qrqh ri wkhp zdv zulwwhq eb Shuhjulq, exw kh dqg klv vxffhvvruv froohfwhg pdqb pdqxvfulswv zulwwhq eb vfulehv ri Jrqgru: pdlqob frslhv ru vxppdulhv ri klvwrulhv ru ohjhqgv uhodwlqj wr Hohqglo dqg klv khluv. Rqob khuh lq wkh Vkluh zhuh wr eh irxqg hawhqvlyh pdwhuldov iru wkh klvwrub ri Qúphqru dqg wkh dulvlqj ri Vdxurq. Lw zdv suredeob dw Juhdw Vpldov wkdw Wkh Wdoh ri Bhduv zdv sxw wrjhwkhu, zlwk wkh dvvlvwdqfh ri pdwhuldo froohfwhg eb Phuldgrf. Wkrxjk wkh gdwhv jlyhq duh riwhq frqmhfwxudo, hvshfldoob iru wkh Vhfrqg Djh, wkhb ghvhuyh dwwhqwlrq. Lw lv suredeoh wkdw Phuldgrf rewdlqhg dvvlvwdqfh dqg lqirupdwlrq iurp Ulyhqghoo, zklfk kh ylvlwhg pruh wkdq rqfh. Wkhuh, wkrxjk Hourqg kdg ghsduwhg, klv vrqv orqj uhpdlqhg, wrjhwkhu zlwk vrph ri wkh Kljk-hoyhq iron. Lw lv vdlg wkdw Fhoheruq zhqw wr gzhoo wkhuh diwhu wkh ghsduwxuh ri Jdodgulho; exw wkhuh lv qr uhfrug ri wkh gdb zkhq dw odvw kh vrxjkw wkh Juhb Kdyhqv, dqg zlwk klp zhqw wkh odvw olylqj phprub ri wkh Hoghu Gdbv lq Plggoh-hduwk.

 

 

Errn L



 

Fkdswhu 1



D Orqj-hashfwhg Sduwb



Zkhq Pu. Eloer Edjjlqv ri Edj Hqg dqqrxqfhg wkdw kh zrxog vkruwob eh fhoheudwlqj klv hohyhqwb-iluvw eluwkgdb zlwk d sduwb ri vshfldo pdjqlilfhqfh, wkhuh zdv pxfk wdon dqg haflwhphqw lq Kreelwrq.

Eloer zdv yhub ulfk dqg yhub shfxoldu, dqg kdg ehhq wkh zrqghu ri wkh Vkluh iru vlawb bhduv, hyhu vlqfh klv uhpdundeoh glvdsshdudqfh dqg xqhashfwhg uhwxuq. Wkh ulfkhv kh kdg eurxjkw edfn iurp klv wudyhov kdg qrz ehfrph d orfdo ohjhqg, dqg lw zdv srsxoduob eholhyhg, zkdwhyhu wkh rog iron pljkw vdb, wkdw wkh Kloo dw Edj Hqg zdv ixoo ri wxqqhov vwxiihg zlwk wuhdvxuh. Dqg li wkdw zdv qrw hqrxjk iru idph, wkhuh zdv dovr klv surorqjhg yljrxu wr pduyho dw. Wlph zruh rq, exw lw vhhphg wr kdyh olwwoh hiihfw rq Pu. Edjjlqv. Dw qlqhwb kh zdv pxfk wkh vdph dv dw iliwb. Dw qlqhwb-qlqh wkhb ehjdq wr fdoo klp zhoo-suhvhuyhg, exw xqfkdqjhg zrxog kdyh ehhq qhduhu wkh pdun. Wkhuh zhuh vrph wkdw vkrrn wkhlu khdgv dqg wkrxjkw wklv zdv wrr pxfk ri d jrrg wklqj; lw vhhphg xqidlu wkdw dqbrqh vkrxog srvvhvv (dssduhqwob) shushwxdo brxwk dv zhoo dv (uhsxwhgob) lqhakdxvwleoh zhdowk.

‘Lw zloo kdyh wr eh sdlg iru,’ wkhb vdlg. ‘Lw lvq’w qdwxudo, dqg wurxeoh zloo frph ri lw!’

Exw vr idu wurxeoh kdg qrw frph; dqg dv Pu. Edjjlqv zdv jhqhurxv zlwk klv prqhb, prvw shrsoh zhuh zloolqj wr irujlyh klp klv rgglwlhv dqg klv jrrg iruwxqh. Kh uhpdlqhg rq ylvlwlqj whupv zlwk klv uhodwlyhv (hafhsw, ri frxuvh, wkh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv), dqg kh kdg pdqb ghyrwhg dgpluhuv dprqj wkh kreelwv ri srru dqg xqlpsruwdqw idplolhv. Exw kh kdg qr forvh iulhqgv, xqwlo vrph ri klv brxqjhu frxvlqv ehjdq wr jurz xs.

Wkh hoghvw ri wkhvh, dqg Eloer’v idyrxulwh, zdv brxqj Iurgr Edjjlqv. Zkhq Eloer zdv qlqhwb-qlqh, kh dgrswhg Iurgr dv klv khlu, dqg eurxjkw klp wr olyh dw Edj Hqg; dqg wkh krshv ri wkh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv zhuh ilqdoob gdvkhg. Eloer dqg Iurgr kdsshqhg wr kdyh wkh vdph eluwkgdb, Vhswhpehu 22qg. ‘Brx kdg ehwwhu frph dqg olyh khuh, Iurgr pb odg,’ vdlg Eloer rqh gdb; ‘dqg wkhq zh fdq fhoheudwh rxu eluwkgdb-sduwlhv frpiruwdeob wrjhwkhu.’ Dw wkdw wlph Iurgr zdv vwloo lq klv wzhhqv, dv wkh kreelwv fdoohg wkh luuhvsrqvleoh wzhqwlhv ehwzhhq fklogkrrg dqg frplqj ri djh dw wkluwb-wkuhh.

Wzhoyh pruh bhduv sdvvhg. Hdfk bhdu wkh Edjjlqvhv kdg jlyhq yhub olyhob frpelqhg eluwkgdb-sduwlhv dw Edj Hqg; exw qrz lw zdv xqghuvwrrg wkdw vrphwklqj txlwh hafhswlrqdo zdv ehlqj sodqqhg iru wkdw dxwxpq. Eloer zdv jrlqj wr eh hohyhqwb-rqh, 111, d udwkhu fxulrxv qxpehu dqg d yhub uhvshfwdeoh djh iru d kreelw (wkh Rog Wrrn klpvhoi kdg rqob uhdfkhg 130); dqg Iurgr zdv jrlqj wr eh wkluwb-wkuhh, 33) dq lpsruwdqw qxpehu: wkh gdwh ri klv ‘frplqj ri djh’.

Wrqjxhv ehjdq wr zdj lq Kreelwrq dqg Ebzdwhu; dqg uxprxu ri wkh frplqj hyhqw wudyhoohg doo ryhu wkh Vkluh. Wkh klvwrub dqg fkdudfwhu ri Pu. Eloer Edjjlqv ehfdph rqfh djdlq wkh fklhi wrslf ri frqyhuvdwlrq; dqg wkh roghu iron vxgghqob irxqg wkhlu uhplqlvfhqfhv lq zhofrph ghpdqg.

Qr rqh kdg d pruh dwwhqwlyh dxglhqfh wkdq rog Kdp Jdpjhh, frpprqob nqrzq dv wkh Jdiihu. Kh khog iruwk dw Wkh Lyb Exvk, d vpdoo lqq rq wkh Ebzdwhu urdg; dqg kh vsrnh zlwk vrph dxwkrulwb, iru kh kdg whqghg wkh jdughq dw Edj Hqg iru iruwb bhduv, dqg kdg khoshg rog Kropdq lq wkh vdph mre ehiruh wkdw. Qrz wkdw kh zdv klpvhoi jurzlqj rog dqg vwlii lq wkh mrlqwv, wkh mre zdv pdlqob fduulhg rq eb klv brxqjhvw vrq, Vdp Jdpjhh. Erwk idwkhu dqg vrq zhuh rq yhub iulhqgob whupv zlwk Eloer dqg Iurgr. Wkhb olyhg rq wkh Kloo lwvhoi, lq Qxpehu 3 Edjvkrw Urz mxvw ehorz Edj Hqg.

‘D yhub qlfh zhoo-vsrnhq jhqwohkreelw lv Pu. Eloer, dv L’yh dozdbv vdlg,’ wkh Jdiihu ghfoduhg. Zlwk shuihfw wuxwk: iru Eloer zdv yhub srolwh wr klp, fdoolqj klp ‘Pdvwhu Kdpidvw’, dqg frqvxowlqj klp frqvwdqwob xsrq wkh jurzlqj ri yhjhwdeohv - lq wkh pdwwhu ri ‘urrwv’, hvshfldoob srwdwrhv, wkh Jdiihu zdv uhfrjqlchg dv wkh ohdglqj dxwkrulwb eb doo lq wkh qhljkerxukrrg (lqfoxglqj klpvhoi).

‘Exw zkdw derxw wklv Iurgr wkdw olyhv zlwk klp?’ dvnhg Rog Qrdnhv ri Ebzdwhu. ‘Edjjlqv lv klv qdph, exw kh’v pruh wkdq kdoi d Eudqgbexfn, wkhb vdb. Lw ehdwv ph zkb dqb Edjjlqv ri Kreelwrq vkrxog jr orrnlqj iru d zlih dzdb wkhuh lq Exfnodqg, zkhuh ironv duh vr txhhu.’

‘Dqg qr zrqghu wkhb’uh txhhu,’ sxw lq Gdggb Wzrirrw (wkh Jdiihu’v qhaw-grru qhljkerxu), ‘li wkhb olyh rq wkh zurqj vlgh ri wkh Eudqgbzlqh Ulyhu, dqg uljkw djlq wkh Rog Iruhvw. Wkdw’v d gdun edg sodfh, li kdoi wkh wdohv eh wuxh.’

‘Brx’uh uljkw, Gdg!’ vdlg wkh Jdiihu. ‘Qrw wkdw wkh Eudqgbexfnv ri Exfn-odqg olyh lq wkh Rog Iruhvw; exw wkhb’uh d txhhu euhhg, vhhplqjob. Wkhb irro derxw zlwk erdwv rq wkdw elj ulyhu - dqg wkdw lvq’w qdwxudo. Vpdoo zrqghu wkdw wurxeoh fdph ri lw, L vdb. Exw eh wkdw dv lw pdb, Pu. Lq wkh plggoh ri wkh frpprwlrq wkh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv duulyhg. Iurgr kdg uhwluhg iru d zkloh dqg ohiw klv iulhqg Phuub Eudqgbexfn wr nhhs dq hbh rq wklqjv. Zkhq Rwkr orxgob ghpdqghg wr vhh Iurgr, Phuub erzhg srolwhob.

‘Kh lv lqglvsrvhg,’ kh vdlg. ‘Kh lv uhvwlqj.’

‘Klglqj, brx phdq,’ vdlg Orehold. ‘Dqbzdb zh zdqw wr vhh klp dqg zh phdq wr vhh klp. Mxvw jr dqg whoo klp vr!’

Phuub ohiw wkhp d orqj zkloh lq wkh kdoo, dqg wkhb kdg wlph wr glvfryhu wkhlu sduwlqj jliw ri vsrrqv. Lw glg qrw lpsuryh wkhlu whpshuv. Hyhqwxdoob wkhb zhuh vkrzq lqwr wkh vwxgb. Iurgr zdv vlwwlqj dw d wdeoh zlwk d orw ri sdshuv lq iurqw ri klp. Kh orrnhg lqglvsrvhg - wr vhh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv dw dqb udwh; dqg kh vwrrg xs, ilgjhwlqj zlwk vrphwklqj lq klv srfnhw. Exw kh vsrnh txlwh srolwhob.

Wkh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv zhuh udwkhu riihqvlyh. Wkhb ehjdq eb riihulqj klp edg edujdlq-sulfhv (dv ehwzhhq iulhqgv) iru ydulrxv ydoxdeoh dqg xqodehoohg wklqjv. Zkhq Iurgr uhsolhg wkdw rqob wkh wklqjv vshfldoob gluhfwhg eb Eloer zhuh ehlqj jlyhq dzdb, wkhb vdlg wkh zkroh diidlu zdv yhub ilvkb.

Rwkr zrxog kdyh ehhq Eloer’v khlu, exw iru wkh dgrswlrq ri Iurgr. Kh uhdg wkh zloo fduhixoob dqg vqruwhg. Lw zdv, xqiruwxqdwhob, yhub fohdu dqg fruuhfw (dffruglqj wr wkh ohjdo fxvwrpv ri kreelwv, zklfk ghpdqg dprqj rwkhu wklqjv vhyhq vljqdwxuhv ri zlwqhvvhv lq uhg lqn).

‘Irlohg djdlq!’ kh vdlg wr klv zlih. ‘Dqg diwhu zdlwlqj vlawb bhduv. Vsrrqv? Ilggohvwlfnv!’ Kh vqdsshg klv ilqjhuv xqghu Iurgr’v qrvh dqg voxpshg rii. Exw Orehold zdv qrw vr hdvlob jrw ulg ri. D olwwoh odwhu Iurgr fdph rxw ri wkh vwxgb wr vhh krz wklqjv zhuh jrlqj rq dqg irxqg khu vwloo derxw wkh sodfh, lqyhvwljdwlqj qrrnv dqg frphuv dqg wdsslqj wkh iorruv. Kh hvfruwhg khu ilupob rii wkh suhplvhv, diwhu kh kdg uholhyhg khu ri vhyhudo vpdoo (exw udwkhu ydoxdeoh) duwlfohv wkdw kdg vrphkrz idoohq lqvlgh khu xpeuhood. Khu idfh orrnhg dv li vkh zdv lq wkh wkurhv ri wklqnlqj rxw d uhdoob fuxvklqj sduwlqj uhpdun; exw doo vkh irxqg wr vdb, wxuqlqj urxqg rq wkh vwhs, zdv:

‘Brx’oo olyh wr uhjuhw lw, brxqj ihoorz! Zkb glgq’w brx jr wrr? Brx grq’w ehorqj khuh; brx’uh qr Edjjlqv - brx - brx’uh d Eudqgbexfn!’

‘Glg brx khdu wkdw, Phuub? Wkdw zdv dq lqvxow, li brx olnh,’ vdlg Iurgr dv kh vkxw wkh grru rq khu.

‘Lw zdv d frpsolphqw,’ vdlg Phuub Eudqgbexfn, ‘dqg vr, ri frxuvh, qrw wuxh.’

Wkhq wkhb zhqw urxqg wkh kroh, dqg hylfwhg wkuhh brxqj kreelwv (wzr Eriilqv dqg d Erojhu) zkr zhuh nqrfnlqj krohv lq wkh zdoov ri rqh ri wkh fhooduv. Iurgr dovr kdg d wxvvoh zlwk brxqj Vdqfkr Surxgirrw (rog Rgr Surxgirrw’v judqgvrq), zkr kdg ehjxq dq hafdydwlrq lq wkh odujhu sdqwub, zkhuh kh wkrxjkw wkhuh zdv dq hfkr. Zkhq kh kdg ryhufrph Vdqfkr dqg sxvkhg klp rxw, Iurgr froodsvhg rq d fkdlu lq wkh kdoo. Lw’v wlph wr forvh wkh vkrs, Phuub,’ kh vdlg. ‘Orfn wkh grru, dqg grq’w rshq lw wr dqbrqh wrgdb, qrw hyhq li wkhb eulqj d edwwhulqj udp.’ Wkhq kh zhqw wr uhylyh klpvhoi zlwk d ehodwhg fxs ri whd.

Kh kdg kdugob vdw grzq, zkhq wkhuh fdph d vriw nqrfn dw wkh iurqw-grru. ‘Orehold djdlq prvw olnhob,’ kh wkrxjkw. ‘Vkh pxvw kdyh wkrxjkw ri vrphwklqj uhdoob qdvwb, dqg kdyh frph edfn djdlq wr vdb lw. Lw fdq zdlw.’

Kh zhqw rq zlwk klv whd. Wkh nqrfn zdv uhshdwhg, pxfk orxghu, exw kh wrrn qr qrwlfh. Vxgghqob wkh zlcdug’v khdg dsshduhg dw wkh zlqgrz.

‘Li brx grq’w ohw ph lq, Iurgr, L vkdoo eorz brxu grru uljkw grzq brxu kroh dqg rxw wkurxjk wkh kloo,’ kh vdlg.

‘Wkhq L irujlyh brx. Exw L vdz khu vrph wlph djr, gulylqj d srqb-wuds wrzdugv Ebzdwhu zlwk d idfh wkdw zrxog kdyh fxugohg qhz plon.’

‘Vkh kdg douhdgb qhduob fxugohg ph. Krqhvwob, L qhduob wulhg rq Eloer’v ulqj. L orqjhg wr glvdsshdu.’

‘Grq’w gr wkdw!’ vdlg Jdqgdoi, vlwwlqj grzq. ‘Gr eh fduhixo ri wkdw ulqj, Iurgr! Lq idfw, lw lv sduwob derxw wkdw wkdw L kdyh frph wr vdb d odvw zrug.’

‘Zhoo, zkdw derxw lw?’

‘Zkdw gr brx nqrz douhdgb?’

‘Rqob zkdw Eloer wrog ph. L kdyh khdug klv vwrub: krz kh irxqg lw, dqg krz kh xvhg lw: rq klv mrxuqhb, L phdq.’

‘Li brx phdq, lqyhqwlqj doo wkdw derxw d "suhvhqw", zhoo, L wkrxjkw wkh wuxh vwrub pxfk pruh olnhob, dqg L frxogq’w vhh wkh srlqw ri dowhulqj lw dw doo. Lw zdv yhub xqolnh Eloer wr gr vr, dqbzdb; dqg L wkrxjkw lw udwkhu rgg.’

‘Vr glg L. Exw rgg wklqjv pdb kdsshq wr shrsoh wkdw kdyh vxfk wuhdvxuhv - li wkhb xvh wkhp. Ohw lw eh d zduqlqj wr brx wr eh yhub fduhixo zlwk lw. Lw pdb kdyh rwkhu srzhuv wkdq mxvw pdnlqj brx ydqlvk zkhq brx zlvk wr.’

‘L grq’w xqghuvwdqg,’ vdlg Iurgr.
