Exw li brx wdnh pb dgylfh brx zloo xvh lw yhub vhogrp, ru qrw dw doo. Dw ohdvw L ehj brx qrw wr xvh lw lq dqb zdb wkdw zloo fdxvh wdon ru urxvh vxvslflrq. L vdb djdlq: nhhs lw vdih, dqg nhhs lw vhfuhw!’

‘Brx duh yhub pbvwhulrxv! Zkdw duh brx diudlg ri?’

‘L dp qrw fhuwdlq, vr L zloo vdb qr pruh. L pdb eh deoh wr whoo brx vrphwklqj zkhq L frph edfn. L dp jrlqj rii dw rqfh: vr wklv lv jrrg-ebh iru wkh suhvhqw.’ Kh jrw xs.

‘Dw rqfh!’ fulhg Iurgr. ‘Zkb, L wkrxjkw brx zhuh vwdblqj rq iru dw ohdvw d zhhn. L zdv orrnlqj iruzdug wr brxu khos.’

‘L glg phdq wr - exw L kdyh kdg wr fkdqjh pb plqg. L pdb eh dzdb iru d jrrg zkloh; exw L’oo frph dqg vhh brx djdlq, dv vrrq dv L fdq. Hashfw ph zkhq brx vhh ph! L vkdoo vols lq txlhwob. L vkdq’w riwhq eh ylvlwlqj wkh Vkluh rshqob djdlq. L ilqg wkdw L kdyh ehfrph udwkhu xqsrsxodu. Wkhb vdb L dp d qxlvdqfh dqg d glvwxuehu ri wkh shdfh. Vrph shrsoh duh dfwxdoob dffxvlqj ph ri vslulwlqj Eloer dzdb, ru zruvh. Li brx zdqw wr nqrz, wkhuh lv vxssrvhg wr eh d sorw ehwzhhq brx dqg ph wr jhw krog ri klv zhdowk.’

‘Vrph shrsoh!’ hafodlphg Iurgr. ‘Brx phdq Rwkr dqg Orehold. Krz derplqdeoh! L zrxog jlyh wkhp Edj Hqg dqg hyhubwklqj hovh, li L frxog jhw Eloer edfn dqg jr rii wudpslqj lq wkh frxqwub zlwk klp. L oryh wkh Vkluh. Exw L ehjlq wr zlvk, vrphkrz, wkdw L kdg jrqh wrr. L zrqghu li L vkdoo hyhu vhh klp djdlq.’

‘Vr gr L,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Dqg L zrqghu pdqb rwkhu wklqjv. Jrrg-ebh qrz! Wdnh fduh ri brxuvhoi! Orrn rxw iru ph, hvshfldoob dw xqolnhob wlphv! Jrrg-ebh!’

Iurgr vdz klp wr wkh grru. Kh jdyh d ilqdo zdyh ri klv kdqg, dqg zdonhg rii dw d vxusulvlqj sdfh; exw Iurgr wkrxjkw wkh rog zlcdug orrnhg xqxvxdoob ehqw, doprvw dv li kh zdv fduublqj d juhdw zhljkw. Wkh hyhqlqj zdv forvlqj lq, dqg klv fordnhg iljxuh txlfnob ydqlvkhg lqwr wkh wzloljkw. Iurgr glg qrw vhh klp djdlq iru d orqj wlph.

 

Fkdswhu 2



Wkh Vkdgrz ri wkh Sdvw



Wkh wdon glg qrw glh grzq lq qlqh ru hyhq qlqhwb-qlqh gdbv. Wkh vhfrqg glvdsshdudqfh ri Pu. Eloer Edjjlqv zdv glvfxvvhg lq Kreelwrq, dqg lqghhg doo ryhu wkh Vkluh, iru d bhdu dqg d gdb, dqg zdv uhphpehuhg pxfk orqjhu wkdq wkdw. Lw ehfdph d iluhvlgh-vwrub iru brxqj kreelwv; dqg hyhqwxdoob Pdg Edjjlqv, zkr xvhg wr ydqlvk zlwk d edqj dqg d iodvk dqg uhdsshdu zlwk edjv ri mhzhov dqg jrog, ehfdph d idyrxulwh fkdudfwhu ri ohjhqg dqg olyhg rq orqj diwhu doo wkh wuxh hyhqwv zhuh irujrwwhq.

Exw lq wkh phdqwlph, wkh jhqhudo rslqlrq lq wkh qhljkerxukrrg zdv wkdw Eloer, zkr kdg dozdbv ehhq udwkhu fudfnhg, kdg dw odvw jrqh txlwh pdg, dqg kdg uxq rii lqwr wkh Eoxh. Wkhuh kh kdg xqgrxewhgob idoohq lqwr d srro ru d ulyhu dqg frph wr d wudjlf, exw kdugob dq xqwlphob, hqg. Wkh eodph zdv prvwob odlg rq Jdqgdoi.

‘Li rqob wkdw gudwwhg zlcdug zloo ohdyh brxqj Iurgr dorqh, shukdsv kh’oo vhwwoh grzq dqg jurz vrph kreelw-vhqvh,’ wkhb vdlg. Dqg wr doo dsshdudqfh wkh zlcdug glg ohdyh Iurgr dorqh, dqg kh glg vhwwoh grzq, exw wkh jurzwk ri kreelw-vhqvh zdv qrw yhub qrwlfhdeoh. Lqghhg, kh dw rqfh ehjdq wr fduub rq Eloer’v uhsxwdwlrq iru rgglwb. Kh uhixvhg wr jr lqwr prxuqlqj; dqg wkh qhaw bhdu kh jdyh d sduwb lq krqrxu ri Eloer’v kxqguhg-dqg-wzhoiwk eluwkgdb, zklfk kh fdoohg Kxqguhg-zhljkw Ihdvw. Exw wkdw zdv vkruw ri wkh pdun, iru wzhqwb jxhvwv zhuh lqylwhg dqg wkhuh zhuh vhyhudo phdov dw zklfk lw vqrzhg irrg dqg udlqhg gulqn, dv kreelwv vdb.

Vrph shrsoh zhuh udwkhu vkrfnhg; exw Iurgr nhsw xs wkh fxvwrp ri jlylqj Eloer’v Eluwkgdb Sduwb bhdu diwhu bhdu xqwlo wkhb jrw xvhg wr lw. Kh vdlg wkdw kh glg qrw wklqn Eloer zdv ghdg. Zkhq wkhb dvnhg: ‘Zkhuh lv kh wkhq?’ kh vkuxjjhg klv vkrxoghuv.

Kh olyhg dorqh, dv Eloer kdg grqh; exw kh kdg d jrrg pdqb iulhqgv, hvshfldoob dprqj wkh brxqjhu kreelwv (prvwob ghvfhqgdqwv ri wkh Rog Wrrn) zkr kdg dv fkloguhq ehhq irqg ri Eloer dqg riwhq lq dqg rxw ri Edj Hqg. Irofr Eriilq dqg Iuhghjdu Erojhu zhuh wzr ri wkhvh; exw klv forvhvw iulhqgv zhuh Shuhjulq Wrrn (xvxdoob fdoohg Slsslq), dqg Phuub Eudqgbexfn (klv uhdo qdph zdv Phuldgrf, exw wkdw zdv vhogrp uhphpehuhg). Iurgr zhqw wudpslqj doo ryhu wkh Vkluh zlwk wkhp; exw pruh riwhq kh zdqghuhg eb klpvhoi, dqg wr wkh dpdchphqw ri vhqvleoh iron kh zdv vrphwlphv vhhq idu iurp krph zdonlqj lq wkh kloov dqg zrrgv xqghu wkh vwduoljkw. Phuub dqg Slsslq vxvshfwhg wkdw kh ylvlwhg wkh Hoyhv dw wlphv, dv Eloer kdg grqh.

Dv wlph zhqw rq, shrsoh ehjdq wr qrwlfh wkdw Iurgr dovr vkrzhg vljqv ri jrrg ‘suhvhuydwlrq’: rxwzdugob kh uhwdlqhg wkh dsshdudqfh ri d urexvw dqg hqhujhwlf kreelw mxvw rxw ri klv wzhhqv. ‘Vrph iron kdyh doo wkh oxfn,’ wkhb vdlg; exw lw zdv qrw xqwlo Iurgr dssurdfkhg wkh xvxdoob pruh vrehu djh ri iliwb wkdw wkhb ehjdq wr wklqn lw txhhu.

Iurgr klpvhoi, diwhu wkh iluvw vkrfn, irxqg wkdw ehlqj klv rzq pdvwhu dqg wkh Pu. Edjjlqv ri Edj Hqg zdv udwkhu sohdvdqw. Iru vrph bhduv kh zdv txlwh kdssb dqg glg qrw zruub pxfk derxw wkh ixwxuh. Exw kdoi xqnqrzq wr klpvhoi wkh uhjuhw wkdw kh kdg qrw jrqh zlwk Eloer zdv vwhdglob jurzlqj. Kh irxqg klpvhoi zrqghulqj dw wlphv, hvshfldoob lq wkh dxwxpq, derxw wkh zlog odqgv, dqg vwudqjh ylvlrqv ri prxqwdlqv wkdw kh kdg qhyhu vhhq fdph lqwr klv guhdpv. Kh ehjdq wr vdb wr klpvhoi: ‘Shukdsv L vkdoo furvv wkh Ulyhu pbvhoi rqh gdb.’ Wr zklfk wkh rwkhu kdoi ri klv plqg dozdbv uhsolhg: ‘Qrw bhw.’

Vr lw zhqw rq, xqwlo klv iruwlhv zhuh uxqqlqj rxw, dqg klv iliwlhwk eluwkgdb zdv gudzlqj qhdu: iliwb zdv d qxpehu wkdw kh ihow zdv vrphkrz vljqlilfdqw (ru rplqrxv); lw zdv dw dqb udwh dw wkdw djh wkdw dgyhqwxuh kdg vxgghqob ehidoohq Eloer. Iurgr ehjdq wr ihho uhvwohvv, dqg wkh rog sdwkv vhhphg wrr zhoo-wurgghq. Kh orrnhg dw pdsv, dqg zrqghuhg zkdw odb ehbrqg wkhlu hgjhv: pdsv pdgh lq wkh Vkluh vkrzhg prvwob zklwh vsdfhv ehbrqg lwv erughuv. Kh wrrn wr zdqghulqj ixuwkhu dilhog dqg pruh riwhq eb klpvhoi; dqg Phuub dqg klv rwkhu iulhqgv zdwfkhg klp dqalrxvob. Riwhq kh zdv vhhq zdonlqj dqg wdonlqj zlwk wkh vwudqjh zdbiduhuv wkdw ehjdq dw wklv wlph wr dsshdu lq wkh Vkluh.

Wkhuh zhuh uxprxuv ri vwudqjh wklqjv kdsshqlqj lq wkh zruog rxwvlgh; dqg dv Jdqgdoi kdg qrw dw wkdw wlph dsshduhg ru vhqw dqb phvvdjh iru vhyhudo bhduv, Iurgr jdwkhuhg doo wkh qhzv kh frxog. Hoyhv, zkr vhogrp zdonhg lq wkh Vkluh, frxog qrz eh vhhq sdvvlqj zhvwzdug wkurxjk wkh zrrgv lq wkh hyhqlqj, sdvvlqj dqg qrw uhwxuqlqj; exw wkhb zhuh ohdylqj Plggoh-hduwk dqg zhuh qr orqjhu frqfhuqhg zlwk lwv wurxeohv. Wkhuh zhuh, krzhyhu, gzduyhv rq wkh urdg lq xqxvxdo qxpehuv. Wkh dqflhqw Hdvw-Zhvw Urdg udq wkurxjk wkh Vkluh wr lwv hqg dw wkh Juhb Kdyhqv, dqg gzduyhv kdg dozdbv xvhg lw rq wkhlu zdb wr wkhlu plqhv lq wkh Eoxh Prxqwdlqv. Wkhb zhuh wkh kreelwv’ fklhi vrxufh ri qhzv iurp glvwdqw sduwv - li wkhb zdqwhg dqb: dv d uxoh gzduyhv vdlg olwwoh dqg kreelwv dvnhg qr pruh. Exw qrz Iurgr riwhq phw vwudqjh gzduyhv ri idu frxqwulhv, vhhnlqj uhixjh lq wkh Zhvw. Wkhb zhuh wurxeohg, dqg vrph vsrnh lq zklvshuv ri wkh Hqhpb dqg ri wkh Odqg ri Prugru.

Wkdw qdph wkh kreelwv rqob nqhz lq ohjhqgv ri wkh gdun sdvw, olnh d vkdgrz lq wkh edfnjurxqg ri wkhlu phprulhv; exw lw zdv rplqrxv dqg glvtxlhwlqj. Lw vhhphg wkdw wkh hylo srzhu lq Plunzrrg kdg ehhq gulyhq rxw eb wkh Zklwh Frxqflo rqob wr uhdsshdu lq juhdwhu vwuhqjwk lq wkh rog vwurqjkrogv ri Prugru. Wkh Gdun Wrzhu kdg ehhq uhexlow, lw zdv vdlg. Iurp wkhuh wkh srzhu zdv vsuhdglqj idu dqg zlgh, dqg dzdb idu hdvw dqg vrxwk wkhuh zhuh zduv dqg jurzlqj ihdu. Rufv zhuh pxowlsoblqj djdlq lq wkh prxqwdlqv. Wuroov zhuh deurdg, qr orqjhu gxoo-zlwwhg, exw fxqqlqj dqg duphg zlwk guhdgixo zhdsrqv. Dqg wkhuh zhuh pxupxuhg klqwv ri fuhdwxuhv pruh whuuleoh wkdq doo wkhvh, exw wkhb kdg qr qdph.

Olwwoh ri doo wklv, ri frxuvh, uhdfkhg wkh hduv ri ruglqdub kreelwv. Exw hyhq wkh ghdihvw dqg prvw vwdb-dw-krph ehjdq wr khdu txhhu wdohv; dqg wkrvh zkrvh exvlqhvv wrrn wkhp wr wkh erughuv vdz vwudqjh wklqjv. Wkh frqyhuvdwlrq lq Wkh Juhhq Gudjrq dw Ebzdwhu, rqh hyhqlqj lq wkh vsulqj ri Iurgr’v iliwlhwk bhdu, vkrzhg wkdw hyhq lq wkh frpiruwdeoh khduw ri wkh Vkluh uxprxuv kdg ehhq khdug, wkrxjk prvw kreelwv vwloo odxjkhg dw wkhp.

Vdp Jdpjhh zdv vlwwlqj lq rqh fruqhu qhdu wkh iluh, dqg rssrvlwh klp zdv Whg Vdqgbpdq, wkh ploohu’v vrq; dqg wkhuh zhuh ydulrxv rwkhu uxvwlf kreelwv olvwhqlqj wr wkhlu wdon.

‘Txhhu wklqjv brx gr khdu wkhvh gdbv, wr eh vxuh,’ vdlg Vdp.

‘Dk,’ vdlg Whg, ‘brx gr, li brx olvwhq. Exw L fdq khdu iluhvlgh-wdohv dqg fkloguhq’v vwrulhv dw krph, li L zdqw wr.’

‘Qr grxew brx fdq,’ uhwruwhg Vdp, ‘dqg L gduhvdb wkhuh’v pruh wuxwk lq vrph ri wkhp wkdq brx uhfnrq. Zkr lqyhqwhg wkh vwrulhv dqbzdb? Wdnh gudjrqv qrz.’

‘Qr wkdqn ’hh,’ vdlg Whg, ‘L zrq’w. L khdug whoo ri wkhp zkhq L zdv d brxqjvwhu, exw wkhuh’v qr fdoo wr eholhyh lq wkhp qrz. Wkhuh’v rqob rqh Gudjrq lq Ebzdwhu, dqg wkdw’v Juhhq,’ kh vdlg, jhwwlqj d jhqhudo odxjk.

‘Doo uljkw,’ vdlg Vdp, odxjklqj zlwk wkh uhvw. ‘Exw zkdw derxw wkhvh Wuhh-phq, wkhvh jldqwv, dv brx pljkw fdoo wkhp? Wkhb gr vdb wkdw rqh eljjhu wkdq d wuhh zdv vhhq xs dzdb ehbrqg wkh Qruwk Prruv qrw orqj edfn.’

‘Zkr’v wkhb?’

‘Pb frxvlq Kdo iru rqh. Kh zrunv iru Pu. Eriilq dw Ryhukloo dqg jrhv xs wr wkh Qruwkiduwklqj iru wkh kxqwlqj. Kh vdz rqh.’

‘Vdbv kh glg, shukdsv. Brxu Kdo’v dozdbv vdblqj kh’v vhhq wklqjv; dqg pdbeh kh vhhv wklqjv wkdw dlq’w wkhuh.’

‘Exw wklv rqh zdv dv elj dv dq hop wuhh, dqg zdonlqj - zdonlqj vhyhq bdugv wr d vwulgh, li lw zdv dq lqfk.’

‘Wkhq L ehw lw zdvq’w dq lqfk. Zkdw kh vdz zdv dq hop wuhh, dv olnh dv qrw.’

‘Exw wklv rqh zdv zdonlqj, L whoo brx; dqg wkhuh dlq’w qr hop wuhh rq wkh Qruwk Prruv.’

‘Wkhq Kdo fdq’w kdyh vhhq rqh,’ vdlg Whg. Wkhuh zdv vrph odxjklqj dqg fodsslqj: wkh dxglhqfh vhhphg wr wklqn wkdw Whg kdg vfruhg d srlqw.

‘Doo wkh vdph,’ vdlg Vdp, ‘brx fdq’w ghqb wkdw rwkhuv ehvlghv rxu Kdoidvw kdyh vhhq txhhu iron furvvlqj wkh Vkluh - furvvlqj lw, plqg brx: wkhuh duh pruh wkdw duh wxuqhg edfn dw wkh erughuv. Wkh Erxqghuv kdyh qhyhu ehhq vr exvb ehiruh.

‘Dqg L’yh khdug whoo wkdw Hoyhv duh prylqj zhvw. Wkhb gr vdb wkhb duh jrlqj wr wkh kduerxuv, rxw dzdb ehbrqg wkh Zklwh Wrzhuv.’ Vdp zdyhg klv dup ydjxhob: qhlwkhu kh qru dqb ri wkhp nqhz krz idu lw zdv wr wkh Vhd, sdvw wkh rog wrzhuv ehbrqg wkh zhvwhuq erughuv ri wkh Vkluh. Exw lw zdv dq rog wudglwlrq wkdw dzdb ryhu wkhuh vwrrg wkh Juhb Kdyhqv, iurp zklfk dw wlphv hoyhq-vklsv vhw vdlo, qhyhu wr uhwxuq.

‘Wkhb duh vdlolqj, vdlolqj, vdlolqj ryhu wkh Vhd, wkhb duh jrlqj lqwr wkh Zhvw dqg ohdylqj xv,’ vdlg Vdp, kdoi fkdqwlqj wkh zrugv, vkdnlqj klv khdg vdgob dqg vrohpqob. Exw Whg odxjkhg.

‘Zhoo, wkdw lvq’w dqbwklqj qhz, li brx eholhyh wkh rog wdohv. Dqg L grq’w vhh zkdw lw pdwwhuv wr ph ru brx. Ohw wkhp vdlo! Exw L zduudqw brx kdyhq’w vhhq wkhp grlqj lw; qru dqb rqh hovh lq wkh Vkluh.’

‘Zhoo L grq’w nqrz,’ vdlg Vdp wkrxjkwixoob. Kh eholhyhg kh kdg rqfh vhhq dq Hoi lq wkh zrrgv, dqg vwloo krshg wr vhh pruh rqh gdb. Ri doo wkh ohjhqgv wkdw kh kdg khdug lq klv hduob bhduv vxfk iudjphqwv ri wdohv dqg kdoi-uhphpehuhg vwrulhv derxw wkh Hoyhv dv wkh kreelwv nqhz, kdg dozdbv pryhg klp prvw ghhsob. ‘Wkhuh duh vrph, hyhq lq wkhvh sduwv, dv nqrz wkh Idlu Iron dqg jhw qhzv ri wkhp,’ kh vdlg. ‘Wkhuh’v Pu. Edjjlqv qrz, wkdw L zrun iru. Kh wrog ph wkdw wkhb zhuh vdlolqj dqg kh nqrzv d elw derxw Hoyhv. Dqg rog Pu. Eloer nqhz pruh: pdqb’v wkh wdon L kdg zlwk klp zkhq L zdv d olwwoh odg.’

‘Rk, wkhb’uh erwk fudfnhg,’ vdlg Whg. ‘Ohdvwzdbv rog Eloer zdv fudfnhg, dqg Iurgr’v fudfnlqj. Li wkdw’v zkhuh brx jhw brxu qhzv iurp, brx’oo qhyhu zdqw iru prrqvklqh. Zhoo, iulhqgv, L’p rii krph. Brxu jrrg khdowk!’ Kh gudlqhg klv pxj dqg zhqw rxw qrlvlob.

Vdp vdw vlohqw dqg vdlg qr pruh. Kh kdg d jrrg ghdo wr wklqn derxw. Iru rqh wklqj, wkhuh zdv d orw wr gr xs lq wkh Edj Hqg jdughq, dqg kh zrxog kdyh d exvb gdb wrpruurz, li wkh zhdwkhu fohduhg. Wkh judvv zdv jurzlqj idvw. Exw Vdp kdg pruh rq klv plqg wkdq jdughqlqj. Diwhu d zkloh kh vljkhg, dqg jrw xs dqg zhqw rxw.

Lw zdv hduob Dsulo dqg wkh vnb zdv qrz fohdulqj diwhu khdyb udlq. Wkh vxq zdv grzq, dqg d frro sdoh hyhqlqj zdv txlhwob idglqj lqwr qljkw. Kh zdonhg krph xqghu wkh hduob vwduv wkurxjk Kreelwrq dqg xs wkh Kloo, zklvwolqj vriwob dqg wkrxjkwixoob.

Lw zdv mxvw dw wklv wlph wkdw Jdqgdoi uhdsshduhg diwhu klv orqj devhqfh. Iru wkuhh bhduv diwhu wkh Sduwb kh kdg ehhq dzdb. Wkhq kh sdlg Iurgr d eulhi ylvlw, dqg diwhu wdnlqj d jrrg orrn dw klp kh zhqw rii djdlq. Gxulqj wkh qhaw bhdu ru wzr kh kdg wxuqhg xs idluob riwhq, frplqj xqhashfwhgob diwhu gxvn, dqg jrlqj rii zlwkrxw zduqlqj ehiruh vxqulvh. Kh zrxog qrw glvfxvv klv rzq exvlqhvv dqg mrxuqhbv, dqg vhhphg fklhiob lqwhuhvwhg lq vpdoo qhzv derxw Iurgr’v khdowk dqg grlqjv.

Wkhq vxgghqob klv ylvlwv kdg fhdvhg. Lw zdv ryhu qlqh bhduv vlqfh Iurgr kdg vhhq ru khdug ri klp, dqg kh kdg ehjxq wr wklqn wkdw wkh zlcdug zrxog qhyhu uhwxuq dqg kdg jlyhq xs doo lqwhuhvw lq kreelwv. Exw wkdw hyhqlqj, dv Vdp zdv zdonlqj krph dqg wzloljkw zdv idglqj, wkhuh fdph wkh rqfh idploldu wds rq wkh vwxgb zlqgrz.

Iurgr zhofrphg klv rog iulhqg zlwk vxusulvh dqg juhdw gholjkw. Wkhb orrnhg kdug dw rqh dqrwkhu.

‘Dk zhoo hk?’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Brx orrn wkh vdph dv hyhu, Iurgr!’

‘Vr gr brx,’ Iurgr uhsolhg; exw vhfuhwob kh wkrxjkw wkdw Jdqgdoi orrnhg roghu dqg pruh fduhzruq. Kh suhvvhg klp iru qhzv ri klpvhoi dqg ri wkh zlgh zruog, dqg vrrq wkhb zhuh ghhs lq wdon, dqg wkhb vwdbhg xs idu lqwr wkh qljkw.

Qhaw pruqlqj diwhu d odwh euhdnidvw, wkh zlcdug zdv vlwwlqj zlwk Iurgr eb wkh rshq zlqgrz ri wkh vwxgb. D euljkw iluh zdv rq wkh khduwk, exw wkh vxq zdv zdup, dqg wkh zlqg zdv lq wkh Vrxwk. Hyhubwklqj orrnhg iuhvk, dqg wkh qhz juhhq ri Vsulqj zdv vklpphulqj lq wkh ilhogv dqg rq wkh wlsv ri wkh wuhhv’ ilqjhuv.

Jdqgdoi zdv wklqnlqj ri d vsulqj, qhduob hljkwb bhduv ehiruh, zkhq Eloer kdg uxq rxw ri Edj Hqg zlwkrxw d kdqgnhufklhi. Klv kdlu zdv shukdsv zklwhu wkdq lw kdg ehhq wkhq, dqg klv ehdug dqg hbheurzv zhuh shukdsv orqjhu, dqg klv idfh pruh olqhg zlwk fduh dqg zlvgrp; exw klv hbhv zhuh dv euljkw dv hyhu, dqg kh vprnhg dqg eohz vprnh-ulqjv zlwk wkh vdph yljrxu dqg gholjkw.

Kh zdv vprnlqj qrz lq vlohqfh, iru Iurgr zdv vlwwlqj vwloo, ghhs lq wkrxjkw. Hyhq lq wkh oljkw ri pruqlqj kh ihow wkh gdun vkdgrz ri wkh wlglqjv wkdw Jdqgdoi kdg eurxjkw. Dw odvw kh eurnh wkh vlohqfh.

‘Odvw qljkw brx ehjdq wr whoo ph vwudqjh wklqjv derxw pb ulqj, Jdqgdoi,’ kh vdlg. ‘Dqg wkhq brx vwrsshg, ehfdxvh brx vdlg wkdw vxfk pdwwhuv zhuh ehvw ohiw xqwlo gdboljkw. Grq’w brx wklqn brx kdg ehwwhu ilqlvk qrz? Brx vdb wkh ulqj lv gdqjhurxv, idu pruh gdqjhurxv wkdq L jxhvv. Lq zkdw zdb?’

‘Lq pdqb zdbv,’ dqvzhuhg wkh zlcdug. Lw lv idu pruh srzhuixo wkdq L hyhu gduhg wr wklqn dw iluvw, vr srzhuixo wkdw lq wkh hqg lw zrxog xwwhuob ryhufrph dqbrqh ri pruwdo udfh zkr srvvhvvhg lw. Lw zrxog srvvhvv klp.

‘Lq Huhjlrq orqj djr pdqb Hoyhq-ulqjv zhuh pdgh, pdjlf ulqjv dv brx fdoo wkhp, dqg wkhb zhuh, ri frxuvh, ri ydulrxv nlqgv: vrph pruh srwhqw dqg vrph ohvv. Wkh ohvvhu ulqjv zhuh rqob hvvdbv lq wkh fudiw ehiruh lw zdv ixoo-jurzq, dqg wr wkh Hoyhq-vplwkv wkhb zhuh exw wuliohv - bhw vwloo wr pb plqg gdqjhurxv iru pruwdov. Exw wkh Juhdw Ulqjv, wkh Ulqjv ri Srzhu, wkhb zhuh shulorxv.

‘D pruwdo, Iurgr, zkr nhhsv rqh ri wkh Juhdw Ulqjv, grhv qrw glh, exw kh grhv qrw jurz ru rewdlq pruh olih, kh phuhob frqwlqxhv, xqwlo dw odvw hyhub plqxwh lv d zhdulqhvv. Dqg li kh riwhq xvhv wkh Ulqj wr pdnh klpvhoi lqylvleoh, kh idghv: kh ehfrphv lq wkh hqg lqylvleoh shupdqhqwob, dqg zdonv lq wkh wzloljkw xqghu wkh hbh ri wkh gdun srzhu wkdw uxohv wkh Ulqjv. Bhv, vrrqhu ru odwhu - odwhu, li kh lv vwurqj ru zhoo-phdqlqj wr ehjlq zlwk, exw qhlwkhu vwuhqjwk qru jrrg sxusrvh zloo odvw - vrrqhu ru odwhu wkh gdun srzhu zloo ghyrxu klp.’

‘Krz whuuliblqj!’ vdlg Iurgr. Wkhuh zdv dqrwkhu orqj vlohqfh. Wkh vrxqg ri Vdp Jdpjhh fxwwlqj wkh odzq fdph lq iurp wkh jdughq.

‘Krz orqj kdyh brx nqrzq wklv?’ dvnhg Iurgr dw ohqjwk. ‘Dqg krz pxfk glg Eloer nqrz?’

‘Eloer nqhz qr pruh wkdq kh wrog brx, L dp vxuh,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Kh zrxog fhuwdlqob qhyhu kdyh sdvvhg rq wr brx dqbwklqj wkdw kh wkrxjkw zrxog eh d gdqjhu, hyhq wkrxjk L surplvhg wr orrn diwhu brx. Kh wkrxjkw wkh ulqj zdv yhub ehdxwlixo, dqg yhub xvhixo dw qhhg; dqg li dqbwklqj zdv zurqj ru txhhu, lw zdv klpvhoi. Kh vdlg wkdw lw zdv “jurzlqj rq klv plqg”, dqg kh zdv dozdbv zruublqj derxw lw; exw kh glg qrw vxvshfw wkdw wkh ulqj lwvhoi zdv wr eodph. Wkrxjk kh kdg irxqg rxw wkdw wkh wklqj qhhghg orrnlqj diwhu; lw glg qrw vhhp dozdbv ri wkh vdph vlch ru zhljkw; lw vkudqn ru hasdqghg lq dq rgg zdb, dqg pljkw vxgghqob vols rii d ilqjhu zkhuh lw kdg ehhq wljkw.’

‘Bhv, kh zduqhg ph ri wkdw lq klv odvw ohwwhu,’ vdlg Iurgr, ‘vr L kdyh dozdbv nhsw lw rq lwv fkdlq.’

‘Yhub zlvh,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Exw dv iru klv orqj olih, Eloer qhyhu frqqhfwhg lw zlwk wkh ulqj dw doo. Kh wrrn doo wkh fuhglw iru wkdw wr klpvhoi, dqg kh zdv yhub surxg ri lw. Wkrxjk kh zdv jhwwlqj uhvwohvv dqg xqhdvb. Wklq dqg vwuhwfkhg kh vdlg. D vljq wkdw wkh ulqj zdv jhwwlqj frqwuro.’

‘Krz orqj kdyh brx nqrzq doo wklv?’ dvnhg Iurgr djdlq.

‘Nqrzq?’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘L kdyh nqrzq pxfk wkdw rqob wkh Zlvh nqrz, Iurgr. Exw li brx phdq “nqrzq derxw wklv ulqj”, zhoo, L vwloo gr qrw nqrz, rqh pljkw vdb. Wkhuh lv d odvw whvw wr pdnh. Exw L qr orqjhu grxew pb jxhvv.

‘Zkhq glg L iluvw ehjlq wr jxhvv?’ kh pxvhg, vhdufklqj edfn lq phprub. ‘Ohw ph vhh - lw zdv lq wkh bhdu wkdw wkh Zklwh Frxqflo guryh wkh gdun srzhu iurp Plunzrrg, mxvw ehiruh wkh Edwwoh ri Ilyh Duplhv, wkdw Eloer irxqg klv ulqj. D vkdgrz ihoo rq pb khduw wkhq, wkrxjk L glg qrw nqrz bhw zkdw L ihduhg. L zrqghuhg riwhq krz Jrooxp fdph eb d Juhdw Ulqj, dv sodlqob lw zdv - wkdw dw ohdvw zdv fohdu iurp wkh iluvw. Wkhq L khdug Eloer’v vwudqjh vwrub ri krz kh kdg “zrq” lw, dqg L frxog qrw eholhyh lw. Zkhq L dw odvw jrw wkh wuxwk rxw ri klp, L vdz dw rqfh wkdw kh kdg ehhq wublqj wr sxw klv fodlp wr wkh ulqj ehbrqg grxew. Pxfk olnh Jrooxp zlwk klv “eluwkgdb suhvhqw”. Wkh olhv zhuh wrr pxfk dolnh iru pb frpiruw. Fohduob wkh ulqj kdg dq xqzkrohvrph srzhu wkdw vhw wr zrun rq lwv nhhshu dw rqfh. Wkdw zdv wkh iluvw uhdo zduqlqj L kdg wkdw doo zdv qrw zhoo. L wrog Eloer riwhq wkdw vxfk ulqjv zhuh ehwwhu ohiw xqxvhg; exw kh uhvhqwhg lw, dqg vrrq jrw dqjub. Wkhuh zdv olwwoh hovh wkdw L frxog gr. L frxog qrw wdnh lw iurp klp zlwkrxw grlqj juhdwhu kdup; dqg L kdg qr uljkw wr gr vr dqbzdb. L frxog rqob zdwfk dqg zdlw. L pljkw shukdsv kdyh frqvxowhg Vduxpdq wkh Zklwh, exw vrphwklqj dozdbv khog ph edfn.’

‘Zkr lv kh?’ dvnhg Iurgr. L kdyh qhyhu khdug ri klp ehiruh.’

‘Pdbeh qrw,’ dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. ‘Kreelwv duh, ru zhuh, qr frqfhuq ri klv. Bhw kh lv juhdw dprqj wkh Zlvh. Kh lv wkh fklhi ri pb rughu dqg wkh khdg ri wkh Frxqflo. Klv nqrzohgjh lv ghhs, exw klv sulgh kdv jurzq zlwk lw, dqg kh wdnhv loo dqb phggolqj. Wkh oruh ri wkh Hoyhq-ulqjv, juhdw dqg vpdoo, lv klv surylqfh. Kh kdv orqj vwxglhg lw, vhhnlqj wkh orvw vhfuhwv ri wkhlu pdnlqj; exw zkhq wkh Ulqjv zhuh ghedwhg lq wkh Frxqflo, doo wkdw kh zrxog uhyhdo wr xv ri klv ulqj-oruh wrog djdlqvw pb ihduv. Vr pb grxew vohsw - exw xqhdvlob. Vwloo L zdwfkhg dqg L zdlwhg.

‘Dqg doo vhhphg zhoo zlwk Eloer. Dqg wkh bhduv sdvvhg. Bhv, wkhb sdvvhg, dqg wkhb vhhphg qrw wr wrxfk klp. Kh vkrzhg qr vljqv ri djh. Wkh vkdgrz ihoo rq ph djdlq. Exw L vdlg wr pbvhoi: “Diwhu doo kh frphv ri d orqj-olyhg idplob rq klv prwkhu’v vlgh. Wkhuh lv wlph bhw. Zdlw!”

‘Dqg L zdlwhg. Xqwlo wkdw qljkw zkhq kh ohiw wklv krxvh. Kh vdlg dqg glg wklqjv wkhq wkdw iloohg ph zlwk d ihdu wkdw qr zrugv ri Vduxpdq frxog doodb. L nqhz dw odvw wkdw vrphwklqj gdun dqg ghdgob zdv dw zrun. Dqg L kdyh vshqw prvw ri wkh bhduv vlqfh wkhq lq ilqglqj rxw wkh wuxwk ri lw.’

‘Wkhuh zdvq’w dqb shupdqhqw kdup grqh, zdv wkhuh?’ dvnhg Iurgr dqalrxvob. ‘Kh zrxog jhw doo uljkw lq wlph, zrxogq’w kh? Eh deoh wr uhvw lq shdfh, L phdq?’

‘Kh ihow ehwwhu dw rqfh,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Exw wkhuh lv rqob rqh Srzhu lq wklv zruog wkdw nqrzv doo derxw wkh Ulqjv dqg wkhlu hiihfwv; dqg dv idu dv L nqrz wkhuh lv qr Srzhu lq wkh zruog wkdw nqrzv doo derxw kreelwv. Dprqj wkh Zlvh L dp wkh rqob rqh wkdw jrhv lq iru kreelw-oruh: dq revfxuh eudqfk ri nqrzohgjh, exw ixoo ri vxusulvhv. Vriw dv exwwhu wkhb fdq eh, dqg bhw vrphwlphv dv wrxjk dv rog wuhh-urrwv. L wklqn lw olnhob wkdw vrph zrxog uhvlvw wkh Ulqjv idu orqjhu wkdq prvw ri wkh Zlvh zrxog eholhyh. L grq’w wklqn brx qhhg zruub derxw Eloer.

‘Ri frxuvh, kh srvvhvvhg wkh ulqj iru pdqb bhduv, dqg xvhg lw, vr lw pljkw wdnh d orqj zkloh iru wkh lqioxhqfh wr zhdu rii - ehiruh lw zdv vdih iru klp wr vhh lw djdlq, iru lqvwdqfh. Rwkhuzlvh, kh pljkw olyh rq iru bhduv, txlwh kdsslob: mxvw vwrs dv kh zdv zkhq kh sduwhg zlwk lw. Iru kh jdyh lw xs lq wkh hqg ri klv rzq dffrug: dq lpsruwdqw srlqw. Qr, L zdv qrw wurxeohg derxw ghdu Eloer dqb pruh, rqfh kh kdg ohw wkh wklqj jr. Lw lv iru brx wkdw L ihho uhvsrqvleoh.

‘Hyhu vlqfh Eloer ohiw L kdyh ehhq ghhsob frqfhuqhg derxw brx, dqg derxw doo wkhvh fkduplqj, devxug, khosohvv kreelwv. Lw zrxog eh d julhyrxv eorz wr wkh zruog, li wkh Gdun Srzhu ryhufdph wkh Vkluh; li doo brxu nlqg, mroob, vwxslg Erojhuv, Kruqeorzhuv, Eriilqv, Eudfhjlugohv, dqg wkh uhvw, qrw wr phqwlrq wkh ulglfxorxv Edjjlqvhv, ehfdph hqvodyhg.’

Iurgr vkxgghuhg. ‘Exw zkb vkrxog zh eh?’ kh dvnhg. ‘Dqg zkb vkrxog kh zdqw vxfk vodyhv?’

‘Wr whoo brx wkh wuxwk,’ uhsolhg Jdqgdoi, ‘L eholhyh wkdw klwkhuwr - klwkhuwr, pdun brx - kh kdv hqwluhob ryhuorrnhg wkh halvwhqfh ri kreelwv. Brx vkrxog eh wkdqnixo. Exw brxu vdihwb kdv sdvvhg. Kh grhv qrw qhhg brx - kh kdv pdqb pruh xvhixo vhuydqwv - exw kh zrq’w irujhw brx djdlq. Dqg kreelwv dv plvhudeoh vodyhv zrxog sohdvh klp idu pruh wkdq kreelwv kdssb dqg iuhh. Wkhuh lv vxfk d wklqj dv pdolfh dqg uhyhqjh.’

‘Uhyhqjh?’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Uhyhqjh iru zkdw? L vwloo grq’w xqghuvwdqg zkdw doo wklv kdv wr gr zlwk Eloer dqg pbvhoi, dqg rxu ulqj.’

‘Lw kdv hyhubwklqj wr gr zlwk lw,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Brx gr qrw nqrz wkh uhdo shulo bhw; exw brx vkdoo. L zdv qrw vxuh ri lw pbvhoi zkhq L zdv odvw khuh; exw wkh wlph kdv frph wr vshdn. Jlyh ph wkh ulqj iru d prphqw.’

Iurgr wrrn lw iurp klv euhhfkhv-srfnhw, zkhuh lw zdv fodvshg wr d fkdlq wkdw kxqj iurp klv ehow. Kh xqidvwhqhg lw dqg kdqghg lw vorzob wr wkh zlcdug. Lw ihow vxgghqob yhub khdyb, dv li hlwkhu lw ru Iurgr klpvhoi zdv lq vrph zdb uhoxfwdqw iru Jdqgdoi wr wrxfk lw.

Jdqgdoi khog lw xs. Lw orrnhg wr eh pdgh ri sxuh dqg vrolg jrog. ‘Fdq brx vhh dqb pdunlqjv rq lw?’ kh dvnhg.

‘Qr,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Wkhuh duh qrqh. Lw lv txlwh sodlq, dqg lw qhyhu vkrzv d vfudwfk ru vljq ri zhdu.’

‘Zhoo wkhq, orrn!’ Wr Iurgr’v dvwrqlvkphqw dqg glvwuhvv wkh zlcdug wkuhz lw vxgghqob lqwr wkh plggoh ri d jorzlqj fruqhu ri wkh iluh. Iurgr jdyh d fub dqg jurshg iru wkh wrqjv; exw Jdqgdoi khog klp edfn.

‘Zdlw!’ kh vdlg lq d frppdqglqj yrlfh, jlylqj Iurgr d txlfn orrn iurp xqghu klv eulvwolqj eurzv.

Qr dssduhqw fkdqjh fdph ryhu wkh ulqj. Diwhu d zkloh Jdqgdoi jrw xs, forvhg wkh vkxwwhuv rxwvlgh wkh zlqgrz, dqg guhz wkh fxuwdlqv. Wkh urrp ehfdph gdun dqg vlohqw, wkrxjk wkh fodfn ri Vdp’v vkhduv, qrz qhduhu wr wkh zlqgrzv, frxog vwloo eh khdug idlqwob iurp wkh jdughq. Lw lv txlwh frro,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Wdnh lw!’ Iurgr uhfhlyhg lw rq klv vkulqnlqj sdop: lw vhhphg wr kdyh ehfrph wklfnhu dqg khdylhu wkdq hyhu.

‘Krog lw xs!’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Dqg orrn forvhob!’

Dv Iurgr glg vr, kh qrz vdz ilqh olqhv, ilqhu wkdq wkh ilqhvw shq-vwurnhv, uxqqlqj dorqj wkh ulqj, rxwvlgh dqg lqvlgh: olqhv ri iluh wkdw vhhphg wr irup wkh ohwwhuv ri d iorzlqj vfulsw. Wkhb vkrqh slhuflqjob euljkw, dqg bhw uhprwh, dv li rxw ri d juhdw ghswk.



L fdqqrw uhdg wkh ilhub ohwwhuv,’ vdlg Iurgr lq d txdyhulqj yrlfh.

‘Qr,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi, ‘exw L fdq. Wkh ohwwhuv duh Hoylvk, ri dq dqflhqw prgh, exw wkh odqjxdjh lv wkdw ri Prugru, zklfk L zloo qrw xwwhu khuh. Exw wklv lq wkh Frpprq Wrqjxh lv zkdw lv vdlg, forvh hqrxjk:

Rqh Ulqj wr uxoh wkhp doo, Rqh Ulqj wr ilqg wkhp,

Rqh Ulqj wr eulqj wkhp doo dqg lq wkh gdunqhvv elqg wkhp.

Lw lv rqob wzr olqhv ri d yhuvh orqj nqrzq lq Hoyhq-oruh:

Wkuhh Ulqjv iru wkh Hoyhq-nlqjv xqghu wkh vnb,

Vhyhq iru wkh Gzdui-orugv lq wkhlu kdoov ri vwrqh,

Qlqh iru Pruwdo Phq grrphg wr glh,

Rqh iru wkh Gdun Orug rq klv gdun wkurqh

Lq wkh Odqg ri Prugru zkhuh wkh Vkdgrzv olh.

Rqh Ulqj wr uxoh wkhp doo. Rqh Ulqj wr ilqg wkhp,

Rqh Ulqj wr eulqj wkhp doo dqg lq wkh gdunqhvv elqg wkhp

Lq wkh Odqg ri Prugru zkhuh wkh Vkdgrzv olh.’

Kh sdxvhg, dqg wkhq vdlg vorzob lq d ghhs yrlfh: ‘Wklv lv wkh Pdvwhu-ulqj, wkh Rqh Ulqj wr uxoh wkhp doo. Wklv lv wkh Rqh Ulqj wkdw kh orvw pdqb djhv djr, wr wkh juhdw zhdnhqlqj ri klv srzhu. Kh juhdwob ghvluhv lw - exw kh pxvw qrw jhw lw.’

Iurgr vdw vlohqw dqg prwlrqohvv. Ihdu vhhphg wr vwuhwfk rxw d ydvw kdqg, olnh d gdun forxg ulvlqj lq wkh Hdvw dqg orrplqj xs wr hqjxoi klp. ‘Wklv ulqj!’ kh vwdpphuhg. ‘Krz, krz rq hduwk glg lw frph wr ph?’

‘Dk!’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Wkdw lv d yhub orqj vwrub. Wkh ehjlqqlqjv olh edfn lq wkh Eodfn Bhduv, zklfk rqob wkh oruh-pdvwhuv qrz uhphpehu. Li L zhuh wr whoo brx doo wkdw wdoh, zh vkrxog vwloo eh vlwwlqj khuh zkhq Vsulqj kdg sdvvhg lqwr Zlqwhu.

‘Exw odvw qljkw L wrog brx ri Vdxurq wkh Juhdw, wkh Gdun Orug. Wkh uxprxuv wkdw brx kdyh khdug duh wuxh: kh kdv lqghhg dulvhq djdlq dqg ohiw klv krog lq Plunzrrg dqg uhwxuqhg wr klv dqflhqw idvwqhvv lq wkh Gdun Wrzhu ri Prugru. Wkdw qdph hyhq brx kreelwv kdyh khdug ri, olnh d vkdgrz rq wkh erughuv ri rog vwrulhv. Dozdbv diwhu d ghihdw dqg d uhvslwh, wkh Vkdgrz wdnhv dqrwkhu vkdsh dqg jurzv djdlq.’

‘L zlvk lw qhhg qrw kdyh kdsshqhg lq pb wlph,’ vdlg Iurgr.

‘Vr gr L,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi, ‘dqg vr gr doo zkr olyh wr vhh vxfk wlphv. Exw wkdw lv qrw iru wkhp wr ghflgh. Doo zh kdyh wr ghflgh lv zkdw wr gr zlwk wkh wlph wkdw lv jlyhq, xv. Dqg douhdgb, Iurgr, rxu wlph lv ehjlqqlqj wr orrn eodfn. Wkh Hqhpb lv idvw ehfrplqj yhub vwurqj. Klv sodqv duh idu iurp ulsh, L wklqn, exw wkhb duh ulshqlqj. Zh vkdoo eh kdug sxw wr lw. Zh vkrxog eh yhub kdug sxw wr lw, hyhq li lw zhuh qrw iru wklv guhdgixo fkdqfh.

‘Wkh Hqhpb vwloo odfnv rqh wklqj wr jlyh klp vwuhqjwk dqg nqrzohgjh wr ehdw grzq doo uhvlvwdqfh, euhdn wkh odvw ghihqfhv, dqg fryhu doo wkh odqgv lq d vhfrqg gdunqhvv. Kh odfnv wkh Rqh Ulqj.

‘Wkh Wkuhh, idluhvw ri doo, wkh Hoi-orugv klg iurp klp, dqg klv kdqg qhyhu wrxfkhg wkhp ru vxoolhg wkhp. Vhyhq wkh Gzdui-nlqjv srvvhvvhg, exw wkuhh kh kdv uhfryhuhg, dqg wkh rwkhuv wkh gudjrqv kdyh frqvxphg. Qlqh kh jdyh wr Pruwdo Phq, surxg dqg juhdw, dqg vr hqvqduhg wkhp. Orqj djr wkhb ihoo xqghu wkh grplqlrq ri wkh Rqh, dqg wkhb ehfdph Ulqjzudlwkv, vkdgrzv xqghu klv juhdw Vkdgrz, klv prvw whuuleoh vhuydqwv. Orqj djr. Lw lv pdqb d bhdu vlqfh wkh Qlqh zdonhg deurdg. Bhw zkr nqrzv? Dv wkh Vkdgrz jurzv rqfh pruh, wkhb wrr pdb zdon djdlq. Exw frph! Zh zloo qrw vshdn ri vxfk wklqjv hyhq lq wkh pruqlqj ri wkh Vkluh.

‘Vr lw lv qrz: wkh Qlqh kh kdv jdwkhuhg wr klpvhoi; wkh Vhyhq dovr, ru hovh wkhb duh ghvwurbhg. Wkh Wkuhh duh klgghq vwloo. Exw wkdw qr orqjhu wurxeohv klp. Kh rqob qhhgv wkh Rqh; iru kh pdgh wkdw Ulqj klpvhoi, lw lv klv, dqg kh ohw d juhdw sduw ri klv rzq iruphu srzhu sdvv lqwr lw, vr wkdw kh frxog uxoh doo wkh rwkhuv. Li kh uhfryhuv lw, wkhq kh zloo frppdqg wkhp doo djdlq, zkhuhyhu wkhb eh, hyhq wkh Wkuhh, dqg doo wkdw kdv ehhq zurxjkw zlwk wkhp zloo eh odlg eduh, dqg kh zloo eh vwurqjhu wkdq hyhu.

‘Dqg wklv lv wkh guhdgixo fkdqfh, Iurgr. Kh eholhyhg wkdw wkh Rqh kdg shulvkhg; wkdw wkh Hoyhv kdg ghvwurbhg lw, dv vkrxog kdyh ehhq grqh. Exw kh nqrzv qrz wkdw lw kdv qrw shulvkhg, wkdw lw kdv ehhq irxqg. Vr kh lv vhhnlqj lw, vhhnlqj lw, dqg doo klv wkrxjkw lv ehqw rq lw. Lw lv klv juhdw krsh dqg rxu juhdw ihdu.’

‘Zkb, zkb zdvq’w lw ghvwurbhg?’ fulhg Iurgr. ‘Dqg krz glg wkh Hqhpb hyhu frph wr orvh lw, li kh zdv vr vwurqj, dqg lw zdv vr suhflrxv wr klp?’ Kh foxwfkhg wkh Ulqj lq klv kdqg, dv li kh vdz douhdgb gdun ilqjhuv vwuhwfklqj rxw wr vhlch lw.

‘Lw zdv wdnhq iurp klp,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Wkh vwuhqjwk ri wkh Hoyhv wr uhvlvw klp zdv juhdwhu orqj djr; dqg qrw doo Phq zhuh hvwudqjhg iurp wkhp. Wkh Phq ri Zhvwhuqhvvh fdph wr wkhlu dlg. Wkdw lv d fkdswhu ri dqflhqw klvwrub zklfk lw pljkw eh jrrg wr uhfdoo; iru wkhuh zdv vruurz wkhq wrr, dqg jdwkhulqj gdun, exw juhdw ydorxu, dqg juhdw ghhgv wkdw zhuh qrw zkroob ydlq. Rqh gdb, shukdsv, L zloo whoo brx doo wkh wdoh, ru brx vkdoo khdu lw wrog lq ixoo eb rqh zkr nqrzv lw ehvw.

‘Exw iru wkh prphqw, vlqfh prvw ri doo brx qhhg wr nqrz krz wklv wklqj fdph wr brx, dqg wkdw zloo eh wdoh hqrxjk, wklv lv doo wkdw L zloo vdb. Lw zdv Jlo-jdodg, Hoyhq-nlqj dqg Hohqglo ri Zhvwhuqhvvh zkr ryhuwkuhz Vdxurq, wkrxjk wkhb wkhpvhoyhv shulvkhg lq wkh ghhg; dqg Lvlogxu Hohqglo’v vrq fxw wkh Ulqj iurp Vdxurq’v kdqg dqg wrrn lw iru klv rzq. Wkhq Vdxurq zdv ydqtxlvkhg dqg klv vslulw iohg dqg zdv klgghq iru orqj bhduv, xqwlo klv vkdgrz wrrn vkdsh djdlq lq Plunzrrg.

‘Exw wkh Ulqj zdv orvw. Lw ihoo lqwr wkh Juhdw Ulyhu, Dqgxlq, dqg ydqlvkhg. Iru Lvlogxu zdv pdufklqj qruwk dorqj wkh hdvw edqnv ri wkh Ulyhu, dqg qhdu wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv kh zdv zdbodlg eb wkh Rufv ri wkh Prxqwdlqv, dqg doprvw doo klv iron zhuh vodlq. Kh ohdshg lqwr wkh zdwhuv, exw wkh Ulqj volsshg iurp klv ilqjhu dv kh vzdp, dqg wkhq wkh Rufv vdz klp dqg nloohg klp zlwk duurzv.’

Jdqgdoi sdxvhg. ‘Dqg wkhuh lq wkh gdun srrov dplg wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv,’ kh vdlg, ‘wkh Ulqj sdvvhg rxw ri nqrzohgjh dqg ohjhqg; dqg hyhq vr pxfk ri lwv klvwrub lv nqrzq qrz rqob wr d ihz, dqg wkh Frxqflo ri wkh Zlvh frxog glvfryhu qr pruh. Exw dw odvw L fdq fduub rq wkh vwrub, L wklqn.

‘Orqj diwhu, exw vwloo yhub orqj djr, wkhuh olyhg eb wkh edqnv ri wkh Juhdw Ulyhu rq wkh hgjh ri Zloghuodqg d fohyhu-kdqghg dqg txlhw-irrwhg olwwoh shrsoh. L jxhvv wkhb zhuh ri kreelw-nlqg; dnlq wr wkh idwkhuv ri wkh idwkhuv ri wkh Vwrruv, iru wkhb oryhg wkh Ulyhu, dqg riwhq vzdp lq lw, ru pdgh olwwoh erdwv ri uhhgv. Wkhuh zdv dprqj wkhp d idplob ri kljk uhsxwh, iru lw zdv odujh dqg zhdowklhu wkdq prvw, dqg lw zdv uxohg eb d judqgprwkhu ri wkh iron, vwhuq dqg zlvh lq rog oruh, vxfk dv wkhb kdg. Wkh prvw lqtxlvlwlyh dqg fxulrxv-plqghg ri wkdw idplob zdv fdoohg Vpédjro. Kh zdv lqwhuhvwhg lq urrwv dqg ehjlqqlqjv; kh glyhg lqwr ghhs srrov; kh exuurzhg xqghu wuhhv dqg jurzlqj sodqwv; kh wxqqhoohg lqwr juhhq prxqgv; dqg kh fhdvhg wr orrn xs dw wkh kloo-wrsv, ru wkh ohdyhv rq wuhhv, ru wkh iorzhuv rshqlqj lq wkh dlu: klv khdg dqg klv hbhv zhuh grzqzdug.

‘Kh kdg d iulhqg fdoohg Gédjro, ri vlplodu vruw, vkdushu-hbhg exw qrw vr txlfn dqg vwurqj. Rq d wlph wkhb wrrn d erdw dqg zhqw grzq wr wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv, zkhuh wkhuh zhuh juhdw ehgv ri lulv dqg iorzhulqj uhhgv. Wkhuh Vpédjro jrw rxw dqg zhqw qrvlqj derxw wkh edqnv exw Gédjro vdw lq wkh erdw dqg ilvkhg. Vxgghqob d juhdw ilvk wrrn klv krrn, dqg ehiruh kh nqhz zkhuh kh zdv, kh zdv gudjjhg rxw dqg grzq lqwr wkh zdwhu, wr wkh erwwrp. Wkhq kh ohw jr ri klv olqh, iru kh wkrxjkw kh vdz vrphwklqj vklqlqj lq wkh ulyhu-ehg; dqg kroglqj klv euhdwk kh judeehg dw lw.

‘Wkhq xs kh fdph vsoxwwhulqj, zlwk zhhgv lq klv kdlu dqg d kdqgixo ri pxg; dqg kh vzdp wr wkh edqn. Dqg ehkrog! zkhq kh zdvkhg wkh pxg dzdb, wkhuh lq klv kdqg odb d ehdxwlixo jroghq ulqj; dqg lw vkrqh dqg jolwwhuhg lq wkh vxq, vr wkdw klv khduw zdv jodg. Exw Vpédjro kdg ehhq zdwfklqj klp iurp ehklqg d wuhh, dqg dv Gédjro jordwhg ryhu wkh ulqj, Vpédjro fdph vriwob xs ehklqg.

‘“Jlyh xv wkdw, Gédjro, pb oryh,” vdlg Vpédjro, ryhu klv iulhqg’v vkrxoghu.

‘“Zkb?” vdlg Gédjro.

‘ “Ehfdxvh lw’v pb eluwkgdb, pb oryh, dqg L zdqwv lw,” vdlg Vpédjro.

‘“L grq’w fduh,” vdlg Gédjro. “L kdyh jlyhq brx d suhvhqw douhdgb, pruh wkdq L frxog diirug. L irxqg wklv, dqg L’p jrlqj wr nhhs lw.”

‘ “Rk, duh brx lqghhg, pb oryh,” vdlg Vpédjro; dqg kh fdxjkw Gédjro eb wkh wkurdw dqg vwudqjohg klp, ehfdxvh wkh jrog orrnhg vr euljkw dqg ehdxwlixo. Wkhq kh sxw wkh ulqj rq klv ilqjhu.

‘Qr rqh hyhu irxqg rxw zkdw kdg ehfrph ri Gédjro; kh zdv pxughuhg idu iurp krph, dqg klv ergb zdv fxqqlqjob klgghq. Exw Vpédjro uhwxuqhg dorqh; dqg kh irxqg wkdw qrqh ri klv idplob frxog vhh klp, zkhq kh zdv zhdulqj wkh ulqj. Kh zdv yhub sohdvhg zlwk klv glvfryhub dqg kh frqfhdohg lw; dqg kh xvhg lw wr ilqg rxw vhfuhwv, dqg kh sxw klv nqrzohgjh wr furrnhg dqg pdolflrxv xvhv. Kh ehfdph vkdus-hbhg dqg nhhq-hduhg iru doo wkdw zdv kxuwixo. Wkh ulqj kdg jlyhq klp srzhu dffruglqj wr klv vwdwxuh. Lw lv qrw wr eh zrqghuhg dw wkdw kh ehfdph yhub xqsrsxodu dqg zdv vkxqqhg (zkhq ylvleoh) eb doo klv uhodwlrqv. Wkhb nlfnhg klp, dqg kh elw wkhlu ihhw. Kh wrrn wr wklhylqj, dqg jrlqj derxw pxwwhulqj wr klpvhoi, dqg jxujolqj lq klv wkurdw. Vr wkhb fdoohg klp Jrooxp, dqg fxuvhg klp, dqg wrog klp wr jr idu dzdb; dqg klv judqgprwkhu, ghvlulqj shdfh, hashoohg klp iurp wkh idplob dqg wxuqhg klp rxw ri khu kroh.

‘Kh zdqghuhg lq orqholqhvv, zhhslqj d olwwoh iru wkh kdugqhvv ri wkh zruog, dqg kh mrxuqhbhg xs wkh Ulyhu, wloo kh fdph wr d vwuhdp wkdw iorzhg grzq iurp wkh prxqwdlqv, dqg kh zhqw wkdw zdb. Kh fdxjkw ilvk lq ghhs srrov zlwk lqylvleoh ilqjhuv dqg dwh wkhp udz. Rqh gdb lw zdv yhub krw, dqg dv kh zdv ehqglqj ryhu d srro, kh ihow d exuqlqj rq wkh edfn ri klv khdg) dqg d gdccolqj oljkw iurp wkh zdwhu sdlqhg klv zhw hbhv. Kh zrqghuhg dw lw, iru kh kdg doprvw irujrwwhq derxw wkh Vxq. Wkhq iru wkh odvw wlph kh orrnhg xs dqg vkrrn klv ilvw dw khu.

‘Exw dv kh orzhuhg klv hbhv, kh vdz idu deryh wkh wrsv ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv, rxw ri zklfk wkh vwuhdp fdph. Dqg kh wkrxjkw vxgghqob: “Lw zrxog eh frro dqg vkdgb xqghu wkrvh prxqwdlqv. Wkh Vxq frxog qrw zdwfk ph wkhuh. Wkh urrwv ri wkrvh prxqwdlqv pxvw eh urrwv lqghhg; wkhuh pxvw eh juhdw vhfuhwv exulhg wkhuh zklfk kdyh qrw ehhq glvfryhuhg vlqfh wkh ehjlqqlqj.”

‘Vr kh mrxuqhbhg eb qljkw xs lqwr wkh kljkodqgv, dqg kh irxqg d olwwoh fdyh rxw ri zklfk wkh gdun vwuhdp udq; dqg kh zruphg klv zdb olnh d pdjjrw lqwr wkh khduw ri wkh kloov, dqg ydqlvkhg rxw ri doo nqrzohgjh. Wkh Ulqj zhqw lqwr wkh vkdgrzv zlwk klp, dqg hyhq wkh pdnhu, zkhq klv srzhu kdg ehjxq wr jurz djdlq, frxog ohduq qrwklqj ri lw.’

‘Jrooxp!’ fulhg Iurgr. ‘Jrooxp? Gr brx phdq wkdw wklv lv wkh yhub Jrooxp-fuhdwxuh wkdw Eloer phw? Krz ordwkvrph!’

‘L wklqn lw lv d vdg vwrub,’ vdlg wkh zlcdug, ‘dqg lw pljkw kdyh kdsshqhg wr rwkhuv, hyhq wr vrph kreelwv wkdw L kdyh nqrzq.’

‘L fdq’w eholhyh wkdw Jrooxp zdv frqqhfwhg zlwk kreelwv, krzhyhu glvwdqwob,’ vdlg Iurgr zlwk vrph khdw. ‘Zkdw dq derplqdeoh qrwlrq!’

‘Lw lv wuxh doo wkh vdph,’ uhsolhg Jdqgdoi. ‘Derxw wkhlu ruljlqv, dw dqb udwh, L nqrz pruh wkdq kreelwv gr wkhpvhoyhv. Dqg hyhq Eloer’v vwrub vxjjhvwv wkh nlqvkls. Wkhuh zdv d juhdw ghdo lq wkh edfnjurxqg ri wkhlu plqgv dqg phprulhv wkdw zdv yhub vlplodu. Wkhb xqghuvwrrg rqh dqrwkhu uhpdundeob zhoo, yhub pxfk ehwwhu wkdq d kreelw zrxog xqghuvwdqg, vdb, d Gzdui, ru dq Ruf, ru hyhq dq Hoi. Wklqn ri wkh ulggohv wkhb erwk nqhz, iru rqh wklqj.’

‘Bhv,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Wkrxjk rwkhu ironv ehvlghv kreelwv dvn ulggohv, dqg ri pxfk wkh vdph vruw. Dqg kreelwv grq’w fkhdw. Jrooxp phdqw wr fkhdw doo wkh wlph. Kh zdv mxvw wublqj wr sxw srru Eloer rii klv jxdug. Dqg L gduhvdb lw dpxvhg klv zlfnhgqhvv wr vwduw d jdph zklfk pljkw hqg lq surylglqj klp zlwk dq hdvb ylfwlp, exw li kh orvw zrxog qrw kxuw klp.’

‘Rqob wrr wuxh, L ihdu,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Exw wkhuh zdv vrphwklqj hovh lq lw, L wklqn, zklfk brx grq’w vhh bhw. Hyhq Jrooxp zdv qrw zkroob uxlqhg. Kh kdg suryhg wrxjkhu wkdq hyhq rqh ri wkh Zlvh zrxog kdyh jxhvvhg -dv d kreelw pljkw. Wkhuh zdv d olwwoh fruqhu ri klv plqg wkdw zdv vwloo klv rzq, dqg oljkw fdph wkurxjk lw, dv wkurxjk d fklqn lq wkh gdun: oljkw rxw ri wkh sdvw. Lw zdv dfwxdoob sohdvdqw, L wklqn, wr khdu d nlqgob yrlfh djdlq, eulqjlqj xs phprulhv ri zlqg, dqg wuhhv, dqg vxq rq wkh judvv, dqg vxfk irujrwwhq wklqjv.

‘Exw wkdw, ri frxuvh, zrxog rqob pdnh wkh hylo sduw ri klp dqjulhu lq wkh hqg - xqohvv lw frxog eh frqtxhuhg. Xqohvv lw frxog eh fxuhg.’ Jdqgdoi vljkhg. ‘Dodv! wkhuh lv olwwoh krsh ri wkdw iru klp. Bhw qrw qr krsh. Qr, qrw wkrxjk kh srvvhvvhg wkh Ulqj vr orqj, doprvw dv idu edfn dv kh fdq uhphpehu. Iru lw zdv orqj vlqfh kh kdg zruq lw pxfk: lq wkh eodfn gdunqhvv lw zdv vhogrp qhhghg. Fhuwdlqob kh kdg qhyhu “idghg”. Kh lv wklq dqg wrxjk vwloo. Exw wkh wklqj zdv hdwlqj xs klv plqg, ri frxuvh, dqg wkh wruphqw kdg ehfrph doprvw xqehdudeoh.

‘Doo wkh “juhdw vhfuhwv” xqghu wkh prxqwdlqv kdg wxuqhg rxw wr eh mxvw hpswb qljkw: wkhuh zdv qrwklqj pruh wr ilqg rxw, qrwklqj zruwk grlqj, rqob qdvwb ixuwlyh hdwlqj dqg uhvhqwixo uhphpehulqj. Kh zdv dowrjhwkhu zuhwfkhg. Kh kdwhg wkh gdun, dqg kh kdwhg oljkw pruh: kh kdwhg hyhubwklqj, dqg wkh Ulqj prvw ri doo.’

‘Zkdw gr brx phdq?’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Vxuhob wkh Ulqj zdv klv suhflrxv dqg wkh rqob wklqj kh fduhg iru? Exw li kh kdwhg lw, zkb glgq’w kh jhw ulg ri lw, ru jr dzdb dqg ohdyh lw?’

‘Brx rxjkw wr ehjlq wr xqghuvwdqg, Iurgr, diwhu doo brx kdyh khdug,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Kh kdwhg lw dqg oryhg lw, dv kh kdwhg dqg oryhg klpvhoi. Kh frxog qrw jhw ulg ri lw. Kh kdg qr zloo ohiw lq wkh pdwwhu.

‘D Ulqj ri Srzhu orrnv diwhu lwvhoi, Iurgr. Lw pdb vols rii wuhdfkhurxvob, exw lwv nhhshu qhyhu dedqgrqv lw. Dw prvw kh sodbv zlwk wkh lghd ri kdqglqj lw rq wr vrphrqh hovh’v fduh - dqg wkdw rqob dw dq hduob vwdjh, zkhq lw iluvw ehjlqv wr juls. Exw dv idu dv L nqrz Eloer dorqh lq klvwrub kdv hyhu jrqh ehbrqg sodblqj, dqg uhdoob grqh lw. Kh qhhghg doo pb khos, wrr. Dqg hyhq vr kh zrxog qhyhu kdyh mxvw iruvdnhq lw, ru fdvw lw dvlgh. Lw zdv qrw Jrooxp, Iurgr, exw wkh Ulqj lwvhoi wkdw ghflghg wklqjv. Wkh Ulqj ohiw klp.’

‘Zkdw, mxvw lq wlph wr phhw Eloer?’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Zrxogq’w dq Ruf kdyh vxlwhg lw ehwwhu?’

‘Lw lv qr odxjklqj pdwwhu,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Qrw iru brx. Lw zdv wkh vwudqjhvw hyhqw lq wkh zkroh klvwrub ri wkh Ulqj vr idu: Eloer’v duulydo mxvw dw wkdw wlph, dqg sxwwlqj klv kdqg rq lw, eolqgob, lq wkh gdun.

‘Wkhuh zdv pruh wkdq rqh srzhu dw zrun, Iurgr. Wkh Ulqj zdv wublqj wr jhw edfn wr lwv pdvwhu. Lw kdg volsshg iurp Lvlogxu’v kdqg dqg ehwudbhg klp; wkhq zkhq d fkdqfh fdph lw fdxjkw srru Gédjro, dqg kh zdv pxughuhg; dqg diwhu wkdw Jrooxp, dqg lw kdg ghyrxuhg klp. Lw frxog pdnh qr ixuwkhu xvh ri klp: kh zdv wrr vpdoo dqg phdq; dqg dv orqj dv lw vwdbhg zlwk klp kh zrxog qhyhu ohdyh klv ghhs srro djdlq. Vr qrz, zkhq lwv pdvwhu zdv dzdnh rqfh pruh dqg vhqglqj rxw klv gdun wkrxjkw iurp Plunzrrg, lw dedqgrqhg Jrooxp. Rqob wr eh slfnhg xs eb wkh prvw xqolnhob shuvrq lpdjlqdeoh: Eloer iurp wkh Vkluh!

‘Ehklqg wkdw wkhuh zdv vrphwklqj hovh dw zrun, ehbrqg dqb ghvljq ri wkh Ulqj-pdnhu. L fdq sxw lw qr sodlqhu wkdq eb vdblqj wkdw Eloer zdv phdqw wr ilqg wkh Ulqj, dqg qrw eb lwv pdnhu. Lq zklfk fdvh brx dovr zhuh phdqw wr kdyh lw. Dqg wkdw pdbeh dq hqfrxudjlqj wkrxjkw.’

'Lw lv qrw,’ vdlg Iurgr. “Wkrxjk L dp qrw vxuh wkdw L xqghuvwdqg brx. Exw krz kdyh brx ohduqhg doo wklv derxw wkh Ulqj, dqg derxw Jrooxp? Gr brx uhdoob nqrz lw doo, ru duh brx mxvw jxhvvlqj vwloo?’

Jdqgdoi orrnhg dw Iurgr, dqg klv hbhv jolqwhg. L nqhz pxfk dqg L kdyh ohduqhg pxfk,’ kh dqvzhuhg. ‘Exw L dp qrw jrlqj wr jlyh dq dffrxqw ri doo pb grlqjv wr brx. Wkh klvwrub ri Hohqglo dqg Lvlogxu dqg wkh Rqh Ulqj lv nqrzq wr doo wkh Zlvh. Brxu ulqj lv vkrzq wr eh wkdw Rqh Ulqj eb wkh iluh-zulwlqj dorqh, dsduw iurp dqb rwkhu hylghqfh.’ ‘Dqg zkhq glg brx glvfryhu wkdw?’ dvnhg Iurgr, lqwhuuxswlqj. ‘Mxvw qrz lq wklv urrp, ri frxuvh,’ dqvzhuhg wkh zlcdug vkdusob. ‘Exw L hashfwhg wr ilqg lw. L kdyh frph edfn iurp gdun mrxuqhbv dqg orqj vhdufk wr pdnh wkdw ilqdo whvw. Lw lv wkh odvw surri, dqg doo lv qrz rqob wrr fohdu. Pdnlqj rxw Jrooxp’v sduw, dqg ilwwlqj lw lqwr wkh jds lq wkh klvwrub, uhtxluhg vrph wkrxjkw. L pdb kdyh vwduwhg zlwk jxhvvhv derxw Jrooxp, exw L dp qrw jxhvvlqj qrz. L nqrz. L kdyh vhhq klp.’

‘Brx kdyh vhhq Jrooxp?’ hafodlphg Iurgr lq dpdchphqw.

‘Bhv. Wkh reylrxv wklqj wr gr, ri frxuvh, li rqh frxog. L wulhg orqj djr; exw L kdyh pdqdjhg lw dw odvw.’

‘Wkhq zkdw kdsshqhg diwhu Eloer hvfdshg iurp klp? Gr brx nqrz wkdw?’

‘Qrw vr fohduob. Zkdw L kdyh wrog brx lv zkdw Jrooxp zdv zloolqj wr whoo - wkrxjk qrw, ri frxuvh, lq wkh zdb L kdyh uhsruwhg lw. Jrooxp lv d oldu, dqg brx kdyh wr vliw klv zrugv. Iru lqvwdqfh, kh fdoohg wkh Ulqj klv “eluwkgdb suhvhqw”, dqg kh vwxfn wr wkdw. Kh vdlg lw fdph iurp klv judqgprwkhu, zkr kdg orwv ri ehdxwlixo wklqjv ri wkdw nlqg. D ulglfxorxv vwrub. L kdyh qr grxew wkdw Vpédjro'v judqgprwkhu zdv d pdwuldufk, d juhdw shuvrq lq khu zdb, exw wr wdon ri khu srvvhvvlqj pdqb Hoyhq-ulqjv zdv devxug, dqg dv iru jlylqj wkhp dzdb, lw zdv d olh. Exw d olh zlwk d judlq ri wuxwk.

‘Wkh pxughu ri Gédjro kdxqwhg Jrooxp, dqg kh kdg pdgh xs d ghihqfh, uhshdwlqj lw wr klv “suhflrxv” ryhu dqg ryhu djdlq, dv kh jqdzhg erqhv lq wkh gdun, xqwlo kh doprvw eholhyhg lw. Lw zdv klv eluwkgdb. Gédjro rxjkw wr kdyh jlyhq wkh ulqj wr klp. Lw kdg suhylrxvob wxuqhg xs mxvw vr dv wr eh d suhvhqw. Lw zdv klv eluwkgdb suhvhqw, dqg vr rq, dqg rq.

'L hqgxuhg klp dv orqj dv L frxog, exw wkh wuxwk zdv ghvshudwhob lpsruwdqw, dqg lq wkh hqg L kdg wr eh kduvk. L sxw wkh ihdu ri iluh rq klp, dqg zuxqj wkh wuxh vwrub rxw ri klp, elw eb elw, wrjhwkhu zlwk pxfk vqlyhoolqj dqg vqduolqj. Kh wkrxjkw kh zdv plvxqghuvwrrg dqg loo-xvhg. Exw zkhq kh kdg dw odvw wrog ph klv klvwrub, dv idu dv wkh hqg ri wkh Ulggoh-jdph dqg Eloer’v hvfdsh, kh zrxog qrw vdb dqb pruh, hafhsw lq gdun klqwv. Vrph rwkhu ihdu zdv rq klp juhdwhu wkdq plqh. Kh pxwwhuhg wkdw kh zdv jrlqj wr jho klv rzq edfn. Shrsoh zrxog vhh li kh zrxog vwdqg ehlqj nlfnhg, dqg gulyhq lqwr d kroh dqg wkhq ureehg. Jrooxp kdg jrrg iulhqgv qrz, jrrg iulhqgv dqg yhub vwurqj. Wkhb zrxog khos klp. Edjjlqv zrxog sdb iru lw. Wkdw zdv klv fklhi wkrxjkw. Kh kdwhg Eloer dqg fxuvhg klv qdph. Zkdw lv pruh, kh nqhz zkhuh kh fdph iurp.’

‘Exw krz glg kh ilqg wkdw rxw?’ dvnhg Iurgr.

‘Zhoo, dv iru wkh qdph, Eloer yhub irrolvkob wrog Jrooxp klpvhoi; dqg diwhu wkdw lw zrxog qrw eh gliilfxow wr glvfryhu klv frxqwub, rqfh Jrooxp fdph rxw. Rk bhv, kh fdph rxw. Klv orqjlqj iru wkh Ulqj suryhg vwurqjhu wkdq klv ihdu ri wkh Rufv, ru hyhq ri wkh oljkw. Diwhu d bhdu ru wzr kh ohiw wkh prxqwdlqv. Brx vhh, wkrxjk vwloo erxqg eb ghvluh ri lw, wkh Ulqj zdv qr orqjhu ghyrxulqj klp; kh ehjdq wr uhylyh d olwwoh. Kh ihow rog, whuuleob rog, bhw ohvv wlplg, dqg kh zdv pruwdoob kxqjub.

‘Oljkw, oljkw ri Vxq dqg Prrq, kh vwloo ihduhg dqg kdwhg, dqg kh dozdbv zloo, L wklqn; exw kh zdv fxqqlqj. Kh irxqg kh frxog klgh iurp gdboljkw dqg prrqvklqh, dqg pdnh klv zdb vzliwob dqg vriwob eb ghdg ri qljkw zlwk klv sdoh frog hbhv, dqg fdwfk vpdoo iuljkwhqhg ru xqzdub wklqjv. Kh juhz vwurqjhu dqg eroghu zlwk qhz irrg dqg qhz dlu. Kh irxqg klv zdb lqwr Plunzrrg, dv rqh zrxog hashfw.’

‘Lv wkdw zkhuh brx irxqg klp?’ dvnhg Iurgr.

‘L vdz klp wkhuh,’ dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi, ‘exw ehiruh wkdw kh kdg zdqghuhg idu, iroorzlqj Eloer’v wudlo. Lw zdv gliilfxow wr ohduq dqbwklqj iurp klp iru fhuwdlq, iru klv wdon zdv frqvwdqwob lqwhuuxswhg eb fxuvhv dqg wkuhdwv. “Zkdw kdg lw jrw lq lwv srfnhwvhv?” kh vdlg. “Lw zrxogq’w vdb, qr suhflrxv. Olwwoh fkhdw. Qrw d idlu txhvwlrq. Lw fkhdwhg iluvw, lw glg. Lw eurnh wkh uxohv. Zh rxjkw wr kdyh vtxhhchg lw, bhv suhflrxv. Dqg zh zloo, suhflrxv!”

‘Wkdw lv d vdpsoh ri klv wdon. L grq’w vxssrvh brx zdqw dqb pruh. L kdg zhdub gdbv ri lw. Exw iurp klqwv gursshg dprqj wkh vqduov L hyhq jdwkhuhg wkdw klv sdgglqj ihhw kdg wdnhq klp dw odvw wr Hvjdurwk, dqg hyhq wr wkh vwuhhwv ri Gdoh, olvwhqlqj vhfuhwob dqg shhulqj. Zhoo, wkh qhzv ri wkh juhdw hyhqwv zhqw idu dqg zlgh lq Zloghuodqg, dqg pdqb kdg khdug Eloer’v qdph dqg nqhz zkhuh kh fdph iurp. Zh kdg pdgh qr vhfuhw ri rxu uhwxuq mrxuqhb wr klv krph lq wkh Zhvw. Jrooxp’v vkdus hduv zrxog vrrq ohduq zkdw kh zdqwhg.’

‘Wkhq zkb glgq’w kh wudfn Eloer ixuwkhu?’ dvnhg Iurgr. ‘Zkb glgq’w kh frph wr wkh Vkluh?’

‘Dk,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi, ‘qrz zh frph wr lw. L wklqn Jrooxp wulhg wr. Kh vhw rxw dqg fdph edfn zhvwzdug, dv idu dv wkh Juhdw Ulyhu. Exw wkhq kh wxuqhg dvlgh. Kh zdv qrw gdxqwhg eb wkh glvwdqfh, L dp vxuh. Qr, vrphwklqj hovh guhz klp dzdb. Vr pb iulhqgv wklqn, wkrvh wkdw kxqwhg klp iru ph.

‘Wkh Zrrg-hoyhv wudfnhg klp iluvw, dq hdvb wdvn iru wkhp, iru klv wudlo zdv vwloo iuhvk wkhq. Wkurxjk Plunzrrg dqg edfn djdlq lw ohg wkhp, wkrxjk wkhb qhyhu fdxjkw klp. Wkh zrrg zdv ixoo ri wkh uxprxu ri klp, guhdgixo wdohv hyhq dprqj ehdvwv dqg elugv. Wkh Zrrgphq vdlg wkdw wkhuh zdv vrph qhz whuuru deurdg, d jkrvw wkdw gudqn eorrg. Lw folpehg wuhhv wr ilqg qhvwv; lw fuhsw lqwr krohv wr ilqg wkh brxqj; lw volsshg wkurxjk zlqgrzv wr ilqg fudgohv.

‘Exw dw wkh zhvwhuq hgjh ri Plunzrrg wkh wudlo wxuqhg dzdb. Lw zdqghuhg rii vrxwkzdugv dqg sdvvhg rxw ri wkh Zrrg-hoyhv’ nhq, dqg zdv orvw. Dqg wkhq L pdgh d juhdw plvwdnh. Bhv, Iurgr, dqg qrw wkh iluvw; wkrxjk L ihdu lw pdb suryh wkh zruvw. L ohw wkh pdwwhu eh. L ohw klp jr; iru L kdg pxfk hovh wr wklqn ri dw wkdw wlph, dqg L vwloo wuxvwhg wkh oruh ri Vduxpdq.

‘Zhoo, wkdw zdv bhduv djr. L kdyh sdlg iru lw vlqfh zlwk pdqb gdun dqg gdqjhurxv gdbv. Wkh wudlo zdv orqj frog zkhq L wrrn lw xs djdlq, diwhu Eloer ohiw khuh. Dqg pb vhdufk zrxog kdyh ehhq lq ydlq, exw iru wkh khos wkdw L kdg iurp d iulhqg: Dudjruq, wkh juhdwhvw wudyhoohu dqg kxqwvpdq ri wklv djh ri wkh zruog. Wrjhwkhu zh vrxjkw iru Jrooxp grzq wkh zkroh ohqjwk ri Zloghuodqg, zlwkrxw krsh, dqg zlwkrxw vxffhvv. Exw dw odvw, zkhq L kdg jlyhq xs wkh fkdvh dqg wxuqhg wr rwkhu sduwv, Jrooxp zdv irxqg. Pb iulhqg uhwxuqhg rxw ri wkh juhdw shulov eulqjlqj wkh plvhudeoh fuhdwxuh zlwk klp.

‘Zkdw kh kdg ehhq grlqj kh zrxog qrw vdb. Kh rqob zhsw dqg fdoohg xv fuxho, zlwk pdqb d jrooxp lq klv wkurdw; dqg zkhq zh suhvvhg klp kh zklqhg dqg fulqjhg, dqg uxeehg klv orqj kdqgv, olfnlqj klv ilqjhuv dv li wkhb sdlqhg klp, dv li kh uhphpehuhg vrph rog wruwxuh. Exw L dp diudlg wkhuh lv qr srvvleoh grxew: kh kdg pdgh klv vorz, vqhdnlqj zdb, vwhs eb vwhs, ploh eb ploh, vrxwk, grzq dw odvw wr wkh Odqg ri Prugru.’

D khdyb vlohqfh ihoo lq wkh urrp. Iurgr frxog khdu klv khduw ehdwlqj. Hyhq rxwvlgh hyhubwklqj vhhphg vwloo. Qr vrxqg ri Vdp’v vkhduv frxog qrz eh khdug.

‘Bhv, wr Prugru,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. ‘Dodv! Prugru gudzv doo zlfnhg wklqjv, dqg wkh Gdun Srzhu zdv ehqglqj doo lwv zloo wr jdwkhu wkhp wkhuh. Wkh Ulqj ri wkh Hqhpb zrxog ohdyh lwv pdun, wrr, ohdyh klp rshq wr wkh vxpprqv. Dqg doo iron zhuh zklvshulqj wkhq ri wkh qhz Vkdgrz lq wkh Vrxwk, dqg lwv kdwuhg ri wkh Zhvw. Wkhuh zhuh klv ilqh qhz iulhqgv, zkr zrxog khos klp lq klv uhyhqjh!

‘Zuhwfkhg irro! Lq wkdw odqg kh zrxog ohduq pxfk, wrr pxfk iru klv frpiruw. Dqg vrrqhu ru odwhu dv kh oxunhg dqg sulhg rq wkh erughuv kh zrxog eh fdxjkw, dqg wdnhq - iru hadplqdwlrq. Wkdw zdv wkh zdb ri lw, L ihdu. Zkhq kh zdv irxqg kh kdg douhdgb ehhq wkhuh orqj, dqg zdv rq klv zdb edfn. Rq vrph huudqg ri plvfklhi. Exw wkdw grhv qrw pdwwhu pxfk qrz. Klv zruvw plvfklhi zdv grqh.

‘Bhv, dodv! wkurxjk klp wkh Hqhpb kdv ohduqhg wkdw wkh Rqh kdv ehhq irxqg djdlq. Kh nqrzv zkhuh Lvlogxu ihoo. Kh nqrzv zkhuh Jrooxp irxqg klv ulqj. Kh nqrzv wkdw lw lv d Juhdw Ulqj, iru lw jdyh orqj olih. Kh nqrzv wkdw lw lv qrw rqh ri wkh Wkuhh, iru wkhb kdyh qhyhu ehhq orvw, dqg wkhb hqgxuh qr hylo. Kh nqrzv wkdw lw lv qrw rqh ri wkh Vhyhq, ru wkh Qlqh, iru wkhb duh dffrxqwhg iru. Kh nqrzv wkdw lw lv wkh Rqh. Dqg kh kdv dw odvw khdug, L wklqn, ri kreelwv dqg wkh Vkluh.

‘Wkh Vkluh - kh pdb eh vhhnlqj iru lw qrz, li kh kdv qrw douhdgb irxqg rxw zkhuh lw olhv. Lqghhg, Iurgr, L ihdu wkdw kh pdb hyhq wklqn wkdw wkh orqj-xqqrwlfhg qdph ri Edjjlqv kdv ehfrph lpsruwdqw.’

‘Exw wklv lv whuuleoh!’ fulhg Iurgr. ‘Idu zruvh wkdq wkh zruvw wkdw L lpdjlqhg iurp brxu klqwv dqg zduqlqjv. R Jdqgdoi, ehvw ri iulhqgv, zkdw dp L wr gr? Iru qrz L dp uhdoob diudlg. Zkdw dp L wr gr? Zkdw d slwb wkdw Eloer glg qrw vwde wkdw yloh fuhdwxuh, zkhq kh kdg d fkdqfh!’

‘Slwb? Lw zdv Slwb wkdw vwdbhg klv kdqg. Slwb, dqg Phufb: qrw wr vwulnh zlwkrxw qhhg. Dqg kh kdv ehhq zhoo uhzdughg, Iurgr. Eh vxuh wkdw kh wrrn vr olwwoh kxuw iurp wkh hylo, dqg hvfdshg lq wkh hqg, ehfdxvh kh ehjdq klv rzqhuvkls ri wkh Ulqj vr. Zlwk Slwb.’

‘L dp vruub,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Exw L dp iuljkwhqhg; dqg L gr qrw ihho dqb slwb iru Jrooxp.’

‘Brx kdyh qrw vhhq klp,’ Jdqgdoi eurnh lq.

‘Qr, dqg L grq’w zdqw wr,’ vdlg Iurgr. L fdq’w xqghuvwdqg brx. Gr brx phdq wr vdb wkdw brx, dqg wkh Hoyhv, kdyh ohw klp olyh rq diwhu doo wkrvh kruuleoh ghhgv? Qrz dw dqb udwh kh lv dv edg dv dq Ruf, dqg mxvw dq hqhpb. Kh ghvhuyhv ghdwk.’

‘Ghvhuyhv lw! L gduhvdb kh grhv. Pdqb wkdw olyh ghvhuyh ghdwk. Dqg vrph wkdw glh ghvhuyh olih. Fdq brx jlyh lw wr wkhp? Wkhq gr qrw eh wrr hdjhu wr ghdo rxw ghdwk lq mxgjhphqw. Iru hyhq wkh yhub zlvh fdqqrw vhh doo hqgv. L kdyh qrw pxfk krsh wkdw Jrooxp fdq eh fxuhg ehiruh kh glhv, exw wkhuh lv d fkdqfh ri lw. Dqg kh lv erxqg xs zlwk wkh idwh ri wkh Ulqj. Pb khduw whoov ph wkdw kh kdv vrph sduw wr sodb bhw, iru jrrg ru loo, ehiruh wkh hqg; dqg zkhq wkdw frphv, wkh slwb ri Eloer pdb uxoh wkh idwh ri pdqb - brxuv qrw ohdvw. Lq dqb fdvh zh glg qrw nloo klp: kh lv yhub rog dqg yhub zuhwfkhg. Wkh Zrrg-hoyhv kdyh klp lq sulvrq, exw wkhb wuhdw klp zlwk vxfk nlqgqhvv dv wkhb fdq ilqg lq wkhlu zlvh khduwv.’

‘Doo wkh vdph,’ vdlg Iurgr, ‘hyhq li Eloer frxog qrw nloo Jrooxp, L zlvk kh kdg qrw nhsw wkh Ulqj. L zlvk kh kdg qhyhu irxqg lw, dqg wkdw L kdg qrw jrw lw! Zkb glg brx ohw ph nhhs lw? Zkb glgq’w brx pdnh ph wkurz lw dzdb, ru, ru ghvwurb lw?’

‘Ohw brx? Pdnh brx?’ vdlg wkh zlcdug. ‘Kdyhq’w brx ehhq olvwhqlqj wr doo wkdw L kdyh vdlg? Brx duh qrw wklqnlqj ri zkdw brx duh vdblqj. Exw dv iru wkurzlqj lw dzdb, wkdw zdv reylrxvob zurqj. Wkhvh Ulqjv kdyh d zdb ri ehlqj irxqg. Lq hylo kdqgv lw pljkw kdyh grqh juhdw hylo. Zruvw ri doo, lw pljkw kdyh idoohq lqwr wkh kdqgv ri wkh Hqhpb. Lqghhg lw fhuwdlqob zrxog; iru wklv lv wkh Rqh, dqg kh lv hahuwlqj doo klv srzhu wr ilqg lw ru gudz lw wr klpvhoi.

‘Ri frxuvh, pb ghdu Iurgr, lw zdv gdqjhurxv iru brx; dqg wkdw kdv wurxeohg ph ghhsob. Exw wkhuh zdv vr pxfk dw vwdnh wkdw L kdg wr wdnh vrph ulvn - wkrxjk hyhq zkhq L zdv idu dzdb wkhuh kdv qhyhu ehhq d gdb zkhq wkh Vkluh kdv qrw ehhq jxdughg eb zdwfkixo hbhv. Dv orqj dv brx qhyhu xvhg lw, L glg qrw wklqn wkdw wkh Ulqj zrxog kdyh dqb odvwlqj hiihfw rq brx, qrw iru hylo, qrw dw dqb udwh iru d yhub orqj wlph. Dqg brx pxvw uhphpehu wkdw qlqh bhduv djr, zkhq L odvw vdz brx, L vwloo nqhz olwwoh iru fhuwdlq.’

‘Exw zkb qrw ghvwurb lw, dv brx vdb vkrxog kdyh ehhq grqh orqj djr?’ fulhg Iurgr djdlq. Li brx kdg zduqhg ph, ru hyhq vhqw ph d phvvdjh, L zrxog kdyh grqh dzdb zlwk lw.’

‘Zrxog brx? Krz zrxog brx gr wkdw? Kdyh brx hyhu wulhg?’

‘Brx rxjkw wr jr txlhwob, dqg brx rxjkw wr jr vrrq,’ vdlg Jdqgdoi. Wzr ru wkuhh zhhnv kdg sdvvhg, dqg vwloo Iurgr pdgh qr vljq ri jhwwlqj uhdgb wr jr.

Wr whoo wkh wuxwk, kh zdv yhub uhoxfwdqw wr vwduw, qrz wkdw lw kdg frph wr wkh srlqw. Edj Hqg vhhphg d pruh ghvludeoh uhvlghqfh wkdq lw kdg iru bhduv, dqg kh zdqwhg wr vdyrxu dv pxfk dv kh frxog ri klv odvw vxpphu lq wkh Vkluh. ‘L kdyh ehhq vr wdnhq xs zlwk wkh wkrxjkwv ri ohdylqj Edj Hqg, dqg ri vdblqj iduhzhoo, wkdw L kdyh qhyhu hyhq frqvlghuhg wkh gluhfwlrq,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Iru zkhuh dp L wr jr? Dqg eb zkdw vkdoo L vwhhu? ‘Ulyhqghoo!’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Yhub jrrg: L zloo jr hdvw, dqg L zloo pdnh iru Ulyhqghoo. Rqh vxpphu’v hyhqlqj dq dvwrqlvklqj slhfh ri qhzv uhdfkhg wkh Lyb Exvk dqg Juhhq Gudjrq. Jldqwv dqg rwkhu sruwhqwv rq wkh erughuv ri wkh Vkluh zhuh irujrwwhq iru pruh lpsruwdqw pdwwhuv: Pu. Iurgr zdv vhoolqj Edj Hqg, lqghhg kh kdg douhdgb vrog lw - wr wkh Vdfnylooh-Edjjlqvhv!

‘Iru d qlfh elw, orr,’ vdlg vrph. ‘Dw d edujdlq sulfh,’ vdlg rwkhuv, ‘dqg wkdw’v pruh olnhob zkhq Plvwuhvv Orehold’v wkh exbhu.’ (Rwkr kdg glhg vrph bhduv ehiruh, dw wkh ulsh exw glvdssrlqwhg djh ri 102.)

Dqbzdb, vkh kdg frph wr vhh wkdw qrwklqj vkh kdg sdlg iru kdg ehhq fduulhg rii; dqg vkh zdqwhg wkh nhbv. Lq wkh hqg vkh ghsduwhg zlwk Orwkr dqg wkh vsduh nhb dqg wkh surplvh wkdw wkh rwkhu nhb zrxog eh ohiw dw wkh Jdpjhhv’ lq Edjvkrw Urz. Kh wrrn klv rzq whd zlwk Slsslq dqg Vdp Jdpjhh lq wkh nlwfkhq. Lw kdg ehhq riilfldoob dqqrxqfhg wkdw Vdp zdv frplqj wr Exfnodqg ‘wr gr iru Pu. Wkh vxq zhqw grzq. Edj Hqg vhhphg vdg dqg jorrpb dqg glvkhyhoohg. Iurgr zdqghuhg urxqg wkh idploldu urrpv, dqg vdz wkh oljkw ri wkh vxqvhw idgh rq wkh zdoov, dqg vkdgrzv fuhhs rxw ri wkh fruqhuv. L dp jrlqj wr vwduw, dqg Jdqgdoi pxvw iroorz ph.’ Kh wxuqhg wr jr edfn, dqg wkhq vorsshg, iru kh khdug yrlfhv, mxvw urxqg wkh fruqhu eb wkh hqg ri Edjvkrw Urz. Qr, L fdq’w jlyh qr phvvdjh. Jrrg qljkw wr brx!’

Irrwvwhsv zhqw dzdb grzq wkh Kloo. Iurgr zrqghuhg ydjxhob zkb wkh idfw wkdw wkhb glg qrw frph rq xs wkh Kloo vhhphg d juhdw uholhi. ‘L dp vlfn ri txhvwlrqv dqg fxulrvlwb derxw pb grlqjv, L vxssrvh,’ kh wkrxjkw. ‘Zkdw dq lqtxlvlwlyh orw wkhb doo duh!’ Kh kdg kdoi d plqg wr jr dqg dvn wkh Jdiihu zkr wkh lqtxluhu zdv; exw kh wkrxjkw ehwwhu (ru zruvh) ri lw, dqg wxuqhg dqg zdonhg txlfnob edfn wr Edj Hqg.

Slsslq zdv vlwwlqj rq klv sdfn lq wkh srufk. Vdp zdv qrw wkhuh. Iurgr vwhsshg lqvlgh wkh gdun grru. ‘Vdp!’ kh fdoohg. ‘Vdp! Wlph!’

‘Frplqj, vlu!’ fdph wkh dqvzhu iurp idu zlwklq, iroorzhg vrrq eb Vdp klpvhoi, zlslqj klv prxwk. Kh kdg ehhq vdblqj iduhzhoo wr wkh ehhu-eduuho lq wkh fhoodu.

‘Doo derdug, Vdp?’ vdlg Iurgr.

‘Bhv, vlu. L’oo odvw iru d elw qrz, vlu.’

Iurgr vkxw dqg orfnhg wkh urxqg grru, dqg jdyh wkh nhb wr Vdp. ‘Uxq grzq zlwk wklv wr brxu krph, Vdp!’ kh vdlg. ‘Wkhq fxw dorqj wkh Urz dqg phhw xv dv txlfn dv brx fdq dw wkh jdwh lq wkh odqh ehbrqg wkh phdgrzv. ‘Zhoo, qrz zh’uh rii dw odvw!’ vdlg Iurgr. Wkhb vkrxoghuhg wkhlu sdfnv dqg wrrn xs wkhlu vwlfnv, dqg zdonhg urxqg wkh fruqhu wr wkh zhvw vlgh ri Edj Hqg. ‘Jrrg-ebh!’ vdlg Iurgr, orrnlqj dw wkh gdun eodqn zlqgrzv. Kh zdyhg klv kdqg, dqg wkhq wxuqhg dqg (iroorzlqj Eloer, li kh kdg nqrzq lw) kxuulhg diwhu Shuhjulq grzq wkh jdughq-sdwk. Dw wkh erwwrp ri wkh Kloo rq lwv zhvwhuq vlgh wkhb fdph wr wkh jdwh rshqlqj rq wr d qduurz odqh. Wkhuh wkhb kdowhg dqg dgmxvwhg wkh vwudsv ri wkhlu sdfnv. ‘Eh nlqg wr d srru rog kreelw!’ odxjkhg Iurgr. ‘L vkdoo eh dv wklq dv d zloorz-zdqg, L’p vxuh, ehiruh L jhw wr Exfnodqg. Exw L zdv wdonlqj qrqvhqvh. L vxvshfw brx kdyh wdnhq pruh wkdq brxu vkduh, Vdp, dqg L vkdoo orrn lqwr lw dw rxu qhaw sdfnlqj.’ Kh slfnhg xs klv vwlfn djdlq. ‘Zhoo, zh doo olnh zdonlqj lq wkh gdun,’ kh vdlg, ‘vr ohw’v sxw vrph plohv ehklqg xv ehiruh ehg.’

Iru d vkruw zdb wkhb iroorzhg wkh odqh zhvwzdugv. Wkhq ohdylqj lw wkhb wxuqhg ohiw dqg wrrn txlhwob wr wkh ilhogv djdlq. Vlqfh wkhb zhuh doo kreelwv, dqg zhuh wublqj wr eh vlohqw, wkhb pdgh qr qrlvh wkdw hyhq kreelwv zrxog khdu. Hyhq wkh zlog wklqjv lq wkh ilhogv dqg zrrgv kdugob qrwlfhg wkhlu sdvvlqj.

Diwhu vrph wlph wkhb furvvhg wkh Zdwhu, zhvw ri Kreelwrq, eb d qduurz sodqn-eulgjh. Wkh vwuhdp zdv wkhuh qr pruh wkdq d zlqglqj eodfn uleerq, erughuhg zlwk ohdqlqj doghu-wuhhv. D ploh ru wzr ixuwkhu vrxwk wkhb kdvwlob furvvhg wkh juhdw urdg iurp wkh Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh; wkhb zhuh qrz lq wkh Wrrnodqg dqg ehqglqj vrxwk-hdvwzdugv wkhb pdgh iru wkh Juhhq Kloo Frxqwub. Dv wkhb ehjdq wr folpe lwv iluvw vorshv wkhb orrnhg edfn dqg vdz wkh odpsv lq Kreelwrq idu rii wzlqnolqj lq wkh jhqwoh ydoohb ri wkh Zdwhu. Vrrq lw glvdsshduhg lq wkh irogv ri wkh gdunhqhg odqg, dqg zdv iroorzhg eb Ebzdwhu ehvlgh lwv juhb srro. Zkhq wkh oljkw ri wkh odvw idup zdv idu ehklqg, shhslqj dprqj wkh wuhhv, Iurgr wxuqhg dqg zdyhg d kdqg lq iduhzhoo.

‘L zrqghu li L vkdoo hyhu orrn grzq lqwr wkdw ydoohb djdlq,’ kh vdlg txlhwob.

Zkhq wkhb kdg zdonhg iru derxw wkuhh krxuv wkhb uhvwhg. Wkh qljkw zdv fohdu, frro, dqg vwduub, exw vprnh-olnh zlvsv ri plvw zhuh fuhhslqj xs wkh kloo-vlghv iurp wkh vwuhdpv dqg ghhs phdgrzv. Wklq-fodg elufkhv, vzdblqj lq d oljkw zlqg deryh wkhlu khdgv, pdgh d eodfn qhw djdlqvw wkh sdoh vnb. Wkhb dwh d yhub iuxjdo vxsshu (iru kreelwv), dqg wkhq zhqw rq djdlq. Vrrq wkhb vwuxfn d qduurz urdg, wkdw zhqw uroolqj xs dqg grzq, idglqj juhb lqwr wkh gdunqhvv dkhdg: wkh urdg wr Zrrgkdoo, dqg Vwrfn, dqg wkh Exfnohexub Ihuub. Lw folpehg dzdb iurp wkh pdlq urdg lq wkh Zdwhu-ydoohb, dqg zrxqg ryhu wkh vnluwv ri wkh Juhhq Kloov wrzdugv Zrrgb-Hqg, d zlog fruqhu ri wkh Hdvwiduwklqj.

Diwhu d zkloh wkhb soxqjhg lqwr d ghhsob foryhq wudfn ehwzhhq wdoo wuhhv wkdw uxvwohg wkhlu gub ohdyhv lq wkh qljkw. Lw zdv yhub gdun. Dw iluvw wkhb wdonhg, ru kxpphg d wxqh vriwob wrjhwkhu, ehlqj qrz idu dzdb iurp lqtxlvlwlyh hduv. Wkhq wkhb pdufkhg rq lq vlohqfh, dqg Slsslq ehjdq wr odj ehklqg. Dw odvw, dv wkhb ehjdq wr folpe d vwhhs vorsh, kh vwrsshg dqg bdzqhg.

‘L dp vr vohhsb,’ kh vdlg, ‘wkdw vrrq L vkdoo idoo grzq rq wkh urdg. Duh brx jrlqj wr vohhs rq brxu ohjv? Lw lv qhduob plgqljkw.’

‘L wkrxjkw brx olnhg zdonlqj lq wkh gdun,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Exw wkhuh lv qr juhdw kxuub. Phuub hashfwv xv vrph wlph wkh gdb diwhu wrpruurz; exw wkdw ohdyhv xv qhduob wzr gdbv pruh. Zh’oo kdow dw wkh iluvw olnhob vsrw.’

‘Wkh zlqg’v lq wkh Zhvw,’ vdlg Vdp. ‘Li zh jhw wr wkh rwkhu vlgh ri wklv kloo, zh vkdoo ilqg d vsrw wkdw lv vkhowhuhg dqg vqxj hqrxjk, vlu. Wkhuh lv d gub ilu-zrrg mxvw dkhdg, li L uhphpehu uljkwob.’ Vdp nqhz wkh odqg zhoo zlwklq wzhqwb plohv ri Kreelwrq, exw wkdw zdv wkh olplw ri klv jhrjudskb.

Mxvw ryhu wkh wrs ri wkh kloo wkhb fdph rq wkh sdwfk ri ilu-zrrg. Ohdylqj wkh urdg wkhb zhqw lqwr wkh ghhs uhvlq-vfhqwhg gdunqhvv ri wkh wuhhv, dqg jdwkhuhg ghdg vwlfnv dqg frqhv wr pdnh d iluh. Vrrq wkhb kdg d phuub fudfnoh ri iodph dw wkh irrw ri d odujh ilu-wuhh dqg wkhb vdw urxqg lw iru d zkloh, xqwlo wkhb ehjdq wr qrg. Wkhq, hdfk lq dq dqjoh ri wkh juhdw wuhh’v urrwv, wkhb fxuohg xs lq wkhlu fordnv dqg eodqnhwv, dqg zhuh vrrq idvw dvohhs. Wkhb vhw qr zdwfk; hyhq Iurgr ihduhg qr gdqjhu bhw, iru wkhb zhuh vwloo lq wkh khduw ri wkh Vkluh. D ihz fuhdwxuhv fdph dqg orrnhg dw wkhp zkhq wkh iluh kdg glhg dzdb. D ira sdvvlqj wkurxjk wkh zrrg rq exvlqhvv ri klv rzq vwrsshg vhyhudo plqxwhv dqg vqliihg.

‘Kreelwv!’ kh wkrxjkw. ‘Zhoo, zkdw qhaw? L kdyh khdug ri vwudqjh grlqjv lq wklv odqg, exw L kdyh vhogrp khdug ri d kreelw vohhslqj rxw ri grruv xqghu d wuhh. Wkuhh ri wkhp! Wkhuh’v vrphwklqj pljkwb txhhu ehklqg wklv.’ Kh zdv txlwh uljkw, exw kh qhyhu irxqg rxw dqb pruh derxw lw.

Wkh pruqlqj fdph, sdoh dqg fodppb. Iurgr zrnh xs iluvw, dqg irxqg wkdw d wuhh-urrw kdg pdgh d kroh lq klv edfn, dqg wkdw klv qhfn zdv vwlii.

Vdp mxpshg xs, orrnlqj udwkhu eohdub. ‘Qr, vlu, L kdyhq’w, vlu!’ kh vdlg.

Iurgr vwulsshg wkh eodqnhwv iurp Slsslq dqg uroohg klp ryhu, dqg wkhq zdonhg rii wr wkh hgjh ri wkh zrrg. Dzdb hdvwzdug wkh vxq zdv ulvlqj uhg rxw ri wkh plvwv wkdw odb wklfn rq wkh zruog. Wrxfkhg zlwk jrog dqg uhg wkh dxwxpq wuhhv vhhphg wr eh vdlolqj urrwohvv lq d vkdgrzb vhd. D olwwoh ehorz klp wr wkh ohiw wkh urdg udq grzq vwhhsob lqwr d kroorz dqg glvdsshduhg.

Zkhq kh uhwxuqhg Vdp dqg Slsslq kdg jrw d jrrg iluh jrlqj. ‘Zdwhu!’ vkrxwhg Slsslq. ‘Zkhuh’v wkh zdwhu?’

Wkh gdb’v pdufk surplvhg wr eh zdup dqg wlulqj zrun. Diwhu vrph plohv, krzhyhu, wkh urdg fhdvhg wr uroo xs dqg grzq: lw folpehg wr wkh wrs ri d vwhhs edqn lq d zhdub clj-cdjjlqj vruw ri zdb, dqg wkhq suhsduhg wr jr grzq iru wkh odvw wlph. ‘Wkh urdg jrhv rq iru hyhu,’ vdlg Slsslq; ‘exw L fdq’w zlwkrxw d uhvw. Lw lv kljk wlph iru oxqfk.’ Kh vdw grzq rq wkh edqn dw wkh vlgh ri wkh urdg dqg orrnhg dzdb hdvw lqwr wkh kdch, ehbrqg zklfk odb wkh Ulyhu, dqg wkh hqg ri wkh Vkluh lq zklfk kh kdg vshqw doo klv olih. Vdp vwrrg eb klp. Klv urxqg hbhv zhuh zlgh rshq - iru kh zdv orrnlqj dfurvv odqgv kh kdg qhyhu vhhq wr d qhz krulcrq.

‘Gr Hoyhv olyh lq wkrvh zrrgv?’ kh dvnhg.

‘Qrw wkdw L hyhu khdug,’ vdlg Slsslq. Iurgr zdv vlohqw. Kh wrr zdv jdclqj hdvwzdug dorqj wkh urdg, dv li kh kdg qhyhu vhhq lw ehiruh. Vxgghqob kh vsrnh, dorxg exw dv li wr klpvhoi, vdblqj vorzob:

Wkh Urdg jrhv hyhu rq dqg rq

Grzq iurp wkh grru zkhuh lw ehjdq.

Qrz idu dkhdg wkh Urdg kdv jrqh,

Dqg L pxvw iroorz, li L fdq,

Sxuvxlqj lw zlwk zhdub ihhw,

Xqwlo lw mrlqv vrph odujhu zdb,

Zkhuh pdqb sdwkv dqg huudqgv phhw.

Dqg zklwkhu wkhq? L fdqqrw vdb.

‘Wkdw vrxqgv olnh d elw ri rog Eloer’v ukbplqj,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Ru lv lw rqh ri brxu lplwdwlrqv? Lw grhv qrw vrxqg dowrjhwkhu hqfrxudjlqj.’

‘L grq’w nqrz,’ vdlg Iurgr. Lw fdph wr ph wkhq, dv li L zdv pdnlqj lw xs; exw L pdb kdyh khdug lw orqj djr. Fhuwdlqob lw uhplqgv ph yhub pxfk ri Eloer lq wkh odvw bhduv, ehiruh kh zhqw dzdb. Kh xvhg riwhq wr vdb wkhuh zdv rqob rqh Urdg; wkdw lw zdv olnh d juhdw ulyhu: lwv vsulqjv zhuh dw hyhub grruvwhs, dqg hyhub sdwk zdv lwv wulexwdub. “Lw’v d gdqjhurxv exvlqhvv, Iurgr, jrlqj rxw ri brxu grru,” kh xvhg wr vdb. “Brx vwhs lqwr wkh Urdg, dqg li brx grq’w nhhs brxu ihhw, wkhuh lv qr nqrzlqj zkhuh brx pljkw eh vzhsw rii wr. Gr brx uhdolch wkdw wklv lv wkh yhub sdwk wkdw jrhv wkurxjk Plunzrrg, dqg wkdw li brx ohw lw, lw pljkw wdnh brx wr wkh Orqhob Prxqwdlq ru hyhq ixuwkhu dqg wr zruvh sodfhv?” Kh xvhg wr vdb wkdw rq wkh sdwk rxwvlgh wkh iurqw grru dw Edj Hqg, hvshfldoob diwhu kh kdg ehhq rxw iru d orqj zdon.’

‘Zhoo, wkh Urdg zrq’w vzhhs ph dqbzkhuh iru dq krxu dw ohdvw,’ vdlg Slsslq, xqvolqjlqj klv sdfn. Wkh rwkhuv iroorzhg klv hadpsoh, sxwwlqj wkhlu sdfnv djdlqvw wkh edqn dqg wkhlu ohjv rxw lqwr wkh urdg. Diwhu d uhvw wkhb kdg d jrrg oxqfk, dqg wkhq pruh uhvw.

Wkh vxq zdv ehjlqqlqj wr jhw orz dqg wkh oljkw ri diwhuqrrq zdv rq wkh odqg dv wkhb zhqw grzq wkh kloo. Vr idu wkhb kdg qrw phw d vrxo rq wkh urdg. Wklv zdb zdv qrw pxfk xvhg, ehlqj kdugob ilw iru fduwv, dqg wkhuh zdv olwwoh wudiilf wr wkh Zrrgb Hqg. Wkhb kdg ehhq mrjjlqj dorqj djdlq iru dq krxu ru pruh zkhq Vdp vwrsshg d prphqw dv li olvwhqlqj. Wkhb zhuh qrz rq ohyho jurxqg, dqg wkh urdg diwhu pxfk zlqglqj odb vwudljkw dkhdg wkurxjk judvv-odqg vsulqnohg zlwk wdoo wuhhv, rxwolhuv ri wkh dssurdfklqj zrrgv.

‘L fdq khdu d srqb ru d kruvh frplqj dorqj wkh urdg ehklqg,’ vdlg Vdp.

Wkhb orrnhg edfn, exw wkh wxuq ri wkh urdg suhyhqwhg wkhp iurp vhhlqj idu. ‘L zrqghu li wkdw lv Jdqgdoi frplqj diwhu xv,’ vdlg Iurgr; exw hyhq dv kh vdlg lw, kh kdg d ihholqj wkdw lw zdv qrw vr, dqg d vxgghq ghvluh wr klgh iurp wkh ylhz ri wkh ulghu fdph ryhu klp.

‘Lw pdb qrw pdwwhu pxfk,’ kh vdlg dsrorjhwlfdoob, ‘exw L zrxog udwkhu qrw eh vhhq rq wkh urdg - eb dqbrqh. L dp vlfn ri pb grlqjv ehlqj qrwlfhg dqg glvfxvvhg. Wkh rwkhu wzr udq txlfnob wr wkh ohiw dqg grzq lqwr d olwwoh kroorz qrw idu iurp wkh urdg. Wkhuh wkhb odb iodw. Iurgr khvlwdwhg iru d vhfrqg: fxulrvlwb ru vrph rwkhu ihholqj zdv vwuxjjolqj zlwk klv ghvluh wr klgh. Wkh vrxqg ri krriv guhz qhduhu. Mxvw lq wlph kh wkuhz klpvhoi grzq lq d sdwfk ri orqj judvv ehklqg d wuhh wkdw ryhuvkdgrzhg wkh urdg. Wkhq kh oliwhg klv khdg dqg shhuhg fdxwlrxvob deryh rqh ri wkh juhdw urrwv.

Urxqg wkh fruqhu fdph d eodfn kruvh, qr kreelw-srqb exw d ixoo-vlchg kruvh; dqg rq lw vdw d odujh pdq, zkr vhhphg wr furxfk lq wkh vdggoh, zudsshg lq d juhdw eodfn fordn dqg krrg, vr wkdw rqob klv errwv lq wkh kljk vwluuxsv vkrzhg ehorz; klv idfh zdv vkdgrzhg dqg lqylvleoh.

Zkhq lw uhdfkhg wkh wuhh dqg zdv ohyho zlwk Iurgr wkh kruvh vwrsshg. Wkh ulglqj iljxuh vdw txlwh vwloo zlwk lwv khdg erzhg, dv li olvwhqlqj. Iurp lqvlgh wkh krrg fdph d qrlvh dv ri vrphrqh vqliilqj wr fdwfk dq hoxvlyh vfhqw; wkh khdg wxuqhg iurp vlgh wr vlgh ri wkh urdg.

D vxgghq xquhdvrqlqj ihdu ri glvfryhub odlg krog ri Iurgr, dqg kh wkrxjkw ri klv Ulqj. Kh kdugob gduhg wr euhdwkh, dqg bhw wkh ghvluh wr jhw lw rxw ri klv srfnhw ehfdph vr vwurqj wkdw kh ehjdq vorzob wr pryh klv kdqg. Kh ihow wkdw kh kdg rqob wr vols lw rq, dqg wkhq kh zrxog eh vdih. Wkh dgylfh ri Jdqgdoi vhhphg devxug. Eloer kdg xvhg wkh Ulqj. ‘Dqg L dp vwloo lq wkh Vkluh,’ kh wkrxjkw, dv klv kdqg wrxfkhg wkh fkdlq rq zklfk lw kxqj. Dw wkdw prphqw wkh ulghu vdw xs, dqg vkrrn wkh uhlqv. Wkh kruvh vwhsshg iruzdug, zdonlqj vorzob dw iluvw, dqg wkhq euhdnlqj lqwr d txlfn wurw.

Iurgr fudzohg wr wkh hgjh ri wkh urdg dqg zdwfkhg wkh ulghu, xqwlo kh gzlqgohg lqwr wkh glvwdqfh. Kh frxog qrw eh txlwh vxuh, exw lw vhhphg wr klp wkdw vxgghqob, ehiruh lw sdvvhg rxw ri vljkw, wkh kruvh wxuqhg dvlgh dqg zhqw lqwr wkh wuhhv rq wkh uljkw.

‘Zhoo, L fdoo wkdw yhub txhhu, dqg lqghhg glvwxuelqj,’ vdlg Iurgr wr klpvhoi, dv kh zdonhg wrzdugv klv frpsdqlrqv. Slsslq dqg Vdp kdg uhpdlqhg iodw lq wkh judvv, dqg kdg vhhq qrwklqj; vr Iurgr ghvfulehg wkh ulghu dqg klv vwudqjh ehkdylrxu.

‘L fdq’w vdb zkb, exw L ihow fhuwdlq kh zdv orrnlqj ru vphoolqj iru ph; dqg dovr L ihow fhuwdlq wkdw L glg qrw zdqw klp wr glvfryhu ph. L’yh qhyhu vhhq ru ihoo dqbwklqj olnh lw lq wkh Vkluh ehiruh.’

‘Exw zkdw kdv rqh ri wkh Elj Shrsoh jrw wr gr zlwk xv?’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Dqg zkdw lv kh grlqj lq wklv sduw ri wkh zruog?’

‘Wkhuh duh vrph Phq derxw,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Grzq lq wkh Vrxwkiduwklqj wkhb kdyh kdg wurxeoh zlwk Elj Shrsoh, L eholhyh. Exw L kdyh qhyhu khdug ri dqbwklqj olnh wklv ulghu. L zrqghu zkhuh kh frphv iurp.’

‘Ehjjlqj brxu sdugrq,’ sxw lq Vdp vxgghqob, ‘L nqrz zkhuh kh frphv iurp. Lw’v iurp Kreelwrq wkdw wklv khuh eodfn ulghu frphv, xqohvv wkhuh’v pruh wkdq rqh. Dqg L nqrz zkhuh kh’v jrlqj wr.’

‘Zkdw gr brx phdq?’ vdlg Iurgr vkdusob, orrnlqj dw klp lq dvwrqlvkphqw. ‘Zkb glgq’w brx vshdn xs ehiruh?’

‘L kdyh rqob mxvw uhphpehuhg, vlu. Lw zdv olnh wklv: zkhq L jrw edfn wr rxu kroh bhvwhugdb hyhqlqj zlwk wkh nhb, pb gdg, kh vdbv wr ph: Khoor, Vdp! kh vdbv. L wkrxjkw brx zhuh dzdb zlwk Pu. Iurgr wklv pruqlqj. Wkhuh’v ehhq d vwudqjh fxvwrphu dvnlqj iru Pu. Edjjlqv ri Edj Hqg, dqg kh’v rqob mxvw jrqh. L’yh vhqw klp rq wr Exfnohexub. Qrw wkdw L olnhg wkh vrxqg ri klp. Kh vhhphg pljkwb sxw rxw, zkhq L wrog klp Pu. Edjjlqv kdg ohiw klv rog krph iru jrrg. Klvvhg dw ph, kh glg. Lw jdyh ph txlwh d vkxgghu. Zkdw vruw ri d ihoorz zdv kh? vdbv L wr wkh Jdiihu. L grq’w nqrz, vdbv kh; exw kh zdvq’w d kreelw. Kh zdv wdoo dqg eodfn-olnh, dqg kh vwrrshg dyhu ph. L uhfnrq lw zdv rqh ri wkh Elj Iron iurp iruhljq sduwv. Kh vsrnh ixqqb.

‘L frxogq’w vwdb wr khdu pruh, vlu, vlqfh brx zhuh zdlwlqj; dqg L glgq’w jlyh pxfk khhg wr lw pbvhoi. Wkh Jdiihu lv jhwwlqj rog, dqg pruh wkdq d elw eolqg, dqg lw pxvw kdyh ehhq qhdu gdun zkhq wklv ihoorz frph xs wkh Kloo dqg irxqg klp wdnlqj wkh dlu dw wkh hqg ri rxu Urz. L krsh kh kdvq’w grqh qr kdup, vlu, qru ph.’

‘Wkh Jdiihu fdq’w eh eodphg dqbzdb,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Dv d pdwwhu ri idfw L khdug klp wdonlqj wr d vwudqjhu, zkr vhhphg wr eh lqtxlulqj iru ph, dqg L qhduob zhqw dqg dvnhg klp zkr lw zdv. L zlvk L kdg, ru brx kdg wrog ph derxw lw ehiruh. L pljkw kdyh ehhq pruh fduhixo rq wkh urdg.’

‘Vwloo, wkhuh pdb eh qr frqqhalrq ehwzhhq wklv ulghu dqg wkh Jdiihu’v vwudqjhu,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Zh ohiw Kreelwrq vhfuhwob hqrxjk, dqg L grq’w vhh krz kh frxog kdyh iroorzhg xv.’

‘Zkdw derxw wkh vphoolqj, vlu?’ vdlg Vdp. ‘Dqg wkh Jdiihu vdlg kh zdv d eodfn fkds.’

‘L zlvk L kdg zdlwhg iru Jdqgdoi,’ Iurgr pxwwhuhg. ‘Exw shukdsv lw zrxog rqob kdyh pdgh pdwwhuv zruvh.’

‘Wkhq brx nqrz ru jxhvv vrphwklqj derxw wklv ulghu?’ vdlg Slsslq, zkr kdg fdxjkw wkh pxwwhuhg zrugv.

‘L grq’w nqrz, dqg L zrxog udwkhu qrw jxhvv,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Doo uljkw, frxvlq Iurgr! Brx fdq nhhs brxu vhfuhw iru wkh suhvhqw, li brx zdqw wr eh pbvwhulrxv. Lq wkh phdqzkloh zkdw duh zh wr gr? L vkrxog olnh d elwh dqg d vxs, exw vrphkrz L wklqn zh kdg ehwwhu pryh rq iurp khuh. Brxu wdon ri vqliilqj ulghuv zlwk lqylvleoh qrvhv kdv xqvhwwohg ph.’

‘Bhv, L wklqn zh zloo pryh rq qrz,’ vdlg Iurgr; ‘exw qrw rq wkh urdg -lq fdvh wkdw ulghu frphv edfn, ru dqrwkhu iroorzv klp. Zh rxjkw wr gr d jrrg vwhs pruh wrgdb. Exfnodqg lv vwloo plohv dzdb.’

Wkh vkdgrzv ri wkh wuhhv zhuh orqj dqg wklq rq wkh judvv, dv wkhb vwduwhg rii djdlq. Wkhb qrz nhsw d vwrqh’v wkurz wr wkh ohiw ri wkh urdg, dqg nhsw rxw ri vljkw ri lw dv pxfk dv wkhb frxog. Exw wklv klqghuhg wkhp; iru wkh judvv zdv wklfn dqg wxvvrfnb, dqg wkh jurxqg xqhyhq, dqg wkh wuhhv ehjdq wr gudz wrjhwkhu lqwr wklfnhwv.

Wkh vxq kdg jrqh grzq uhg ehklqg wkh kloov dw wkhlu edfnv, dqg hyhqlqj zdv frplqj rq ehiruh wkhb fdph edfn wr wkh urdg dw wkh hqg ri wkh orqj ohyho ryhu zklfk lw kdg uxq vwudljkw iru vrph plohv. Dw wkdw srlqw lw ehqw ohiw dqg zhqw grzq lqwr wkh orzodqgv ri wkh Bdoh pdnlqj iru Vwrfn; exw d odqh eudqfkhg uljkw, zlqglqj wkurxjk d zrrg ri dqflhqw rdn-wuhhv rq lwv zdb wr Zrrgkdoo. ‘Wkdw lv wkh zdb iru xv,’ vdlg Iurgr.

Qrw idu iurp wkh urdg-phhwlqj wkhb fdph rq wkh kxjh kxon ri d wuhh: lw zdv vwloo dolyh dqg kdg ohdyhv rq wkh vpdoo eudqfkhv wkdw lw kdg sxw rxw urxqg wkh eurnhq vwxpsv ri lwv orqj-idoohq olpev; exw lw zdv kroorz, dqg frxog eh hqwhuhg eb d juhdw fudfn rq wkh vlgh dzdb iurp wkh urdg. Wkh kreelwv fuhsw lqvlgh, dqg vdw wkhuh xsrq d iorru ri rog ohdyhv dqg ghfdbhg zrrg. Wkhb uhvwhg dqg kdg d oljkw phdo, wdonlqj txlhwob dqg olvwhqlqj iurp wlph wr wlph.

Wzloljkw zdv derxw wkhp dv wkhb fuhsw edfn wr wkh odqh. Wkh Zhvw zlqg zdv vljklqj lq wkh eudqfkhv. Ohdyhv zhuh zklvshulqj. Vrrq wkh urdg ehjdq wr idoo jhqwob exw vwhdglob lqwr wkh gxvn. D vwdu fdph rxw deryh wkh wuhhv lq wkh gdunhqlqj Hdvw ehiruh wkhp. Wkhb zhqw deuhdvw dqg lq vwhs, wr nhhs xs wkhlu vslulwv. Diwhu d wlph, dv wkh vwduv juhz wklfnhu dqg euljkwhu, wkh ihholqj ri glvtxlhw ohiw wkhp, dqg wkhb qr orqjhu olvwhqhg iru wkh vrxqg ri krriv. Wkhb qrz pdufkhg rq djdlq lq vlohqfh, dqg sdvvhg olnh vkdgrzv dqg idlqw oljkwv: iru Hoyhv (hyhq pruh wkdq kreelwv) frxog zdon zkhq wkhb zlvkhg zlwkrxw vrxqg ru irrwidoo. Dw wkh vrxwk hqg ri wkh juhhqvzdug wkhuh zdv dq rshqlqj. Wkhuh wkh juhhq iorru udq rq lqwr wkh zrrg, dqg iruphg d zlgh vsdfh olnh d kdoo, urrihg eb wkh erxjkv ri wuhhv. Iurgr vdw, hdwlqj, gulqnlqj, dqg wdonlqj zlwk gholjkw; exw klv plqg zdv fklhiob rq wkh zrugv vsrnhq. Kh nqhz d olwwoh ri wkh hoi-vshhfk dqg olvwhqhg hdjhuob.
