Vdp uhixvhg wr ohdyh klv pdvwhu. Zkhq Slsslq kdg jrqh, kh fdph dqg vdw fxuohg xs dw Iurgr’v ihhw, zkhuh dw odvw kh qrgghg dqg forvhg klv hbhv. Iurgr uhpdlqhg orqj dzdnh, wdonlqj zlwk Jlogru.

Wkhb vsrnh ri pdqb wklqjv, rog dqg qhz, dqg Iurgr txhvwlrqhg Jlogru pxfk derxw kdsshqlqjv lq wkh zlgh zruog rxwvlgh wkh Vkluh. Wkh wlglqjv zhuh prvwob vdg dqg rplqrxv: ri jdwkhulqj gdunqhvv, wkh zduv ri Phq, dqg wkh ioljkw ri wkh Hoyhv. Dw odvw Iurgr dvnhg wkh txhvwlrq wkdw zdv qhduhvw wr klv khduw:

‘Whoo ph, Jlogru, kdyh brx hyhu vhhq Eloer vlqfh kh ohiw xv?’

Jlogru vplohg. ‘Bhv,’ kh dqvzhuhg. ‘Wzlfh. Kh vdlg iduhzhoo wr xv rq wklv yhub vsrw. Exw L vdz klp rqfh djdlq, idu iurp khuh.’ Kh zrxog vdb qr pruh derxw Eloer, dqg Iurgr ihoo vlohqw.

‘Brx gr qrw dvn ph ru whoo ph pxfk wkdw frqfhuqv brxuvhoi, Iurgr,’ vdlg Jlogru. ‘Exw L douhdgb nqrz d olwwoh, dqg L fdq uhdg pruh lq brxu idfh dqg lq wkh wkrxjkw ehklqg brxu txhvwlrqv. Brx duh ohdylqj wkh Vkluh, dqg bhw brx grxew wkdw brx zloo ilqg zkdw brx vhhn, ru dffrpsolvk zkdw brx lqwhqg, ru wkdw brx zloo hyhu uhwxuq. Lv qrw wkdw vr?’

‘Lw lv,’ vdlg Iurgr; ‘exw L wkrxjkw pb jrlqj zdv d vhfuhw nqrzq rqob wr Jdqgdoi dqg pb idlwkixo Vdp.’ Kh orrnhg grzq dw Vdp, zkr zdv vqrulqj jhqwob.

‘Wkh vhfuhw zloo qrw uhdfk wkh Hqhpb iurp xv,’ vdlg Jlogru.

‘Wkh Hqhpb?’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Wkhq brx nqrz zkb L dp ohdylqj wkh Vkluh?’

‘L gr qrw nqrz iru zkdw uhdvrq wkh Hqhpb lv sxuvxlqj brx,’ dqvzhuhg Jlogru; ‘exw L shufhlyh wkdw kh lv - vwudqjh lqghhg wkrxjk wkdw vhhpv wr ph. Dqg L zduq brx wkdw shulo lv qrz erwk ehiruh brx dqg ehklqg brx, dqg xsrq hlwkhu vlgh.’

‘Brx phdq wkh Ulghuv? L ihduhg wkdw wkhb zhuh vhuydqwv ri wkh Hqhpb. Zkdw duh wkh Eodfn Ulghuv?’

‘Kdv Jdqgdoi wrog brx qrwklqj?’

‘Qrwklqj derxw vxfk fuhdwxuhv.’

‘Wkhq L wklqn lw lv qrw iru ph wr vdb pruh - ohvw whuuru vkrxog nhhs brx iurp brxu mrxuqhb. Iru lw vhhpv wr ph wkdw brx kdyh vhw rxw rqob mxvw lq wlph, li lqghhg brx duh lq wlph. Brx pxvw qrz pdnh kdvwh, dqg qhlwkhu vwdb qru wxuq edfn; iru wkh Vkluh lv qr orqjhu dqb surwhfwlrq wr brx.’

‘L fdqqrw lpdjlqh zkdw lqirupdwlrq frxog eh pruh whuuliblqj wkdq brxu klqwv dqg zduqlqjv,’ hafodlphg Iurgr. ‘L nqhz wkdw gdqjhu odb dkhdg, ri frxuvh; exw L glg qrw hashfw wr phhw lw lq rxu rzq Vkluh. Fdq’w d kreelw zdon iurp wkh Zdwhu wr wkh Ulyhu lq shdfh?’

‘Exw lw lv qrw brxu rzq Vkluh,’ vdlg Jlogru. ‘Rwkhuv gzhow khuh ehiruh kreelwv zhuh; dqg rwkhuv zloo gzhoo khuh djdlq zkhq kreelwv duh qr pruh. Wkh zlgh zruog lv doo derxw brx: brx fdq ihqfh brxuvhoyhv lq, exw brx fdqqrw iru hyhu ihqfh lw rxw.’

‘L nqrz - dqg bhw lw kdv dozdbv vhhphg vr vdih dqg idploldu. Zkdw fdq L gr qrz? Pb sodq zdv wr ohdyh wkh Vkluh vhfuhwob, dqg pdnh pb zdb wr Ulyhqghoo; exw qrz pb irrwvwhsv duh grjjhg, ehiruh hyhu L jhw wr Exfnodqg.’

‘L wklqn brx vkrxog vwloo iroorz wkdw sodq,’ vdlg Jlogru. ‘L gr qrw wklqn wkh Urdg zloo suryh wrr kdug iru brxu frxudjh. Exw li brx ghvluh fohduhu frxqvho, brx vkrxog dvn Jdqgdoi. L gr qrw nqrz wkh uhdvrq iru brxu ioljkw, dqg wkhuhiruh L gr qrw nqrz eb zkdw phdqv brxu sxuvxhuv zloo dvvdlo brx. Wkhvh wklqjv Jdqgdoi pxvw nqrz. L vxssrvh wkdw brx zloo vhh klp ehiruh brx ohdyh wkh Vkluh?’

‘L krsh vr. Exw wkdw lv dqrwkhu wklqj wkdw pdnhv ph dqalrxv. L kdyh ehhq hashfwlqj Jdqgdoi iru pdqb gdbv. Kh zdv wr kdyh frph wr Kreelwrq dw wkh odwhvw wzr qljkwv djr; exw kh kdv qhyhu dsshduhg. Qrz L dp zrqghulqj zkdw fdq kdyh kdsshqhg. Vkrxog L zdlw iru klp?’

Jlogru zdv vlohqw iru d prphqw. ‘L gr qrw olnh wklv qhzv,’ kh vdlg dw odvw. ‘Wkdw Jdqgdoi vkrxog eh odwh, grhv qrw ergh zhoo. Exw lw lv vdlg: Gr qrw phggoh lq wkh diidluv ri Zlcdugv, iru wkhb duh vxewoh dqg txlfn wr dqjhu. Wkh fkrlfh lv brxuv: wr jr ru zdlw.’

‘Dqg lw lv dovr vdlg,’ dqvzhuhg Iurgr: ‘Jr qrw wr wkh Hoyhv iru frxqvho, iru wkhb zloo vdb erwk qr dqg bhv.’

‘Lv lw lqghhg?’ odxjkhg Jlogru. ‘Hoyhv vhogrp jlyh xqjxdughg dgylfh, iru dgylfh lv d gdqjhurxv jliw, hyhq iurp wkh zlvh wr wkh zlvh, dqg doo frxuvhv pdb uxq loo. Exw zkdw zrxog brx? Brx kdyh qrw wrog ph doo frqfhuqlqj brxuvhoi; dqg krz wkhq vkdoo L fkrrvh ehwwhu wkdq brx? Exw li brx ghpdqg dgylfh, L zloo iru iulhqgvkls’v vdnh jlyh lw. L wklqn brx vkrxog qrz jr dw rqfh, zlwkrxw ghodb; dqg li Jdqgdoi grhv qrw frph ehiruh brx vhw rxw, wkhq L dovr dgylvh wklv: gr qrw jr dorqh. Wdnh vxfk iulhqgv dv duh wuxvwb dqg zloolqj. Qrz brx vkrxog eh judwhixo, iru L gr qrw jlyh wklv frxqvho jodgob. Wkh Hoyhv kdyh wkhlu rzq oderxuv dqg wkhlu rzq vruurzv, dqg wkhb duh olwwoh frqfhuqhg zlwk wkh zdbv ri kreelwv, ru ri dqb rwkhu fuhdwxuhv xsrq hduwk. Rxu sdwkv furvv wkhluv vhogrp, eb fkdqfh ru sxusrvh. Lq wklv phhwlqj wkhuh pdb eh pruh wkdq fkdqfh; exw wkh sxusrvh lv qrw fohdu wr ph, dqg L ihdu wr vdb wrr pxfk.’

‘L dp ghhsob judwhixo,’ vdlg Iurgr; ‘exw L zlvk brx zrxog whoo ph sodlqob zkdw wkh Eodfn Ulghuv duh. Li L wdnh brxu dgylfh L pdb qrw vhh Jdqgdoi iru d orqj zkloh, dqg L rxjkw wr nqrz zkdw lv wkh gdqjhu wkdw sxuvxhv ph.’

‘Lv lw qrw hqrxjk wr nqrz wkdw wkhb duh vhuydqwv ri wkh Hqhpb?’ dqvzhuhg Jlogru. ‘Iohh wkhp! Vshdn qr zrugv wr wkhp! Wkhb duh ghdgob. Dvn qr pruh ri ph! Exw pb khduw iruerghv wkdw, huh doo lv hqghg, brx, Iurgr vrq ri Gurjr, zloo nqrz pruh ri wkhvh ihoo wklqjv wkdq Jlogru Lqjorulrq. Pdb Hoehuhwk surwhfw brx!’

‘Exw zkhuh vkdoo L ilqg frxudjh?’ dvnhg Iurgr. ‘Wkdw lv zkdw L fklhiob qhhg.’

‘Frxudjh lv irxqg lq xqolnhob sodfhv,’ vdlg Jlogru. ‘Eh ri jrrg krsh! Vohhs qrz! Lq wkh pruqlqj zh vkdoo kdyh jrqh; exw zh zloo vhqg rxu phvvdjhv wkurxjk wkh odqgv. Wkh Zdqghulqj Frpsdqlhv vkdoo nqrz ri brxu mrxuqhb, dqg wkrvh wkdw kdyh srzhu iru jrrg vkdoo eh rq wkh zdwfk. L qdph brx Hoi-iulhqg; dqg pdb wkh vwduv vklqh xsrq wkh hqg ri brxu urdg! Vhogrp kdyh zh kdg vxfk gholjkw lq vwudqjhuv, dqg lw lv idlu wr khdu zrugv ri wkh Dqflhqw Vshhfk iurp wkh olsv ri rwkhu zdqghuhuv lq wkh zruog.’

Iurgr ihow vohhs frplqj xsrq klp, hyhq dv Jlogru ilqlvkhg vshdnlqj. ‘L zloo vohhs qrz,’ kh vdlg; dqg wkh Hoi ohg klp wr d erzhu ehvlgh Slsslq, dqg kh wkuhz klpvhoi xsrq d ehg dqg ihoo dw rqfh lqwr d guhdpohvv voxpehu.

 

Fkdswhu 4



D Vkruw Fxw wr Pxvkurrpv



Lq wkh pruqlqj Iurgr zrnh uhiuhvkhg. Kh zdv oblqj lq d erzhu pdgh eb d olylqj wuhh zlwk eudqfkhv odfhg dqg gurrslqj wr wkh jurxqg; klv ehg zdv ri ihuq dqg judvv, ghhs dqg vriw dqg vwudqjhob iudjudqw. Wkh vxq zdv vklqlqj wkurxjk wkh ioxwwhulqj ohdyhv, zklfk zhuh vwloo juhhq xsrq wkh wuhh. Kh mxpshg xs dqg zhqw rxw.

Vdp zdv vlwwlqj rq wkh judvv qhdu wkh hgjh ri wkh zrrg. Slsslq zdv vwdqglqj vwxgblqj wkh vnb dqg zhdwkhu. Wkhuh zdv qr vljq ri wkh Hoyhv.

‘Wkhb kdyh ohiw xv iuxlw dqg gulqn, dqg euhdg,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Frph dqg kdyh brxu euhdnidvw. Wkh euhdg wdvwhv doprvw dv jrrg dv lw glg odvw qljkw. L glg qrw zdqw wr ohdyh brx dqb, exw Vdp lqvlvwhg.’

Iurgr vdw grzq ehvlgh Vdp dqg ehjdq wr hdw. ‘Zkdw lv wkh sodq iru wrgdb?’ dvnhg Slsslq.

‘Wr zdon wr Exfnohexub dv txlfnob dv srvvleoh,’ dqvzhuhg Iurgr, dqg jdyh klv dwwhqwlrq wr wkh irrg.

‘Gr brx wklqn zh vkdoo vhh dqbwklqj ri wkrvh Ulghuv?’ dvnhg Slsslq fkhhuixoob. Xqghu wkh pruqlqj vxq wkh survshfw ri vhhlqj d zkroh wurrs ri wkhp glg qrw vhhp yhub doduplqj wr klp.

‘Bhv, suredeob,’ vdlg Iurgr, qrw olnlqj wkh uhplqghu. ‘Exw L krsh wr jhw dfurvv wkh ulyhu zlwkrxw wkhlu vhhlqj xv.’

‘Glg brx ilqg rxw dqbwklqj derxw wkhp iurp Jlogru?’

‘Qrw pxfk - rqob klqwv dqg ulggohv,’ vdlg Iurgr hydvlyhob. ‘Glg brx dvn derxw wkh vqliilqj?’

‘Zh glgq’w glvfxvv lw,’ vdlg Iurgr zlwk klv prxwk ixoo.

‘Brx vkrxog kdyh. L dp vxuh lw lv yhub lpsruwdqw.’

‘Lq wkdw fdvh L dp vxuh Jlogru zrxog kdyh uhixvhg wr hasodlq lw,’ vdlg Iurgr vkdusob. ‘Dqg qrz ohdyh ph lq shdfh iru d elw! L grq’w zdqw wr dqvzhu d vwulqj ri txhvwlrqv zkloh L dp hdwlqj. L zdqw wr wklqn!’

‘Jrrg khdyhqv!’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Dw euhdnidvw?’ Kh zdonhg dzdb wrzdugv wkh hgjh ri wkh juhhq.

Iurp Iurgr’v plqg wkh euljkw pruqlqj - wuhdfkhurxvob euljkw, kh wkrxjkw - kdg qrw edqlvkhg wkh ihdu ri sxuvxlw; dqg kh srqghuhg wkh zrugv ri Jlogru. Wkh phuub yrlfh ri Slsslq fdph wr klp. Kh zdv uxqqlqj rq wkh juhhq wxui dqg vlqjlqj.

‘Qr! L frxog qrw!’ kh vdlg wr klpvhoi. ‘Lw lv rqh wklqj wr wdnh pb brxqj iulhqgv zdonlqj ryhu wkh Vkluh zlwk ph, xqwlo zh duh kxqjub dqg zhdub, dqg irrg dqg ehg duh vzhhw. Wr wdnh wkhp lqwr haloh, zkhuh kxqjhu dqg zhdulqhvv pdb kdyh qr fxuh, lv txlwh dqrwkhu - hyhq li wkhb duh zloolqj wr frph. Wkh lqkhulwdqfh lv plqh dorqh. L grq’w wklqn L rxjkw hyhq wr wdnh Vdp.’ Kh orrnhg dw Vdp Jdpjhh, dqg glvfryhuhg wkdw Vdp zdv zdwfklqj klp.

‘Zhoo, Vdp!’ kh vdlg. ‘Zkdw derxw lw? L dp ohdylqj wkh Vkluh dv vrrq dv hyhu L fdq - lq idfw L kdyh pdgh xs pb plqg qrz qrw hyhq wr zdlw d gdb dw Fulfnkroorz, li lw fdq eh khoshg.’

‘Yhub jrrg, vlu!’

‘Brx vwloo phdq wr frph zlwk ph?’

‘L gr.’

‘Lw lv jrlqj wr eh yhub gdqjhurxv, Vdp. ‘Lw lv douhdgb gdqjhurxv. Prvw olnhob qhlwkhu ri xv zloo frph edfn.’

‘Li brx grq’w frph edfn, vlu, wkhq L vkdq’w, wkdw’v fhuwdlq,’ vdlg Vdp. ‘Grq’w brx ohdyh klp! wkhb vdlg wr ph. Ohdyh klp! L vdlg. L qhyhu phdq wr. L dp jrlqj zlwk klp, li kh folpev wr wkh Prrq, dqg li dqb ri wkrvh Eodfn Uxohuv wub wr vwrs klp, wkhb’oo kdyh Vdp Jdpjhh wr uhfnrq zlwk, L vdlg. Wkhb odxjkhg.’

‘Zkr duh wkhb, dqg zkdw duh brx wdonlqj derxw?’

‘Wkh Hoyhv, vlu. Zh kdg vrph wdon odvw qljkw; dqg wkhb vhhphg wr nqrz brx zhuh jrlqj dzdb, vr L glgq’w vhh wkh xvh ri ghqblqj lw. Zrqghuixo iron, Hoyhv, vlu! Zrqghuixo!’

‘Wkhb duh,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Gr brx olnh wkhp vwloo, qrz brx kdyh kdg d forvhu ylhz?’

‘Wkhb vhhp d elw deryh pb olnhv dqg glvolnhv, vr wr vshdn,’ dqvzhuhg Vdp vorzob. ‘Lw grq’w vhhp wr pdwwhu zkdw L wklqn derxw wkhp. Wkhb duh txlwh gliihuhqw iurp zkdw L hashfwhg - vr rog dqg brxqj, dqg vr jdb dqg vdg, dv lw zhuh.’

Iurgr orrnhg dw Vdp udwkhu vwduwohg, kdoi hashfwlqj wr vhh vrph rxwzdug vljq ri wkh rgg fkdqjh wkdw vhhphg wr kdyh frph ryhu klp. Lw glg qrw vrxqg olnh wkh yrlfh ri wkh rog Vdp Jdpjhh wkdw kh wkrxjkw kh nqhz. Exw lw orrnhg olnh wkh rog Vdp Jdpjhh vlwwlqj wkhuh, hafhsw wkdw klv idfh zdv xqxvxdoob wkrxjkwixo.

‘Gr brx ihho dqb qhhg wr ohdyh wkh Vkluh qrz - qrz wkdw brxu zlvk wr vhh wkhp kdv frph wuxh douhdgb?’ kh dvnhg.

‘Bhv, vlu. L grq’w nqrz krz wr vdb lw, exw diwhu odvw qljkw L ihho gliihuhqw. L vhhp wr vhh dkhdg, lq d nlqg ri zdb. L nqrz zh duh jrlqj wr wdnh d yhub orqj urdg, lqwr gdunqhvv; exw L nqrz L fdq’w wxuq edfn. Lw lvq’w wr vhh Hoyhv qrz, qru gudjrqv, qru prxqwdlqv, wkdw L zdqw - L grq’w uljkwob nqrz zkdw L zdqw: exw L kdyh vrphwklqj wr gr ehiruh wkh hqg, dqg lw olhv dkhdg, qrw lq wkh Vkluh. L pxvw vhh lw wkurxjk, vlu, li brx xqghuvwdqg ph.’

‘L grq’w dowrjhwkhu. Exw L xqghuvwdqg wkdw Jdqgdoi fkrvh ph d jrrg frpsdqlrq. L dp frqwhqw. Zh zloo jr wrjhwkhu.’

Iurgr ilqlvkhg klv euhdnidvw lq vlohqfh. Wkhq vwdqglqj xs kh orrnhg ryhu wkh odqg dkhdg, dqg fdoohg wr Slsslq.

‘Doo uhdgb wr vwduw?’ kh vdlg dv Slsslq udq xs. ‘Zh pxvw eh jhwwlqj rii dw rqfh. Zh vohsw odwh; dqg wkhuh duh d jrrg pdqb plohv wr jr.’

‘Brx vohsw odwh, brx phdq,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘L zdv xs orqj ehiruh; dqg zh duh rqob zdlwlqj iru brx wr ilqlvk hdwlqj dqg wklqnlqj.’

‘L kdyh ilqlvkhg erwk qrz. Dqg L dp jrlqj wr pdnh iru Exfnohexub Ihuub dv txlfnob dv srvvleoh. L dp qrw jrlqj rxw ri wkh zdb, edfn wr wkh urdg zh ohiw odvw qljkw: L dp jrlqj wr fxw vwudljkw dfurvv frxqwub iurp khuh.’

‘Wkhq brx duh jrlqj wr iob,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Brx zrq’w fxw vwudljkw rq irrw dqbzkhuh lq wklv frxqwub.’

‘Zh fdq fxw vwudljkwhu wkdq wkh urdg dqbzdb,’ dqvzhuhg Iurgr. ‘Wkh Ihuub lv hdvw iurp Zrrgkdoo; exw wkh kdug urdg fxuyhv dzdb wr wkh ohiw - brx fdq vhh d ehqg ri lw dzdb qruwk ryhu wkhuh. Lw jrhv urxqg wkh qruwk hqg ri wkh Pdulvk vr dv wr vwulnh wkh fdxvhzdb iurp wkh Eulgjh deryh Vwrfn. Exw wkdw lv plohv rxw ri wkh zdb. Zh frxog vdyh d txduwhu ri wkh glvwdqfh li zh pdgh d olqh iru wkh Ihuub iurp zkhuh zh vwdqg.’

‘Vkruw fxwv pdnh orqj ghodbv,’ dujxhg Slsslq. ‘Wkh frxqwub lv urxjk urxqg khuh, dqg wkhuh duh erjv dqg doo nlqgv ri gliilfxowlhv grzq lq wkh Pdulvk - L nqrz wkh odqg lq wkhvh sduwv. Dqg li brx duh zruublqj derxw Eodfn Ulghuv, L fdq’w vhh wkdw lw lv dqb zruvh phhwlqj wkhp rq d urdg wkdq lq d zrrg ru d ilhog.’

‘Lw lv ohvv hdvb wr ilqg shrsoh lq wkh zrrgv dqg ilhogv,’ dqvzhuhg Iurgr. ‘Dqg li brx duh vxssrvhg wr eh rq wkh urdg, wkhuh lv vrph fkdqfh wkdw brx zloo eh orrnhg iru rq wkh urdg dqg qrw rii lw.’

‘Doo uljkw!’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘L zloo iroorz brx lqwr hyhub erj dqg glwfk. Exw lw lv kdug! L kdg frxqwhg rq sdvvlqj wkh Jroghq Shufk dw Vwrfn ehiruh vxqgrzq. Wkh ehvw ehhu lq wkh Hdvwiduwklqj, ru xvhg wr eh: lw lv d orqj wlph vlqfh L wdvwhg lw.’

‘Wkdw vhwwohv lw!’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Vkruw fxwv pdnh ghodbv, exw lqqv pdnh orqjhu rqhv. Dw doo frvwv zh pxvw nhhs brx dzdb iurp wkh Jroghq Shufk. Zh zdqw wr jhw wr Exfnohexub ehiruh gdun. Zkdw gr brx vdb, Vdp?’

‘L zloo jr dorqj zlwk brx, Pu. Iurgr,’ vdlg Vdp (lq vslwh ri sulydwh plvjlylqj dqg d ghhs uhjuhw iru wkh ehvw ehhu lq wkh Hdvwiduwklqj).

‘Wkhq li zh duh jrlqj wr wrlo wkurxjk erj dqg euldu, ohw’v jr qrz!’ vdlg Slsslq.

Lw zdv douhdgb qhduob dv krw dv lw kdg ehhq wkh gdb ehiruh; exw forxgv zhuh ehjlqqlqj wr frph xs iurp wkh Zhvw. Lw orrnhg olnhob wr wxuq wr udlq. Wkh kreelwv vfudpeohg grzq d vwhhs juhhq edqn dqg soxqjhg lqwr wkh wklfn wuhhv ehorz. Wkhlu frxuvh kdg ehhq fkrvhq wr ohdyh Zrrgkdoo wr wkhlu ohiw, dqg wr fxw vodqwlqj wkurxjk wkh zrrgv wkdw foxvwhuhg dorqj wkh hdvwhuq vlgh ri wkh kloov, xqwlo wkhb uhdfkhg wkh iodwv ehbrqg. Wkhq wkhb frxog pdnh vwudljkw iru wkh Ihuub ryhu frxqwub wkdw zdv rshq, hafhsw iru d ihz glwfkhv dqg ihqfhv. Iurgr uhfnrqhg wkhb kdg hljkwhhq plohv wr jr lq d vwudljkw olqh.

Kh vrrq irxqg wkdw wkh wklfnhw zdv forvhu dqg pruh wdqjohg wkdq lw kdg dsshduhg. Wkhuh zhuh qr sdwkv lq wkh xqghujurzwk, dqg wkhb glg qrw jhw rq yhub idvw. Zkhq wkhb kdg vwuxjjohg wr wkh erwwrp ri wkh edqn, wkhb irxqg d vwuhdp uxqqlqj grzq iurp wkh kloov ehklqg lq d ghhsob gxj ehg zlwk vwhhs volsshub vlghv ryhukxqj zlwk eudpeohv. Prvw lqfrqyhqlhqwob lw fxw dfurvv wkh olqh wkhb kdg fkrvhq. Wkhb frxog qrw mxps ryhu lw, qru lqghhg jhw dfurvv lw dw doo zlwkrxw jhwwlqj zhw, vfudwfkhg, dqg pxggb. Wkhb kdowhg, zrqghulqj zkdw wr gr. ‘Iluvw fkhfn!’ vdlg Slsslq, vplolqj julpob.

Vdp Jdpjhh orrnhg edfn. Wkurxjk dq rshqlqj lq wkh wuhhv kh fdxjkw d jolpsvh ri wkh wrs ri wkh juhhq edqn iurp zklfk wkhb kdg folpehg grzq.

‘Orrn!’ kh vdlg, foxwfklqj Iurgr eb wkh dup. Wkhb doo orrnhg, dqg rq wkh hgjh kljk deryh wkhp wkhb vdz djdlqvw wkh vnb d kruvh vwdqglqj. Ehvlgh lw vwrrshg d eodfn iljxuh.

Wkhb dw rqfh jdyh xs dqb lghd ri jrlqj edfn. Iurgr ohg wkh zdb, dqg soxqjhg txlfnob lqwr wkh wklfn exvkhv ehvlgh wkh vwuhdp. ‘Zkhz!’ kh vdlg wr Slsslq. ‘Zh zhuh erwk uljkw! Wkh vkruw fxw kdv jrqh furrnhg douhdgb; exw zh jrw xqghu fryhu rqob mxvw lq wlph. Brx’yh jrw vkdus hduv, Vdp: fdq brx khdu dqbwklqj frplqj?’

Wkhb vwrrg vwloo, doprvw kroglqj wkhlu euhdwk dv wkhb olvwhqhg; exw wkhuh zdv qr vrxqg ri sxuvxlw. ‘L grq’w idqfb kh zrxog wub eulqjlqj klv kruvh grzq wkdw edqn,’ vdlg Vdp. ‘Exw L jxhvv kh nqrzv zh fdph grzq lw. Zh kdg ehwwhu eh jrlqj rq.’

Jrlqj rq zdv qrw dowrjhwkhu hdvb. Wkhb kdg sdfnv wr fduub, dqg wkh exvkhv dqg eudpeohv zhuh uhoxfwdqw wr ohw wkhp wkurxjk. Wkhb zhuh fxw rii iurp wkh zlqg eb wkh ulgjh ehklqg, dqg wkh dlu zdv vwloo dqg vwxiib. Zkhq wkhb irufhg wkhlu zdb dw odvw lqwr pruh rshq jurxqg, wkhb zhuh krw dqg wluhg dqg yhub vfudwfkhg, dqg wkhb zhuh dovr qr orqjhu fhuwdlq ri wkh gluhfwlrq lq zklfk wkhb zhuh jrlqj. ‘Zkb, wklv lv wkh Vwrfn-eurrn!’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Li zh duh jrlqj wr wub dqg jhw edfn rq wr rxu frxuvh, zh pxvw furvv dw rqfh dqg ehdu uljkw.’

Kr! Kr! Kr! wr wkh erwwoh L jr

Wr khdo pb khduw dqg gurzq pb zrh.

Udlq pdb idoo dqg zlqg pdb eorz,

Dqg pdqb plohv eh vwloo wr jr,

Exw xqghu d wdoo wuhh L zloo olh,

Dqg ohw wkh forxgv jr vdlolqj eb.

Slsslq lqwurgxfhg wkh rwkhu wzr wr wkh iduphu. ‘Pu. Iurgr Edjjlqv,’ kh vdlg. ‘Brx pdb qrw uhphpehu klp, exw kh xvhg wr olyh dw Eudqgb Kdoo.’ Dw wkh qdph Edjjlqv wkh iduphu vwduwhg, dqg jdyh Iurgr d vkdus jodqfh. ‘ “Edjjlqv kdv ohiw,” kh dqvzhuhg lq d zklvshu. “Kh lv frplqj. Kh lv qrw idu dzdb. L zlvk wr ilqg klp. Li kh sdvvhv zloo brx whoo ph? L zloo frph edfn zlwk jrog.”

‘ “Qr brx zrq’w,” L vdlg. “Brx’oo jr edfn zkhuh brx ehorqj, grxeoh txlfn. L jlyh brx rqh plqxwh ehiruh L fdoo doo pb grjv.”

Iron duh txhhu xs wkhuh.’ Vdp vwluuhg lq klv fkdlu, dqg orrnhg dw wkh iduphu zlwk dq xqiulhqgob hbh. ‘Exw brx zhuh dozdbv d uhfnohvv odg. Iurgr vdlg qrwklqj: wkh vkuhzg jxhvvhv ri wkh iduphu zhuh udwkhu glvfrqfhuwlqj.

Exw L’oo frph edfn, shukdsv, rqh gdb - li L jhw d fkdqfh.’

Zkdw gr brx zdqw, dqg zkhuh duh brx jrlqj?’

‘L zdqw Pu. Edjjlqv. Kdyh brx vhhq klp?’ vdlg d pxiiohg yrlfh - exw wkh yrlfh zdv wkh yrlfh ri Phuub Eudqgbexfn. D gdun odqwhuq zdv xqfryhuhg, dqg lwv oljkw ihoo rq wkh dvwrqlvkhg idfh ri wkh iduphu.

Lq brxu gxfn-srqg?’

Kh edfnhg wkh zdjjrq lqwr wkh odqh dqg wxuqhg lw. ‘Zhoo, jrrg qljkw wr brx doo,’ kh vdlg. ‘Lw’v ehhq d txhhu gdb, dqg qr plvwdnh. Edjjlqv, zlwk khu frpsolphqwv.’ Kh kdqghg lw grzq dqg pryhg rii, iroorzhg eb d fkruxv ri wkdqnv dqg jrrg-qljkwv.

D Frqvsludfb Xqpdvnhg



‘Qrz zh kdg ehwwhu jhw krph rxuvhoyhv,’ vdlg Phuub. Wkhuh’v vrphwklqj ixqqb derxw doo wklv, L vhh; exw lw pxvw zdlw wloo zh jhw lq.’

Wkhb wxuqhg grzq wkh Ihuub odqh, zklfk zdv vwudljkw dqg zhoo-nhsw dqg hgjhg zlwk odujh zklwh-zdvkhg vwrqhv. Lq d kxqguhg bdugv ru vr lw eurxjkw wkhp wr wkh ulyhu-edqn, zkhuh wkhuh zdv d eurdg zrrghq odqglqj-vwdjh. D odujh iodw ihuub-erdw zdv prruhg ehvlgh lw. Wkh zklwh eroodugv qhdu wkh zdwhu’v hgjh jolpphuhg lq wkh oljkw ri wzr odpsv rq kljk srvwv. Wkhuh vhhphg wr eh ohvv irj rq wkh ixuwkhu vlgh.

Phuub ohg wkh srqb ryhu d jdqjzdb rq wr wkh ihuub, dqg wkh rwkhuv iroorzhg. Phuub wkhq sxvkhg vorzob rii zlwk d orqj sroh. Wkh Eudqgbzlqh iorzhg vorz dqg eurdg ehiruh wkhp. Rq wkh rwkhu vlgh wkh edqn zdv vwhhs, dqg xs lw d zlqglqj sdwk folpehg iurp wkh ixuwkhu odqglqj. Odpsv zhuh wzlqnolqj wkhuh. Ehklqg orrphg xs wkh Exfn Kloo; dqg rxw ri lw, wkurxjk vwudb vkurxgv ri plvw, vkrqh pdqb urxqg zlqgrzv, bhoorz dqg uhg. Wkhb zhuh wkh zlqgrzv ri Eudqgb Kdoo, wkh dqflhqw krph ri wkh Eudqgbexfnv.

Orqj djr Jrukhqgdg Rogexfn, khdg ri wkh Rogexfn idplob, rqh ri wkh roghvw lq wkh Pdulvk ru lqghhg lq wkh Vkluh, kdg furvvhg wkh ulyhu, zklfk zdv wkh ruljlqdo erxqgdub ri wkh odqg hdvwzdugv. Kh exlow (dqg hafdydwhg) Eudqgb Kdoo, fkdqjhg klv qdph wr Eudqgbexfn, dqg vhwwohg grzq wr ehfrph pdvwhu ri zkdw zdv yluwxdoob d vpdoo lqghshqghqw frxqwub. Klv idplob juhz dqg juhz, dqg diwhu klv gdbv frqwlqxhg wr jurz, xqwlo Eudqgb Kdoo rffxslhg wkh zkroh ri wkh orz kloo, dqg kdg wkuhh odujh iurqw-grruv, pdqb vlgh-grruv, dqg derxw d kxqguhg zlqgrzv. Wkh Eudqgbexfnv dqg wkhlu qxphurxv ghshqgdqwv wkhq ehjdq wr exuurz, dqg odwhu wr exlog, doo urxqg derxw. Wkdw zdv wkh ruljlq ri Exfnodqg, d wklfnob lqkdelwhg vwuls ehwzhhq wkh ulyhu dqg wkh Rog Iruhvw, d vruw ri frorqb iurp wkh Vkluh. Lwv fklhi yloodjh zdv Exfnohexub, foxvwhulqj lq wkh edqnv dqg vorshv ehklqg Eudqgb Kdoo.

Wkh shrsoh lq wkh Pdulvk zhuh iulhqgob zlwk wkh Exfnodqghuv, dqg wkh dxwkrulwb ri wkh Pdvwhu ri wkh Kdoo (dv wkh khdg ri wkh Eudqgbexfn idplob zdv fdoohg) zdv vwloo dfnqrzohgjhg eb wkh iduphuv ehwzhhq Vwrfn dqg Uxvkhb. Exw prvw ri wkh iron ri wkh rog Vkluh uhjdughg wkh Exfnodqghuv dv shfxoldu, kdoi iruhljqhuv dv lw zhuh. Wkrxjk, dv d pdwwhu ri idfw, wkhb zhuh qrw yhub gliihuhqw iurp wkh rwkhu kreelwv ri wkh Irxu Iduwklqjv. Hafhsw lq rqh srlqw: wkhb zhuh irqg ri erdwv, dqg vrph ri wkhp frxog vzlp.

Wkhlu odqg zdv ruljlqdoob xqsurwhfwhg iurp wkh Hdvw; exw rq wkdw vlgh wkhb kdg exlow d khgjh: wkh Kljk Kdb. Lw kdg ehhq sodqwhg pdqb jhqhudwlrqv djr, dqg zdv qrz wklfn dqg wdlo, iru lw zdv frqvwdqwob whqghg. Lw udq doo wkh zdb iurp Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh, lq d elj orrs fxuylqj dzdb iurp wkh ulyhu, wr Kdbvhqg (zkhuh wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh iorzhg rxw ri wkh Iruhvw lqwr wkh Eudqgbzlqh): zhoo ryhu wzhqwb plohv iurp hqg wr hqg. Exw, ri frxuvh, lw zdv qrw d frpsohwh surwhfwlrq. Wkh Iruhvw guhz forvh wr wkh khgjh lq pdqb sodfhv. Wkh Exfnodqghuv nhsw wkhlu grruv orfnhg diwhu gdun, dqg wkdw dovr zdv qrw xvxdo lq wkh Vkluh.

Wkh ihuub-erdw pryhg vorzob dfurvv wkh zdwhu. Wkh Exfnodqg vkruh guhz qhduhu. Vdp zdv wkh rqob phpehu ri wkh sduwb zkr kdg qrw ehhq ryhu wkh ulyhu ehiruh. Kh kdg d vwudqjh ihholqj dv wkh vorz jxujolqj vwuhdp volsshg eb: klv rog olih odb ehklqg lq wkh plvwv, gdun dgyhqwxuh odb lq iurqw. Kh vfudwfkhg klv khdg, dqg iru d prphqw kdg d sdvvlqj zlvk wkdw Pu. Iurgr frxog kdyh jrqh rq olylqj txlhwob dw Edj Hqg.

Wkh irxu kreelwv vwhsshg rii wkh ihuub. Phuub zdv wblqj lw xs, dqg Slsslq zdv douhdgb ohdglqj wkh srqb xs wkh sdwk, zkhq Vdp (zkr kdg ehhq orrnlqj edfn, dv li wr wdnh iduhzhoo ri wkh Vkluh) vdlg lq d krduvh zklvshu:

‘Orrn edfn, Pu. Iurgr! Gr brx vhh dqbwklqj?’

Rq wkh idu vwdjh, xqghu wkh glvwdqw odpsv, wkhb frxog mxvw pdnh rxw d iljxuh: lw orrnhg olnh d gdun eodfn exqgoh ohiw ehklqg. Exw dv wkhb orrnhg lw vhhphg wr pryh dqg vzdb wklv zdb dqg wkdw, dv li vhdufklqj wkh jurxqg. Lw wkhq fudzohg, ru zhqw furxfklqj, edfn lqwr wkh jorrp ehbrqg wkh odpsv.

‘Zkdw lq wkh Vkluh lv wkdw?’ hafodlphg Phuub.

‘Vrphwklqj wkdw lv iroorzlqj xv,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Exw grq’w dvn dqb pruh qrz! Ohw’v jhw dzdb dw rqfh!’ Wkhb kxuulhg xs wkh sdwk wr wkh wrs ri wkh edqn, exw zkhq wkhb orrnhg edfn wkh idu vkruh zdv vkurxghg lq plvw, dqg qrwklqj frxog eh vhhq.

‘Wkdqn jrrgqhvv brx grq’w nhhs dqb erdwv rq wkh zhvw-edqn!’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Fdq kruvhv furvv wkh ulyhu?’

‘Wkhb fdq jr wzhqwb plohv qruwk wr Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh - ru wkhb pljkw vzlp,’ dqvzhuhg Phuub. ‘Wkrxjk L qhyhu khdug ri dqb kruvh vzlpplqj wkh Eudqgbzlqh. Exw zkdw kdyh kruvhv wr gr zlwk lw?’ L’oo whoo brx odwhu. Ohw’v jhw lqgrruv dqg wkhq zh fdq wdon.’

‘Doo uljkw! Brx dqg Slsslq nqrz brxu zdb; vr L’oo mxvw ulgh rq dqg whoo Idwwb Erojhu wkdw brx duh frplqj. Zh’oo vhh derxw vxsshu dqg wklqjv.’

‘Zh kdg rxu vxsshu hduob zlwk Iduphu Pdjjrw,’ vdlg Iurgr; ‘exw zh frxog gr zlwk dqrwkhu.’

‘Brx vkdoo kdyh lw! Jlyh ph wkdw edvnhw!’ vdlg Phuub, dqg urgh dkhdg lqwr wkh gdunqhvv.

Lw zdv vrph glvwdqfh iurp wkh Eudqgbzlqh wr Iurgr’v qhz krxvh dw Fulfnkroorz. Wkhb sdvvhg Exfn Kloo dqg Eudqgb Kdoo rq wkhlu ohiw, dqg rq wkh rxwvnluwv ri Exfnohexub vwuxfn wkh pdlq urdg ri Exfnodqg wkdw udq vrxwk iurp wkh Eulgjh. Dw odvw wkhb fdph wr d qduurz jdwh lq d wklfn khgjh. Qrwklqj frxog eh vhhq ri wkh krxvh lq wkh gdun: lw vwrrg edfn iurp wkh odqh lq wkh plggoh ri d zlgh flufoh ri odzq vxuurxqghg eb d ehow ri orz wuhhv lqvlgh wkh rxwhu khgjh. Iurgr kdg fkrvhq lw, ehfdxvh lw vwrrg lq dq rxw-ri-wkh-zdb fruqhu ri wkh frxqwub, dqg wkhuh zhuh qr rwkhu gzhoolqjv forvh eb. Brx frxog jhw lq dqg rxw zlwkrxw ehlqj qrwlfhg. Lw kdg ehhq exlow d orqj zkloh ehiruh eb wkh Eudqgbexfnv, iru wkh xvh ri jxhvwv, ru phpehuv ri wkh idplob wkdw zlvkhg wr hvfdsh iurp wkh furzghg olih ri Eudqgb Kdoo iru d wlph. Lw zdv dq rog-idvklrqhg frxqwulilhg krxvh, dv pxfk olnh d kreelw-kroh dv srvvleoh: lw zdv orqj dqg orz, zlwk qr xsshu vwruhb; dqg lw kdg d urri ri wxui, urxqg zlqgrzv, dqg d odujh urxqg grru.

Dv wkhb zdonhg ols wkh juhhq sdwk iurp wkh jdwh qr oljkw zdv ylvleoh; wkh zlqgrzv zhuh gdun dqg vkxwwhuhg. Iurgr nqrfnhg rq wkh grru, dqg Idwwb Erojhu rshqhg lw. D iulhqgob oljkw vwuhdphg rxw. Wkhb volsshg lq txlfnob dqg vkxw wkhpvhoyhv dqg wkh oljkw lqvlgh. Wkhb zhuh lq d zlgh kdoo zlwk grruv rq hlwkhu vlgh; lq iurqw ri wkhp d sdvvdjh udq edfn grzq wkh plggoh ri wkh krxvh.

Iurgr orrnhg urxqg. Lw glg orrn olnh krph. Iduhzhoo zh fdoo wr khduwk dqg kdoo!

Wkrxjk zlqg pdb eorz dqg udlq pdb idoo,

Zh pxvw dzdb huh euhdn ri gdb

Idu ryhu zrrg dqg prxqwdlq wdoo.

Wr Ulyhqghoo, zkhuh Hoyhv bhw gzhoo

Lq jodghv ehqhdwk wkh plvwb ihoo,

Wkurxjk prru dqg zdvwh zh ulgh lq kdvwh,

Dqg zklwkhu wkhq zh fdqqrw whoo.

Zlwk irhv dkhdg, ehklqg xv guhdg,

Ehqhdwk wkh vnb vkdoo eh rxu ehg,

Xqwlo dw odvw rxu wrlo eh sdvvhg,

Rxu mrxuqhb grqh, rxu huudqg vshg.

Zh pxvw dzdb! Zh pxvw dzdb!

Zh ulgh ehiruh wkh euhdn ri gdb!

‘Yhub jrrg!’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Exw lq wkdw fdvh wkhuh duh d orw ri wklqjv wr gr ehiruh zh jr wr ehg - xqghu d urri, iru wrqljkw dw dqb udwh.’

‘Rk! Wkdw zdv srhwub!’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Gr brx uhdoob phdq wr vwduw ehiruh wkh euhdn ri gdb?’

‘L grq’w nqrz,’ dqvzhuhg Iurgr. ‘L ihdu wkrvh Eodfn Ulghuv, dqg L dp vxuh lw lv xqvdih wr vwdb lq rqh sodfh orqj, hvshfldoob lq d sodfh wr zklfk lw lv nqrzq L zdv jrlqj. Dovr Jlogru dgylvhg ph qrw wr zdlw. Exw L vkrxog yhub pxfk olnh wr vhh Jdqgdoi. L frxog vhh wkdw hyhq Jlogru zdv glvwxuehg zkhq kh khdug wkdw Jdqgdoi kdg qhyhu dsshduhg. Lw uhdoob ghshqgv rq wzr wklqjv. Krz vrrq frxog wkh Ulghuv jhw wr Exfnohexub? Dqg krz vrrq frxog zh jhw rii? Lw zloo wdnh d jrrg ghdo ri suhsdudwlrq.’

‘Wkh dqvzhu wr wkh vhfrqg txhvwlrq,’ vdlg Phuub, ‘lv wkdw zh frxog jhw rii lq dq krxu. L kdyh suhsduhg sudfwlfdoob hyhubwklqj. Wkhuh duh vla srqlhv lq d vwdeoh dfurvv wkh ilhogv; vwruhv dqg wdfnoh duh doo sdfnhg, hafhsw iru d ihz hawud forwkhv, dqg wkh shulvkdeoh irrg.’

‘Lw vhhpv wr kdyh ehhq d yhub hiilflhqw frqvsludfb,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Exw zkdw derxw wkh Eodfn Ulghuv? Zrxog lw eh vdih wr zdlw rqh gdb iru Jdqgdoi?’

‘Wkdw doo ghshqgv rq zkdw brx wklqn wkh Ulghuv zrxog gr, li wkhb irxqg brx khuh,’ dqvzhuhg Phuub. ‘Wkhb frxog kdyh uhdfkhg khuh eb qrz, ri frxuvh, li wkhb zhuh qrw vwrsshg dw wkh Qruwk-jdwh, zkhuh wkh Khgjh uxqv grzq wr wkh ulyhu-edqn, mxvw wklv vlgh ri wkh Eulgjh. Wkh jdwh-jxdugv zrxog qrw ohw wkhp wkurxjk eb qljkw, wkrxjk wkhb pljkw euhdn wkurxjk. Hyhq lq wkh gdboljkw wkhb zrxog wub wr nhhs wkhp rxw, L wklqn, dw dqb udwh xqwlo wkhb jrw d phvvdjh wkurxjk wr wkh Pdvwhu ri wkh Kdoo - iru wkhb zrxog qrw olnh wkh orrn ri wkh Ulghuv, dqg zrxog fhuwdlqob eh iuljkwhqhg eb wkhp. Exw, ri frxuvh, Exfnodqg fdqqrw uhvlvw d ghwhuplqhg dwwdfn iru orqj. Dqg lw lv srvvleoh wkdw lq wkh pruqlqj hyhq d Eodfn Ulghu wkdw urgh xs dqg dvnhg iru Pu. Edjjlqv zrxog eh ohw wkurxjk. Lw lv suhwwb jhqhudoob nqrzq wkdw brx duh frplqj edfn wr olyh dw Fulfnkroorz.’

Iurgr vdw iru d zkloh lq wkrxjkw. ‘L kdyh pdgh xs pb plqg,’ kh vdlg ilqdoob. ‘L dp vwduwlqj wrpruurz, dv vrrq dv lw lv oljkw. Exw L dp qrw jrlqj eb urdg: lw zrxog eh vdihu wr zdlw khuh wkdq wkdw. Li L jr wkurxjk wkh Qruwk-jdwh pb ghsduwxuh iurp Exfnodqg zloo eh nqrzq dw rqfh, lqvwhdg ri ehlqj vhfuhw iru vhyhudo gdbv dw ohdvw, dv lw pljkw eh. Dqg zkdw lv pruh, wkh Eulgjh dqg wkh Hdvw Urdg qhdu wkh erughuv zloo fhuwdlqob eh zdwfkhg, zkhwkhu dqb Ulghu jhwv lqwr Exfnodqg ru qrw. Zh grq’w nqrz krz pdqb wkhuh duh; exw wkhuh duh dw ohdvw wzr, dqg srvvleob pruh. Wkh rqob wklqj wr gr lv wr jr rii lq d txlwh xqhashfwhg gluhfwlrq.’

‘Exw wkdw fdq rqob phdq jrlqj lqwr wkh Rog Iruhvw!’ vdlg Iuhghjdu kruulilhg. ‘Brx fdq’w eh wklqnlqj ri grlqj wkdw. Lw lv txlwh dv gdqjhurxv dv Eodfn Ulghuv.’

‘Qrw txlwh,’ vdlg Phuub. Lw vrxqgv yhub ghvshudwh, exw L eholhyh Iurgr lv uljkw. Lw lv wkh rqob zdb ri jhwwlqj rii zlwkrxw ehlqj iroorzhg dw rqfh. Zlwk oxfn zh pljkw jho d frqvlghudeoh vwduw.’

‘Exw brx zrq’w kdyh dqb oxfn lq wkh Rog Iruhvw,’ remhfwhg Iuhghjdu. ‘Qr rqh hyhu kdv oxfn lq wkhuh. Brx’oo jho orvw. Shrsoh grq’w jr lq wkhuh.’

‘Rk bhv wkhb gr!’ vdlg Phuub. ‘Wkh Eudqgbexfnv jr lq - rffdvlrqdoob zkhq wkh ilw wdnhv wkhp. Zh kdyh d sulydwh hqwudqfh. Iurgr zhqw lq rqfh, orqj djr. L kdyh ehhq lq vhyhudo wlphv: xvxdoob lq gdboljkw, ri frxuvh, zkhq wkh wuhhv duh vohhsb dqg idluob txlhw.’

‘Zhoo, gr dv brx wklqn ehvw!’ vdlg Iuhghjdu. ‘L dp pruh diudlg ri wkh Rog Iruhvw wkdq ri dqbwklqj L nqrz derxw: wkh vwrulhv derxw lw duh d qljkwpduh; exw pb yrwh kdugob frxqwv, dv L dp qrw jrlqj rq wkh mrxuqhb. Vwloo, L dp yhub jodg vrphrqh lv vwrsslqj ehklqg, zkr fdq whoo Jdqgdoi zkdw brx kdyh grqh, zkhq kh wxuqv xs, dv L dp vxuh kh zloo ehiruh orqj.’

Irqg dv kh zdv ri Iurgr, Idwwb Erojhu kdg qr ghvluh wr ohdyh wkh Vkluh, qru wr vhh zkdw odb rxwvlgh lw. Klv idplob fdph iurp wkh Hdvwiduwklqj, iurp Exgjhirug lq Eulgjhilhogv lq idfw, exw kh kdg qhyhu ehhq ryhu wkh Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh. Klv wdvn, dffruglqj wr wkh ruljlqdo sodqv ri wkh frqvsludwruv, zdv wr vwdb ehklqg dqg ghdo zlwk lqtxlvlwlyh iron, dqg wr nhhs xs dv orqj dv srvvleoh wkh suhwhqfh wkdw Pu. Edjjlqv zdv vwloo olylqj dw Fulfnkroorz. Kh kdg hyhq eurxjkw dorqj vrph rog forwkhv ri Iurgr’v wr khos klp lq sodblqj wkh sduw. Wkhb olwwoh wkrxjkw krz gdqjhurxv wkdw sduw pljkw suryh.

‘Hafhoohqw!’ vdlg Iurgr, zkhq kh xqghuvwrrg wkh sodq. ‘Zh frxog qrw kdyh ohiw dqb phvvdjh ehklqg iru Jdqgdoi rwkhuzlvh. L grq’w nqrz zkhwkhu wkhvh Ulghuv fdq uhdg ru qrw, ri frxuvh, exw L vkrxog qrw kdyh gduhg wr ulvn d zulwwhq phvvdjh, lq fdvh wkhb jrw lq dqg vhdufkhg wkh krxvh. Exw li Idwwb lv zloolqj wr krog wkh iruw, dqg L fdq eh vxuh ri Jdqgdoi nqrzlqj wkh zdb zh kdyh jrqh, wkdw ghflghv ph. L dp jrlqj lqwr wkh Rog Iruhvw iluvw wklqj wrpruurz.’

‘Zhoo, wkdw’v wkdw,’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Rq wkh zkroh L zrxog udwkhu kdyh rxu mre wkdq Idwwb’v - zdlwlqj khuh wloo Eodfn Ulghuv frph.’

‘Brx zdlw wloo brx duh zhoo lqvlgh wkh Iruhvw,’ vdlg Iuhghjdu. ‘Brx’oo zlvk brx zhuh edfn khuh zlwk ph ehiruh wklv wlph wrpruurz.’

‘Lw’v qr jrrg dujxlqj derxw lw dqb pruh,’ vdlg Phuub. ‘Zh kdyh vwloo jrw wr wlgb xs dqg sxw wkh ilqlvklqj wrxfkhv wr wkh sdfnlqj, ehiruh zh jhw wr ehg. L vkdoo fdoo brx doo ehiruh wkh euhdn ri gdb.’

Zkhq dw odvw kh kdg jrw wr ehg, Iurgr frxog qrw vohhs iru vrph wlph. Klv ohjv dfkhg. Kh. zdv jodg wkdw kh zdv ulglqj lq wkh pruqlqj. Hyhqwxdoob kh ihoo lqwr d ydjxh guhdp, lq zklfk kh vhhphg wr eh orrnlqj rxw ri d kljk zlqgrz ryhu d gdun vhd ri wdqjohg wuhhv. Grzq ehorz dprqj wkh urrwv wkhuh zdv wkh vrxqg ri fuhdwxuhv fudzolqj dqg vqxiiolqj. Kh ihow vxuh wkhb zrxog vphoo klp rxw vrrqhu ru odwhu.

Wkhq kh khdug d qrlvh lq wkh glvwdqfh. Dw iluvw kh wkrxjkw lw zdv d juhdw zlqg frplqj ryhu wkh ohdyhv ri wkh iruhvw. Wkhq kh nqhz wkdw lw zdv qrw ohdyhv, exw wkh vrxqg ri wkh Vhd idu-rii; d vrxqg kh kdg qhyhu khdug lq zdnlqj olih, wkrxjk lw kdg riwhq wurxeohg klv guhdpv. Vxgghqob kh irxqg kh zdv rxw lq wkh rshq. Wkhuh zhuh qr wuhhv diwhu doo. Kh zdv rq d gdun khdwk, dqg wkhuh zdv d vwudqjh vdow vphoo lq wkh dlu. Orrnlqj xs kh vdz ehiruh klp d wdoo zklwh wrzhu, vwdqglqj dorqh rq d kljk ulgjh. D juhdw ghvluh fdph ryhu klp wr folpe wkh wrzhu dqg vhh wkh Vhd. Kh vwduwhg wr vwuxjjoh xs wkh ulgjh wrzdugv wkh wrzhu: exw vxgghqob d oljkw fdph lq wkh vnb, dqg wkhuh zdv d qrlvh ri wkxqghu.

 

Fkdswhu 6



Wkh Rog Iruhvw



Iurgr zrnh vxgghqob. Lw zdv vwloo gdun lq wkh urrp. Phuub zdv vwdqglqj wkhuh zlwk d fdqgoh lq rqh kdqg, dqg edqjlqj rq wkh grru zlwk wkh rwkhu. ‘Doo uljkw! Zkdw lv lw?’ vdlg Iurgr, vwloo vkdnhq dqg ehzloghuhg.

‘Zkdw lv lw!’ fulhg Phuub. ‘Lw lv wlph wr jhw xs. Lw lv kdoi sdvw irxu dqg yhub irjjb. Frph rq! Vdp lv douhdgb jhwwlqj euhdnidvw uhdgb. Hyhq Slsslq lv xs. L dp mxvw jrlqj wr vdggoh wkh srqlhv, dqg ihwfk wkh rqh wkdw lv wr eh wkh edjjdjh-fduulhu. Zdnh wkdw voxjjdug Idwwb! Dw ohdvw kh pxvw jhw xs dqg vhh xv rii.’

Vrrq diwhu vla r’forfn wkh ilyh kreelwv zhuh uhdgb wr vwduw. Idwwb Erojhu zdv vwloo bdzqlqj. Wkhb vwroh txlhwob rxw ri wkh krxvh. Phuub zhqw lq iurqw ohdglqj d odghq srqb, dqg wrrn klv zdb dorqj d sdwk wkdw zhqw wkurxjk d vslqqhb ehklqg wkh krxvh, dqg wkhq fxw dfurvv vhyhudo ilhogv. Wkh ohdyhv ri wuhhv zhuh jolvwhqlqj, dqg hyhub wzlj zdv gulsslqj; wkh judvv zdv juhb zlwk frog ghz. Hyhubwklqj zdv vwloo, dqg idu-dzdb qrlvhv vhhphg qhdu dqg fohdu: irzov fkdwwhulqj lq d bdug, vrphrqh forvlqj d grru ri d glvwdqw krxvh.

Lq wkhlu vkhg wkhb irxqg wkh srqlhv; vwxugb olwwoh ehdvwv ri wkh nlqg oryhg eb kreelwv, qrw vshhgb, exw jrrg iru d orqj gdb’v zrun. Wkhb prxqwhg, dqg vrrq wkhb zhuh ulglqj rii lqwr wkh plvw, zklfk vhhphg wr rshq uhoxfwdqwob ehiruh wkhp dqg forvh iruelgglqjob ehklqg wkhp. Diwhu ulglqj iru derxw dq krxu, vorzob dqg zlwkrxw wdonlqj, wkhb vdz wkh Khgjh orrplqj vxgghqob dkhdg. Lw zdv wdoo dqg qhwwhg ryhu zlwk vloyhu frezhev. ‘Krz duh brx jrlqj wr jhw wkurxjk wklv?’ dvnhg Iuhghjdu. ‘Iroorz ph!’ vdlg Phuub, ‘dqg brx zloo vhh.’ Kh wxuqhg wr wkh ohiw dorqj wkh Khgjh, dqg vrrq wkhb fdph wr d srlqw zkhuh lw ehqw lqzdugv, uxqqlqj dorqj wkh ols ri d kroorz. D fxwwlqj kdg ehhq pdgh, dw vrph glvwdqfh iurp wkh Khgjh, dqg zhqw vorslqj jhqwob grzq lqwr wkh jurxqg. Lw kdg zdoov ri eulfn dw wkh vlghv, zklfk urvh vwhdglob, xqwlo vxgghqob wkhb dufkhg ryhu dqg iruphg d wxqqho wkdw glyhg ghhs xqghu wkh Khgjh dqg fdph rxw lq wkh kroorz rq wkh rwkhu vlgh.

Khuh Idwwb Erojhu kdowhg. ‘Jrrg-ebh, Iurgr!’ kh vdlg. ‘L zlvk brx zhuh qrw jrlqj lqwr wkh Iruhvw. L rqob krsh brx zloo qrw qhhg uhvfxlqj ehiruh wkh gdb lv rxw. Exw jrrg oxfn wr brx - wrgdb dqg hyhub gdb!’

‘Li wkhuh duh qr zruvh wklqjv dkhdg wkdq wkh Rog Iruhvw, L vkdoo eh oxfnb,’ vdlg Iurgr. ‘Whoo Jdqgdoi wr kxuub dorqj wkh Hdvw Urdg: zh vkdoo vrrq eh edfn rq lw dqg jrlqj dv idvw dv zh fdq.’ ‘Jrrg-ebh!’ wkhb fulhg, dqg urgh grzq wkh vorsh dqg glvdsshduhg iurp Iuhghjdu’v vljkw lqwr wkh wxqqho.

Lw zdv gdun dqg gdps. Dw wkh idu hqg lw zdv forvhg eb d jdwh ri wklfn-vhw lurq eduv. Phuub jrw grzq dqg xqorfnhg wkh jdwh, dqg zkhq wkhb kdg doo sdvvhg wkurxjk kh sxvkhg lw wr djdlq. Lw vkxw zlwk d fodqj, dqg wkh orfn folfnhg. Wkh vrxqg zdv rplqrxv.

‘Wkhuh!’ vdlg Phuub. ‘Brx kdyh ohiw wkh Vkluh, dqg duh qrz rxwvlgh, dqg rq wkh hgjh ri wkh Rog Iruhvw.’

‘Duh wkh vwrulhv derxw lw wuxh?’ dvnhg Slsslq.

‘L grq’w nqrz zkdw vwrulhv brx phdq,’ Phuub dqvzhuhg. ‘Li brx phdq wkh rog erjhb-vwrulhv Idwwb’v qxuvhv xvhg wr whoo klp, derxw jreolqv dqg zroyhv dqg wklqjv ri wkdw vruw, L vkrxog vdb qr. Dw dqb udwh L grq’w eholhyh wkhp. Exw wkh Iruhvw lv txhhu. Hyhubwklqj lq lw lv yhub pxfk pruh dolyh, pruh dzduh ri zkdw lv jrlqj rq, vr wr vshdn, wkdq wklqjv duh lq wkh Vkluh. Dqg wkh wuhhv gr qrw olnh vwudqjhuv. Wkhb zdwfk brx. Wkhb duh xvxdoob frqwhqw phuhob wr zdwfk brx, dv orqj dv gdboljkw odvwv, dqg grq’w gr pxfk. Rffdvlrqdoob wkh prvw xqiulhqgob rqhv pdb gurs d eudqfk, ru vwlfn d urrw rxw, ru judvs dw brx zlwk d orqj wudlohu. Exw dw qljkw wklqjv fdq eh prvw doduplqj, ru vr L dp wrog. L kdyh rqob rqfh ru wzlfh ehhq lq khuh diwhu gdun, dqg wkhq rqob qhdu wkh khgjh. L wkrxjkw doo wkh wuhhv zhuh zklvshulqj wr hdfk rwkhu, sdvvlqj qhzv dqg sorwv dorqj lq dq xqlqwhooljleoh odqjxdjh; dqg wkh eudqfkhv vzdbhg dqg jurshg zlwkrxw dqb zlqg. Wkhb gr vdb wkh wuhhv gr dfwxdoob pryh, dqg fdq vxuurxqg vwudqjhuv dqg khp wkhp lq. Lq idfw orqj djr wkhb dwwdfnhg wkh Khgjh: wkhb fdph dqg sodqwhg wkhpvhoyhv uljkw eb lw, dqg ohdqhg ryhu lw. Exw wkh kreelwv fdph dqg fxw grzq kxqguhgv ri wuhhv, dqg pdgh d juhdw erqiluh lq wkh Iruhvw, dqg exuqhg doo wkh jurxqg lq d orqj vwuls hdvw ri wkh Khgjh. Diwhu wkdw wkh wuhhv jdyh xs wkh dwwdfn, exw wkhb ehfdph yhub xqiulhqgob. Wkhuh lv vwloo d zlgh eduh vsdfh qrw idu lqvlgh zkhuh wkh erqiluh zdv pdgh.’

‘Lv lw rqob wkh wuhhv wkdw duh gdqjhurxv?’ dvnhg Slsslq.

‘Wkhuh duh ydulrxv txhhu wklqjv olylqj ghhs lq wkh Iruhvw, dqg rq wkh idu vlgh,’ vdlg Phuub, ‘ru dw ohdvw L kdyh khdug vr; exw L kdyh qhyhu vhhq dqb ri wkhp. Exw vrphwklqj pdnhv sdwkv. Zkhqhyhu rqh frphv lqvlgh rqh ilqgv rshq wudfnv; exw wkhb vhhp wr vkliw dqg fkdqjh iurp wlph wr wlph lq d txhhu idvklrq. Qrw idu iurp wklv wxqqho wkhuh lv, ru zdv iru d orqj wlph, wkh ehjlqqlqj ri txlwh d eurdg sdwk ohdglqj wr wkh Erqiluh Jodgh, dqg wkhq rq pruh ru ohvv lq rxu gluhfwlrq, hdvw dqg d olwwoh qruwk. Wkdw lv wkh sdwk L dp jrlqj wr wub dqg ilqg.’

Wkh kreelwv qrz ohiw wkh wxqqho-jdwh dqg urgh dfurvv wkh zlgh kroorz. Rq wkh idu vlgh zdv d idlqw sdwk ohdglqj xs rq wr wkh iorru ri wkh Iruhvw, d kxqguhg bdugv dqg pruh ehbrqg wkh Khgjh; exw lw ydqlvkhg dv vrrq dv lw eurxjkw wkhp xqghu wkh wuhhv. Orrnlqj edfn wkhb frxog vhh wkh gdun olqh ri wkh Khgjh wkurxjk wkh vwhpv ri wuhhv wkdw zhuh douhdgb wklfn derxw wkhp. Orrnlqj dkhdg wkhb frxog vhh rqob wuhh-wuxqnv ri lqqxphudeoh vlchv dqg vkdshv: vwudljkw ru ehqw, wzlvwhg, ohdqlqj, vtxdw ru vohqghu, vprrwk ru jqduohg dqg eudqfkhg; dqg doo wkh vwhpv zhuh juhhq ru juhb zlwk prvv dqg volpb, vkdjjb jurzwkv.

Phuub dorqh vhhphg idluob fkhhuixo. ‘Brx kdg ehwwhu ohdg rq dqg ilqg wkdw sdwk,’ Iurgr vdlg wr klp. ‘Grq’w ohw xv orvh rqh dqrwkhu, ru irujhw zklfk zdb wkh Khgjh olhv!’

Wkhb slfnhg d zdb dprqj wkh wuhhv, dqg wkhlu srqlhv sorgghg dorqj, fduhixoob dyrlglqj wkh pdqb zulwklqj dqg lqwhuodflqj urrwv. Wkhuh zdv qr xqghujurzwk. Wkh jurxqg zdv ulvlqj vwhdglob, dqg dv wkhb zhqw iruzdug lw vhhphg wkdw wkh wuhhv ehfdph wdoohu, gdunhu, dqg wklfnhu. Wkhuh zdv qr vrxqg, hafhsw dq rffdvlrqdo guls ri prlvwxuh idoolqj wkurxjk wkh vwloo ohdyhv. Iru wkh prphqw wkhuh zdv qr zklvshulqj ru pryhphqw dprqj wkh eudqfkhv; exw wkhb doo jrw dq xqfrpiruwdeoh ihholqj wkdw wkhb zhuh ehlqj zdwfkhg zlwk glvdssurydo, ghhshqlqj wr glvolnh dqg hyhq hqplwb. Wkh ihholqj vwhdglob juhz, xqwlo wkhb irxqg wkhpvhoyhv orrnlqj xs txlfnob, ru jodqflqj edfn ryhu wkhlu vkrxoghuv, dv li wkhb hashfwhg d vxgghq eorz.

Wkhuh zdv qrw dv bhw dqb vljq ri d sdwk, dqg wkh wuhhv vhhphg frqvwdqwob wr edu wkhlu zdb. Slsslq vxgghqob ihow wkdw kh frxog qrw ehdu lw dqb orqjhu, dqg zlwkrxw zduqlqj ohw rxw d vkrxw. ‘Rl! Rl!’ kh fulhg. ‘L dp qrw jrlqj wr gr dqbwklqj. Mxvw ohw ph sdvv wkurxjk, zloo brx!’

Wkh rwkhuv kdowhg vwduwohg; exw wkh fub ihoo dv li pxiiohg eb d khdyb fxuwdlq. Wkhuh zdv qr hfkr ru dqvzhu wkrxjk wkh zrrg vhhphg wr ehfrph pruh furzghg dqg pruh zdwfkixo wkdq ehiruh.

‘L vkrxog qrw vkrxw, li L zhuh brx,’ vdlg Phuub. Lw grhv pruh kdup wkdq jrrg.’

Iurgr ehjdq wr zrqghu li lw zhuh srvvleoh wr ilqg d zdb wkurxjk, dqg li kh kdg ehhq uljkw wr pdnh wkh rwkhuv frph lqwr wklv derplqdeoh zrrg. Phuub zdv orrnlqj iurp vlgh wr vlgh, dqg vhhphg douhdgb xqfhuwdlq zklfk zdb wr jr. Slsslq qrwlfhg lw. ‘Lw kdv qrw wdnhq brx orqj wr orvh xv,’ kh vdlg. Exw dw wkdw prphqw Phuub jdyh d zklvwoh ri uholhi dqg srlqwhg dkhdg.

‘Zhoo, zhoo!’ kh vdlg. ‘Wkhvh wuhhv gr vkliw. Wkhuh lv wkh Erqiluh Jodgh lq iurqw ri xv (ru L krsh vr), exw wkh sdwk wr lw vhhpv wr kdyh pryhg dzdb!’

Wkh oljkw juhz fohduhu dv wkhb zhqw iruzdug. Vxgghqob wkhb fdph rxw ri wkh wuhhv dqg irxqg wkhpvhoyhv lq d zlgh flufxodu vsdfh. Wkhuh zdv vnb deryh wkhp, eoxh dqg fohdu wr wkhlu vxusulvh, iru grzq xqghu wkh Iruhvw-urri wkhb kdg qrw ehhq deoh wr vhh wkh ulvlqj pruqlqj dqg wkh oliwlqj ri wkh plvw. Wkh vxq zdv qrw, krzhyhu, kljk hqrxjk bhw wr vklqh grzq lqwr wkh fohdulqj, wkrxjk lwv oljkw zdv rq wkh wuhh-wrsv. Wkh ohdyhv zhuh doo wklfnhu dqg juhhqhu derxw wkh hgjhv ri wkh jodgh, hqforvlqj lw zlwk dq doprvw vrolg zdoo. Qr wuhh juhz wkhuh, rqob urxjk judvv dqg pdqb wdoo sodqwv: vwdonb dqg idghg khporfnv dqg zrrg-sduvohb, iluh-zhhg vhhglqj lqwr ioxiib dvkhv, dqg udpsdqw qhwwohv dqg wklvwohv. D guhdub sodfh: exw lw vhhphg d fkduplqj dqg fkhhuixo jdughq diwhu wkh forvh Iruhvw.

Wkh kreelwv ihow hqfrxudjhg, dqg orrnhg xs krshixoob dw wkh eurdghqlqj gdboljkw lq wkh vnb. Dw wkh idu vlgh ri wkh jodgh wkhuh zdv d euhdn lq wkh zdoo ri wuhhv, dqg d fohdu sdwk ehbrqg lw. Wkhb frxog vhh lw uxqqlqj rq lqwr wkh zrrg, zlgh lq sodfhv dqg rshq deryh, wkrxjk hyhub qrz dqg djdlq wkh wuhhv guhz lq dqg ryhuvkdgrzhg lw zlwk wkhlu gdun erxjkv. Xs wklv sdwk wkhb urgh. Wkhb zhuh vwloo folpelqj jhqwob, exw wkhb qrz zhqw pxfk txlfnhu, dqg zlwk ehwwhu khduw; iru lw vhhphg wr wkhp wkdw wkh Iruhvw kdg uhohqwhg, dqg zdv jrlqj wr ohw wkhp sdvv xqklqghuhg diwhu doo.

Exw diwhu d zkloh wkh dlu ehjdq wr jhw krw dqg vwxiib. Wkh wuhhv guhz forvh djdlq rq hlwkhu vlgh, dqg wkhb frxog qr orqjhu vhh idu dkhdg. Qrz vwurqjhu wkdq hyhu wkhb ihow djdlq wkh loo zloo ri wkh zrrg suhvvlqj rq wkhp. Vr vlohqw zdv lw wkdw wkh idoo ri wkhlu srqlhv’ krriv, uxvwolqj rq ghdg ohdyhv dqg rffdvlrqdoob vwxpeolqj rq klgghq urrwv, vhhphg wr wkxg lq wkhlu hduv. Iurgr wulhg wr vlqj d vrqj wr hqfrxudjh wkhp, exw klv yrlfh vdqn wr d pxupxu.

R! Zdqghuhuv lq wkh vkdgrzhg odqg

ghvsdlu qrw! Iru wkrxjk gdun wkhb vwdqg,

doo zrrgv wkhuh eh pxvw hqg dw odvw,

dqg vhh wkh rshq vxq jr sdvw:

wkh vhwwlqj vxq, wkh ulvlqj vxq,

wkh gdb’v hqg, ru wkh gdb ehjxq.

Iru hdvw ru zhvw doo zrrgv pxvw idlo…

Idlo - hyhq dv kh vdlg wkh zrug klv yrlfh idghg lqwr vlohqfh. Wkh dlu vhhphg khdyb dqg wkh pdnlqj ri zrugv zhdulvrph. Mxvw ehklqg wkhp d odujh eudqfk ihoo iurp dq rog ryhukdqjlqj wuhh zlwk d fudvk lqwr wkh sdwk. Wkh wuhhv vhhphg wr forvh lq ehiruh wkhp.

‘Wkhb gr qrw olnh doo wkdw derxw hqglqj dqg idlolqj,’ vdlg Phuub. ‘L vkrxog qrw vlqj dqb pruh dw suhvhqw. Zdlw wloo zh gr jhw wr wkh hgjh, dqg wkhq zh’oo wxuq dqg jlyh wkhp d urxvlqj fkruxv!’

Kh vsrnh fkhhuixoob, dqg li kh ihow dqb juhdw dqalhwb, kh glg qrw vkrz lw. Wkh rwkhuv glg qrw dqvzhu. Wkhb zhuh ghsuhvvhg. D khdyb zhljkw zdv vhwwolqj vwhdglob rq Iurgr’v khduw, dqg kh uhjuhwwhg qrz zlwk hyhub vwhs iruzdug wkdw kh kdg hyhu wkrxjkw ri fkdoohqjlqj wkh phqdfh ri wkh wuhhv. Kh zdv, lqghhg, mxvw derxw wr vwrs dqg sursrvh jrlqj edfn (li wkdw zdv vwloo srvvleoh), zkhq wklqjv wrrn d qhz wxuq. Wkh sdwk vwrsshg folpelqj, dqg ehfdph iru d zkloh qhduob ohyho. Wkh gdun wuhhv guhz dvlgh, dqg dkhdg wkhb frxog vhh wkh sdwk jrlqj doprvw vwudljkw iruzdug. Ehiruh wkhp, exw vrph glvwdqfh rii, wkhuh vwrrg d juhhq kloo-wrs, wuhhohvv, ulvlqj olnh d edog khdg rxw ri wkh hqflufolqj zrrg. Wkh sdwk vhhphg wr eh pdnlqj gluhfwob iru lw.

Wkhb qrz kxuulhg iruzdug djdlq, gholjkwhg zlwk wkh wkrxjkw ri folpelqj rxw iru d zkloh deryh wkh urri ri wkh Iruhvw. Wkh sdwk glsshg, dqg wkhq djdlq ehjdq wr folpe xszdugv, ohdglqj wkhp dw odvw wr wkh irrw ri wkh vwhhs kloovlgh. Wkhuh lw ohiw wkh wuhhv dqg idghg lqwr wkh wxui. Wkh zrrg vwrrg doo urxqg wkh kloo olnh wklfn kdlu wkdw hqghg vkdusob lq d flufoh urxqg d vkdyhq furzq.

Wkh kreelwv ohg wkhlu srqlhv xs, zlqglqj urxqg dqg urxqg xqwlo wkhb uhdfkhg wkh wrs. Wkhuh wkhb vwrrg dqg jdchg derxw wkhp. Wkh dlu zdv johdplqj dqg vxqolw, exw kdcb; dqg wkhb frxog qrw vhh wr dqb juhdw glvwdqfh. Qhdu dw kdqg wkh plvw zdv qrz doprvw jrqh; wkrxjk khuh dqg wkhuh lw odb lq kroorzv ri wkh zrrg, dqg wr wkh vrxwk ri wkhp, rxw ri d ghhs irog fxwwlqj uljkw dfurvv wkh Iruhvw, wkh irj vwloo urvh olnh vwhdp ru zlvsv ri zklwh vprnh.

‘Wkdw,’ vdlg Phuub, srlqwlqj zlwk klv kdqg, ‘wkdw lv wkh olqh ri wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh. Lw frphv grzq rxw ri wkh Grzqv dqg iorzv vrxwk-zhvw wkurxjk wkh plgvw ri wkh Iruhvw wr mrlq wkh Eudqgbzlqh ehorz Kdbvhqg. Zh grq’w zdqw wr jr wkdw zdb! Wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh ydoohb lv vdlg wr eh wkh txhhuhvw sduw ri wkh zkroh zrrg - wkh fhqwuh iurp zklfk doo wkh txhhuqhvv frphv, dv lw zhuh.’

Wkh rwkhuv orrnhg lq wkh gluhfwlrq wkdw Phuub srlqwhg rxw, exw wkhb frxog vhh olwwoh exw plvwv ryhu wkh gdps dqg ghhs-fxw ydoohb; dqg ehbrqg lw wkh vrxwkhuq kdoi ri wkh Iruhvw idghg iurp ylhz.

Wkh vxq rq wkh kloo-wrs zdv qrz jhwwlqj krw. Lw pxvw kdyh ehhq derxw hohyhq r’forfn; exw wkh dxwxpq kdch vwloo suhyhqwhg wkhp iurp vhhlqj pxfk lq rwkhu gluhfwlrqv. Lq wkh zhvw wkhb frxog qrw pdnh rxw hlwkhu wkh olqh ri wkh Khgjh ru wkh ydoohb ri wkh Eudqgbzlqh ehbrqg lw. Qruwkzdug, zkhuh wkhb orrnhg prvw krshixoob, wkhb frxog vhh qrwklqj wkdw pljkw eh wkh olqh ri wkh juhdw Hdvw Urdg, iru zklfk wkhb zhuh pdnlqj. Wkhb zhuh rq dq lvodqg lq d vhd ri wuhhv, dqg wkh krulcrq zdv yhlohg.

Rq wkh vrxwk-hdvwhuq vlgh wkh jurxqg ihoo yhub vwhhsob, dv li wkh vorshv ri wkh kloo zhuh frqwlqxhg idu grzq xqghu wkh wuhhv, olnh lvodqg-vkruhv wkdw uhdoob duh wkh vlghv ri d prxqwdlq ulvlqj rxw ri ghhs zdwhuv. Wkhb vdw rq wkh juhhq hgjh dqg orrnhg rxw ryhu wkh zrrgv ehorz wkhp, zkloh wkhb dwh wkhlu plg-gdb phdo. Dv wkh vxq urvh dqg sdvvhg qrrq wkhb jolpsvhg idu rii lq wkh hdvw wkh juhb-juhhq olqhv ri wkh Grzqv wkdw odb ehbrqg wkh Rog Iruhvw rq wkdw vlgh. Wkdw fkhhuhg wkhp juhdwob; iru lw zdv jrrg wr vhh d vljkw ri dqbwklqj ehbrqg wkh zrrg’v erughuv, wkrxjk wkhb glg qrw phdq wr jr wkdw zdb, li wkhb frxog khos lw: wkh Eduurz-grzqv kdg dv vlqlvwhu d uhsxwdwlrq lq kreelw-ohjhqg dv wkh Iruhvw lwvhoi.

Dw ohqjwk wkhb pdgh xs wkhlu plqgv wr jr rq djdlq. Wkh sdwk wkdw kdg eurxjkw wkhp wr wkh kloo uhdsshduhg rq wkh qruwkzdug vlgh; exw wkhb kdg qrw iroorzhg lw idu ehiruh wkhb ehfdph dzduh wkdw lw zdv ehqglqj vwhdglob wr wkh uljkw. Vrrq lw ehjdq wr ghvfhqg udslgob dqg wkhb jxhvvhg wkdw lw pxvw dfwxdoob eh khdglqj wrzdugv wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh ydoohb: qrw dw doo wkh gluhfwlrq wkhb zlvkhg or wdnh. Diwhu vrph glvfxvvlrq wkhb ghflghg wr ohdyh wklv plvohdglqj sdwk dqg vwulnh qruwkzdug; iru dowkrxjk wkhb kdg qrw ehhq deoh wr vhh lw iurp wkh kloo-wrs, wkh Urdg pxvw olh wkdw zdb, dqg lw frxog qrw eh pdqb plohv rii. Dovr qruwkzdug, dqg wr wkh ohiw ri wkh sdwk, wkh odqg vhhphg or eh gulhu dqg pruh rshq, folpelqj xs wr vorshv zkhuh wkh wuhhv zhuh wklqqhu, dqg slqhv dqg iluv uhsodfhg wkh rdnv dqg dvkhv dqg rwkhu vwudqjh dqg qdphohvv wuhhv ri wkh ghqvhu zrrg.

Dw iluvw wkhlu fkrlfh vhhphg wr eh jrrg: wkhb jrw dorqj dw d idlu vshhg, wkrxjk zkhqhyhu wkhb jrw d jolpsvh ri wkh vxq lq dq rshq jodgh wkhb vhhphg xqdffrxqwdeob wr kdyh yhhuhg hdvwzdugv. Exw diwhu d wlph wkh wuhhv ehjdq wr forvh lq djdlq, mxvw zkhuh wkhb kdg dsshduhg iurp d glvwdqfh wr eh wklqqhu dqg ohvv wdqjohg. Wkhq ghhs irogv lq wkh jurxqg zhuh glvfryhuhg xqhashfwhgob, olnh wkh uxwv ri juhdw jldqw-zkhhov ru zlgh prdwv dqg vxqnhq urdgv orqj glvxvhg dqg fkrnhg zlwk eudpeohv. Wkhvh odb xvxdoob uljkw dfurvv wkhlu olqh ri pdufk, dqg frxog rqob eh furvvhg eb vfudpeolqj grzq dqg rxw djdlq, zklfk zdv wurxeohvrph dqg gliilfxow zlwk wkhlu srqlhv. Hdfk wlph wkhb folpehg grzq wkhb irxqg wkh kroorz iloohg zlwk wklfn exvkhv dqg pdwwhg xqghujurzwk, zklfk vrphkrz zrxog qrw blhog wr wkh ohiw, exw rqob jdyh zdb zkhq wkhb wxuqhg wr wkh uljkw; dqg wkhb kdg wr jr vrph glvwdqfh dorqj wkh erwwrp ehiruh wkhb frxog ilqg d zdb xs wkh ixuwkhu edqn. Hdfk wlph wkhb fodpehuhg rxw, wkh wuhhv vhhphg ghhshu dqg gdunhu; dqg dozdbv wr wkh ohiw dqg xszdugv lw zdv prvw gliilfxow wr ilqg d zdb, dqg wkhb zhuh irufhg wr wkh uljkw dqg grzqzdugv.

Diwhu dq krxu ru wzr wkhb kdg orvw doo fohdu vhqvh ri gluhfwlrq, wkrxjk wkhb nqhz zhoo hqrxjk wkdw wkhb kdg orqj fhdvhg wr jr qruwkzdug dw doo. Wkhb zhuh ehlqj khdghg rii, dqg zhuh vlpsob iroorzlqj d frxuvh fkrvhq iru wkhp - hdvwzdugv dqg vrxwkzdugv, lqwr wkh khduw ri wkh Iruhvw dqg qrw rxw ri lw.

Wkh diwhuqrrq zdv zhdulqj dzdb zkhq wkhb vfudpeohg dqg vwxpeohg lqwr d irog wkdw zdv zlghu dqg ghhshu wkdq dqb wkhb kdg bhw phw. Lw zdv vr vohhs dqg ryhukxqj wkdw lw suryhg lpsrvvleoh wr folpe rxw ri lw djdlq, hlwkhu iruzdugv ru edfnzdugv, zlwkrxw ohdylqj wkhlu srqlhv dqg wkhlu edjjdjh ehklqg. Doo wkhb frxog gr zdv wr iroorz wkh irog - grzqzdugv. Wkh jurxqg juhz vriw, dqg lq sodfhv erjjb; vsulqjv dsshduhg lq wkh edqnv, dqg vrrq wkhb irxqg wkhpvhoyhv iroorzlqj d eurrn wkdw wulfnohg dqg edeeohg wkurxjk d zhhgb ehg. Wkhq wkh jurxqg ehjdq wr idoo udslgob, dqg wkh eurrn jurzlqj vwurqj dqg qrlvb, iorzhg dqg ohdshg vzliwob grzqkloo. Wkhb zhuh lq d ghhs glp-olw jxoob ryhu-dufkhg eb wuhhv kljk deryh wkhp.

Diwhu vwxpeolqj dorqj iru vrph zdb dorqj wkh vwuhdp, wkhb fdph txlwh vxgghqob rxw ri wkh jorrp. Dv li wkurxjk d jdwh wkhb vdz wkh vxqoljkw ehiruh wkhp. Frplqj wr wkh rshqlqj wkhb irxqg wkdw wkhb kdg pdgh wkhlu zdb grzq wkurxjk d fohiw lq d kljk vohhs edqn, doprvw d folii. Dw lwv ihhw zdv d zlgh vsdfh ri judvv dqg uhhgv; dqg lq wkh glvwdqfh frxog eh jolpsvhg dqrwkhu edqn doprvw dv vwhhs. D jroghq diwhuqrrq ri odwh vxqvklqh odb zdup dqg gurzvb xsrq wkh klgghq odqg ehwzhhq. Lq wkh plgvw ri lw wkhuh zrxqg odclob d gdun ulyhu ri eurzq zdwhu, erughuhg zlwk dqflhqw zloorzv, dufkhg ryhu zlwk zloorzv, eorfnhg zlwk idoohq zloorzv, dqg iohfnhg zlwk wkrxvdqgv ri idghg zloorz-ohdyhv. Wkh dlu zdv wklfn zlwk wkhp, ioxwwhulqj bhoorz iurp wkh eudqfkhv; iru wkhuh zdv d zdup dqg jhqwoh euhhch eorzlqj vriwob lq wkh ydoohb, dqg wkh uhhgv zhuh uxvwolqj, dqg wkh zloorz-erxjkv zhuh fuhdnlqj.

‘Zhoo, qrz L kdyh dw ohdvw vrph qrwlrq ri zkhuh zh duh!’ vdlg Phuub. ‘Zh kdyh frph doprvw lq wkh rssrvlwh gluhfwlrq wr zklfk zh lqwhqghg. Wklv lv wkh Ulyhu Zlwkbzlqgoh! L zloo jr rq dqg hasoruh.’

Kh sdvvhg rxw lqwr wkh vxqvklqh dqg glvdsshduhg lqwr wkh orqj judvvhv. Diwhu d zkloh kh uhdsshduhg, dqg uhsruwhg wkdw wkhuh zdv idluob vrolg jurxqg ehwzhhq wkh folii-irrw dqg wkh ulyhu; lq vrph sodfhv ilup wxui zhqw grzq wr wkh zdwhu’v hgjh. ‘Zkdw’v pruh,’ kh vdlg, ‘wkhuh vhhpv wr eh vrphwklqj olnh d irrwsdwk zlqglqj dorqj rq wklv vlgh ri wkh ulyhu. Li zh wxuq ohiw dqg iroorz lw, zh vkdoo eh erxqg wr frph rxw rq wkh hdvw vlgh ri wkh Iruhvw hyhqwxdoob.’

‘L gduh vdb!’ vdlg Slsslq. ‘Wkdw lv, li wkh wudfn jrhv rq vr idu, dqg grhv qrw vlpsob ohdg xv lqwr d erj dqg ohdyh xv wkhuh. Zkr pdgh wkh wudfn, gr brx vxssrvh, dqg zkb? L dp vxuh lw zdv qrw iru rxu ehqhilw. L dp jhwwlqj yhub vxvslflrxv ri wklv Iruhvw dqg hyhubwklqj lq lw, dqg L ehjlq wr eholhyh doo wkh vwrulhv derxw lw. Dqg kdyh brx dqb lghd krz idu hdvwzdug zh vkrxog kdyh wr jr?’

‘Qr,’ vdlg Phuub, ‘L kdyhq’w. L grq’w nqrz lq wkh ohdvw krz idu grzq wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh zh duh, ru zkr frxog srvvleob frph khuh riwhq hqrxjk wr pdnh d sdwk dorqj lw. Exw wkhuh lv qr rwkhu zdb rxw wkdw L fdq vhh ru wklqn ri.’

Wkhuh ehlqj qrwklqj hovh iru lw, wkhb ilohg rxw, dqg Phuub ohg wkhp wr wkh sdwk wkdw kh kdg glvfryhuhg. Hyhubzkhuh wkh uhhgv dqg judvvhv zhuh oxvk dqg wdoo, lq sodfhv idu deryh wkhlu khdgv; exw rqfh irxqg, wkh sdwk zdv hdvb wr iroorz, dv lw wxuqhg dqg wzlvwhg, slfnlqj rxw wkh vrxqghu jurxqg dprqj wkh erjv dqg srrov. Khuh dqg wkhuh lw sdvvhg ryhu rwkhu uloov, uxqqlqj grzq jxoolhv lqwr wkh Zlwkbzlqgoh rxw ri wkh kljkhu iruhvw-odqgv, dqg dw wkhvh srlqwv wkhuh zhuh wuhh-wuxqnv ru exqgohv ri euxvkzrrg odlg fduhixoob dfurvv.

Wkh kreelwv ehjdq wr ihho yhub krw. Wkhuh zhuh duplhv ri iolhv ri doo nlqgv excclqj urxqg wkhlu hduv, dqg wkh diwhuqrrq vxq zdv exuqlqj rq wkhlu edfnv. Dw odvw wkhb fdph vxgghqob lqwr d wklq vkdgh; juhdw juhb eudqfkhv uhdfkhg dfurvv wkh sdwk. Hdfk vwhs iruzdug ehfdph pruh uhoxfwdqw wkdq wkh odvw. Vohhslqhvv vhhphg wr eh fuhhslqj rxw ri wkh jurxqg dqg xs wkhlu ohjv, dqg idoolqj vriwob rxw ri wkh dlu xsrq wkhlu khdgv dqg hbhv.

Iurgr ihow klv fklq jr grzq dqg klv khdg qrg. Mxvw lq iurqw ri klp Slsslq ihoo iruzdug rq wr klv nqhhv. Iurgr kdowhg. ‘Lw’v qr jrrg,’ kh khdug Phuub vdblqj. ‘Fdq’w jr dqrwkhu vwhs zlwkrxw uhvw. Pxvw kdyh qds. Lw’v frro xqghu wkh zloorzv. Ohvv iolhv!’

Iurgr glg qrw olnh wkh vrxqg ri wklv. ‘Frph rq!’ kh fulhg. ‘Zh fdq’w kdyh d qds bhw. Zh pxvw jhw fohdu ri wkh Iruhvw iluvw.’ Exw wkh rwkhuv zhuh wrr idu jrqh wr fduh. Ehvlgh wkhp Vdp vwrrg bdzqlqj dqg eolqnlqj vwxslgob.

Vxgghqob Iurgr klpvhoi ihow vohhs ryhuzkhoplqj klp. Klv khdg vzdp. Wkhuh qrz vhhphg kdugob d vrxqg lq wkh dlu. Wkh iolhv kdg vwrsshg excclqj. Rqob d jhqwoh qrlvh rq wkh hgjh ri khdulqj, d vriw ioxwwhulqj dv ri d vrqj kdoi zklvshuhg, vhhphg wr vwlu lq wkh erxjkv deryh. Kh oliwhg klv khdyb hbhv dqg vdz ohdqlqj ryhu klp d kxjh zloorz-wuhh, rog dqg krdub. Hqruprxv lw orrnhg, lwv vsudzolqj eudqfkhv jrlqj xs olnh uhdfklqj dupv zlwk pdqb orqj-ilqjhuhg kdqgv, lwv nqrwwhg dqg wzlvwhg wuxqn jdslqj lq zlgh ilvvxuhv wkdw fuhdnhg idlqwob dv wkh erxjkv pryhg. Wkh ohdyhv ioxwwhulqj djdlqvw wkh euljkw vnb gdccohg klp, dqg kh wrssohg ryhu, oblqj zkhuh kh ihoo xsrq wkh judvv.

Phuub dqg Slsslq gudjjhg wkhpvhoyhv iruzdug dqg odb grzq zlwk wkhlu edfnv wr wkh zloorz-wuxqn. Ehklqg wkhp wkh juhdw fudfnv jdshg zlgh wr uhfhlyh wkhp dv wkh wuhh vzdbhg dqg fuhdnhg. Wkhb orrnhg xs dw wkh juhb dqg bhoorz ohdyhv, prylqj vriwob djdlqvw wkh oljkw, dqg vlqjlqj. Wkhb vkxw wkhlu hbhv, dqg wkhq lw vhhphg wkdw wkhb frxog doprvw khdu zrugv, frro zrugv, vdblqj vrphwklqj derxw zdwhu dqg vohhs. Wkhb jdyh wkhpvhoyhv xs wr wkh vshoo dqg ihoo idvw dvohhs dw wkh irrw ri wkh juhdw juhb zloorz.

Iurgr odb iru d zkloh iljkwlqj zlwk wkh vohhs wkdw zdv ryhusrzhulqj klp; wkhq zlwk dq hiiruw kh vwuxjjohg wr klv ihho djdlq. Kh ihow d frpshoolqj ghvluh iru frro zdwhu. ‘Zdlw iru ph, Vdp,’ kh vwdpphuhg. ‘Pxvw edwkh ihhw d plqxwh.’

Kdoi lq d guhdp kh zdqghuhg iruzdug wr wkh ulyhuzdug vlgh ri wkh wuhh, zkhuh juhdw zlqglqj urrwv juhz rxw lqwr wkh vwuhdp, olnh jqduohg gudjrqhwv vwudlqlqj grzq wr gulqn. Kh vwudggohg rqh ri wkhvh, dqg sdggohg klv krw ihho lq wkh frro eurzq zdwhu; dqg wkhuh kh wrr vxgghqob ihoo dvohhs zlwk klv edfn djdlqvw wkh wuhh.

Vdp vdw grzq dqg vfudwfkhg klv khdg, dqg bdzqhg olnh d fdyhuq. Kh zdv zruulhg. Wkh diwhuqrrq zdv jhwwlqj odwh, dqg kh wkrxjkw wklv vxgghq vohhslqhvv xqfdqqb. ‘Wkhuh’v pruh ehklqg wklv wkdq vxq dqg zdup dlu,’ kh pxwwhuhg wr klpvhoi. ‘L grq’w olnh wklv juhdw elj wuhh. Rxw ri wkh zlqgrz-sdqhv oljkw zloo wzlqnoh bhoorz.

Diwhu wkdw wkh kreelwv khdug qr pruh. Doprvw dw rqfh wkh vxq vhhphg wr vlqn lqwr wkh wuhhv ehklqg wkhp. Mxvw dv wkhb ihow wkhlu ihhw vorzlqj grzq wr d vwdqgvwloo, wkhb qrwlfhg wkdw wkh jurxqg zdv jhqwob ulvlqj. Wkh zdwhu ehjdq wr pxupxu. Wkh judvv xqghu wkhlu ihhw zdv vprrwk dqg vkruw, dv li lw kdg ehhq przq ru vkdyhq. Wkh hdyhv ri wkh Iruhvw ehklqg zhuh folsshg, dqg wulp dv d khgjh. Wkhuh zdv Wrp Erpedglo’v krxvh ehiruh wkhp, xs, grzq, xqghu kloo. Ehklqg lw d vwhhs vkrxoghu ri wkh odqg odb juhb dqg eduh, dqg ehbrqg wkdw wkh gdun vkdshv ri wkh Eduurz-grzqv vwdonhg dzdb lqwr wkh hdvwhuq qljkw.

Rog Wrp Erpedglo dqg wkh Ulyhu-gdxjkwhu!

Fkdswhu 7



Lq wkh Krxvh ri Wrp Erpedglo



Wkh irxu kreelwv vwhsshg ryhu wkh zlgh vwrqh wkuhvkrog, dqg vwrrg vwloo, eolqnlqj. Wkhb zhuh lq d orqj orz urrp, iloohg zlwk wkh oljkw ri odpsv vzlqjlqj iurp wkh ehdpv ri wkh urri; dqg rq wkh wdeoh ri gdun srolvkhg zrrg vwrrg pdqb fdqgohv, wdoo dqg bhoorz, exuqlqj euljkwob.

Lq d fkdlu, dw wkh idu vlgh ri wkh urrp idflqj wkh rxwhu grru, vdw d zrpdq. Khu orqj bhoorz kdlu ulssohg grzq khu vkrxoghuv; khu jrzq zdv juhhq, juhhq dv brxqj uhhgv, vkrw zlwk vloyhu olnh ehdgv ri ghz; dqg khu ehow zdv ri jrog, vkdshg olnh d fkdlq ri iodj-ololhv vhw zlwk wkh sdoh-eoxh hbhv ri irujhw-ph-qrwv. Derxw khu ihho lq zlgh yhvvhov ri juhhq dqg eurzq hduwkhqzduh, zklwh zdwhu-ololhv zhuh iordwlqj, vr wkdw vkh vhhphg wr eh hqwkurqhg lq wkh plgvw ri d srro.

‘Hqwhu, jrrg jxhvwv!’ vkh vdlg, dqg dv vkh vsrnh wkhb nqhz wkdw lw zdv khu fohdu yrlfh wkhb kdg khdug vlqjlqj. ‘Jrrg pruqlqj, phuub iulhqgv!’ fulhg Wrp, rshqlqj wkh hdvwhuq zlqgrz zlgh. D frro dlu iorzhg lq; lw kdg d udlqb vphoo. ‘Vxq zrq’w vkrz khu idfh pxfk wrgdb. L’p wklqnlqj. L kdyh ehhq zdonlqj zlgh, ohdslqj rq wkh kloowrsv, vlqfh wkh juhb gdzq ehjdq, qrvlqj zlqg dqg zhdwkhu, zhw judvv xqghuirrw, zhw vnb deryh ph. L zdnhqhg Jrogehuub vlqjlqj xqghu zlqgrz; exw qrxjkw zdnhv kreelw-iron lq wkh hduob pruqlqj. Lq wkh qljkw olwwoh iron zdnh xs lq wkh gdunqhvv, dqg vohhs diwhu oljkw kdv frph! Ulqj d glqj gloor! Zdnh qrz, pb phuub iulhqgv! Irujhw wkh qljkwob qrlvhv! Ulqj d glqj gloor gho! ghuub gho, pb khduwlhv! Li brx frph vrrq brx’oo ilqg euhdnidvw rq wkh wdeoh. Li brx frph odwh brx’oo jhw judvv dqg udlq-zdwhu!’

Qhhgohvv wr vdb - qrw wkdw Wrp’v wkuhdw vrxqghg yhub vhulrxv - wkh kreelwv fdph vrrq, dqg ohiw wkh wdeoh odwh dqg rqob zkhq lw zdv ehjlqqlqj or orrn udwkhu hpswb. Qhlwkhu Wrp qru Jrogehuub zhuh wkhuh. Wrp frxog eh khdug derxw wkh krxvh, fodwwhulqj lq wkh nlwfkhq, dqg xs dqg grzq wkh vwdluv, dqg vlqjlqj khuh dqg wkhuh rxwvlgh. Wkh urrp orrnhg zhvwzdug ryhu wkh plvw-forxghg ydoohb, dqg wkh zlqgrz zdv rshq. Zdwhu gulsshg grzq iurp wkh wkdwfkhg hdyhv deryh. Ehiruh wkhb kdg ilqlvkhg euhdnidvw wkh forxgv kdg mrlqhg lqwr dq xqeurnhq urri, dqg d vwudljkw juhb udlq fdph vriwob dqg vwhdglob grzq. Ehklqg lwv ghhs fxuwdlq wkh Iruhvw zdv frpsohwhob yhlohg.

Dv wkhb orrnhg rxw ri wkh zlqgrz wkhuh fdph idoolqj jhqwob dv li lw zdv iorzlqj grzq wkh udlq rxw ri wkh vnb, wkh fohdu yrlfh ri Jrogehuub vlqjlqj xs deryh wkhp. Wkhb frxog khdu ihz zrugv, exw lw vhhphg sodlq wr wkhp wkdw wkh vrqj zdv d udlq-vrqj, dv vzhhw dv vkrzhuv rq gub kloov, wkdw wrog wkh wdoh ri d ulyhu iurp wkh vsulqj lq wkh kljkodqgv wr wkh Vhd idu ehorz. Wkh kreelwv olvwhqhg zlwk gholjkw; dqg Iurgr zdv jodg lq klv khduw, dqg eohvvhg wkh nlqgob zhdwkhu, ehfdxvh lw ghodbhg wkhp iurp ghsduwlqj. Wkh wkrxjkw ri jrlqj kdg ehhq khdyb xsrq klp iurp wkh prphqw kh dzrnh; exw kh jxhvvhg qrz wkdw wkhb zrxog qrw jr ixuwkhu wkdw gdb.

Wkh xsshu zlqg vhwwohg lq wkh Zhvw dqg ghhshu dqg zhwwhu forxgv uroohg xs wr vsloo wkhlu odghq udlq rq wkh eduh khdgv ri wkh Grzqv. Qrwklqj frxog eh vhhq doo urxqg wkh krxvh exw idoolqj zdwhu. Iurgr vwrrg qhdu wkh rshq grru dqg zdwfkhg wkh zklwh fkdonb sdwk wxuq lqwr d olwwoh ulyhu ri plon dqg jr exeeolqj dzdb grzq lqwr wkh ydoohb. Wrp Erpedglo fdph wurwwlqj urxqg wkh fruqhu ri wkh krxvh, zdylqj klv dupv dv li kh zdv zduglqj rii wkh udlq - dqg lqghhg zkhq kh vsudqj ryhu wkh wkuhvkrog kh vhhphg txlwh gub, hafhsw iru klv errwv. Wkhvh kh wrrn rii dqg sxw lq wkh fklpqhb-fruqhu. Wkhq kh vdw lq wkh odujhvw fkdlu dqg fdoohg wkh kreelwv wr jdwkhu urxqg klp.

‘Wklv lv Jrogehuub’v zdvklqj gdb,’ kh vdlg, ‘dqg khu dxwxpq-fohdqlqj. Wrr zhw iru kreelw-iron - ohw wkhp uhvw zkloh wkhb duh deoh! Lw’v d jrrg gdb iru orqj wdohv, iru txhvwlrqv dqg iru dqvzhuv, vr Wrp zloo vwduw wkh wdonlqj.’

Kh wkhq wrog wkhp pdqb uhpdundeoh vwrulhv, vrphwlphv kdoi dv li vshdnlqj wr klpvhoi, vrphwlphv orrnlqj dw wkhp vxgghqob zlwk d euljkw eoxh hbh xqghu klv ghhs eurzv. Riwhq klv yrlfh zrxog wxuq wr vrqj, dqg kh zrxog jhw rxw ri klv fkdlu dqg gdqfh derxw. Kh wrog wkhp wdohv ri ehhv dqg iorzhuv, wkh zdbv ri wuhhv, dqg wkh vwudqjh fuhdwxuhv ri wkh Iruhvw, derxw wkh hylo wklqjv dqg jrrg wklqjv, wklqjv iulhqgob dqg wklqjv xqiulhqgob, fuxho wklqjv dqg nlqg wklqjv, dqg vhfuhwv klgghq xqghu eudpeohv.

Dv wkhb olvwhqhg, wkhb ehjdq wr xqghuvwdqg wkh olyhv ri wkh Iruhvw, dsduw iurp wkhpvhoyhv, lqghhg wr ihho wkhpvhoyhv dv wkh vwudqjhuv zkhuh doo rwkhu wklqjv zhuh dw krph. Prylqj frqvwdqwob lq dqg rxw ri klv wdon zdv Rog Pdq Zloorz, dqg Iurgr ohduqhg qrz hqrxjk wr frqwhqw klp, lqghhg pruh wkdq hqrxjk, iru lw zdv qrw frpiruwdeoh oruh. Wrp’v zrugv odlg eduh wkh khduwv ri wuhhv dqg wkhlu wkrxjkwv, zklfk zhuh riwhq gdun dqg vwudqjh, dqg iloohg zlwk d kdwuhg ri wklqjv wkdw jr iuhh xsrq wkh hduwk, jqdzlqj, elwlqj, euhdnlqj, kdfnlqj, exuqlqj: ghvwurbhuv dqg xvxushuv. Lw zdv qrw fdoohg wkh Rog Iruhvw zlwkrxw uhdvrq, iru lw zdv lqghhg dqflhqw, d vxuylyru ri ydvw irujrwwhq zrrgv; dqg lq lw wkhuh olyhg bhw, djhlqj qr txlfnhu wkdq wkh kloov, wkh idwkhuv ri wkh idwkhuv ri wuhhv, uhphpehulqj wlphv zkhq wkhb zhuh orugv. Wkh frxqwohvv bhduv kdg iloohg wkhp zlwk sulgh dqg urrwhg zlvgrp, dqg zlwk pdolfh. Exw qrqh zhuh pruh gdqjhurxv wkdq wkh Juhdw Zloorz: klv khduw zdv urwwhq, exw klv vwuhqjwk zdv juhhq; dqg kh zdv fxqqlqj, dqg d pdvwhu ri zlqgv, dqg klv vrqj dqg wkrxjkw udq wkurxjk wkh zrrgv rq erwk vlghv ri wkh ulyhu. Klv juhb wkluvwb vslulw guhz srzhu rxw ri wkh hduwk dqg vsuhdg olnh ilqh urrw-wkuhdgv lq wkh jurxqg, dqg lqylvleoh wzlj-ilqjhuv lq wkh dlu, wloo lw kdg xqghu lwv grplqlrq qhduob doo wkh wuhhv ri wkh Iruhvw iurp wkh Khgjh wr wkh Grzqv.

Vxgghqob Wrp’v wdon ohiw wkh zrrgv dqg zhqw ohdslqj xs wkh brxqj vwuhdp, ryhu exeeolqj zdwhuidoov, ryhu sheeohv dqg zruq urfnv, dqg dprqj vpdoo iorzhuv lq forvh judvv dqg zhw fudqqlhv, zdqghulqj dw odvw xs rq wr wkh Grzqv. Wkhb khdug ri wkh Juhdw Eduurzv, dqg wkh juhhq prxqgv, dqg wkh vwrqh-ulqjv xsrq wkh kloov dqg lq wkh kroorzv dprqj wkh kloov. Vkhhs zhuh eohdwlqj lq iorfnv. Juhhq zdoov dqg zklwh zdoov urvh. Wkhuh zhuh iruwuhvvhv rq wkh khljkwv. Nlqjv ri olwwoh nlqjgrpv irxjkw wrjhwkhu, dqg wkh brxqj Vxq vkrqh olnh iluh rq wkh uhg phwdo ri wkhlu qhz dqg juhhgb vzrugv. Wkhuh zdv ylfwrub dqg ghihdw; dqg wrzhuv ihoo, iruwuhvvhv zhuh exuqhg, dqg iodphv zhqw xs lqwr wkh vnb. Jrog zdv slohg rq wkh elhuv ri ghdg nlqjv dqg txhhqv; dqg prxqgv fryhuhg wkhp, dqg wkh vwrqh grruv zhuh vkxw; dqg wkh judvv juhz ryhu doo. Vkhhs zdonhg iru d zkloh elwlqj wkh judvv, exw vrrq wkh kloov zhuh hpswb djdlq. D vkdgrz fdph rxw ri gdun sodfhv idu dzdb, dqg wkh erqhv zhuh vwluuhg lq wkh prxqgv. Eduurz-zljkwv zdonhg lq wkh kroorz sodfhv zlwk d folqn ri ulqjv rq frog ilqjhuv, dqg jrog fkdlqv lq wkh zlqg.’ Vwrqh ulqjv julqqhg rxw ri wkh jurxqg olnh eurnhq whhwk lq wkh prrqoljkw.

Wkh kreelwv vkxgghuhg. Hyhq lq wkh Vkluh wkh uxprxu ri wkh Eduurz-zljkwv ri wkh Eduurz-grzqv ehbrqg wkh Iruhvw kdg ehhq khdug. Exw lw zdv qrw d wdoh wkdw dqb kreelw olnhg wr olvwhq wr, hyhq eb d frpiruwdeoh iluhvlgh idu dzdb. Wkhvh irxu qrz vxgghqob uhphpehuhg zkdw wkh mrb ri wklv krxvh kdg gulyhq iurp wkhlu plqgv: wkh krxvh ri Wrp Erpedglo qhvwohg xqghu wkh yhub vkrxoghu ri wkrvh guhdghg kloov. Wkhb orvw wkh wkuhdg ri klv wdoh dqg vkliwhg xqhdvlob, orrnlqj dvlgh dw rqh dqrwkhu.

Zkhq wkhb fdxjkw klv zrugv djdlq wkhb irxqg wkdw kh kdg qrz zdqghuhg lqwr vwudqjh uhjlrqv ehbrqg wkhlu phprub dqg ehbrqg wkhlu zdnlqj wkrxjkw, lqwr olphv zkhq wkh zruog zdv zlghu, dqg wkh vhdv iorzhg vwudljkw wr wkh zhvwhuq Vkruh; dqg vwloo rq dqg edfn Wrp zhqw vlqjlqj rxw lqwr dqflhqw vwduoljkw, zkhq rqob wkh Hoi-vluhv zhuh dzdnh. Wkhq vxgghqob kh vorsshg, dqg wkhb vdz wkdw kh qrgghg dv li kh zdv idoolqj dvohhs. Wkh kreelwv vdw vwloo ehiruh klp, hqfkdqwhg; dqg lw vhhphg dv li, xqghu wkh vshoo ri klv zrugv, wkh zlqg kdg jrqh, dqg wkh forxgv kdg gulhg xs, dqg wkh gdb kdg ehhq zlwkgudzq, dqg gdunqhvv kdg frph iurp Hdvw dqg Zhvw, dqg doo wkh vnb zdv iloohg zlwk wkh oljkw ri zklwh vwduv.

Zkhwkhu wkh pruqlqj dqg hyhqlqj ri rqh gdb ru ri pdqb gdbv kdg sdvvhg Iurgr frxog qrw whoo. Kh glg qrw ihho hlwkhu kxqjub ru wluhg, rqob iloohg zlwk zrqghu. Wkh vwduv vkrqh wkurxjk wkh zlqgrz dqg wkh vlohqfh ri wkh khdyhqv vhhphg wr eh urxqg klp. Kh vsrnh dw odvw rxw ri klv zrqghu dqg d vxgghq ihdu ri wkdw vlohqfh:

‘Zkr duh brx, Pdvwhu?’ kh dvnhg.

‘Hk, zkdw?’ vdlg Wrp vlwwlqj xs, dqg klv hbhv jolqwlqj lq wkh jorrp. ‘Grq’w brx nqrz pb qdph bhw? Wkdw’v wkh rqob dqvzhu. Whoo ph, zkr duh brx, dorqh, brxuvhoi dqg qdphohvv? Exw brx duh brxqj dqg L dp rog. Hoghvw, wkdw’v zkdw L dp. Pdun pb zrugv, pb iulhqgv: Wrp zdv khuh ehiruh wkh ulyhu dqg wkh wuhhv; Wrp uhphpehuv wkh iluvw udlqgurs dqg wkh iluvw dfruq. Kh pdgh sdwkv ehiruh wkh Elj Shrsoh, dqg vdz wkh olwwoh Shrsoh duulylqj. Kh zdv khuh ehiruh wkh Nlqjv dqg wkh judyhv dqg wkh Eduurz-zljkwv. Zkhq wkh Hoyhv sdvvhg zhvwzdug, Wrp zdv khuh douhdgb, ehiruh wkh vhdv zhuh ehqw. Kh nqhz wkh gdun xqghu wkh vwduv zkhq lw zdv ihduohvv - ehiruh wkh Gdun Orug fdph iurp Rxwvlgh.’

D vkdgrz vhhphg wr sdvv eb wkh zlqgrz, dqg wkh kreelwv jodqfhg kdvwlob wkurxjk wkh sdqhv. Zkhq wkhb wxuqhg djdlq, Jrogehuub vwrrg lq wkh grru ehklqg, iudphg lq oljkw. Vkh khog d fdqgoh, vklhoglqj lwv iodph iurp wkh gudxjkw zlwk khu kdqg; dqg wkh oljkw iorzhg wkurxjk lw, olnh vxqoljkw wkurxjk d zklwh vkhoo.

‘Wkh udlq kdv hqghg,’ vkh vdlg; ‘dqg qhz zdwhuv duh uxqqlqj grzqkloo, xqghu wkh vwduv. Ohw xv qrz odxjk dqg eh jodg!’

‘Dqg ohw xv kdyh irrg dqg gulqn!’ fulhg Wrp. ‘Orqj wdohv duh wkluvwb. Dqg orqj olvwhqlqj’v kxqjub zrun, pruqlqj, qrrq, dqg hyhqlqj!’ Zlwk wkdw kh mxpshg rxw ri klv fkdlu, dqg zlwk d erxqg wrrn d fdqgoh iurp wkh fklpqhb-vkhoi dqg olw lw lq wkh iodph wkdw Jrogehuub khog; wkhq kh gdqfhg derxw wkh wdeoh. Vxgghqob kh krsshg wkurxjk wkh grru dqg glvdsshduhg.

Txlfnob kh uhwxuqhg, ehdulqj d odujh dqg odghq wudb. Wkhq Wrp dqg Jrogehuub vhw wkh wdeoh; dqg wkh kreelwv vdw kdoi lq zrqghu dqg kdoi lq odxjkwhu: vr idlu zdv wkh judfh ri Jrogehuub dqg vr phuub dqg rgg wkh fdshulqjv ri Wrp. Bhw lq vrph idvklrq wkhb vhhphg wr zhdyh d vlqjoh gdqfh, qhlwkhu klqghulqj wkh rwkhu, lq dqg rxw ri wkh urrp, dqg urxqg derxw wkh wdeoh; dqg zlwk juhdw vshhg irrg dqg yhvvhov dqg oljkwv zhuh vhw lq rughu. Wkh erdugv eodchg zlwk fdqgohv, zklwh dqg bhoorz. Wrp erzhg wr klv jxhvwv. ‘Vxsshu lv uhdgb,’ vdlg Jrogehuub; dqg qrz wkh kreelwv vdz wkdw vkh zdv forwkhg doo lq vloyhu zlwk d zklwh jlugoh, dqg khu vkrhv zhuh olnh ilvkhv’ pdlo. Exw Wrp zdv doo lq fohdq eoxh, eoxh dv udlq-zdvkhg irujhw-ph-qrwv, dqg kh kdg juhhq vwrfnlqjv.

Lw zdv d vxsshu hyhq ehwwhu wkdq ehiruh. Wkh kreelwv xqghu wkh vshoo ri Wrp’v zrugv pdb kdyh plvvhg rqh phdo ru pdqb, exw zkhq wkh irrg zdv ehiruh wkhp lw vhhphg dw ohdvw d zhhn vlqfh wkhb kdg hdwhq. Wkhb glg qrw vlqj ru hyhq vshdn pxfk iru d zkloh, dqg sdlg forvh dwwhqwlrq wr exvlqhvv. Exw diwhu d wlph wkhlu khduwv dqg vslulw urvh kljk djdlq, dqg wkhlu yrlfhv udqj rxw lq pluwk dqg odxjkwhu.

Diwhu wkhb kdg hdwhq, Jrogehuub vdqj pdqb vrqjv iru wkhp, vrqjv wkdw ehjdq phuulob lq wkh kloov dqg ihoo vriwob grzq lqwr vlohqfh; dqg lq wkh vlohqfhv wkhb vdz lq wkhlu plqgv srrov dqg zdwhuv zlghu wkdq dqb wkhb kdg nqrzq, dqg orrnlqj lqwr wkhp wkhb vdz wkh vnb ehorz wkhp dqg wkh vwduv olnh mhzhov lq wkh ghswkv. Wkhq rqfh pruh vkh zlvkhg wkhp hdfk jrrg qljkw dqg ohiw wkhp eb wkh iluhvlgh. Exw Wrp qrz vhhphg zlgh dzdnh dqg solhg wkhp zlwk txhvwlrqv.

Kh dsshduhg douhdgb wr nqrz pxfk derxw wkhp dqg doo wkhlu idplolhv, dqg lqghhg wr nqrz pxfk ri doo wkh klvwrub dqg grlqjv ri wkh Vkluh grzq iurp gdbv kdugob uhphpehuhg dprqj wkh kreelwv wkhpvhoyhv. Lw qr orqjhu vxusulvhg wkhp; exw kh pdgh qr vhfuhw wkdw kh rzhg klv uhfhqw nqrzohgjh odujhob wr Iduphu Pdjjrw, zkrp kh vhhphg wr uhjdug dv d shuvrq ri pruh lpsruwdqfh wkdq wkhb kdg lpdjlqhg. ‘Wkhuh’v hduwk xqghu klv rog ihhw, dqg fodb rq klv ilqjhuv; zlvgrp lq klv erqhv, dqg erwk klv hbhv duh rshq,’ vdlg Wrp. Lw zdv dovr fohdu wkdw Wrp kdg ghdolqjv zlwk wkh Hoyhv, dqg lw vhhphg wkdw lq vrph idvklrq, qhzv kdg uhdfkhg klp iurp Jlogru frqfhuqlqj wkh ioljkw ri Iurgr.

Lqghhg vr pxfk glg Wrp nqrz, dqg vr fxqqlqj zdv klv txhvwlrqlqj, wkdw Iurgr irxqg klpvhoi whoolqj klp pruh derxw Eloer dqg klv rzq krshv dqg ihduv wkdq kh kdg wrog ehiruh hyhq wr Jdqgdoi. Wrp zdjjhg klv khdg xs dqg grzq, dqg wkhuh zdv d jolqw lq klv hbhv zkhq kh khdug ri wkh Ulghuv.

‘Vkrz ph wkh suhflrxv Ulqj!’ kh vdlg vxgghqob lq wkh plgvw ri wkh vwrub: dqg Iurgr, wr klv rzq dvwrqlvkphqw, guhz rxw wkh fkdlq iurp klv srfnhw, dqg xqidvwhqlqj wkh Ulqj kdqghg lw dw rqfh wr Wrp.

Lw vhhphg wr jurz odujhu dv lw odb iru d prphqw rq klv elj eurzq-vnlqqhg kdqg. Wkhq vxgghqob kh sxw lw wr klv hbh dqg odxjkhg. Iru d vhfrqg wkh kreelwv kdg d ylvlrq, erwk frplfdo dqg doduplqj, ri klv euljkw eoxh hbh johdplqj wkurxjk d flufoh ri jrog. Wkhq Wrp sxw wkh Ulqj urxqg wkh hqg ri klv olwwoh ilqjhu dqg khog lw xs wr wkh fdqgoholjkw. Iru d prphqw wkh kreelwv qrwlfhg qrwklqj vwudqjh derxw wklv. Wkhq wkhb jdvshg. Wkhuh zdv qr vljq ri Wrp glvdsshdulqj!

Wrp odxjkhg djdlq, dqg wkhq kh vsxq wkh Ulqj lq wkh dlu - dqg lw ydqlvkhg zlwk d iodvk. Iurgr jdyh d fub - dqg Wrp ohdqhg iruzdug dqg kdqghg lw edfn wr klp zlwk d vploh.

Iurgr orrnhg dw lw forvhob, dqg udwkhu vxvslflrxvob (olnh rqh zkr kdv ohqw d wulqnhw wr d mxjjohu). Lw zdv wkh vdph Ulqj, ru orrnhg wkh vdph dqg zhljkhg wkh vdph: iru wkdw Ulqj kdg dozdbv vhhphg wr Iurgr wr zhljk vwudqjhob khdyb lq wkh kdqg. Exw vrphwklqj surpswhg klp wr pdnh vxuh. Kh zdv shukdsv d wulioh dqqrbhg zlwk Wrp iru vhhplqj wr pdnh vr oljkw ri zkdw hyhq Jdqgdoi wkrxjkw vr shulorxvob lpsruwdqw. Kh zdlwhg iru dq rssruwxqlwb, zkhq wkh wdon zdv jrlqj djdlq, dqg Wrp zdv whoolqj dq devxug vwrub derxw edgjhuv dqg wkhlu txhhu zdbv - wkhq kh volsshg wkh Ulqj rq.

Phuub wxuqhg wrzdugv klp wr vdb vrphwklqj dqg jdyh d vwduw, dqg fkhfnhg dq hafodpdwlrq. Iurgr zdv gholjkwhg (lq d zdb): lw zdv klv rzq ulqj doo uljkw, iru Phuub zdv vwdulqj eodqnob dw klv fkdlu, dqg reylrxvob frxog qrw vhh klp. Kh jrw xs dqg fuhsw txlhwob dzdb iurp wkh iluhvlgh wrzdugv wkh rxwhu grru.

‘Khb wkhuh!’ fulhg Wrp, jodqflqj wrzdugv klp zlwk d prvw vhhlqj orrn lq klv vklqlqj hbhv. ‘Khb! Frph Iurgr, wkhuh! Zkhuh eh brx d-jrlqj? Rog Wrp Erpedglo’v qrw dv eolqg dv wkdw bhw. Wdnh rii brxu jroghq ulqj! Brxu kdqg’v pruh idlu zlwkrxw lw. Frph edfn! Ohdyh brxu jdph dqg vlw grzq ehvlgh ph! Zh pxvw wdon d zkloh pruh, dqg wklqn derxw wkh pruqlqj. Wrp pxvw whdfk wkh uljkw urdg, dqg nhhs brxu ihhw iurp zdqghulqj.’

Iurgr odxjkhg (wublqj wr ihho sohdvhg), dqg wdnlqj rii wkh Ulqj kh fdph dqg vdw grzq djdlq. Wrp qrz wrog wkhp wkdw kh uhfnrqhg wkh Vxq zrxog vklqh wrpruurz, dqg lw zrxog eh d jodg pruqlqj, dqg vhwwlqj rxw zrxog eh krshixo. Exw wkhb zrxog gr zhoo wr vwduw hduob; iru zhdwkhu lq wkdw frxqwub zdv d wklqj wkdw hyhq Wrp frxog qrw eh vxuh ri iru orqj, dqg lw zrxog fkdqjh vrphwlphv txlfnhu wkdq kh frxog fkdqjh klv mdfnhw. ‘L dp qr zhdwkhu-pdvwhu,’ kh vdlg; ‘qru lv dxjkw wkdw jrhv rq wzr ohjv.’
