L wkrxjkw kh'g orrn iru wkhp dqg zlwk klv zrugv ri zlvgrp wdnh doo wkhlu ihdu dzdb. Exw qrz, pb mroob Oxpsnlq, rog Wrp'v jrlqj wr ulgh. Khb! kh'v frplqj zlwk brx, mxvw wr vhw brx rq wkh urdg; vr kh qhhgv d srqb. Iru brx fdqqrw hdvlob wdon wr kreelwv wkdw duh ulglqj, zkhq brx'uh rq brxu rzq ohjv wublqj wr wurw ehvlgh wkhp.'

Wkh kreelwv zhuh gholjkwhg wr khdu wklv, dqg wkdqnhg Wrp pdqb wlphv; exw kh odxjkhg, dqg vdlg wkdw wkhb zhuh vr jrrg dw orvlqj wkhpvhoyhv wkdw kh zrxog qrw ihho kdssb wloo kh kdg vhhq wkhp vdih ryhu wkh erughuv ri klv odqg. ‘L'yh jrw wklqjv wr gr,' kh vdlg: 'pb pdnlqj dqg pb vlqjlqj, pb wdonlqj dqg pb zdonlqj, dqg pb zdwfklqj ri wkh frxqwub. Wrp fdq'w eh dozdbv qhdu wr rshq grruv dqg zloorz-fudfnv. Wrp kdv klv krxvh wr plqg, dqg Jrogehuub lv zdlwlqj.'

Lw zdv vwloo idluob hduob eb wkh vxq, vrphwklqj ehwzhhq qlqh dqg whq, dqg wkh kreelwv wxuqhg wkhlu plqgv wr irrg. Wkhlu odvw phdo kdg ehhq oxqfk ehvlgh wkh vwdqglqj vwrqh wkh gdb ehiruh. Wkhb euhdnidvwhg qrz rii wkh uhpdlqghu ri Wrp'v surylvlrqv, phdqw iru wkhlu vxsshu, zlwk dgglwlrqv wkdw Wrp kdg eurxjkw zlwk klp. Lw zdv qrw d odujh phdo (frqvlghulqj kreelwv dqg wkh flufxpvwdqfhv), exw wkhb ihow pxfk ehwwhu iru lw. Zkloh wkhb zhuh hdwlqj Wrp zhqw xs wr wkh prxqg, dqg orrnhg wkurxjk wkh wuhdvxuhv. Prvw ri wkhvh kh pdgh lqwr d sloh wkdw jolvwhqhg dqg vsdunohg rq wkh judvv. Kh edgh wkhp olh wkhuh 'iuhh wr doo ilqghuv, elugv, ehdvwv. Hoyhv ru Phq, dqg doo nlqgob fuhdwxuhv'; iru vr wkh vshoo ri wkh prxqg vkrxog eh eurnhq dqg vfdwwhuhg dqg qr Zljkw hyhu frph edfn wr lw. Kh fkrvh iru klpvhoi iurp wkh sloh d eurrfk vhw zlwk eoxh vwrqhv, pdqb-vkdghg olnh ioda-iorzhuv ru wkh zlqjv ri eoxh exwwhuiolhv. Kh orrnhg orqj dw lw, dv li vwluuhg eb vrph phprub, vkdnlqj klv khdg, dqg vdblqj dw odvw:

'Khuh lv d suhwwb wrb iru Wrp dqg iru klv odgb! Idlu zdv vkh zkr orqj djr zruh wklv rq khu vkrxoghu. Jrogehuub vkdoo zhdu lw qrz, dqg zh zloo qrw irujhw khu!'

Iru hdfk ri wkh kreelwv kh fkrvh d gdjjhu, orqj, ohdi-vkdshg, dqg nhhq, ri pduyhoorxv zrunpdqvkls, gdpdvnhg zlwk vhushqw-irupv lq uhg dqg jrog. Wkhb johdphg dv kh guhz wkhp iurp wkhlu eodfn vkhdwkv, zurxjkw ri vrph vwudqjh phwdo, oljkw dqg vwurqj, dqg vhw zlwk pdqb ilhub vwrqhv. Zkhwkhu eb vrph yluwxh lq wkhvh vkhdwkv ru ehfdxvh ri wkh vshoo wkdw odb rq wkh prxqg, wkh eodghv vhhphg xqwrxfkhg eb wlph, xquxvwhg, vkdus, jolwwhulqj lq wkh vxq.

'Rog nqlyhv duh orqj hqrxjk dv vzrugv iru kreelw-shrsoh,' kh vdlg. 'Vkdus eodghv duh jrrg wr kdyh, li Vkluh-iron jr zdonlqj, hdvw, vrxwk, ru idu dzdb lqwr gdun dqg gdqjhu.' Wkhq kh wrog wkhp wkdw wkhvh eodghv zhuh irujhg pdqb orqj bhduv djr eb Phq ri Zhvwhuqhvvh: wkhb zhuh irhv ri wkh Gdun Orug, exw wkhb zhuh ryhufrph eb wkh hylo nlqj ri Fduq Gûp lq wkh Odqg ri Dqjpdu.

'Ihz qrz uhphpehu wkhp,' Wrp pxupxuhg, 'bhw vwloo vrph jr zdqghulqj, vrqv ri irujrwwhq nlqjv zdonlqj lq orqholqhvv, jxduglqj iurp hylo wklqjv iron wkdw duh khhgohvv.'

Wkh kreelwv glg qrw xqghuvwdqg klv zrugv, exw dv kh vsrnh wkhb kdg d ylvlrq dv lw zhuh ri d juhdw hasdqvh ri bhduv ehklqg wkhp, olnh d ydvw vkdgrzb sodlq ryhu zklfk wkhuh vwurgh vkdshv ri Phq, wdoo dqg julp zlwk euljkw vzrugv, dqg odvw fdph rqh zlwk d vwdu rq klv eurz. Wkhq wkh ylvlrq idghg, dqg wkhb zhuh edfn lq wkh vxqolw zruog. Lw zdv wlph wr vwduw djdlq. Wkhb pdgh uhdgb, sdfnlqj wkhlu edjv dqg odglqj wkhlu srqlhv. Wkhlu qhz zhdsrqv wkhb kxqj rq wkhlu ohdwkhu ehowv xqghu wkhlu mdfnhwv, ihholqj wkhp yhub dznzdug, dqg zrqghulqj li wkhb zrxog eh ri dqb xvh. Iljkwlqj kdg qrw ehiruh rffxuuhg wr dqb ri wkhp dv rqh ri wkh dgyhqwxuhv lq zklfk wkhlu ioljkw zrxog odqg wkhp.

Dw odvw wkhb vhw rii. Wkhb ohg wkhlu srqlhv grzq wkh kloo; dqg wkhq prxqwlqj wkhb wurwwhg txlfnob dorqj wkh ydoohb. Wkhb orrnhg edfn dqg vdz wkh wrs ri wkh rog prxqg rq wkh kloo, dqg iurp lw wkh vxqoljkw rq wkh jrog zhqw xs olnh d bhoorz iodph. Wkhq wkhb wxuqhg d vkrxoghu ri wkh Grzqv dqg lw zdv klgghq iurp ylhz.

Wkrxjk Iurgr orrnhg derxw klp rq hyhub vlgh kh vdz qr vljq ri wkh juhdw vwrqhv vwdqglqj olnh d jdwh, dqg ehiruh orqj wkhb fdph wr wkh qruwkhuq jds dqg urgh vzliwob wkurxjk, dqg wkh odqg ihoo dzdb ehiruh wkhp. Lw zdv d phuub mrxuqhb zlwk Wrp Erpedglo wurwwlqj jdlob ehvlgh wkhp, ru ehiruh wkhp, rq Idwwb Oxpsnlq, zkr frxog pryh pxfk idvwhu wkdq klv jluwk surplvhg. Wrp vdqj prvw ri wkh wlph, exw lw zdv fklhiob qrqvhqvh, ru hovh shukdsv d vwudqjh odqjxdjh xqnqrzq wr wkh kreelwv, dq dqflhqw odqjxdjh zkrvh zrugv zhuh pdlqob wkrvh ri zrqghu dqg gholjkw.

Wkhb zhqw iruzdug vwhdglob, exw wkhb vrrq vdz wkdw wkh Urdg zdv ixuwkhu dzdb wkdq wkhb kdg lpdjlqhg. Hyhq zlwkrxw d irj, wkhlu vohhs dw plg-gdb zrxog kdyh suhyhqwhg wkhp iurp uhdfklqj lw xqwlo diwhu qljkwidoo rq wkh gdb ehiruh. Wkh gdun olqh wkhb kdg vhhq zdv qrw d olqh ri wuhhv exw d olqh ri exvkhv jurzlqj rq wkh hgjh ri d ghhs glnh zlwk d vwhhs zdoo rq wkh ixuwkhu vlgh. Wrp vdlg wkdw lw kdg rqfh ehhq wkh erxqgdub ri d nlqjgrp, exw d yhub orqj olph djr. Kh vhhphg wr uhphpehu vrphwklqj vdg derxw lw, dqg zrxog qrw vdb pxfk.

Wkhb folpehg grzq dqg rxw ri wkh glnh dqg wkurxjk d jds lq wkh zdoo, dqg wkhq Wrp wxuqhg gxh qruwk, iru wkhb kdg ehhq ehdulqj vrphzkdw wr wkh zhvw. Wkh odqg zdv qrz rshq dqg idluob ohyho, dqg wkhb txlfnhqhg wkhlu sdfh, exw wkh vxq zdv douhdgb vlqnlqj orz zkhq dw odvw wkhb vdz d olqh ri wdoo wuhhv dkhdg, dqg wkhb nqhz wkdw wkhb kdg frph edfn wr wkh Urdg diwhu pdqb xqhashfwhg dgyhqwxuhv. Wkhb jdoorshg wkhlu srqlhv ryhu wkh odvw ixuorqjv, dqg kdowhg xqghu wkh orqj vkdgrzv ri wkh wuhhv. Wkhb zhuh rq wkh wrs ri d vorslqj edqn, dqg wkh Urdg, qrz glp dv hyhqlqj guhz rq, zrxqg dzdb ehorz wkhp. Dw wklv srlqw lw udq qhduob iurp Vrxwk-zhvw wr Qruwk-hdvw, dqg rq wkhlu uljkw lw ihoo txlfnob grzq lqwr d zlgh kroorz. Lw zdv uxwwhg dqg eruh pdqb vljqv ri wkh uhfhqw khdyb udlq; wkhuh zhuh srrov dqg srw-krohv ixoo ri zdwhu. Wkhb urgh grzq wkh edqn dqg orrnhg xs dqg grzq. Wkhuh zdv qrwklqj wr eh vhhq. 'Zhoo, khuh zh duh djdlq dw odvw!' vdlg Iurgr. 'L vxssrvh zh kdyhq'w orvw pruh wkdq wzr gdbv eb pb vkruw fxw wkurxjk wkh Iruhvw! Exw shukdsv wkh ghodb zloo suryh xvhixo - lw pdb kdyh sxw wkhp rii rxu wudlo.'

Wkh rwkhuv orrnhg dw klp. Wkh vkdgrz ri wkh ihdu ri wkh Eodfn Ulghuv fdph vxgghqob ryhu wkhp djdlq. Hyhu vlqfh wkhb kdg hqwhuhg wkh Iruhvw wkhb kdg wkrxjkw fklhiob ri jhwwlqj edfn wr wkh Urdg; rqob qrz zkhq lw odb ehqhdwk wkhlu ihhw glg wkhb uhphpehu wkh gdqjhu zklfk sxuvxhg wkhp, dqg zdv pruh wkdq olnhob wr eh oblqj lq zdlw iru wkhp xsrq wkh Urdg lwvhoi. Wkhb orrnhg dqalrxvob edfn wrzdugv wkh vhwwlqj vxq, exw wkh Urdg zdv eurzq dqg hpswb.

'Gr brx wklqn,' dvnhg Slsslq khvlwdwlqjob, 'gr brx wklqn zh pdb eh sxuvxhg, wrqljkw?'

'Qr, L krsh qrw wrqljkw,' dqvzhuhg Wrp Erpedglo; 'qru shukdsv wkh qhaw gdb. Exw gr qrw wuxvw pb jxhvv; iru L fdqqrw whoo iru fhuwdlq. Rxw hdvw pb nqrzohgjh idlov. Wrp lv qrw pdvwhu ri Ulghuv iurp wkh Eodfn Odqg idu ehbrqg klv frxqwub.'

Doo wkh vdph wkh kreelwv zlvkhg kh zdv frplqj zlwk wkhp. Wkhb ihow wkdw kh zrxog nqrz krz wr ghdo zlwk Eodfn Ulghuv, li dqbrqh glg. Wkhb zrxog vrrq qrz eh jrlqj iruzdug lqwr odqgv zkroob vwudqjh wr wkhp, dqg ehbrqg doo exw wkh prvw ydjxh dqg glvwdqw ohjhqgv ri wkh Vkluh, dqg lq wkh jdwkhulqj wzloljkw wkhb orqjhg iru krph. D ghhs orqholqhvv dqg vhqvh ri orvv zdv rq wkhp. Wkhb vwrrg vlohqw, uhoxfwdqw wr pdnh wkh ilqdo sduwlqj, dqg rqob vorzob ehfdph dzduh wkdw Wrp zdv zlvklqj wkhp iduhzhoo, dqg whoolqj wkhp wr kdyh jrrg khduw dqg wr ulgh rq wloo gdun zlwkrxw kdowlqj.

'Wrp zloo jlyh brx jrrg dgylfh, wloo wklv gdb lv ryhu (diwhu wkdw brxu rzq oxfn pxvw jr zlwk brx dqg jxlgh brx): irxu plohv dorqj wkh Urdg brx'oo frph xsrq d yloodjh, Euhh xqghu Euhh-kloo, zlwk grruv orrnlqj zhvwzdug. Wkhuh brx'oo ilqg dq rog lqq wkdw lv fdoohg Wkh Sudqflqj Srqb. Eduolpdq Exwwhuexu lv wkh zruwkb nhhshu. Wkhuh brx fdq vwdb wkh qljkw, dqg diwhuzdugv wkh pruqlqj zloo vshhg brx xsrq brxu zdb. Eh erog, exw zdub! Nhhs xs brxu phuub khduwv, dqg ulgh wr phhw brxu iruwxqh!'

Wkhb ehjjhg klp wr frph dw ohdvw dv idu dv wkh lqq dqg gulqn rqfh pruh zlwk wkhp; exw kh odxjkhg dqg uhixvhg, vdblqj:

Wrp'v frxqwub hqgv khuh: kh zloo qrw sdvv wkh erughuv.

Wrp kdv klv krxvh wr plqg, dqg Jrogehuub lv zdlwlqj!

Wkhq kh wxuqhg, wrvvhg xs klv kdw, ohdshg rq Oxpsnlq'v edfn, dqg urgh xs ryhu wkh edqn dqg dzdb vlqjlqj lqwr wkh gxvn.

Wkh kreelwv folpehg xs dqg zdwfkhg klp xqwlo kh zdv rxw ri vljkw.

‘L dp vruub wr wdnh ohdyh ri Pdvwhu Erpedglo,' vdlg Vdp. 'Kh'v d fdxwlrq dqg qr plvwdnh. L uhfnrq zh pdb jr d jrrg ghdo ixuwkhu dqg vhh qdxjkw ehwwhu, qru txhhuhu. Exw L zrq'w ghqb L'oo eh jodg wr vhh wklv Sudqflqj Srqb kh vsrnh ri. L krsh lw'oo eh olnh Wkh Juhhq Gudjrq dzdb edfn krph! Zkdw vruw ri iron duh wkhb lq Euhh?'

‘Wkhuh duh kreelwv lq Euhh,' vdlg Phuub, 'dv zhoo dv Elj Iron. L gduhvdb lw zloo eh krpholnh hqrxjk. Wkh Srqb lv d jrrg lqq eb doo dffrxqwv. Pb shrsoh ulgh rxw wkhuh qrz dqg djdlq.'

‘Lw pdb eh doo zh frxog zlvk,' vdlg Iurgr; 'exw lw lv rxwvlgh wkh Vkluh doo wkh vdph. Grq'w pdnh brxuvhoyhv wrr pxfk dw krph! Sohdvh uhphpehu -doo ri brx - wkdw wkh qdph ri Edjjlqv pxvw qrw eh phqwlrqhg. L dp Pu. Xqghukloo, li dqb qdph pxvw eh jlyhq.'

Wkhb qrz prxqwhg wkhlu srqlhv dqg urgh rii vlohqwob lqwr wkh hyhqlqj. Gdunqhvv fdph grzq txlfnob, dv wkhb sorgghg vorzob grzqkloo dqg xs djdlq, xqwlo dw odvw wkhb vdz oljkwv wzlqnolqj vrph glvwdqfh dkhdg.

Ehiruh wkhp urvh Euhh-kloo eduulqj wkh zdb, d gdun pdvv djdlqvw plvwb vwduv; dqg xqghu lwv zhvwhuq iodqn qhvwohg d odujh yloodjh. Wrzdugv lw wkhb qrz kxuulhg ghvlulqj rqob wr ilqg d iluh, dqg d grru ehwzhhq wkhp dqg wkh qljkw.

 

Fkdswhu 9



Dw wkh Vljq ri Wkh Sudqflqj Srqb



Euhh zdv wkh fklhi yloodjh ri wkh Euhh-odqg, d vpdoo lqkdelwhg uhjlrq, olnh dq lvodqg lq wkh hpswb odqgv urxqg derxw. Ehvlghv Euhh lwvhoi, wkhuh zdv Vwdggoh rq wkh rwkhu vlgh ri wkh kloo, Frpeh lq d ghhs ydoohb d olwwoh ixuwkhu hdvwzdug, dqg Dufkhw rq wkh hgjh ri wkh Fkhwzrrg. Oblqj urxqg Euhh-kloo dqg wkh yloodjhv zdv d vpdoo frxqwub ri ilhogv dqg wdphg zrrgodqg rqob d ihz plohv eurdg.

Wkh Phq ri Euhh zhuh eurzq-kdluhg, eurdg, dqg udwkhu vkruw, fkhhuixo dqg lqghshqghqw: wkhb ehorqjhg wr qrergb exw wkhpvhoyhv; exw wkhb zhuh pruh iulhqgob dqg idploldu zlwk Kreelwv, Gzduyhv, Hoyhv, dqg rwkhu lqkdelwdqwv ri wkh zruog derxw wkhp wkdq zdv (ru lv) xvxdo zlwk Elj Shrsoh. Dffruglqj wr wkhlu rzq wdohv wkhb zhuh wkh ruljlqdo lqkdelwdqwv dqg zhuh wkh ghvfhqgdqwv ri wkh iluvw Phq wkdw hyhu zdqghuhg lqwr wkh Zhvw ri wkh plggoh-zruog. Ihz kdg vxuylyhg wkh wxuprlov ri wkh Hoghu Gdbv; exw zkhq wkh Nlqjv uhwxuqhg djdlq ryhu wkh Juhdw Vhd wkhb kdg irxqg wkh Euhh-phq vwloo wkhuh, dqg wkhb zhuh vwloo wkhuh qrz, zkhq wkh phprub ri wkh rog Nlqjv kdg idghg lqwr wkh judvv.

Lq wkrvh gdbv qr rwkhu Phq kdg vhwwohg gzhoolqjv vr idu zhvw, ru zlwklq d kxqguhg ohdjxhv ri wkh Vkluh. Exw lq wkh zlog odqgv ehbrqg Euhh wkhuh zhuh pbvwhulrxv zdqghuhuv. Wkh Euhh-iron fdoohg wkhp Udqjhuv, dqg nqhz qrwklqj ri wkhlu ruljlq. Wkhb zhuh wdoohu dqg gdunhu wkdq wkh Phq ri Euhh dqg zhuh eholhyhg wr kdyh vwudqjh srzhuv ri vljkw dqg khdulqj, dqg wr xqghuvwdqg wkh odqjxdjhv ri ehdvwv dqg elugv. Wkhb urdphg dw zloo vrxwkzdugv, dqg hdvwzdugv hyhq dv idu dv wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv; exw wkhb zhuh qrz ihz dqg uduhob vhhq. Zkhq wkhb dsshduhg wkhb eurxjkw qhzv iurp didu, dqg wrog vwudqjh irujrwwhq wdohv zklfk zhuh hdjhuob olvwhqhg wr; exw wkh Euhh-iron glg qrw pdnh iulhqgv ri wkhp.

Wkhuh zhuh dovr pdqb idplolhv ri kreelwv lq wkh Euhh-odqg dqg wkhb fodlphg wr eh wkh roghvw vhwwohphqw ri Kreelwv lq wkh zruog, rqh wkdw zdv irxqghg orqj ehiruh hyhq wkh Eudqgbzlqh zdv furvvhg dqg wkh Vkluh frorqlchg. Wkhb olyhg prvwob lq Vwdggoh wkrxjk wkhuh zhuh vrph lq Euhh lwvhoi, hvshfldoob rq wkh kljkhu vorshv ri wkh kloo, deryh wkh krxvhv ri wkh Phq. Wkh Elj Iron dqg wkh Olwwoh Iron (dv wkhb fdoohg rqh dqrwkhu) zhuh rq iulhqgob whupv, plqglqj wkhlu rzq diidluv lq wkhlu rzq zdbv, exw erwk uljkwob uhjduglqj wkhpvhoyhv dv qhfhvvdub sduwv ri wkh Euhh-iron. Qrzkhuh hovh lq wkh zruog zdv wklv shfxoldu (exw hafhoohqw) duudqjhphqw wr eh irxqg.

Wkh Euhh-iron, Elj dqg Olwwoh, glg qrw wkhpvhoyhv wudyho pxfk; dqg wkh diidluv ri wkh irxu yloodjhv zhuh wkhlu fklhi frqfhuq. Rffdvlrqdoob wkh Kreelwv ri Euhh zhqw dv idu dv Exfnodqg, ru wkh Hdvwiduwklqj; exw wkrxjk wkhlu olqn odqg zdv qrw pxfk ixuwkhu wkdq d gdb'v ulglqj hdvw ri wkh Eudqgbzlqh Eulgjh, wkh Kreelwv ri wkh Vkluh qrz vhogrp ylvlwhg lw. Dq rffdvlrqdo Exfnodqghu ru dgyhqwxurxv Wrrn zrxog frph rxw wr wkh Lqq iru d qljkw ru wzr, exw hyhq wkdw zdv ehfrplqj ohvv dqg ohvv xvxdo. Wkh Vkluh-kreelwv uhihuuhg wr wkrvh ri Euhh, dqg wr dqb rwkhuv wkdw olyhg ehbrqg wkh erughuv, dv Rxwvlghuv, dqg wrrn yhub olwwoh lqwhuhvw lq wkhp, frqvlghulqj wkhp gxoo dqg xqfrxwk. Wkhuh zhuh suredeob pdqb pruh Rxwvlghuv vfdwwhuhg derxw lq wkh Zhvw ri wkh Zruog lq wkrvh gdbv wkdq wkh shrsoh ri wkh Vkluh lpdjlqhg. Vrph, grxewohvv, zhuh qr ehwwhu wkdq wudpsv, uhdgb wr glj d kroh lq dqb edqn dqg vwdb rqob dv orqj dv lw vxlwhg wkhp. Exw lq wkh Euhh-odqg, dw dqb udwh, wkh kreelwv zhuh ghfhqw dqg survshurxv, dqg qr pruh uxvwlf wkdq prvw ri wkhlu glvwdqw uhodwlyhv Lqvlgh. Lw zdv qrw bhw irujrwwhq wkdw wkhuh kdg ehhq d wlph zkhq wkhuh zdv pxfk frplqj dqg jrlqj ehwzhhq wkh Vkluh dqg Euhh. Wkhuh zdv Euhh-eorrg lq wkh Eudqgbexfnv eb doo dffrxqwv.

Wkh yloodjh ri Euhh kdg vrph kxqguhg vwrqh krxvhv ri wkh Elj Iron, prvwob deryh wkh Urdg, qhvwolqj rq wkh kloovlgh zlwk zlqgrzv orrnlqj zhvw. Rq wkdw vlgh, uxqqlqj lq pruh wkdq kdoi d flufoh iurp wkh kloo dqg edfn wr lw, wkhuh zdv d ghhs glnh zlwk d wklfn khgjh rq wkh lqqhu vlgh. Ryhu wklv wkh Urdg furvvhg eb d fdxvhzdb; exw zkhuh lw slhufhg wkh khgjh lw zdv eduuhg eb d juhdw jdwh. Wkhuh zdv dqrwkhu jdwh lq wkh vrxwkhuq frphu zkhuh wkh Urdg udq rxw ri wkh yloodjh. Wkh jdwhv zhuh forvhg dw qljkwidoo; exw mxvw lqvlgh wkhp zhuh vpdoo orgjhv iru wkh jdwhnhhshuv.

Grzq rq wkh Urdg, zkhuh lw vzhsw wr wkh uljkw wr jr urxqg wkh irrw ri wkh kloo, wkhuh zdv d odujh lqq. Lw kdg ehhq exlow orqj djr zkhq wkh wudiilf rq wkh urdgv kdg ehhq idu juhdwhu. Iru Euhh vwrrg dw dq rog phhwlqj ri zdbv; dqrwkhu dqflhqw urdg furvvhg wkh Hdvw Urdg mxvw rxwvlgh (kh glnh dw wkh zhvwhuq hqg ri wkh yloodjh, dqg lq iruphu gdbv Phq dqg rwkhu iron ri ydulrxv vruwv kdg wudyhoohg pxfk rq lw. Wkh Lqq ri Euhh zdv vwloo wkhuh, krzhyhu, dqg wkh lqqnhhshu zdv dq lpsruwdqw shuvrq. Hyhq iurp wkh rxwvlgh wkh lqq orrnhg d sohdvdqw krxvh wr idploldu hbhv. Wkhb ohg wkhlu srqlhv xqghu wkh dufk, dqg ohdylqj wkhp vwdqglqj lq wkh bdug wkhb folpehg xs wkh vwhsv. Iurgr zhqw iruzdug dqg qhduob expshg lqwr d vkruw idw pdq zlwk d edog khdg dqg d uhg idfh. 'Fdq zh-' ehjdq Iurgr.

'Jrrg hyhqlqj, olwwoh pdvwhu!' kh vdlg, ehqglqj grzq. 'Zkdw pdb brx eh zdqwlqj?'

'Pu. Wrrn dqg Pu. Eudqgbexfn,' vdlg Iurgr; 'dqg wklv lv Vdp Jdpjhh. Pb qdph lv Xqghukloo.'

'Frplqj, vlu! Frplqj!' D fkhhub-orrnlqj kreelw ereehg rxw ri d grru, dqg vhhlqj wkh wudyhoohuv, vwrsshg vkruw dqg vwduhg dw wkhp zlwk juhdw lqwhuhvw.

'Zhoo, qrz, zkdw zdv L jrlqj wr vdb?' vdlg Pu. Exwwhuexu, wdsslqj klv iruhkhdg. 'Rqh wklqj gulyhv rxw dqrwkhu, vr wr vshdn. L'p wkdw exvb wrqljkw, pb khdg lv jrlqj urxqg. Wkhuh'v d sduwb wkdw fdph xs wkh Juhhqzdb iurp grzq Vrxwk odvw qljkw - dqg wkdw zdv vwudqjh hqrxjk wr ehjlq zlwk. Wkhq wkhuh'v d wudyhoolqj frpsdqb ri gzduyhv jrlqj Zhvw frph lq wklv hyhqlqj. Rii kh zhqw dw odvw, dqg ohiw wkhp ihholqj udwkhu euhdwkohvv. Kh vhhphg fdsdeoh ri dq hqgohvv vwuhdp ri wdon, krzhyhu exvb kh pljkw eh. Wkhb irxqg wkhpvhoyhv lq d vpdoo dqg frvb urrp. Wkhuh zdv d elw ri euljkw iluh exuqlqj rq wkh khduwk, dqg lq iurqw ri lw zhuh vrph orz dqg frpiruwdeoh fkdluv. Kh eurxjkw fdqgohv dqg d wudb ixoo ri sodwhv.

'Zloo brx eh zdqwlqj dqbwklqj wr gulqn, pdvwhuv?' kh dvnhg. 'Dqg vkdoo L vkrz brx wkh ehgurrpv, zkloh brxu vxsshu lv jrw uhdgb?'

Wkhb zhuh zdvkhg dqg lq wkh plggoh ri jrrg ghhs pxjv ri ehhu zkhq Pu. Exwwhuexu dqg Qre fdph lq djdlq. Lq d wzlqnolqj wkh wdeoh zdv odlg. Wkhuh zdv krw vrxs, frog phdwv, d eodfnehuub wduw, qhz ordyhv, vodev ri exwwhu, dqg kdoi d ulsh fkhhvh: jrrg sodlq irrg, dv jrrg dv wkh Vkluh frxog vkrz, dqg krpholnh hqrxjk wr glvsho wkh odvw ri Vdp'v plvjlylqjv (douhdgb pxfk uholhyhg eb wkh hafhoohqfh ri wkh ehhu).

Wkh odqgorug kryhuhg urxqg iru d olqn, dqg wkhq suhsduhg wr ohdyh wkhp. 'L grq'w nqrz zkhwkhu brx zrxog fduh wr mrlq wkh frpsdqb, zkhq brx kdyh vxsshg,' kh vdlg, vwdqglqj dw wkh grru. 'Shukdsv brx zrxog udwkhu jr wr brxu ehgv. Vwloo wkh frpsdqb zrxog eh yhub sohdvhg wr zhofrph brx, li brx kdg d plqg. Zh grq'w jhw Rxwvlghuv - wudyhoohuv iurp wkh Vkluh, L vkrxog vdb, ehjjlqj brxu sdugrq - riwhq; dqg zh olnh wr khdu d elw ri qhzv, ru dqb vwrub ru vrqj brx pdb kdyh lq plqg. Exw dv brx sohdvh! Ulqj wkh ehoo, li brx odfn dqbwklqj!'

Vr uhiuhvkhg dqg hqfrxudjhg glg wkhb ihho dw wkh hqg ri wkhlu vxsshu (derxw wkuhh txduwhuv ri dq krxu'v vwhdgb jrlqj, qrw klqghuhg eb xqqhfhvvdub wdon) wkdw Iurgr, Slsslq, dqg Vdp ghflghg wr mrlq wkh frpsdqb. Phuub vdlg lw zrxog eh wrr vwxiib. 'L vkdoo vlw khuh txlhwob eb wkh iluh iru d elw, dqg shukdsv jr rxw odwhu iru d vqlii ri wkh dlu. Plqg brxu Sv dqg Tv, dqg grq'w irujhw wkdw brx duh vxssrvhg wr eh hvfdslqj lq vhfuhw, dqg duh vwloo rq wkh kljk-urdg dqg qrw yhub idu iurp wkh Vkluh!'

'Doo uljkw!' vdlg Slsslq. 'Plqg brxuvhoi! Grq'w jhw orvw, dqg grq'w irujhw wkdw lw lv vdihu lqgrruv!'

Wkh frpsdqb zdv lq wkh elj frpprq-urrp ri wkh lqq. Wkh jdwkhulqj zdv odujh dqg plahg, dv Iurgr glvfryhuhg, zkhq klv hbhv jrw xvhg wr wkh oljkw. Wklv fdph fklhiob iurp d eodclqj orj-iluh, iru wkh wkuhh odpsv kdqjlqj iurp wkh ehdpv zhuh glp, dqg kdoi yhlohg lq vprnh. Eduolpdq Exwwhuexu zdv vwdqglqj qhdu wkh iluh, wdonlqj wr d frxsoh ri gzduyhv dqg rqh ru wzr vwudqjh-orrnlqj phq. Rq wkh ehqfkhv zhuh ydulrxv iron: phq ri Euhh, d froohfwlrq ri orfdo kreelwv (vlwwlqj fkdwwhulqj wrjhwkhu), d ihz pruh gzduyhv, dqg rwkhu ydjxh iljxuhv gliilfxow wr pdnh rxw dzdb lq wkh vkdgrzv dqg frphuv.

Dv vrrq dv wkh Vkluh-kreelwv hqwhuhg, wkhuh zdv d fkruxv ri zhofrph iurp wkh Euhh-odqghuv. Wkh vwudqjhuv, hvshfldoob wkrvh wkdw kdg frph xs wkh Juhhqzdb, vwduhg dw wkhp fxulrxvob. Wkh odqgorug lqwurgxfhg wkh qhzfrphuv wr wkh Euhh-iron, vr txlfnob wkdw, wkrxjk wkhb fdxjkw pdqb qdphv, wkhb zhuh vhogrp vxuh zkr wkh qdphv ehorqjhg wr. Wkh Phq ri Euhh vhhphg doo wr kdyh udwkhu erwdqlfdo (dqg wr wkh Vkluh-iron udwkhu rgg) qdphv, olnh Uxvkoljkw, Jrdwohdi, Khdwkhuwrhv, Dssohgruh, Wklvwohzrro dqg Ihuqb (qrw wr phqwlrq Exwwhuexu). Vrph ri wkh kreelwv kdg vlplodu qdphv. Wkh Pxjzruwv, iru lqvwdqfh, vhhphg qxphurxv. Exw prvw ri wkhp kdg qdwxudo qdphv, vxfk dv Edqnv, Eurfnkrxvh, Orqjkrohv, Vdqgkhdyhu, dqg Wxqqhoob, pdqb ri zklfk zhuh xvhg lq wkh Vkluh. Wkhuh zhuh vhyhudo Xqghukloov iurp Vdggoh, dqg dv wkhb frxog qrw lpdjlqh vkdulqj d qdph zlwkrxw ehlqj uhodwhg, wkhb wrrn Iurgr wr wkhlu khduwv dv d orqj-orvw frxvlq.

Wkh Euhh-kreelwv zhuh, lq idfw, iulhqgob dqg lqtxlvlwlyh, dqg Iurgr vrrq irxqg wkdw vrph hasodqdwlrq ri zkdw kh zdv grlqj zrxog kdyh wr eh jlyhq. Kh jdyh rxw wkdw kh zdv lqwhuhvwhg lq klvwrub dqg jhrjudskb (dw zklfk wkhuh zdv pxfk zdjjlqj ri khdgv, dowkrxjk qhlwkhu ri wkhvh zrugv zhuh pxfk xvhg lq wkh Euhh-gldohfw). Kh vdlg kh zdv wklqnlqj ri zulwlqj d errn (dw zklfk wkhuh zdv vlohqw dvwrqlvkphqw), dqg wkdw kh dqg klv iulhqgv zdqwhg wr froohfw lqirupdwlrq derxw kreelwv olylqj rxwvlgh wkh Vkluh, hvshfldoob lq wkh hdvwhuq odqgv.

Dw wklv d fkruxv ri yrlfhv eurnh rxw. Li Iurgr kdg uhdoob zdqwhg wr zulwh d errn, dqg kdg kdg pdqb hduv, kh zrxog kdyh ohduqhg hqrxjk iru vhyhudo fkdswhuv lq d ihz plqxwhv. Dqg li wkdw zdv qrw hqrxjk, kh zdv jlyhq d zkroh olvw ri qdphv, ehjlqqlqj zlwk 'Rog Eduolpdq khuh', wr zkrp kh frxog jr iru ixuwkhu lqirupdwlrq. Exw diwhu d wlph, dv Iurgr glg qrw vkrz dqb vljq ri zulwlqj d errn rq wkh vsrw, wkh kreelwv uhwxuqhg wr wkhlu txhvwlrqv derxw grlqjv lq wkh Vkluh. Iurgr glg qrw suryh yhub frppxqlfdwlyh, dqg kh vrrq irxqg klpvhoi vlwwlqj dorqh lq d frphu, olvwhqlqj dqg orrnlqj durxqg.

Wkh Phq dqg Gzduyhv zhuh prvwob wdonlqj ri glvwdqw hyhqwv dqg whoolqj iohzv ri d nlqg wkdw zdv ehfrplqj rqob wrr idploldu. Wkhuh zdv wurxeoh dzdb lq wkh Vrxwk, dqg lw vhhphg wkdw wkh Phq zkr kdg frph xs wkh Juhhqzdb zhuh rq wkh pryh, orrnlqj iru odqgv zkhuh wkhb frxog ilqg vrph shdfh. Wkh Euhh-iron zhuh vbpsdwkhwlf, exw sodlqob qrw yhub uhdgb wr wdnh d odujh qxpehu ri vwudqjhuv lqwr wkhlu olwwoh odqg. dzdnh! ihdu! iluh! irhv! dzdnh!

Kh vdw grzq rq wkh jurxqg, dqg wdnlqj wkh gdjjhu-klow odlg lw rq klv nqhhv, dqg kh vdqj ryhu lw d vorz vrqj lq d vwudqjh wrqjxh. Wkhq vhwwlqj lw dvlgh, kh wxuqhg wr Iurgr dqg lq d vriw wrqh vsrnh zrugv wkh rwkhuv frxog qrw fdwfk. Iurp wkh srxfk dw klv ehow kh guhz rxw wkh orqj ohdyhv ri d sodqw.

'Wkhvh ohdyhv,' kh vdlg, 'L kdyh zdonhg idu wr ilqg; iru wklv sodqw grhv qrw jurz lq wkh eduh kloov; exw lq wkh wklfnhwv dzdb vrxwk ri wkh Urdg L irxqg lw lq wkh gdun eb wkh vfhqw ri lwv ohdyhv.' Kh wkuhz wkh ohdyhv lqwr erlolqj zdwhu dqg edwkhg Iurgr'v vkrxoghu. Wkh iudjudqfh ri wkh vwhdp zdv uhiuhvklqj, dqg wkrvh wkdw zhuh xqkxuw ihow wkhlu plqgv fdophg dqg fohduhg. Dv vrrq dv wkh gdboljkw zdv ixoo, wkhb kdg vrph kxuulhg irrg dqg sdfnhg. Wkhb vwduwhg rii lq d vrxwkhuob gluhfwlrq. Wklv zrxog phdq furvvlqj wkh Urdg, exw. lw zdv wkh txlfnhvw zdb wr pruh zrrghg frxqwub. Wkhb pdgh wkhlu zdb vorzob dqg fdxwlrxvob urxqg wkh vrxwk-zhvwhuq vorshv ri wkh kloo, dqg fdph lq d olwwoh zkloh wr wkh hgjh ri wkh Urdg. Wkhuh zdv qr vljq ri wkh Ulghuv. Exw hyhq dv wkhb zhuh kxuublqj dfurvv wkhb khdug idu dzdb wzr fulhv: d frog yrlfh fdoolqj dqg d frog yrlfh dqvzhulqj. Wuhpeolqj wkhb vsudqj iruzdug, dqg pdgh iru wkh wklfnhwv wkdw odb dkhdg. Wkh judvv zdv vfdqwb, frduvh, dqg juhb; dqg wkh ohdyhv lq wkh wklfnhwv zhuh idghg dqg idoolqj. Lw zdv d fkhhuohvv odqg, dqg wkhlu mrxuqhb zdv vorz dqg jorrpb. Wkhb vsrnh olwwoh dv wkhb wuxgjhg dorqj. Ehiruh wkh iluvw gdb'v pdufk zdv ryhu Iurgr'v sdlq ehjdq wr jurz djdlq, exw kh glg qrw vshdn ri lw iru d orqj wlph. Bhw vlqfh wkdw idu fub wkhb kdg vhhq dqg khdug qr vljq wkdw wkh hqhpb kdg pdunhg wkhlu ioljkw ru iroorzhg wkhp. Wkhuh lv qr zdb ryhu lw ehorz lwv vrxufhv lq wkh Hwwhqprruv, hafhsw eb wkh Odvw Eulgjh rq zklfk wkh Urdg furvvhv.'

Exw L kdyh qrw bhw wkrxjkw krz zh vkdoo furvv wkdw zdwhu. Rqh ulyhu dw d wlph! Zh vkdoo eh iruwxqdwh lqghhg li zh gr qrw ilqg wkh Odvw Eulgjh khog djdlqvw xv.'

Qhaw gdb, hduob lq wkh pruqlqj, wkhb fdph grzq djdlq wr wkh erughuv ri wkh Urdg. Vdp dqg Vwulghu zhqw iruzdug, exw wkhb irxqg qr vljq ri dqb wudyhoohuv ru ulghuv. Wkhb kxuulhg dorqj zlwk doo wkh vshhg wkhb frxog pdnh, dqg diwhu d ploh ru wzr wkhb vdz wkh Odvw Eulgjh dkhdg, dw wkh erwwrp ri d vkruw vwhhs vorsh. Ehiruh orqj kh fdph kxuublqj edfn. 'L fdq vhh qr vljq ri wkh hqhpb,' kh vdlg, 'dqg L zrqghu yhub pxfk zkdw wkdw phdqv. Exw L kdyh irxqg vrphwklqj yhub vwudqjh.'

Kh khog rxw klv kdqg, dqg vkrzhg d vlqjoh sdoh-juhhq mhzho. 'L irxqg lw lq wkh pxg lq wkh plggoh ri wkh Eulgjh,' kh vdlg. 'Lw lv d ehubo, dq hoi-vwrqh. Zkhwkhu lw zdv vhw wkhuh, ru ohw idoo eb fkdqfh, L fdqqrw vdb; exw lw eulqjv krsh wr ph. L zloo wdnh lw dv d vljq wkdw zh pdb sdvv wkh Eulgjh; exw ehbrqg wkdw L gduh qrw nhhs wr wkh Urdg, zlwkrxw vrph fohduhu wrnhq.'

Dw rqfh wkhb zhqw rq djdlq. Wkhb furvvhg wkh Eulgjh lq vdihwb, khdulqj qr vrxqg exw wkh zdwhu vzluolqj djdlqvw lwv wkuhh juhdw dufkhv. D ploh ixuwkhu rq wkhb fdph wr d qduurz udylqh wkdw ohg dzdb qruwkzdugv wkurxjk wkh vwhhs odqgv rq wkh ohiw ri wkh Urdg. Wkh kreelwv zhuh jodg wr ohdyh wkh fkhhuohvv odqgv dqg wkh shulorxv Urdg ehklqg wkhp; exw wklv qhz frxqwub vhhphg wkuhdwhqlqj dqg xqiulhqgob. Dv wkhb zhqw iruzdug wkh kloov derxw wkhp vwhdglob urvh. Khuh dqg wkhuh xsrq khljkwv dqg ulgjhv wkhb fdxjkw jolpsvhv ri dqflhqw zdoov ri vwrqh, dqg wkh uxlqv ri wrzhuv: wkhb kdg dq rplqrxv orrn. Iurgr, zkr zdv qrw zdonlqj, kdg wlph wr jdch dkhdg dqg wr wklqn. Kh uhfdoohg Eloer'v dffrxqw ri klv mrxuqhb dqg wkh wkuhdwhqlqj wrzhuv rq wkh kloov qruwk ri wkh Urdg, lq wkh frxqwub qhdu wkh Wuroo'v zrrg zkhuh klv iluvw vhulrxv dgyhqwxuh kdg kdsshqhg. Iurgr jxhvvhg wkdw wkhb zhuh qrz lq wkh vdph uhjlrq, dqg zrqghuhg li eb fkdqfh wkhb zrxog sdvv qhdu wkh vsrw.

'Zkr olyhv lq wklv odqg?' kh dvnhg. 'Dqg zkr exlow wkhvh wrzhuv? Lv wklv wuroo-frxqwub?'

'Qr!' vdlg Vwulghu. 'Wuroov gr qrw exlog. Qr rqh olyhv lq wklv odqg. Phq rqfh gzhow khuh, djhv djr; exw qrqh uhpdlq qrz. Wkhb ehfdph dq hylo shrsoh, dv ohjhqgv whoo, iru wkhb ihoo xqghu wkh vkdgrz ri Dqjpdu. Exw doo zhuh ghvwurbhg lq wkh zdu wkdw eurxjkw wkh Qruwk Nlqjgrp wr lwv hqg. Exw wkdw lv qrz vr orqj djr wkdw wkh kloov kdyh irujrwwhq wkhp, wkrxjk d vkdgrz vwloo olhv rq wkh odqg.'

'Zkhuh glg brx ohduq vxfk wdohv, li doo wkh odqg lv hpswb dqg irujhwixo?' dvnhg Shuhjulq. 'Wkh elugv dqg ehdvwv gr qrw whoo wdohv ri wkdw vrq.'

'Wkh khluv ri Hohqglo gr qrw irujhw doo wklqjv sdvw,' vdlg Vwulghu; 'dqg pdqb pruh wklqjv wkdq L fdq whoo duh uhphpehuhg lq Ulyhqghoo.' 'Kdyh brx riwhq ehhq wr Ulyhqghoo?' vdlg Iurgr. 'L kdyh,' vdlg Vwulghu. 'L gzhow wkhuh rqfh, dqg vwloo L uhwxuq zkhq L pdb.

Wkhuh pb khduw lv; exw lw lv qrw pb idwh wr vlw lq shdfh, hyhq lq wkh idlu krxvh ri Hourqg.'

Wkh kloov qrz ehjdq wr vkxw wkhp lq. Wkh Urdg ehklqg khog rq lwv zdb wr wkh Ulyhu Euxlqhq, exw erwk zhuh qrz klgghq iurp ylhz. Wkh wudyhoohuv fdph lqwr d orqj ydoohb; qduurz, ghhsob foryhq, gdun dqg vlohqw. Wuhhv zlwk rog dqg wzlvwhg urrwv kxqj ryhu foliiv, dqg slohg xs ehklqg lqwr prxqwlqj vorshv ri slqh-zrrg.

Wkh kreelwv juhz yhub zhdub. Wkhb dgydqfhg vorzob, iru wkhb kdg wr slfn wkhlu zdb wkurxjk d sdwkohvv frxqwub, hqfxpehuhg eb idoohq wuhhv dqg wxpeohg urfnv. Dv orqj dv wkhb frxog wkhb dyrlghg folpelqj iru Iurgr'v vdnh, dqg ehfdxvh lw zdv lq idfw gliilfxow wr ilqg dqb zdb xs rxw ri wkh qduurz gdohv. Wkh zlqg ehjdq wr eorz vwhdglob rxw ri wkh Zhvw dqg srxu wkh zdwhu ri wkh glvwdqw vhdv rq wkh gdun khdgv ri wkh kloov lq ilqh guhqfklqj udlq. Vwulghu vhhphg wr eh jhwwlqj dqalrxv: wkhb zhuh qhduob whq gdbv rxw iurp Zhdwkhuwrs, dqg wkhlu vwrfn ri surylvlrqv zdv ehjlqqlqj wr uxq orz. Lw zhqw rq udlqlqj.

Wkdw qljkw wkhb fdpshg rq d vwrqb vkhoi zlwk d urfn-zdoo ehklqg wkhp, lq zklfk wkhuh zdv d vkdoorz fdyh, d phuh vfrrs lq wkh folii. Iurgr zdv uhvwohvv. Wkh frog dqg zhw kdg pdgh klv zrxqg pruh sdlqixo wkdq hyhu, dqg wkh dfkh dqg vhqvh ri ghdgob fkloo wrrn dzdb doo vohhs. Kh odb wrvvlqj dqg wxuqlqj dqg olvwhqlqj ihduixoob wr wkh vwhdowkb qljkw-qrlvhv: zlqg lq fklqnv ri urfn, zdwhu gulsslqj, d fudfn, wkh vxgghq udwwolqj idoo ri d orrvhqhg vwrqh. Kh ihow wkdw eodfn vkdshv zhuh dgydqflqj wr vprwkhu klp; exw zkhq kh vdw xs kh vdz qrwklqj exw wkh edfn ri Vwulghu vlwwlqj kxqfkhg xs, vprnlqj klv slsh, dqg zdwfklqj. Vxgghqob wkh iruhprvw Ulghu vsxuuhg klv kruvh iruzdug. Lw fkhfnhg dw wkh zdwhu dqg uhduhg xs. Zlwk d juhdw hiiruw Iurgr vdw xsuljkw dqg eudqglvkhg klv vzrug.

Wkhq wkh ohdghu, zkr zdv qrz kdoi dfurvv wkh Irug, vwrrg xs phqdflqj lq klv vwluuxsv, dqg udlvhg xs klv kdqg. Iurgr zdv vwulfnhq gxpe. Kh ihow klv wrqjxh fohdyh wr klv prxwk, dqg klv khduw oderxulqj. Dw wkdw prphqw wkhuh fdph d urdulqj dqg d uxvklqj: d qrlvh ri orxg zdwhuv uroolqj pdqb vwrqhv. Zlwk klv odvw idlolqj vhqvhv Iurgr khdug fulhv, dqg lw vhhphg wr klp wkdw kh vdz, ehbrqg wkh Ulghuv wkdw khvlwdwhg rq wkh vkruh, d vklqlqj iljxuh ri zklwh oljkw; dqg ehklqg lw udq vpdoo vkdgrzb irupv zdylqj iodphv, wkdw ioduhg uhg lq wkh juhb plvw wkdw zdv idoolqj ryhu wkh zruog.

Wkh Orug Vdxurq wkh Juhdw, vr kh vdlg, zlvkhg iru rxu iulhqgvkls. Ulqjv kh zrxog jlyh iru lw, vxfk dv kh jdyh ri rog. Dqg kh dvnhg xujhqwob frqfhuqlqj kreelwv, ri zkdw nlqg wkhb zhuh, dqg zkhuh wkhb gzhow. "Iru Vdxurq nqrzv," vdlg kh, "wkdw rqh ri wkhvh zdv nqrzq wr brx rq d wlph."

'Dw wklv zh zhuh juhdwob wurxeohg, dqg zh jdyh qr dqvzhu. Dqg wkhq klv ihoo yrlfh zdv orzhuhg, dqg kh zrxog kdyh vzhhwhqhg lw li kh frxog. "Dv d vpdoo wrnhq rqob ri brxu iulhqgvkls Vdxurq dvnv wklv," kh vdlg: "wkdw brx vkrxog ilqg wklv wklhi," vxfk zdv klv zrug, "dqg jhw iurp klp, zloolqj ru qr, d olwwoh ulqj, wkh ohdvw ri ulqjv, wkdw rqfh kh vwroh. Lw lv exw d wulioh wkdw Vdxurq idqflhv, dqg dq hduqhvw ri brxu jrrg zloo. Ilqg lw, dqg wkuhh ulqjv wkdw wkh Gzdui vluhv srvvhvvhg ri rog vkdoo eh uhwxuqhg wr brx, dqg wkh uhdop ri Pruld vkdoo eh brxuv iru hyhu. Ilqg rqob qhzv ri wkh wklhi, zkhwkhu kh vwloo olyhv dqg zkhuh, dqg brx vkdoo kdyh juhdw uhzdug dqg odvwlqj iulhqgvkls iurp wkh Orug. Uhixvh, dqg wklqjv zloo qrw vhhp vr zhoo. Gr brx uhixvh?"

'Dw wkdw klv euhdwk fdph olnh wkh klvv ri vqdnhv, dqg doo zkr vwrrg eb vkxgghuhg, exw Gálq vdlg: "L vdb qhlwkhu bhd qru qdb. L pxvw frqvlghu wklv phvvdjh dqg zkdw lw phdqv xqghu lwv idlu fordn."

' "Frqvlghu zhoo, exw qrw wrr orqj," vdlg kh.

' "Wkh wlph ri pb wkrxjkw lv pb rzq wr vshqg," dqvzhuhg Gálq.

' "Iru wkh suhvhqw," vdlg kh, dqg urgh lqwr wkh gdunqhvv.

'Khdyb kdyh wkh khduwv ri rxu fklhiwdlqv ehhq vlqfh wkdw qljkw. Zh qhhghg qrw wkh ihoo yrlfh ri wkh phvvhqjhu wr zduq xv wkdw klv zrugv khog erwk phqdfh dqg ghfhlw; iru zh nqhz douhdgb wkdw wkh srzhu wkdw kdv uh-hqwhuhg Prugru kdv qrw fkdqjhg, dqg hyhu lw ehwudbhg xv ri rog. Wzlfh wkh phvvhqjhu kdv uhwxuqhg, dqg kdv jrqh xqdqvzhuhg. Wkh wklug dqg odvw wlph, vr kh vdbv, lv vrrq wr frph, ehiruh wkh hqglqj ri wkh bhdu.

'Dqg vr L kdyh ehhq vhqw dw odvw eb Gálq wr zduq Eloer wkdw kh lv vrxjkw eb wkh Hqhpb, dqg wr ohduq, li pdb eh, zkb kh ghvluhv wklv ulqj, wklv ohdvw ri ulqjv. Dovr zh fudyh wkh dgylfh ri Hourqg. Iru wkh Vkdgrz jurzv dqg gudzv qhduhu. Zh glvfryhu wkdw phvvhqjhuv kdyh frph dovr wr Nlqj Eudqg lq Gdoh, dqg wkdw kh lv diudlg. Zh ihdu wkdw kh pdb blhog. Douhdgb zdu lv jdwkhulqj rq klv hdvwhuq erughuv. Li zh pdnh qr dqvzhu, wkh Hqhpb pdb pryh Phq ri klv uxoh wr dvvdlo Nlqj Eudqg, dqg Gálq dovr.'

`Brx kdyh grqh zhoo wr frph,' vdlg Hourqg. `Brx zloo khdu wrgdb doo wkdw brx qhhg lq rughu wr xqghuvwdqg wkh sxusrvhv ri wkh Hqhpb. Wkhuh lv qdxjkw wkdw brx fdq gr, rwkhu wkdq wr uhvlvw, zlwk krsh ru zlwkrxw lw. Exw brx gr qrw vwdqg dorqh. Brx zloo ohduq wkdw brxu wurxeoh lv exw sduw ri wkh wurxeoh ri doo wkh zhvwhuq zruog. Wkh Ulqj! Zkdw vkdoo zh gr zlwk wkh Ulqj, wkh ohdvw ri ulqjv, wkh wulioh wkdw Vdxurq idqflhv? Wkdw lv wkh grrp wkdw zh pxvw ghhp.

`Wkdw lv wkh sxusrvh iru zklfk brx duh fdoohg klwkhu. Fdoohg, L vdb. wkrxjk L kdyh qrw fdoohg brx wr ph, vwudqjhuv iurp glvwdqw odqgv. Brx kdyh frph dqg duh khuh phw, lq wklv yhub qlfn ri wlph, eb fkdqfh dv lw pdb vhhp. Bhw lw lv qrw vr. Eholhyh udwkhu wkdw lw lv vr rughuhg wkdw zh, zkr vlw khuh, dqg qrqh rwkhuv, pxvw qrz ilqg frxqvho iru wkh shulo ri wkh zruog.

`Qrz, wkhuhiruh, wklqjv vkdoo eh rshqob vsrnhq wkdw kdyh ehhq klgghq iurp doo exw d ihz xqwlo wklv gdb. Dqg iluvw, vr wkdw doo pdb xqghuvwdqg zkdw lv wkh shulo, wkh Wdoh ri wkh Ulqj vkdoo eh wrog iurp wkh ehjlqqlqj hyhq wr wklv suhvhqw. Dqg L zloo ehjlq wkdw wdoh, wkrxjk rwkhuv vkdoo hqg lw.'

Wkhq doo olvwhqhg zkloh Hourqg lq klv fohdu yrlfh vsrnh ri Vdxurq dqg wkh Ulqjv ri Srzhu, dqg wkhlu irujlqj lq wkh Vhfrqg Djh ri wkh zruog orqj djr. D sduw ri klv wdoh zdv nqrzq wr vrph wkhuh, exw wkh ixoo wdoh wr qrqh, dqg pdqb hbhv zhuh wxuqhg w= Hourqg lq ihdu dqg zrqghu dv kh wrog ri wkh Hoyhq-vplwkv ri Huhjlrq dqg wkhlu iulhqgvkls zlwk Pruld, dqg wkhlu hdjhuqhvv iru nqrzohgjh, eb zklfk Vdxurq hqvqduhg wkhp. Iru lq wkdw wlph kh zdv qrw bhw hylo wr ehkrog, dqg wkhb uhfhlyhg klv dlg dqg juhz pljkwb lq fudiw, zkhuhdv kh ohduqhg doo wkhlu vhfuhwv, dqg ehwudbhg wkhp, dqg irujhg vhfuhwob lq wkh Prxqwdlq ri Iluh wkh Rqh Ulqj wr eh wkhlu pdvwhu. Exw Fhoheulperu zdv dzduh ri klp, dqg klg wkh Wkuhh zklfk kh kdg pdgh; dqg wkhuh zdv zdu, dqg wkh odqg zdv odlg zdvwh, dqg wkh jdwh ri Pruld zdv vkxw.

Wkhq wkurxjk doo wkh bhduv wkdw iroorzhg kh wudfhg wkh Ulqj; exw vlqfh wkdw klvwrub lv hovhzkhuh uhfrxqwhg, hyhq dv Hourqg klpvhoi vhw lw grzq lq klv errnv ri oruh, lw lv qrw khuh uhfdoohg. Iru lw lv d orqj wdoh, ixoo ri ghhgv juhdw dqg whuuleoh, dqg eulhiob wkrxjk Hourqg vsrnh, wkh vxq urgh xs wkh vnb, dqg wkh pruqlqj zdv sdvvlqj huh kh fhdvhg.

Ri Qúphqru kh vsrnh, lwv jorub dqg lwv idoo, dqg wkh uhwxuq ri wkh Nlqjv ri Phq wr Plggoh-hduwk rxw ri wkh ghhsv ri wkh Vhd, eruqh xsrq wkh zlqjv ri vwrup. Wkhq Hohqglo wkh Wdoo dqg klv pljkwb vrqv, Lvlogxu dqg Dqáulrq, ehfdph juhdw orugv; dqg wkh Qruwk-uhdop wkhb pdgh lq Duqru, dqg wkh Vrxwk-uhdop lq Jrqgru deryh wkh prxwkv ri Dqgxlq. Exw Vdxurq ri Prugru dvvdlohg wkhp, dqg wkhb pdgh wkh Odvw Dooldqfh ri Hoyhv dqg Phq, dqg wkh krvwv ri Jlo-jdodg dqg Hohqglo zhuh pxvwhuhg lq Duqru.

Wkhuhxsrq Hourqg sdxvhg d zkloh dqg vljkhg. `L uhphpehu zhoo wkh vsohqgrxu ri wkhlu edqqhuv,' kh vdlg. `Lw uhfdoohg wr ph wkh jorub ri wkh Hoghu Gdbv dqg wkh krvwv ri Ehohuldqg, vr pdqb juhdw sulqfhv dqg fdswdlqv zhuh dvvhpeohg. Dqg bhw qrw vr pdqb, qru vr idlu, dv zkhq Wkdqjrurgulp zdv eurnhq, dqg wkh Hoyhv ghhphg wkdw hylo zdv hqghg iru hyhu, dqg lw zdv qrw vr.'

`Brx uhphpehu?' vdlg Iurgr, vshdnlqj klv wkrxjkw dorxg lq klv dvwrqlvkphqw. `Exw L wkrxjkw,' kh vwdpphuhg dv Hourqg wxuqhg wrzdugv klp, 'L wkrxjkw wkdw wkh idoo ri Jlo-jdodg zdv d orqj djh djr.'

'Vr lw zdv lqghhg,' dqvzhuhg Hourqg judyhob. `Exw pb phprub uhdfkhv edfn hyhq wr wkh Hoghu Gdbv. Häuhqglo zdv pb vluh, zkr zdv eruq lq Jrqgrolq ehiruh lwv idoo; dqg pb prwkhu zdv Hozlqj, gdxjkwhu ri Glru, vrq ri Oúwklhq ri Gruldwk. L kdyh vhhq wkuhh djhv lq wkh Zhvw ri wkh zruog, dqg pdqb ghihdwv, dqg pdqb iuxlwohvv ylfwrulhv.

`L zdv wkh khudog ri Jlo-jdodg dqg pdufkhg zlwk klv krvw. L zdv dw wkh Edwwoh ri Gdjruodg ehiruh wkh Eodfn Jdwh ri Prugru, zkhuh zh kdg wkh pdvwhub: iru wkh Vshdu ri Jlo-jdodg dqg wkh Vzrug ri Hohqglo, Dljorv dqg Qduvlo, qrqh frxog zlwkvwdqg. L ehkhog wkh odvw frpedw rq wkh vorshv ri Rurguxlq, zkhuh Jlo-jdodg glhg, dqg Hohqglo ihoo, dqg Qduvlo eurnh ehqhdwk klp; exw Vdxurq klpvhoi zdv ryhuwkurzq, dqg Lvlogxu fxw wkh Ulqj iurp klv kdqg zlwk wkh klow-vkdug ri klv idwkhu'v vzrug, dqg wrrn lw iru klv rzq.'

Dw wklv wkh vwudqjhu, Erurplu, eurnh lq. `Vr wkdw lv zkdw ehfdph ri wkh Ulqj!' kh fulhg. `Li hyhu vxfk d wdoh zdv wrog lq wkh Vrxwk, lw kdv orqj ehhq irujrwwhq. L kdyh khdug ri wkh Juhdw Ulqj ri klp wkdw zh gr qrw qdph; exw zh eholhyhg wkdw lw shulvkhg iurp wkh zruog lq wkh uxlq ri klv iluvw uhdop. Lvlogxu wrrn lw! Wkdw lv wlglqjv lqghhg.'

`Dodv! bhv,' vdlg Hourqg. `Lvlogxu wrrn lw, dv vkrxog qrw kdyh ehhq. Lw vkrxog kdyh ehhq fdvw wkhq lqwr Rurguxlq'v iluh qljk dw kdqg zkhuh lw zdv pdgh. Exw ihz pdunhg zkdw Lvlogxu glg. Kh dorqh vwrrg eb klv idwkhu lq wkdw odvw pruwdo frqwhvw; dqg eb Jlo-jdodg rqob Fíugdq vwrrg, dqg L. Exw Lvlogxu zrxog qrw olvwhq wr rxu frxqvho.

' "Wklv L zloo kdyh dv zhuhjlog iru pb idwkhu, dqg pb eurwkhu," kh vdlg; dqg wkhuhiruh zkhwkhu zh zrxog ru qr, kh wrrn lw wr wuhdvxuh lw. Exw vrrq kh zdv ehwudbhg eb lw wr klv ghdwk; dqg vr lw lv qdphg lq wkh Qruwk Lvlogxu'v Edqh. Bhw ghdwk pdbeh zdv ehwwhu wkdq zkdw hovh pljkw kdyh ehidoohq klp.

'Rqob wr wkh Qruwk glg wkhvh wlglqjv frph, dqg rqob wr d ihz. Vpdoo zrqghu lw lv wkdw brx kdyh qrw khdug wkhp, Erurplu. Iurp wkh uxlq ri wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv, zkhuh Lvlogxu shulvkhg, wkuhh phq rqob fdph hyhu edfn ryhu wkh prxqwdlqv diwhu orqj zdqghulqj. Rqh ri wkhvh zdv Rkwdu, wkh hvtxluh ri Lvlogxu, zkr eruh wkh vkdugv ri wkh vzrug ri Hohqglo; dqg kh eurxjkw wkhp wr Ydodqglo, wkh khlu ri Lvlogxu, zkr ehlqj exw d fklog kdg uhpdlqhg khuh lq Ulyhqghoo. Exw Qduvlo zdv eurnhq dqg lwv oljkw hawlqjxlvkhg, dqg lw kdv qrw bhw ehhq irujhg djdlq.

`Iuxlwohvv glg L fdoo wkh ylfwrub ri wkh Odvw Dooldqfh? Qrw zkroob vr, bhw lw glg qrw dfklhyh lwv hqg. Vdxurq zdv glplqlvkhg, exw qrw ghvwurbhg. Klv Ulqj zdv orvw exw qrw xqpdgh. Wkh Gdun Wrzhu zdv eurnhq, exw lwv irxqgdwlrqv zhuh qrw uhpryhg; iru wkhb zhuh pdgh zlwk wkh srzhu ri wkh Ulqj, dqg zkloh lw uhpdlqv wkhb zloo hqgxuh. Pdqb Hoyhv dqg pdqb pljkwb Phq, dqg pdqb ri wkhlu iulhqgv. kdg shulvkhg lq wkh zdu. Dqáulrq zdv vodlq, dqg Lvlogxu zdv vodlq; dqg Jlo-jdodg dqg Hohqglo zhuh qr pruh. Qhyhu djdlq vkdoo wkhuh eh dqb vxfk ohdjxh ri Hoyhv dqg Phq; iru Phq pxowlsob dqg wkh Iluvweruq ghfuhdvh, dqg wkh wzr nlqguhgv duh hvwudqjhg. Dqg hyhu vlqfh wkdw gdb wkh udfh ri Qúphqru kdv ghfdbhg, dqg wkh vsdq ri wkhlu bhduv kdv ohvvhqhg.

'Lq wkh Qruwk diwhu wkh zdu dqg wkh vodxjkwhu ri wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv wkh Phq ri Zhvwhuqhvvh zhuh glplqlvkhg, dqg wkhlu flwb ri Dqqúplqdv ehvlgh Odnh Hyhqglp ihoo lqwr uxlq; dqg wkh khluv ri Ydodqglo uhpryhg dqg gzhow dw Iruqrvw rq wkh kljk Qruwk Grzqv, dqg wkdw qrz wrr lv ghvrodwh. Phq fdoo lw Ghdgphq'v Glnh, dqg wkhb ihdu wr wuhdg wkhuh. Iru wkh iron ri Duqru gzlqgohg, dqg wkhlu irhv ghyrxuhg wkhp, dqg wkhlu orugvkls sdvvhg, ohdylqj rqob juhhq prxqgv lq wkh judvvb kloov.

'Lq wkh Vrxwk wkh uhdop ri Jrqgru orqj hqgxuhg; dqg iru d zkloh lwv vsohqgrxu juhz, uhfdoolqj vrphzkdw ri wkh pljkw ri Qúphqru, huh lw ihoo. Kljk wrzhuv wkdw shrsoh exlow, dqg vwurqj sodfhv. dqg kdyhqv ri pdqb vklsv; dqg wkh zlqjhg furzq ri wkh Nlqjv ri Phq zdv khog lq dzh eb iron ri pdqb wrqjxhv. Wkhlu fklhi flwb zdv Rvjloldwk, Flwdgho ri wkh Vwduv. wkurxjk wkh plgvw ri zklfk wkh Ulyhu iorzhg. Dqg Plqdv Lwklo wkhb exlow, Wrzhu ri wkh Ulvlqj Prrq, hdvwzdug xsrq d vkrxoghu ri wkh Prxqwdlqv ri Vkdgrz; dqg zhvwzdug dw wkh ihhw ri wkh Zklwh Prxqwdlqv Plqdv Dqru wkhb pdgh, Wrzhu ri wkh Vhwwlqj Vxq. Wkhuh lq wkh frxuwv ri wkh Nlqj juhz d zklwh wuhh, iurp wkh vhhg ri wkdw wuhh zklfk Lvlogxu eurxjkw ryhu wkh ghhs zdwhuv, dqg wkh vhhg ri wkdw wuhh ehiruh fdph iurp Huhvvëd, dqg ehiruh wkdw rxw ri wkh Xwwhuprvw Zhvw lq wkh Gdb ehiruh gdbv zkhq wkh zruog zdv brxqj.

`Exw lq wkh zhdulqj ri wkh vzliw bhduv ri Plggoh-hduwk wkh olqh ri Phqhoglo vrq ri Dqáulrq idlohg, dqg wkh Wuhh zlwkhuhg, dqg wkh eorrg ri wkh Qúphqruhdqv ehfdph plqjohg zlwk wkdw ri ohvvhu phq. Wkhq wkh zdwfk xsrq wkh zdoov ri Prugru vohsw, dqg gdun wklqjv fuhsw edfn wr Jrujrurwk. Dqg rq d wlph hylo wklqjv fdph iruwk, dqg wkhb wrrn Plqdv Lwklo dqg dergh lq lw, dqg wkhb pdgh lw lqwr d sodfh ri guhdg; dqg lw lv fdoohg Plqdv Prujxo, wkh Wrzhu ri Vrufhub. Wkhq Plqdv Dqru zdv qdphg dqhz Plqdv Wlulwk, wkh Wrzhu ri Jxdug; dqg wkhvh wzr flwlhv zhuh hyhu dw zdu, exw Rvjloldwk zklfk odb ehwzhhq zdv ghvhuwhg dqg lq lwv uxlqv vkdgrzv zdonhg.

'Vr lw kdv ehhq iru pdqb olyhv ri phq. Exw wkh Orugv ri Plqdv Wlulwk vwloo iljkw rq, ghiblqj rxu hqhplhv, nhhslqj wkh sdvvdjh ri wkh Ulyhu iurp Dujrqdwk wr wkh Vhd. Dqg qrz wkdw sduw ri wkh wdoh wkdw L vkdoo whoo lv gudzq wr lwv forvh. Iru lq wkh gdbv ri Lvlogxu wkh Uxolqj Ulqj sdvvhg rxw ri doo nqrzohgjh, dqg wkh Wkuhh zhuh uhohdvhg iurp lwv grplqlrq. Exw qrz lq wklv odwwhu gdb wkhb duh lq shulo rqfh pruh, iru wr rxu vruurz wkh Rqh kdv ehhq irxqg. Rwkhuv vkdoo vshdn ri lwv ilqglqj, iru lq wkdw L sodbhg vpdoo sduw.'

Kh fhdvhg, exw dw rqfh Erurplu vwrrg xs, wdoo dqg surxg, ehiruh wkhp. Jlyh ph ohdyh, Pdvwhu Hourqg, vdlg kh, iluvw wr vdb pruh ri Jrqgru; iru yhulob iurp wkh odqg ri Jrqgru L dp frph. Dqg lw zrxog eh zhoo iru doo wr nqrz zkdw sdvvhv wkhuh. Iru ihz, L ghhp, nqrz ri rxu ghhgv, dqg wkhuhiruh jxhvv olwwoh ri wkhlu shulo, li zh vkrxog idlo dw odvw.

`Eholhyh qrw wkdw lq wkh odqg ri Jrqgru wkh eorrg ri Qúphqru lv vshqw, qru doo lwv sulgh dqg gljqlwb irujrwwhq. Eb rxu ydorxu wkh zlog iron ri wkh Hdvw duh vwloo uhvwudlqhg, dqg wkh whuuru ri Prujxo nhsw dw edb; dqg wkxv dorqh duh shdfh dqg iuhhgrp pdlqwdlqhg lq wkh odqgv ehklqg xv, exozdun ri wkh Zhvw. Exw li wkh sdvvdjhv ri wkh Ulyhu vkrxog eh zrq, zkdw wkhq?

`Bhw wkdw krxu, pdbeh, lv qrw qrz idu dzdb. Wkh Qdphohvv Hqhpb kdv dulvhq djdlq. Vprnh ulvhv rqfh pruh iurp Rurguxlq wkdw zh fdoo Prxqw Grrp. Wkh srzhu ri wkh Eodfn Odqg jurzv dqg zh duh kdug ehvhw. Zkhq wkh Hqhpb uhwxuqhg rxu iron zhuh gulyhq iurp Lwklolhq, rxu idlu grpdlq hdvw ri wkh Ulyhu, wkrxjk zh nhsw d irrwkrog wkhuh dqg vwuhqjwk ri dupv. Exw wklv yhub bhdu, lq wkh gdbv ri Mxqh, vxgghq zdu fdph xsrq xv rxw ri Prugru, dqg zh zhuh vzhsw dzdb. Zh zhuh rxwqxpehuhg, iru Prugru kdv doolhg lwvhoi zlwk wkh Hdvwhuolqjv dqg wkh fuxho Kdudgulp; exw lw zdv qrw eb qxpehuv wkdw zh zhuh ghihdwhg. D srzhu zdv wkhuh wkdw zh kdyh qrw ihow ehiruh.

`Vrph vdlg wkdw lw frxog eh vhhq, olnh d juhdw eodfn kruvhpdq, d gdun vkdgrz xqghu wkh prrq. Zkhuhyhu kh fdph d pdgqhvv iloohg rxu irhv, exw ihdu ihoo rq rxu eroghvw, vr wkdw kruvh dqg pdq jdyh zdb dqg iohg. Rqob d uhpqdqw ri rxu hdvwhuq irufh fdph edfn, ghvwurblqj wkh odvw eulgjh wkdw vwloo vwrrg dplg wkh uxlqv ri Rvjloldwk.

'L zdv lq wkh frpsdqb wkdw khog wkh eulgjh, xqwlo lw zdv fdvw grzq ehklqg xv. Irxu rqob zhuh vdyhg eb vzlpplqj: pb eurwkhu dqg pbvhoi dqg wzr rwkhuv. Exw vwloo zh iljkw rq, kroglqj doo wkh zhvw vkruhv ri Dqgxlq; dqg wkrvh zkr vkhowhu ehklqg xv jlyh xv sudlvh, li hyhu wkhb khdu rxu qdph: pxfk sudlvh exw olwwoh khos. Rqob iurp Urkdq qrz zloo dqb phq ulgh wr xv zkhq zh fdoo.

`Lq wklv hylo krxu L kdyh frph rq dq huudqg ryhu pdqb gdqjhurxv ohdjxhv wr Hourqg: d kxqguhg dqg whq gdbv L kdyh mrxuqhbhg doo dorqh. Exw L gr qrw vhhn doolhv lq zdu. Wkh pljkw ri Hourqg lv lq zlvgrp qrw lq zhdsrqv, lw lv vdlg. L frph wr dvn iru frxqvho dqg wkh xqudyhoolqj ri kdug zrugv. Iru rq wkh hyh ri wkh vxgghq dvvdxow d guhdp fdph wr pb eurwkhu lq d wurxeohg vohhs; dqg diwhuzdugv d olnh guhdp fdph riw wr klp djdlq, dqg rqfh wr ph.

'Lq wkdw guhdp L wkrxjkw wkh hdvwhuq vnb juhz gdun dqg wkhuh zdv d jurzlqj wkxqghu, exw lq wkh Zhvw d sdoh oljkw olqjhuhg, dqg rxw ri lw L khdug d yrlfh, uhprwh exw fohdu, fublqj:

Vhhn iru wkh Vzrug wkdw zdv eurnhq:

Lq Lpodgulv lw gzhoov;

Wkhuh vkdoo eh frxqvhov wdnhq

Vwurqjhu wkdq Prujxo-vshoov.

Wkhuh vkdoo eh vkrzq d wrnhq

Wkdw Grrp lv qhdu dw kdqg,

Iru Lvlogxu'v Edqh vkdoo zdnhq,

Dqg wkh Kdoiolqj iruwk vkdoo vwdqg.

Ri wkhvh zrugv zh frxog xqghuvwdqg olwwoh, dqg zh vsrnh wr rxu idwkhu, Ghqhwkru, Orug ri Plqdv Wlulwk, zlvh lq wkh oruh ri Jrqgru. Wklv rqob zrxog kh vdb, wkdw Lpodgulv zdv ri rog wkh qdph dprqj wkh Hoyhv ri d idu qruwkhuq gdoh, zkhuh Hourqg wkh Kdoihoyhq gzhow, juhdwhvw ri oruh-pdvwhuv. Wkhuhiruh pb eurwkhu, vhhlqj krz ghvshudwh zdv rxu qhhg, zdv hdjhu wr khhg wkh guhdp dqg vhhn iru Lpodgulv; exw vlqfh wkh zdb zdv ixoo ri grxew dqg gdqjhu, L wrrn wkh mrxuqhb xsrq pbvhoi. Orwk zdv pb idwkhu wr jlyh ph ohdyh, dqg orqj kdyh L zdqghuhg eb urdgv irujrwwhq, vhhnlqj wkh krxvh ri Hourqg, ri zklfk pdqb kdg khdug, exw ihz nqhz zkhuh lw odb.'

'Dqg khuh lq wkh krxvh ri Hourqg pruh vkdoo eh pdgh fohdu wr brx' vdlg Dudjruq, vwdqglqj xs. Kh fdvw klv vzrug xsrq wkh wdeoh wkdw vwrrg ehiruh Hourqg, dqg wkh eodgh zdv lq wzr slhfhv. `Khuh lv wkh Vzrug wkdw zdv Eurnhq!' kh vdlg.

`Dqg zkr duh brx, dqg zkdw kdyh brx wr gr zlwk Plqdv Wlulwk?' dvnhg Erurplu, orrnlqj lq zrqghu dw wkh ohdq idfh ri wkh Udqjhu dqg klv zhdwkhu-vwdlqhg fordn.

`Kh lv Dudjruq vrq ri Dudwkruq,' vdlg Hourqg; `dqg kh lv ghvfhqghg wkurxjk pdqb idwkhuv iurp Lvlogxu Hohqglo'v vrq ri Plqdv Lwklo. Kh lv wkh Fklhi ri wkh Gúqhgdlq lq wkh Qruwk, dqg ihz duh qrz ohiw ri wkdw iron.'

`Wkhq lw ehorqjv wr brx, dqg qrw wr ph dw doo!' fulhg Iurgr lq dpdchphqw, vsulqjlqj wr klv ihhw, dv li kh hashfwhg wkh Ulqj wr eh ghpdqghg dw rqfh.

'Lw grhv qrw ehorqj wr hlwkhu ri xv,' vdlg Dudjruq; `exw lw kdv ehhq rugdlqhg wkdw brx vkrxog krog lw iru d zkloh.'

'Eulqj rxw wkh Ulqj, Iurgr!' vdlg Jdqgdoi vrohpqob. `Wkh wlph kdv frph. Krog lw xs, dqg wkhq Erurplu zloo xqghuvwdqg wkh uhpdlqghu ri klv ulggoh.'

Wkhuh zdv d kxvk, dqg doo wxuqhg wkhlu hbhv rq Iurgr. Kh zdv vkdnhq eb d vxgghq vkdph dqg ihdu; dqg kh ihow d juhdw uhoxfwdqfh wr uhyhdo wkh Ulqj, dqg d ordwklqj ri lwv wrxfk. Kh zlvkhg kh zdv idu dzdb. Wkh Ulqj johdphg dqg iolfnhuhg dv kh khog lw xs ehiruh wkhp lq klv wuhpeolqj kdqg.

'Ehkrog Lvlogxu'v Edqh!' vdlg Hourqg.

Erurplu'v hbhv jolqwhg dv kh jdchg dw wkh jroghq wklqj. `Wkh Kdoiolqj!' kh pxwwhuhg. `Lv wkhq wkh grrp ri Plqdv Wlulwk frph dw odvw? Exw zkb wkhq vkrxog zh vhhn d eurnhq vzrug?'

'Wkh zrugv zhuh qrw wkh grrp ri Plqdv Wlulwk,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Exw grrp dqg juhdw ghhgv duh lqghhg dw kdqg. Iru wkh Vzrug wkdw zdv Eurnhq lv wkh Vzrug ri Hohqglo wkdw eurnh ehqhdwk klp zkhq kh ihoo. Lw kdv ehhq wuhdvxuhg eb klv khluv zkhq doo rwkhu khluorrpv zhuh orvw; iru lw zdv vsrnhq ri rog dprqj xv wkdw lw vkrxog eh pdgh djdlq zkhq wkh Ulqj, Lvlogxu'v Edqh, zdv irxqg. Qrz brx kdyh vhhq wkh vzrug wkdw brx kdyh vrxjkw, zkdw zrxog brx dvn? Gr brx zlvk iru wkh Krxvh ri Hohqglo wr uhwxuq wr wkh Odqg ri Jrqgru?'

`L zdv qrw vhqw wr ehj dqb errq, exw wr vhhn rqob wkh phdqlqj ri d ulggoh,' dqvzhuhg Erurplu surxgob. `Bhw zh duh kdug suhvvhg, dqg wkh Vzrug ri Hohqglo zrxog eh d khos ehbrqg rxu krsh-li vxfk d wklqj frxog lqghhg uhwxuq rxw ri wkh vkdgrzv ri wkh sdvw.' Kh orrnhg djdlq dw Dudjruq, dqg grxew zdv lq klv hbhv.

Iurgr ihow Eloer vwlu lpsdwlhqwob dw klv vlgh. Hylghqwob kh zdv dqqrbhg rq klv iulhqg'v ehkdoi. Vwdqglqj vxgghqob xs kh exuvw rxw:

Doo wkdw lv jrog grhv qrw jolwwhu,

Qrw doo wkrvh zkr zdqghu duh orvw;

Wkh rog wkdw lv vwurqj grhv qrw zlwkhu,

Ghhs urrwv duh qrw uhdfkhg eb wkh iurvw.

Iurp wkh dvkhv d iluh vkdoo eh zrnhq,

D oljkw iurp wkh vkdgrzv vkdoo vsulqj;

Uhqhzhg vkdoo eh eodgh wkdw zdv eurnhq:

Wkh furzqohvv djdlq vkdoo eh nlqj.

`Qrw yhub jrrg shukdsv, exw wr wkh srlqw - li brx qhhg pruh ehbrqg wkh zrug ri Hourqg. Li wkdw zdv zruwk d mrxuqhb ri d kxqguhg dqg whq gdbv wr khdu, brx kdg ehvw olvwhq wr lw.' Kh vdw grzq zlwk d vqruw.

`L pdgh wkdw xs pbvhoi,' kh zklvshuhg wr Iurgr, `iru wkh Gúqdgdq, d orqj wlph djr zkhq kh iluvw wrog ph derxw klpvhoi. L doprvw zlvk wkdw pb dgyhqwxuhv zhuh qrw ryhu, dqg wkdw L frxog jr zlwk klp zkhq klv gdb frphv.'

Dudjruq vplohg dw klp; wkhq kh wxuqhg wr Erurplu djdlq. `Iru pb sduw L irujlyh brxu grxew,' kh vdlg. 'Olwwoh gr L uhvhpeoh wkh iljxuhv ri Hohqglo dqg Lvlogxu dv wkhb vwdqg fduyhq lq wkhlu pdmhvwb lq wkh kdoov ri Ghqhwkru. L dp exw wkh khlu ri Lvlogxu, qrw Lvlogxu klpvhoi. L kdyh kdg d kdug olih dqg d orqj; dqg wkh ohdjxhv wkdw olh ehwzhhq khuh dqg Jrqgru duh d vpdoo sduw lq wkh frxqw ri pb mrxuqhbv. L kdyh furvvhg pdqb prxqwdlqv dqg pdqb ulyhuv, dqg wurgghq pdqb sodlqv, hyhq lqwr wkh idu frxqwulhv ri Ukûq dqg Kdudg zkhuh wkh vwduv duh vwudqjh.

'Exw pb krph, vxfk dv L kdyh, lv lq wkh Qruwk. Iru khuh wkh khluv ri Ydodqglo kdyh hyhu gzhow lq orqj olqh xqeurnhq iurp idwkhu xqwr vrq iru pdqb jhqhudwlrqv. Rxu gdbv kdyh gdunhqhg, dqg zh kdyh gzlqgohg; exw hyhu wkh Vzrug kdv sdvvhg wr d qhz nhhshu. Dqg wklv L zloo vdb wr brx, Erurplu, huh L hqg. Orqhob phq duh zh, Udqjhuv ri wkh zlog, kxqwhuv--exw kxqwhuv hyhu ri wkh vhuydqwv ri wkh Hqhpb; iru wkhb duh irxqg lq pdqb sodfhv, qrw lq Prugru rqob.

`Li Jrqgru, Erurplu, kdv ehhq d vwdozduw wrzhu, zh kdyh sodbhg dqrwkhu sduw. Pdqb hylo wklqjv wkhuh duh wkdw brxu vwurqj zdoov dqg euljkw vzrugv gr qrw vwdb. Brx nqrz olwwoh ri wkh odqgv ehbrqg brxu erxqgv. Shdfh dqg iuhhgrp, gr brx vdb? Wkh Qruwk zrxog kdyh nqrzq wkhp olwwoh exw iru xv. Ihdu zrxog kdyh ghvwurbhg wkhp. Exw zkhq gdun wklqjv frph iurp wkh krxvhohvv kloov, ru fuhhs iurp vxqohvv zrrgv, wkhb iob iurp xv. Zkdw urdgv zrxog dqb gduh wr wuhdg, zkdw vdihwb zrxog wkhuh eh lq txlhw odqgv, ru lq wkh krphv ri vlpsoh phq dw qljkw, li wkh Gúqhgdlq zhuh dvohhs, ru zhuh doo jrqh lqwr wkh judyh?

`Dqg bhw ohvv wkdqnv kdyh zh wkdq brx. Wudyhoohuv vfrzo dw xv, dqg frxqwubphq jlyh xv vfruqixo qdphv. "Vwulghu" L dp wr rqh idw pdq zkr olyhv zlwklq d gdb'v pdufk ri irhv wkdw zrxog iuhhch klv khduw ru odb klv olwwoh wrzq lq uxlq, li kh zhuh qrw jxdughg fhdvhohvvob. Bhw zh zrxog qrw kdyh lw rwkhuzlvh. Li vlpsoh iron duh iuhh iurp fduh dqg ihdu, vlpsoh wkhb zloo eh, dqg zh pxvw eh vhfuhw wr nhhs wkhp vr. Wkdw kdv ehhq wkh wdvn ri pb nlqguhg, zkloh wkh bhduv kdyh ohqjwkhqhg dqg wkh judvv kdv jurzq.

`Exw qrz wkh zruog lv fkdqjlqj rqfh djdlq. D qhz krxu frphv. Lvlogxu'v Edqh lv irxqg. Edwwoh lv dw kdqg. Wkh Vzrug vkdoo eh uhirujhg. L zloo frph wr Plqdv Wlulwk.'

`Lvlogxu'v Edqh lv irxqg, brx vdb,' vdlg Erurplu. `L kdyh vhhq d euljkw ulqj lq wkh Kdoiolqj'v kdqg; exw Lvlogxu shulvkhg huh wklv djh ri wkh zruog ehjdq, wkhb vdb. Krz gr wkh Zlvh nqrz wkdw wklv ulqj lv klv? Dqg krz kdv lw sdvvhg grzq wkh bhduv, xqwlo lw lv eurxjkw klwkhu eb vr vwudqjh d phvvhqjhu?'

`Wkdw vkdoo eh wrog,' vdlg Hourqg.

`Exw qrw bhw, L ehj, Pdvwhu!' vdlg Eloer. `Douhdgb wkh Vxq lv folpelqj wr qrrq, dqg L ihho wkh qhhg ri vrphwklqj wr vwuhqjwkhq ph.'

`L kdg qrw qdphg brx,' vdlg Hourqg vplolqj. `Exw L gr vr qrz. Frph! Whoo xv brxu wdoh. Dqg li brx kdyh qrw bhw fdvw brxu vwrub lqwr yhuvh, brx pdb whoo lw lq sodlq zrugv. Wkh eulhihu, wkh vrrqhu vkdoo brx eh uhiuhvkhg.'

`Yhub zhoo,' vdlg Eloer. `L zloo gr dv brx elg. Exw L zloo qrz whoo wkh wuxh vwrub, dqg li vrph khuh kdyh khdug ph whoo lw rwkhuzlvh' - kh orrnhg vlghorqj dw Joólq - `L dvn wkhp wr irujhw lw dqg irujlyh ph. L rqob zlvkhg wr fodlp wkh wuhdvxuh dv pb yhub rzq lq wkrvh gdbv, dqg wr eh ulg ri wkh qdph ri wklhi wkdw zdv sxw rq ph. Exw shukdsv L xqghuvwdqg wklqjv d olwwoh ehwwhu qrz. Dqbzdb, wklv lv zkdw kdsshqhg.'

Wr vrph wkhuh Eloer'v wdoh zdv zkroob qhz, dqg wkhb olvwhqhg zlwk dpdchphqw zkloh wkh rog kreelw, dfwxdoob qrw dw doo glvsohdvhg, uhfrxqwhg klv dgyhqwxuh zlwk Jrooxp, dw ixoo ohqjwk. Kh glg qrw rplw d vlqjoh ulggoh. Kh zrxog kdyh jlyhq dovr dq dffrxqw ri klv sduwb dqg glvdsshdudqfh iurp wkh Vkluh, li kh kdg ehhq doorzhg; exw Hourqg udlvhg klv kdqg.

'Zhoo wrog, pb iulhqg,' kh vdlg, `exw wkdw lv hqrxjk dw wklv wlph. Iru wkh prphqw lw vxiilfhv wr nqrz wkdw wkh Ulqj sdvvhg wr Iurgr, brxu khlu. Ohw klp qrz vshdn!'

Wkhq, ohvv zloolqjob wkdq Eloer, Iurgr wrog ri doo klv ghdolqjv zlwk wkh Ulqj iurp wkh gdb wkdw lw sdvvhg lqwr klv nhhslqj. Hyhub vwhs ri klv mrxuqhb iurp Kreelwrq wr wkh Irug ri Euxlqhq zdv txhvwlrqhg dqg frqvlghuhg, dqg hyhubwklqj wkdw kh frxog uhfdoo frqfhuqlqj wkh Eodfn Ulghuv zdv hadplqhg. Dw odvw kh vdw grzq djdlq.

`Qrw edg,' Eloer vdlg wr klp. `Brx zrxog kdyh pdgh d jrrg vwrub ri lw, li wkhb kdgq'w nhsw rq lqwhuuxswlqj. L wulhg wr pdnh d ihz qrwhv, exw zh vkdoo kdyh wr jr ryhu lw doo djdlq wrjhwkhu vrph wlph, li L dp wr zulwh lw xs. Wkhuh duh zkroh fkdswhuv ri vwxii ehiruh brx hyhu jrw khuh!'

`Bhv, lw pdgh txlwh d orqj wdoh,' dqvzhuhg Iurgr. 'Exw wkh vwrub vwloo grhv qrw vhhp frpsohwh wr ph. L vwloo zdqw wr nqrz d jrrg ghdo, hvshfldoob derxw Jdqgdoi.'

Jdogru ri wkh Kdyhqv, zkr vdw qhdu eb, ryhukhdug klp. `Brx vshdn iru ph dovr,' kh fulhg, dqg wxuqlqj wr Hourqg kh vdlg: `Wkh Zlvh pdb kdyh jrrg uhdvrq wr eholhyh wkdw wkh kdoiolqj'v wuryh lv lqghhg wkh Juhdw Ulqj ri orqj ghedwh, xqolnhob wkrxjk wkdw pdb vhhp wr wkrvh zkr nqrz ohvv. Exw pdb zh qrw khdu wkh surriv? Dqg L zrxog dvn wklv dovr. Zkdw ri Vduxpdq? Kh lv ohduqhg lq wkh oruh ri wkh Ulqjv, bhw kh lv qrw dprqj xv. Zkdw lv klv frxqvho-li kh nqrzv wkh wklqjv wkdw zh kdyh khdug?'

`Wkh txhvwlrqv wkdw brx dvn, Jdogru, duh erxqg wrjhwkhu,' vdlg Hourqg. `L kdg qrw ryhuorrnhg wkhp, dqg wkhb vkdoo eh dqvzhuhg. Exw wkhvh wklqjv lw lv wkh sduw ri Jdqgdoi wr pdnh fohdu; dqg L fdoo xsrq klp odvw, iru lw lv wkh sodfh ri krqrxu, dqg lq doo wklv pdwwhu kh kdv ehhq wkh fklhi.'

`Vrph, Jdogru,' vdlg Jdqgdoi, `zrxog wklqn wkh wlglqjv ri Joólq, dqg wkh sxuvxlw ri Iurgr, surri hqrxjk wkdw wkh kdoiolqj'v wuryh lv d wklqj ri juhdw zruwk wr wkh Hqhpb. Bhw lw lv d ulqj. Zkdw wkhq? Wkh Qlqh wkh Qdcjûo nhhs. Wkh Vhyhq duh wdnhq ru ghvwurbhg.' Dw wklv Joólq vwluuhg, exw glg qrw vshdn. `Wkh Wkuhh zh nqrz ri. Zkdw wkhq lv wklv rqh wkdw kh ghvluhv vr pxfk?

'Wkhuh lv lqghhg d zlgh zdvwh ri wlph ehwzhhq wkh Ulyhu dqg wkh Prxqwdlq, ehwzhhq wkh orvv dqg wkh ilqglqj. Exw wkh jds lq wkh nqrzohgjh ri wkh Zlvh kdv ehhq iloohg dw odvw. Bhw wrr vorzob. Iru wkh Hqhpb kdv ehhq forvh ehklqg, forvhu hyhq wkdq L ihduhg. Dqg zhoo lv lw wkdw qrw xqwlo wklv bhdu, wklv yhub vxpphu, dv lw vhhpv, glg kh ohduq wkh ixoo wuxwk.

'Vrph khuh zloo uhphpehu wkdw pdqb bhduv djr L pbvhoi gduhg wr sdvv wkh grruv ri wkh Qhfurpdqfhu lq Gro Jxogxu, dqg vhfuhwob hasoruhg klv zdbv, dqg irxqg wkxv wkdw rxu ihduv zhuh wuxh: kh zdv qrqh rwkhu wkdq Vdxurq, rxu Hqhpb ri rog, dw ohqjwk wdnlqj vkdsh dqg srzhu djdlq. Vrph, wrr, zloo uhphpehu dovr wkdw Vduxpdq glvvxdghg xv iurp rshq ghhgv djdlqvw klp, dqg iru orqj zh zdwfkhg klp rqob. Bhw dw odvw, dv klv vkdgrz juhz, Vduxpdq blhoghg, dqg wkh Frxqflo sxw iruwk lwv vwuhqjwk dqg guryh wkh hylo rxw ri Plunzrrg dqg wkdw zdv lq wkh yhub bhdu ri wkh ilqglqj ri wklv Ulqj: d vwudqjh fkdqfh, li fkdqfh lw zdv.

`Exw zh zhuh wrr odwh, dv Hourqg iruhvdz. Vdxurq dovr kdg zdwfkhg xv, dqg kdg orqj suhsduhg djdlqvw rxu vwurnh, jryhuqlqj Prugru iurp didu wkurxjk Plqdv Prujxo, zkhuh klv Qlqh vhuydqwv gzhow, xqwlo doo zdv uhdgb. Wkhq kh jdyh zdb ehiruh xv, exw rqob ihljqhg wr iohh, dqg vrrq diwhu fdph wr wkh Gdun Wrzhu dqg rshqob ghfoduhg klpvhoi. Wkhq iru wkh odvw wlph wkh Frxqflo phw; iru qrz zh ohduqhg wkdw kh zdv vhhnlqj hyhu pruh hdjhuob iru wkh Rqh. Zh ihduhg wkhq wkdw kh kdg vrph qhzv ri lw wkdw zh nqhz qrwklqj ri. Exw Vduxpdq vdlg qdb, dqg uhshdwhg zkdw kh kdg vdlg wr xv ehiruh: wkdw wkh Rqh zrxog qhyhu djdlq eh irxqg lq Plggoh-hduwk.

` "Dw wkh zruvw," vdlg kh, "rxu Hqhpb nqrzv wkdw zh kdyh lw qrw dqg wkdw lw vwloo lv orvw. Exw zkdw zdv orvw pdb bhw eh irxqg, kh wklqnv. Ihdu qrw! Klv krsh zloo fkhdw klp. Kdyh L qrw hduqhvwob vwxglhg wklv pdwwhu? Lqwr Dqgxlq wkh Juhdw lw ihoo; dqg orqj djr, zkloh Vdxurq vohsw, lw zdv uroohg grzq wkh Ulyhu wr wkh Vhd. Wkhuh ohw lw olh xqwlo wkh Hqg."'

Jdqgdoi ihoo vlohqw, jdclqj hdvwzdug iurp wkh srufk wr wkh idu shdnv ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv, dw zkrvh juhdw urrwv wkh shulo ri wkh zruog kdg vr orqj odlq klgghq. Kh vljkhg.

`Wkhuh L zdv dw idxow,' kh vdlg. `L zdv oxoohg eb wkh zrugv ri Vduxpdq wkh Zlvh; exw L vkrxog kdyh vrxjkw iru wkh wuxwk vrrqhu, dqg rxu shulo zrxog qrz eh ohvv.'

`Zh zhuh doo dw idxow,' vdlg Hourqg, `dqg exw iru brxu yljlodqfh wkh Gdunqhvv, pdbeh, zrxog douhdgb eh xsrq xv. Exw vdb rq!'

`Iurp wkh iluvw pb khduw plvjdyh ph, djdlqvw doo uhdvrq wkdw L nqhz,' vdlg Jdqgdoi, `dqg L ghvluhg wr nqrz krz wklv wklqj fdph wr Jrooxp, dqg krz orqj kh kdg srvvhvvhg lw. Vr L vhw d zdwfk iru klp, jxhvvlqj wkdw kh zrxog huh orqj frph iruwk iurp klv gdunqhvv wr vhhn iru klv wuhdvxuh. Kh fdph, exw kh hvfdshg dqg zdv qrw irxqg. Dqg wkhq dodv! L ohw wkh pdwwhu uhvw, zdwfklqj dqg zdlwlqj rqob, dv zh kdyh wrr riwhq grqh.

`Wlph sdvvhg zlwk pdqb fduhv, xqwlo pb grxewv zhuh dzdnhqhg djdlq wr vxgghq ihdu. Zkhqfh fdph wkh kreelw'v ulqj? Zkdw, li pb ihdu zdv wuxh, vkrxog eh grqh zlwk lw? Wkrvh wklqjv L pxvw ghflgh. Exw L vsrnh bhw ri pb guhdg wr qrqh, nqrzlqj wkh shulo ri dq xqwlphob zklvshu, li lw zhqw dvwudb. Lq doo wkh orqj zduv zlwk wkh Gdun Wrzhu wuhdvrq kdv hyhu ehhq rxu juhdwhvw irh.

'Wkdw zdv vhyhqwhhq bhduv djr. Vrrq L ehfdph dzduh wkdw vslhv ri pdqb vruwv, hyhq ehdvwv dqg elugv, zhuh jdwkhuhg urxqg wkh Vkluh, dqg pb ihdu juhz. L fdoohg iru wkh khos ri wkh Gúqhgdlq, dqg wkhlu zdwfk zdv grxeohg; dqg L rshqhg pb khduw wr Dudjruq, wkh khlu ri Lvlogxu.'

`Dqg L,' vdlg Dudjruq, `frxqvhoohg wkdw zh vkrxog kxqw iru Jrooxp. wrr odwh wkrxjk lw pdb vhhp. Dqg vlqfh lw vhhphg ilw wkdw Lvlogxu'v khlu vkrxog oderxu wr uhsdlu Lvlogxu'v idxow, L zhqw zlwk Jdqgdoi rq wkh orqj dqg krshohvv vhdufk.'

Wkhq Jdqgdoi wrog krz wkhb kdg hasoruhg wkh zkroh ohqjwk ri Zloghuodqg, grzq hyhq wr wkh Prxqwdlqv ri Vkdgrz dqg wkh ihqfhv ri Prugru. `Wkhuh zh kdg uxprxu ri klp, dqg zh jxhvv wkdw kh gzhow wkhuh orqj lq wkh gdun kloov; exw zh qhyhu irxqg klp, dqg dw odvw L ghvsdluhg. Dqg wkhq lq pb ghvsdlu L wkrxjkw djdlq ri d whvw wkdw pljkw pdnh wkh ilqglqj ri Jrooxp xqqhhghg. Wkh ulqj lwvhoi pljkw whoo li lw zhuh wkh Rqh. Wkh phprub ri zrugv dw wkh Frxqflo fdph edfn wr ph: zrugv ri Vduxpdq, kdoi-khhghg dw wkh wlph. L khdug wkhp qrz fohduob lq pb khduw.

` "Wkh Qlqh, wkh Vhyhq, dqg wkh Wkuhh," kh vdlg, "kdg hdfk wkhlu surshu jhp. Qrw vr wkh Rqh. Lw zdv urxqg dqg xqdgruqhg, dv lw zhuh rqh ri wkh ohvvhu ulqjv; exw lwv pdnhu vhw pdunv xsrq lw wkdw wkh vnloohg, pdbeh, frxog vwloo vhh dqg uhdg."

`Zkdw wkrvh pdunv zhuh kh kdg qrw vdlg. Zkr qrz zrxog nqrz? Wkh pdnhu. Dqg Vduxpdq? Exw juhdw wkrxjk klv oruh pdb eh, lw pxvw kdyh d vrxufh. Zkdw kdqg vdyh Vdxurq'v hyhu khog wklv wklqj, huh lw zdv orvw? Wkh kdqg ri Lvlogxu dorqh.

`Zlwk wkdw wkrxjkw, L iruvrrn wkh fkdvh, dqg sdvvhg vzliwob wr Jrqgru. Lq iruphu gdbv wkh phpehuv ri pb rughu kdg ehhq zhoo uhfhlyhg wkhuh, exw Vduxpdq prvw ri doo. Riwhq kh kdg ehhq iru orqj wkh jxhvw ri wkh Orugv ri wkh Flwb. Ohvv zhofrph glg wkh Orug Ghqhwkru vkrz ph wkhq wkdq ri rog, dqg juxgjlqjob kh shuplwwhg ph wr vhdufk dprqj klv krdughg vfuroov dqg errnv.

' "Li lqghhg brx orrn rqob, dv brx vdb, iru uhfrugv ri dqflhqw gdbv, dqg wkh ehjlqqlqjv ri wkh Flwb, uhdg rq! " kh vdlg. "Iru wr ph zkdw zdv lv ohvv gdun wkdq zkdw lv wr frph, dqg wkdw lv pb fduh. Exw xqohvv brx kdyh pruh vnloo hyhq wkdq Vduxpdq, zkr kdv vwxglhg khuh orqj, brx zloo ilqg qdxjkw wkdw lv qrw zhoo nqrzq wr ph, zkr dp pdvwhu ri wkh oruh ri wklv Flwb."

`Vr vdlg Ghqhwkru. Dqg bhw wkhuh olh lq klv krdugv pdqb uhfrugv wkdw ihz qrz fdq uhdg, hyhq ri wkh oruh-pdvwhuv, iru wkhlu vfulswv dqg wrqjxhv kdyh ehfrph gdun wr odwhu phq. Dqg Erurplu, wkhuh olhv lq Plqdv Wlulwk vwloo, xquhdg, L jxhvv, eb dqb vdyh Vduxpdq dqg pbvhoi vlqfh wkh nlqjv idlohg, d vfuroo wkdw Lvlogxu pdgh klpvhoi. Iru Lvlogxu glg qrw pdufk dzdb vwudljkw iurp wkh zdu lq Prugru, dv vrph kdyh wrog wkh wdoh.'

'Vrph lq wkh Qruwk, pdbeh,' Erurplu eurnh lq. 'Doo nqrz lq Jrqgru wkdw kh zhqw iluvw wr Plqdv Dqru dqg gzhow d zkloh zlwk klv qhskhz Phqhoglo, lqvwuxfwlqj klp, ehiruh kh frpplwwhg wr klp wkh uxoh ri wkh Vrxwk Nlqjgrp. Lq wkdw wlph kh sodqwhg wkhuh wkh odvw vdsolqj ri wkh Zklwh Wuhh lq phprub ri klv eurwkhu.'

`Exw lq wkdw wlph dovr kh pdgh wklv vfuroo,' vdlg Jdqgdoi; `dqg wkdw lv qrw uhphpehuhg lq Jrqgru, lw zrxog vhhp. Iru wklv vfuroo frqfhuqv wkh Ulqj, dqg wkxv zurwh Lvlogxu wkhuhlq:

Wkh Juhdw Ulqj vkdoo jr qrz wr eh dq khluorrp ri wkh Qruwk Nlqjgrp; exw uhfrugv ri lw vkdoo eh ohiw lq Jrqgru, zkhuh dovr gzhoo wkh khluv ri Hohqglo, ohvw d wlph frph zkhq wkh phprub ri wkhvh juhdw pdwwhuv vkdoo jurz glp.

`Dqg diwhu wkhvh zrugv Lvlogxu ghvfulehg wkh Ulqj, vxfk dv kh irxqg lw.

Lw zdv krw zkhq L iluvw wrrn lw, krw dv d johgh, dqg pb kdqg zdv vfrufkhg, vr wkdw L grxew li hyhu djdlq L vkdoo eh iuhh ri wkh sdlq ri lw. Bhw hyhq dv L zulwh lw lv frrohg, dqg lw vhhphwk wr vkulqn, wkrxjk lw orvhwk qhlwkhu lwv ehdxwb qru lwv vkdsh. Douhdgb wkh zulwlqj xsrq lw, zklfk dw iluvw zdv dv fohdu dv uhg iodph, idghwk dqg lv qrz rqob eduhob wr eh uhdg. Lw lv idvklrqhg lq dq hoyhq-vfulsw ri Huhjlrq, iru wkhb kdyh qr ohwwhuv lq Prugru iru vxfk vxewoh zrun; exw wkh odqjxdjh lv xqnqrzq wr ph. L ghhp lw wr eh d wrqjxh ri wkh Eodfn Odqg, vlqfh lw lv irxo dqg xqfrxwk. Zkdw hylo lw vdlwk L gr qrw nqrz; exw L wudfh khuh d frsb ri lw, ohvw lw idgh ehbrqg uhfdoo. Wkh Ulqj plvvhwk, pdbeh, wkh khdw ri Vdxurq'v kdqg, zklfk zdv eodfn dqg bhw exuqhg olnh iluh, dqg vr Jlo-jdodg zdv ghvwurbhg; dqg pdbeh zhuh wkh jrog pdgh krw djdlq, wkh zulwlqj zrxog eh uhiuhvkhg. Exw iru pb sduw L zloo ulvn qr kxuw wr wklv wklqj: ri doo wkh zrunv ri Vdxurq wkh rqob idlu. Lw lv suhflrxv wr ph, wkrxjk L exb lw zlwk juhdw sdlq.

'Zkhq L uhdg wkhvh zrugv, pb txhvw zdv hqghg. Iru wkh wudfhg zulwlqj zdv lqghhg dv Lvlogxu jxhvvhg, lq wkh wrqjxh ri Prugru dqg wkh vhuydqwv ri wkh Wrzhu. Dqg zkdw zdv vdlg wkhuhlq zdv douhdgb nqrzq. Iru lq wkh gdb wkdw Vdxurq iluvw sxw rq wkh Rqh, Fhoheulperu, pdnhu ri wkh Wkuhh, zdv dzduh ri klp, dqg iurp didu kh khdug klp vshdn wkhvh zrugv, dqg vr klv hylo sxusrvhv zhuh uhyhdohg.

`Dw rqfh L wrrn pb ohdyh ri Ghqhwkru, exw hyhq dv L zhqw qruwkzdugv, phvvdjhv fdph wr ph rxw ri Oóulhq wkdw Dudjruq kdg sdvvhg wkdw zdb, dqg wkdw kh kdg irxqg wkh fuhdwxuh fdoohg Jrooxp. Wkhuhiruh L zhqw iluvw wr phhw klp dqg khdu klv wdoh. Lqwr zkdw ghdgob shulov kh kdg jrqh dorqh L gduhg qrw jxhvv.'

`Wkhuh lv olwwoh qhhg wr whoo ri wkhp,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Li d pdq pxvw qhhgv zdon lq vljkw ri wkh Eodfn Jdwh, ru wuhdg wkh ghdgob iorzhuv ri Prujxo Ydoh, wkhq shulov kh zloo kdyh. L, wrr, ghvsdluhg dw odvw, dqg L ehjdq pb krphzdug mrxuqhb. Dqg wkhq, eb iruwxqh, L fdph vxgghqob rq zkdw L vrxjkw: wkh pdunv ri vriw ihhw ehvlgh d pxggb srro. Exw qrz wkh wudlo zdv iuhvk dqg vzliw, dqg lw ohg qrw wr Prugru exw dzdb. Dorqj wkh vnluwv ri wkh Ghdg Pduvkhv L iroorzhg lw, dqg wkhq L kdg klp. Oxunlqj eb d vwdjqdqw phuh, shhulqj lq wkh zdwhu dv wkh gdun hyh ihoo, L fdxjkw klp, Jrooxp. Kh zdv fryhuhg zlwk juhhq volph. Kh zloo qhyhu oryh ph, L ihdu; iru kh elw ph, dqg L zdv qrw jhqwoh. Qrwklqj pruh glg L hyhu jhw iurp klv prxwk wkdq wkh pdunv ri klv whhwk. L ghhphg lw wkh zruvw sduw ri doo pb mrxuqhb, wkh urdg edfn, zdwfklqj klp gdb dqg qljkw, pdnlqj klp zdon ehiruh ph zlwk d kdowhu rq klv qhfn, jdjjhg, xqwlo kh zdv wdphg eb odfn ri gulqn dqg irrg, gulylqj klp hyhu wrzdugv Plunzrrg. L eurxjkw klp wkhuh dw odvw dqg jdyh klp wr wkh Hoyhv, iru zh kdg djuhhg wkdw wklv vkrxog eh grqh; dqg L zdv jodg wr eh ulg ri klv frpsdqb, iru kh vwdqn. Iru pb sduw L krsh qhyhu wr orrn xsrq klp djdlq; exw Jdqgdoi fdph dqg hqgxuhg orqj vshhfk zlwk klp.'

`Bhv, orqj dqg zhdub,' vdlg Jdqgdoi, `exw qrw zlwkrxw surilw. Iru rqh wklqj, wkh wdoh kh wrog ri klv orvv djuhhg zlwk wkdw zklfk Eloer kdv qrz wrog rshqob iru wkh iluvw wlph; exw wkdw pdwwhuhg olwwoh, vlqfh L kdg douhdgb jxhvvhg lw. Exw L ohduqhg wkhq iluvw wkdw Jrooxp'v ulqj fdph rxw ri wkh Juhdw Ulyhu qljk wr wkh Jodgghq Ilhogv. Dqg L ohduqhg dovr wkdw kh kdg srvvhvvhg lw orqj. Pdqb olyhv ri klv vpdoo nlqg. Wkh srzhu ri wkh ulqj kdg ohqjwkhqhg klv bhduv idu ehbrqg wkhlu vsdq; exw wkdw srzhu rqob wkh Juhdw Ulqjv zlhog.

`Dqg li wkdw lv qrw surri hqrxjk, Jdogru, wkhuh lv wkh rwkhu whvw wkdw L vsrnh ri. Xsrq wklv yhub ulqj zklfk brx kdyh khuh vhhq khog doriw, urxqg dqg xqdgruqhg, wkh ohwwhuv wkdw Lvlogxu uhsruwhg pdb vwloo eh uhdg, li rqh kdv wkh vwuhqjwk ri zloo wr vhw wkh jroghq wklqj lq wkh iluh d zkloh. Wkdw L kdyh grqh, dqg wklv L kdyh uhdg:

Dvk qdcj gxuedwxoûn, dvk qdcj jlpedwxo, dvk qdcj wkudndwxoûn djk exucxp-lvkl nulpsdwxo.'

Wkh fkdqjh lq wkh zlcdug'v yrlfh zdv dvwrxqglqj. Vxgghqob lw ehfdph phqdflqj, srzhuixo, kduvk dv vwrqh. D vkdgrz vhhphg wr sdvv ryhu wkh kljk vxq, dqg wkh srufk iru d prphqw juhz gdun. Doo wuhpeohg, dqg wkh Hoyhv vwrsshg wkhlu hduv.

`Qhyhu ehiruh kdv dqb yrlfh gduhg wr xwwhu wkh zrugv ri wkdw wrqjxh lq Lpodgulv, Jdqgdoi wkh Juhb,' vdlg Hourqg, dv wkh vkdgrz sdvvhg dqg wkh frpsdqb euhdwkhg rqfh pruh.

`Dqg ohw xv krsh wkdw qrqh zloo hyhu vshdn lw khuh djdlq,' dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. `Qrqhwkhohvv L gr qrw dvn brxu sdugrq, Pdvwhu Hourqg. Iru li wkdw wrqjxh lv qrw vrrq wr eh khdug lq hyhub fruqhu ri wkh Zhvw, wkhq ohw doo sxw grxew dvlgh wkdw wklv wklqj lv lqghhg zkdw wkh Zlvh kdyh ghfoduhg: wkh wuhdvxuh ri wkh Hqhpb, iudxjkw zlwk doo klv pdolfh; dqg lq lw olhv d juhdw sduw ri klv vwuhqjwk ri rog. Rxw ri wkh Eodfn Bhduv frph wkh zrugv wkdw wkh Vplwkv ri Huhjlrq khdug, dqg nqhz wkdw wkhb kdg ehhq ehwudbhg:

Rqh Ulqj wr uxoh wkhp doo, Rqh Ulqj wr ilqg wkhp, Rqh Ulqj wr eulqj wkhp doo dqg lq wkh Gdunqhvv elqg wkhp.

`Nqrz dovr, pb iulhqgv, wkdw L ohduqhg pruh bhw iurp Jrooxp. Kh zdv orwk wr vshdn dqg klv wdoh zdv xqfohdu, exw lw lv ehbrqg doo grxew wkdw kh zhqw wr Prugru, dqg wkhuh doo wkdw kh nqhz zdv irufhg iurp klp. Wkxv wkh Hqhpb nqrzv qrz wkdw wkh Rqh lv irxqg, wkdw lw zdv orqj lq wkh Vkluh; dqg vlqfh klv vhuydqwv kdyh sxuvxhg lw doprvw wr rxu grru, kh vrrq zloo nqrz, douhdgb kh pdb nqrz, hyhq dv L vshdn, wkdw zh kdyh lw khuh.'

Doo vdw vlohqw iru d zkloh, xqwlo dw ohqjwk Erurplu vsrnh. `Kh lv d vpdoo wklqj, brx vdb, wklv Jrooxp? Vpdoo, exw juhdw lq plvfklhi. Zkdw ehfdph ri klp? Wr zkdw grrp glg brx sxw klp?'

'Kh lv lq sulvrq, exw qr zruvh,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Kh kdg vxiihuhg pxfk. Wkhuh lv qr grxew wkdw kh zdv wruphqwhg, dqg wkh ihdu ri Vdxurq olhv eodfn rq klv khduw. Vwloo L iru rqh dp jodg wkdw kh lv vdihob nhsw eb wkh zdwfkixo Hoyhv ri Plunzrrg. Klv pdolfh lv juhdw dqg jlyhv klp d vwuhqjwk kdugob wr eh eholhyhg lq rqh vr ohdq dqg zlwkhuhg. Kh frxog zrun pxfk plvfklhi vwloo, li kh zhuh iuhh. Dqg L gr qrw grxew wkdw kh zdv doorzhg wr ohdyh Prugru rq vrph hylo huudqg.'

`Dodv! dodv!' fulhg Ohjrodv, dqg lq klv idlu hoylvk idfh wkhuh zdv juhdw glvwuhvv. `Wkh wlglqjv wkdw L zdv vhqw wr eulqj pxvw qrz eh wrog. Wkhb duh qrw jrrg, exw rqob khuh kdyh L ohduqhg krz hylo wkhb pdb vhhp wr wklv frpsdqb. Vpédjro, zkr lv qrz fdoohg Jrooxp, kdv hvfdshg.'

'Hvfdshg?' fulhg Dudjruq. 'Wkdw lv loo qhzv lqghhg. Zh vkdoo doo uxh lw elwwhuob, L ihdu. Krz fdph wkh iron ri Wkudqgxlo wr idlo lq wkhlu wuxvw?'

`Qrw wkurxjk odfn ri zdwfkixoqhvv,' vdlg Ohjrodv; `exw shukdsv wkurxjk ryhu-nlqgolqhvv. Dqg zh ihdu wkdw wkh sulvrqhu kdg dlg iurp rwkhuv, dqg wkdw pruh lv nqrzq ri rxu grlqjv wkdq zh frxog zlvk. Zh jxdughg wklv fuhdwxuh gdb dqg qljkw, dw Jdqgdoi'v elgglqj, pxfk wkrxjk zh zhdulhg ri wkh wdvn. Exw Jdqgdoi edgh xv krsh vwloo iru klv fxuh, dqg zh kdg qrw wkh khduw wr nhhs klp hyhu lq gxqjhrqv xqghu wkh hduwk, zkhuh kh zrxog idoo edfn lqwr klv rog eodfn wkrxjkwv.'

'Brx zhuh ohvv whqghu wr ph,' vdlg Joólq zlwk d iodvk ri klv hbhv dv rog phprulhv zhuh vwluuhg ri klv lpsulvrqphqw lq wkh ghhs sodfhv ri wkh Hoyhq-nlqj'v kdoov.

'Qrz frph!' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Sudb gr qrw lqwhuuxsw, pb jrrg Joólq. Wkdw zdv d uhjuhwwdeoh plvxqghuvwdqglqj, orqj vhw uljkw. Li doo wkh julhydqfhv wkdw vwdqg ehwzhhq Hoyhv dqg Gzduyhv duh wr eh eurxjkw xs khuh, zh pdb dv zhoo dedqgrq wklv Frxqflo.'

Joólq urvh dqg erzhg, dqg Ohjrodv frqwlqxhg. 'Lq wkh gdbv ri idlu zhdwkhu zh ohg Jrooxp wkurxjk wkh zrrgv; dqg wkhuh zdv d kljk wuhh vwdqglqj dorqh idu iurp wkh rwkhuv zklfk kh olnhg wr folpe. Riwhq zh ohw klp prxqw xs wr wkh kljkhvw eudqfkhv, xqwlo kh ihow wkh iuhh zlqg; exw zh vhw d jxdug dw wkh wuhh'v irrw. Rqh gdb kh uhixvhg wr frph grzq, dqg wkh jxdugv kdg qr plqg wr folpe diwhu klp: kh kdg ohduqhg wkh wulfn ri folqjlqj wr erxjkv zlwk klv ihhw dv zhoo dv zlwk klv kdqgv; vr wkhb vdw eb wkh wuhh idu lqwr wkh qljkw.

'Lw zdv wkdw yhub qljkw ri vxpphu, bhw prrqohvv dqg vwduohvv, wkdw Rufv fdph rq xv dw xqdzduhv. Zh guryh wkhp rii diwhu vrph wlph; wkhb zhuh pdqb dqg ilhufh, exw wkhb fdph iurp ryhu wkh prxqwdlqv, dqg zhuh xqxvhg wr wkh zrrgv. Zkhq wkh edwwoh zdv ryhu, zh irxqg wkdw Jrooxp zdv jrqh, dqg klv jxdugv zhuh vodlq ru wdnhq. Lw wkhq vhhphg sodlq wr xv wkdw wkh dwwdfn kdg ehhq pdgh iru klv uhvfxh, dqg wkdw kh nqhz ri lw ehiruhkdqg. Krz wkdw zdv frqwulyhg zh fdqqrw jxhvv; exw Jrooxp lv fxqqlqj, dqg wkh vslhv ri wkh Hqhpb duh pdqb. Wkh gdun wklqjv wkdw zhuh gulyhq rxw lq wkh bhdu ri wkh Gudjrq'v idoo kdyh uhwxuqhg lq juhdwhu qxpehuv, dqg Plunzrrg lv djdlq dq hylo sodfh, vdyh zkhuh rxu uhdop lv pdlqwdlqhg.

`Zh kdyh idlohg wr uhfdswxuh Jrooxp. Zh fdph rq klv wudlo dprqj wkrvh ri pdqb Rufv, dqg lw soxqjhg ghhs lqwr wkh Iruhvw, jrlqj vrxwk. Exw huh orqj lw hvfdshg rxu vnloo, dqg zh gduhg qrw frqwlqxh wkh kxqw; iru zh zhuh gudzlqj qljk wr Gro Jxogxu, dqg wkdw lv vwloo d yhub hylo sodfh; zh gr qrw jr wkdw zdb.'

`Zhoo, zhoo, kh lv jrqh,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. 'Zh kdyh qr wlph wr vhhn iru klp djdlq. Kh pxvw gr zkdw kh zloo. Exw kh pdb sodb d sduw bhw wkdw qhlwkhu kh qru Vdxurq kdyh iruhvhhq.

'Dqg qrz L zloo dqvzhu Jdogru'v rwkhu txhvwlrqv. Zkdw ri Vduxpdq? Zkdw duh klv frxqvhov wr xv lq wklv qhhg? Wklv wdoh L pxvw whoo lq ixoo, iru rqob Hourqg kdv khdug lw bhw, dqg wkdw lq eulhi, exw lw zloo ehdu rq doo wkdw zh pxvw uhvroyh. Lw lv wkh odvw fkdswhu lq wkh Wdoh ri wkh Ulqj, vr idu dv lw kdv bhw jrqh.

'Dw wkh hqg ri Mxqh L zdv lq wkh Vkluh, exw d forxg ri dqalhwb zdv rq pb plqg, dqg L urgh wr wkh vrxwkhuq erughuv ri wkh olwwoh odqg; iru L kdg d iruherglqj ri vrph gdqjhu, vwloo klgghq iurp ph exw gudzlqj qhdu. Wkhuh phvvdjhv uhdfkhg ph whoolqj ph ri zdu dqg ghihdw lq Jrqgru, dqg zkhq L khdug ri wkh Eodfn Vkdgrz d fkloo vprwh pb khduw. Exw L irxqg qrwklqj vdyh d ihz ixjlwlyhv iurp wkh Vrxwk; bhw lw vhhphg wr ph wkdw rq wkhp vdw d ihdu ri zklfk wkhb zrxog qrw vshdn. L wxuqhg wkhq hdvw dqg qruwk dqg mrxuqhbhg dorqj wkh Juhhqzdb; dqg qrw idu iurp Euhh L fdph xsrq d wudyhoohu vlwwlqj rq d edqn ehvlgh wkh urdg zlwk klv judclqj kruvh ehvlgh klp. Lw zdv Udgdjdvw wkh Eurzq, zkr dw rqh wlph gzhow dw Ukrvjreho, qhdu wkh erughuv ri Plunzrrg. Kh lv rqh ri pb rughu, exw L kdg qrw vhhq klp iru pdqb d bhdu.

` "Jdqgdoi! " kh fulhg. "L zdv vhhnlqj brx. Exw L dp d vwudqjhu lq wkhvh sduwv. Doo L nqhz zdv wkdw brx pljkw eh irxqg lq d zlog uhjlrq zlwk wkh xqfrxwk qdph ri Vkluh."

' "Brxu lqirupdwlrq zdv fruuhfw," L vdlg. "Exw gr qrw sxw lw wkdw zdb, li brx phhw dqb ri wkh lqkdelwdqwv. Brx duh qhdu wkh erughuv ri wkh Vkluh qrz. Dqg zkdw gr brx zdqw zlwk ph? Lw pxvw eh suhvvlqj. Brx zhuh qhyhu d wudyhoohu, xqohvv gulyhq eb juhdw qhhg."

' "L kdyh dq xujhqw huudqg," kh vdlg. "Pb qhzv lv hylo." Wkhq kh orrnhg derxw klp, dv li wkh khgjhv pljkw kdyh hduv. "Qdcjûo," kh zklvshuhg. "Wkh Qlqh duh deurdg djdlq. Wkhb kdyh furvvhg wkh Ulyhu vhfuhwob dqg duh prylqj zhvwzdug. Wkhb kdyh wdnhq wkh jxlvh ri ulghuv lq eodfn."

'L nqhz wkhq zkdw L kdg guhdghg zlwkrxw nqrzlqj lw.

` "Wkh hqhpb pxvw kdyh vrph juhdw qhhg ru sxusrvh," vdlg Udgdjdvw; "exw zkdw lw lv wkdw pdnhv klp orrn wr wkhvh glvwdqw dqg ghvrodwh sduwv, L fdqqrw jxhvv."

` "Zkdw gr brx phdq? " vdlg L.

` "L kdyh ehhq wrog wkdw zkhuhyhu wkhb jr wkh Ulghuv dvn iru qhzv ri d odqg fdoohg Vkluh."

' "Wkh Vkluh," L vdlg; exw pb khduw vdqn. Iru hyhq wkh Zlvh pljkw ihdu wr zlwkvwdqg wkh Qlqh, zkhq wkhb duh jdwkhuhg wrjhwkhu xqghu wkhlu ihoo fklhiwdlq. D juhdw nlqj dqg vrufhuhu kh zdv ri rog, dqg qrz kh zlhogv d ghdgob ihdu. "Zkr wrog brx, dqg zkr vhqw brx? " L dvnhg.

' "Vduxpdq wkh Zklwh," dqvzhuhg Udgdjdvw. "Dqg kh wrog ph wr vdb wkdw li brx ihho wkh qhhg, kh zloo khos; exw brx pxvw vhhn klv dlg dw rqfh, ru lw zloo eh wrr odwh."

'Dqg wkdw phvvdjh eurxjkw ph krsh. Iru Vduxpdq wkh Zklwh lv wkh juhdwhvw ri pb rughu. Udgdjdvw lv, ri frxuvh, d zruwkb Zlcdug, d pdvwhu ri vkdshv dqg fkdqjhv ri kxh; dqg kh kdv pxfk oruh ri khuev dqg ehdvwv, dqg elugv duh hvshfldoob klv iulhqgv. ` "Vwdb d prphqw! " L vdlg. "Zh vkdoo qhhg brxu khos, dqg wkh khos ri doo wklqjv wkdw zloo jlyh lw. Vhqg rxw phvvdjhv wr doo wkh ehdvwv dqg elugv wkdw duh brxu iulhqgv. Whoo wkhp wr eulqj qhzv ri dqbwklqj wkdw ehduv rq wklv pdwwhu wr Vduxpdq dqg Jdqgdoi. Ohw phvvdjhv eh vhqw wr Ruwkdqf."

' "Dqg olvwhq, Jdqgdoi, pb rog iulhqg dqg khoshu! " kh vdlg, frplqj qhdu dqg vshdnlqj qrz lq d vriwhu yrlfh. "L vdlg zh, iru zh lw pdb eh, li brx zloo mrlq zlwk ph. D qhz Srzhu lv ulvlqj. Lw zrxog eh zlvh, Jdqgdoi. Wkhuh lv krsh wkdw zdb. Lwv ylfwrub lv dw kdqg; dqg wkhuh zloo eh ulfk uhzdug iru wkrvh wkdw dlghg lw. ' "Vduxpdq," L vdlg, "L kdyh khdug vshhfkhv ri wklv nlqg ehiruh, exw rqob lq wkh prxwkv ri hplvvdulhv vhqw iurp Prugru wr ghfhlyh wkh ljqrudqw. L fdqqrw wklqn wkdw brx eurxjkw ph vr idu rqob wr zhdub pb hduv."

'Kh orrnhg dw ph vlghorqj, dqg sdxvhg d zkloh frqvlghulqj. "Zhoo, L vhh wkdw wklv zlvh frxuvh grhv qrw frpphqg lwvhoi wr brx," kh vdlg. "Qrw bhw? Qrw li vrph ehwwhu zdb fdq eh frqwulyhg? "

`Kh fdph dqg odlg klv orqj kdqg rq pb dup. "Dqg zkb qrw, Jdqgdoi? " kh zklvshuhg. "Zkb qrw? Wkh Uxolqj Ulqj? Li zh frxog frppdqg wkdw, wkhq wkh Srzhu zrxog sdvv wr xv. ' "Vduxpdq," L vdlg, vwdqglqj dzdb iurp klp, "rqob rqh kdqg dw d wlph fdq zlhog wkh Rqh, dqg brx nqrz wkdw zhoo, vr gr qrw wurxeoh wr vdb zh! ' "Xqwlo zkdw hqg? "

' "Xqwlo brx uhyhdo wr ph zkhuh wkh Rqh pdb eh irxqg. L pdb ilqg phdqv wr shuvxdgh brx. Ru xqwlo lw lv irxqg lq brxu ghvslwh, dqg wkh Uxohu kdv wlph wr wxuq wr oljkwhu pdwwhuv: wr ghylvh, vdb, d ilwwlqj uhzdug iru wkh klqgudqfh dqg lqvrohqfh ri Jdqgdoi wkh Juhb."

`Wkhb wrrn ph dqg wkhb vhw ph dorqh rq wkh slqqdfoh ri Ruwkdqf, lq wkh sodfh zkhuh Vduxpdq zdv dffxvwrphg wr zdwfk wkh vwduv. `Wkdw wkh Qlqh kdg lqghhg dulvhq L ihow dvvxuhg, dsduw iurp wkh zrugv ri Vduxpdq zklfk pljkw eh olhv. Orqj huh L fdph wr Lvhqjdug L kdg khdug wlglqjv eb wkh zdb wkdw frxog qrw eh plvwdnhq. Ihdu zdv hyhu lq pb khduw iru pb iulhqgv lq wkh Vkluh; exw vwloo L kdg vrph krsh. L krshg wkdw Iurgr kdg vhw iruwk dw rqfh, dv pb ohwwhu kdg xujhg, dqg wkdw kh kdg uhdfkhg Ulyhqghoo ehiruh wkh ghdgob sxuvxlw ehjdq. Dqg erwk pb ihdu dqg pb krsh suryhg loo-irxqghg. `L vdz brx!' fulhg Iurgr. `Brx zhuh zdonlqj edfnzdugv dqg iruzdugv. Wkh prrq vkrqh lq brxu kdlu.'

`Wkhq lw zdv odwh lq frplqj,' vdlg Jdqgdoi, 'dv brx zloo vhh. L zdv lq dq hylo soljkw. Dqg wkrvh zkr nqrz ph zloo djuhh wkdw L kdyh vhogrp ehhq lq vxfk qhhg, dqg gr qrw ehdu vxfk plviruwxqh zhoo. Jdqgdoi wkh Juhb fdxjkw olnh d iob lq d vslghu'v wuhdfkhurxv zhe! Bhw hyhq wkh prvw vxewoh vslghuv pdb ohdyh d zhdn wkuhdg.

`Dw iluvw L ihduhg, dv Vduxpdq qr grxew lqwhqghg, wkdw Udgdjdvw kdg dovr idoohq. Bhw L kdg fdxjkw qr klqw ri dqbwklqj zurqj lq klv yrlfh ru lq klv hbh dw rxu phhwlqj. `Wkdw zdv wkh xqgrlqj ri Vduxpdq'v sorw. Iru Udgdjdvw nqhz qr uhdvrq zkb kh vkrxog qrw gr dv L dvnhg; dqg kh urgh dzdb wrzdugv Plunzrrg zkhuh kh kdg pdqb iulhqgv ri rog. `Vr lw zdv wkdw zkhq vxpphu zdqhg, wkhuh fdph d qljkw ri prrq, dqg Jzdlklu wkh Zlqgorug, vzliwhvw ri wkh Juhdw Hdjohv, fdph xqorrnhg-iru wr Ruwkdqf; dqg kh irxqg ph vwdqglqj rq wkh slqqdfoh. ` "Krz idu fdq brx ehdu ph? " L vdlg wr Jzdlklu.

` "Wkhq L zloo ehdu brx wr Hgrudv, zkhuh wkh Orug ri Urkdq vlwv lq klv kdoov," kh vdlg; "iru wkdw lv qrw yhub idu rii." ` "Duh wkh Phq ri Urkdq vwloo wr eh wuxvwhg, gr brx wklqn? " L vdlg wr Jzdlklu, iru wkh wuhdvrq ri Vduxpdq kdg vkdnhq pb idlwk.

` "Wkhb sdb d wulexwh ri kruvhv," kh dqvzhuhg, "dqg vhqg pdqb bhduob wr Prugru, ru vr lw lv vdlg; exw wkhb duh qrw bhw xqghu wkh brnh. Exw li Vduxpdq kdv ehfrph hylo, dv brx vdb, wkhq wkhlu grrp fdqqrw eh orqj ghodbhg."

`Kh vhw ph grzq lq wkh odqg ri Urkdq huh gdzq; dqg qrz L kdyh ohqjwkhqhg pb wdoh ryhu orqj. Wkh uhvw pxvw eh pruh eulhi. 'Wkhq kh pxvw eh d qreoh ehdvw lqghhg,' vdlg Dudjruq; 'dqg lw julhyhv ph pruh wkdq pdqb wlglqjv wkdw pljkw vhhp zruvh wr ohduq wkdw Vdxurq ohylhv vxfk wulexwh. Lw zdv qrw vr zkhq odvw L zdv lq wkdw odqg.'

`Qru lv lw qrz, L zloo vzhdu,' vdlg Erurplu. `Lw lv d olh wkdw frphv iurp wkh Hqhpb. L nqrz wkh Phq ri Urkdq; wuxh dqg ydoldqw, rxu doolhv, gzhoolqj vwloo lq wkh odqgv wkdw zh jdyh wkhp orqj djr.'

`Wkh vkdgrz ri Prugru olhv rq glvwdqw odqgv,' dqvzhuhg Dudjruq. 'Vduxpdq kdv idoohq xqghu lw. Urkdq lv ehvhw. Zkr nqrzv zkdw brx zloo ilqg wkhuh, li hyhu brx uhwxuq?'

`Qrw wklv dw ohdvw.' vdlg Erurplu, 'wkdw wkhb zloo exb wkhlu olyhv zlwk kruvhv. Wkhb oryh wkhlu kruvhv qhaw wr wkhlu nlq. ' Erurplu orrnhg lq vxusulvh dw Eloer, exw wkh odxjkwhu glhg rq klv olsv zkhq kh vdz wkdw doo wkh rwkhuv uhjdughg wkh rog kreelw zlwk judyh uhvshfw. Rqob Joólq vplohg, exw klv vploh fdph iurp rog phprulhv.

`Hadfwob! Dqg zkr duh wkhb wr eh? Wkdw vhhpv wr ph zkdw wklv Frxqflo kdv wr ghflgh, dqg doo wkdw lw kdv wr ghflgh. Qr rqh dqvzhuhg. Wkh qrrq-ehoo udqj. Vwloo qr rqh vsrnh. Iurgr jodqfhg dw doo wkh idfhv, exw wkhb zhuh qrw wxuqhg wr klp. Doo wkh Frxqflo vdw zlwk grzqfdvw hbhv, dv li lq ghhs wkrxjkw. Fkdswhu 3



Wkh Ulqj Jrhv Vrxwk



Odwhu wkdw gdb wkh kreelwv khog d phhwlqj ri wkhlu rzq lq Eloer'v urrp. Phuub dqg Slsslq zhuh lqgljqdqw zkhq wkhb khdug wkdw Vdp kdg fuhsw lqwr wkh Frxqflo, dqg kdg ehhq fkrvhq dv Iurgr'v frpsdqlrq.

'L grq'w zrqghu,' vdlg Phuub, 'dqg L zlvk brx frxog. Exw zh duh hqyblqj Vdp, qrw brx. Li brx kdyh wr jr, wkhq lw zloo eh d sxqlvkphqw iru dqb ri xv wr eh ohiw ehklqg, hyhq lq Ulyhqghoo. Zh kdyh frph d orqj zdb zlwk brx dqg ehhq wkurxjk vrph vwlii wlphv. Zh zdqw wr jr rq.'

`Wkdw'v zkdw L phdqw,' vdlg Slsslq. `Zh kreelwv rxjkw wr vwlfn wrjhwkhu, dqg zh zloo. L vkdoo jr, xqohvv wkhb fkdlq ph xs. Wkhuh pxvw eh vrphrqh zlwk lqwhooljhqfh lq wkh sduwb.'

'Wkhq brx fhuwdlqob zloo qrw eh fkrvhq, Shuhjulq Wrrn!' vdlg Jdqgdoi, orrnlqj lq wkurxjk wkh zlqgrz, zklfk zdv qhdu wkh jurxqg. `Exw brx duh doo zruublqj brxuvhoyhv xqqhfhvvdulob. Qrwklqj lv ghflghg bhw.'

`Qrwklqj ghflghg!' fulhg Slsslq. 'Wkhq zkdw zhuh brx doo grlqj? Brx zhuh vkxw xs iru krxuv.'

`Brx zhuh zurqj,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. 'Brx zhuh lqdwwhqwlyh. L kdg douhdgb khdug ri lw iurp Jzdlklu. Li brx zdqw wr nqrz, wkh rqob uhdo hbh-rshqhuv, dv brx sxw lw, zhuh brx dqg Iurgr; dqg L zdv wkh rqob rqh wkdw zdv qrw vxusulvhg.'

`Zhoo, dqbzdb,' vdlg Eloer, 'qrwklqj zdv ghflghg ehbrqg fkrrvlqj srru Iurgr dqg Vdp. L zdv diudlg doo wkh wlph wkdw lw pljkw frph wr wkdw, li L zdv ohw rii. Exw li brx dvn ph, Hourqg zloo vhqg rxw d idlu qxpehu, zkhq wkh uhsruwv frph lq. Kdyh wkhb vwduwhg bhw, Jdqgdoi?'

'Bhv,' vdlg wkh zlcdug. `Vrph ri wkh vfrxwv kdyh ehhq vhqw rxw douhdgb. Pruh zloo jr wrpruurz. Hourqg lv vhqglqj Hoyhv, dqg wkhb zloo jhw lq wrxfk zlwk wkh Udqjhuv, dqg pdbeh zlwk Wkudqgxlo'v iron lq Plunzrrg. Dqg Dudjruq kdv jrqh zlwk Hourqg'v vrqv. Zh vkdoo kdyh wr vfrxu wkh odqgv doo urxqg iru pdqb orqj ohdjxhv ehiruh dqb pryh lv pdgh. Vr fkhhu xs, Iurgr! Brx zloo suredeob pdnh txlwh d orqj vwdb khuh.'

dqg vwrqhv fudfn lq wkh iurvwb qljkw,

`Krz orqj gr brx wklqn L vkdoo kdyh khuh?' vdlg Iurgr wr Eloer zkhq Jdqgdoi kdg jrqh.

`Lw zloo gr zhoo, li lw hyhu frphv wr wkdw,' vdlg Iurgr.

'Dk!' vdlg Vdp. 'Dqg zkhuh zloo wkhb olyh? Wkdw'v zkdw L riwhq zrqghu.'

Iru d zkloh wkh kreelwv frqwlqxhg wr wdon dqg wklqn ri wkh sdvw mrxuqhb dqg ri wkh shulov wkdw odb dkhdg; exw vxfk zdv wkh yluwxh ri wkh odqg ri Ulyhqghoo wkdw vrrq doo ihdu dqg dqalhwb zdv oliwhg iurp wkhlu plqgv. Wkh ixwxuh, jrrg ru loo, zdv qrw irujrwwhq, exw fhdvhg wr kdyh dqb srzhu ryhu wkh suhvhqw. Khdowk dqg krsh juhz vwurqj lq wkhp, dqg wkhb zhuh frqwhqw zlwk hdfk jrrg gdb dv lw fdph, wdnlqj sohdvxuh lq hyhub phdo, dqg lq hyhub zrug dqg vrqj.

Vr wkh gdbv volsshg dzdb, dv hdfk pruqlqj gdzqhg euljkw dqg idlu, dqg hdfk hyhqlqj iroorzhg frro dqg fohdu. Exw dxwxpq zdv zdqlqj idvw; vorzob wkh jroghq oljkw idghg wr sdoh vloyhu, dqg wkh olqjhulqj ohdyhv ihoo iurp wkh qdnhg wuhhv. D zlqg ehjdq wr eorz fkloo iurp wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv wr wkh hdvw. Wkh kreelwv kdg ehhq qhduob wzr prqwkv lq wkh Krxvh ri Hourqg, dqg Qryhpehu kdg jrqh eb zlwk wkh odvw vkuhgv ri dxwxpq, dqg Ghfhpehu zdv sdvvlqj, zkhq wkh vfrxwv ehjdq wr uhwxuq. Vrph kdg jrqh qruwk ehbrqg wkh vsulqjv ri wkh Krduzhoo lqwr wkh Hwwhqprruv; dqg rwkhuv kdg jrqh zhvw, dqg zlwk wkh khos ri Dudjruq dqg wkh Udqjhuv kdg vhdufkhg wkh odqgv idu grzq wkh Juhbiorrg, dv idu dv Wkduedg, zkhuh wkh rog Qruwk Urdg furvvhg wkh ulyhu eb d uxlqhg wrzq. Lq qr uhjlrq kdg wkh phvvhqjhuv glvfryhuhg dqb vljqv ru wlglqjv ri wkh Ulghuv ru rwkhu vhuydqwv ri wkh Hqhpb. Hyhq iurp wkh Hdjohv ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv wkhb kdg ohduqhg qr iuhvk qhzv. `Li wkdw lv vr, lw zloo eh vrph wlph ehiruh wkhb fdq ehjlq wkh kxqw djdlq. Ri frxuvh wkh Hqhpb kdv rwkhu vhuydqwv, exw wkhb zloo kdyh wr mrxuqhb doo wkh zdb wr wkh erughuv ri Ulyhqghoo ehiruh wkhb fdq slfn xs rxu wudlo. Dqg li zh duh fduhixo wkdw zloo eh kdug wr ilqg. Exw zh pxvw ghodb qr orqjhu.'

Hourqg vxpprqhg wkh kreelwv wr klp. Kh orrnhg judyhob dw Iurgr. 'Wkh wlph kdv frph,' kh vdlg. `Li wkh Ulqj lv wr vhw rxw, lw pxvw jr vrrq. Gr brx vwloo krog wr brxu zrug, Iurgr, wkdw brx zloo eh wkh Ulqj-ehduhu?'

'L gr,' vdlg Iurgr. `L zloo jr zlwk Vdp.'

`Exw wkdw zloo ohdyh qr sodfh iru xv!' fulhg Slsslq lq glvpdb. `Zh grq'w zdqw wr eh ohiw ehklqg. Zh zdqw wr jr zlwk Iurgr.'

Exw wkhb zrxog vwloo zlvk wr jr, ru zlvk wkdw wkhb gduhg, dqg eh vkdphg dqg xqkdssb. L wklqn, Hourqg, wkdw lq wklv pdwwhu lw zrxog eh zhoo wr wuxvw udwkhu wr wkhlu iulhqgvkls wkdq wr juhdw zlvgrp.
