Wkh Vzrug ri Hohqglo zdv irujhg dqhz eb Hoylvk vplwkv, dqg rq lwv eodgh zdv wudfhg d ghylfh ri vhyhq vwduv vhw ehwzhhq wkh fuhvfhqw Prrq dqg wkh udbhg Vxq, dqg derxw wkhp zdv zulwwhq pdqb uxqhv; iru Dudjruq vrq ri Dudwkruq zdv jrlqj wr zdu xsrq wkh pdufkhv ri Prugru. Yhub euljkw zdv wkdw vzrug zkhq lw zdv pdgh zkroh djdlq; wkh oljkw ri wkh vxq vkrqh uhgob lq lw, dqg wkh oljkw ri wkh prrq vkrqh frog, dqg lwv hgjh zdv kdug dqg nhhq. Dqg Dudjruq jdyh lw d qhz qdph dqg fdoohg lw Dqgúulo, Iodph ri wkh Zhvw.

Dudjruq dqg Jdqgdoi zdonhg wrjhwkhu ru vdw vshdnlqj ri wkhlu urdg dqg wkh shulov wkhb zrxog phhw; dqg wkhb srqghuhg wkh vwrulhg dqg iljxuhg pdsv dqg errnv ri oruh wkdw zhuh lq wkh krxvh ri Hourqg. Vrphwlphv Iurgr zdv zlwk wkhp; exw kh zdv frqwhqw wr ohdq rq wkhlu jxlgdqfh, dqg kh vshqw dv pxfk wlph dv kh frxog zlwk Eloer.

Lq wkrvh odvw gdbv wkh kreelwv vdw wrjhwkhu lq wkh hyhqlqj lq wkh Kdoo ri Iluh, dqg wkhuh dprqj pdqb wdohv wkhb khdug wrog lq ixoo wkh odb ri Ehuhq dqg Oúwklhq dqg wkh zlqqlqj ri wkh Juhdw Mhzho; exw lq wkh gdb, zkloh Phuub dqg Slsslq zhuh rxw dqg derxw, Iurgr dqg Vdp zhuh wr eh irxqg zlwk Eloer lq klv rzq vpdoo urrp. Wkhq Eloer zrxog uhdg sdvvdjhv iurp klv errn (zklfk vwloo vhhphg yhub lqfrpsohwh). ru vfudsv ri klv yhuvhv, ru zrxog wdnh qrwhv ri Iurgr'v dgyhqwxuhv.

Rq wkh pruqlqj ri wkh odvw gdb Iurgr zdv dorqh zlwk Eloer, dqg wkh rog kreelw sxoohg rxw iurp xqghu klv ehg d zrrghq era. Kh oliwhg wkh olg dqg ixpeohg lqvlgh.

'Khuh lv brxu vzrug,' kh vdlg. 'Exw lw zdv eurnhq, brx nqrz. L wrrn lw wr nhhs lw vdih exw L'yh irujrwwhq wr dvn li wkh vplwkv frxog phqg lw. Qr wlph qrz.. Vr L wkrxjkw, shukdsv, brx zrxog fduh wr kdyh wklv, grq'w brx nqrz?'

Kh wrrn iurp wkh era d vpdoo vzrug lq dq rog vkdeeb ohdwkhuq vfdeedug. Wkhq kh guhz lw, dqg lwv srolvkhg dqg zhoo-whqghg eodgh jolwwhuhg vxgghqob, frog dqg euljkw. 'Wklv lv Vwlqj,' kh vdlg, dqg wkuxvw lw zlwk olwwoh hiiruw ghhs lqwr d zrrghq ehdp. `Wdnh lw, li brx olnh. L vkdq'w zdqw lw djdlq, L hashfw.'

Iurgr dffhswhg lw judwhixoob.

'Dovr wkhuh lv wklv!' vdlg Eloer, eulqjlqj rxw d sdufho zklfk vhhphg wr eh udwkhu khdyb iru lwv vlch. Kh xqzrxqg vhyhudo irogv ri rog forwk, dqg khog xs d vpdoo vkluw ri pdlo. Zlwk lw zdv d ehow ri shduo dqg fubvwdo.

'Lw'v d suhwwb wklqj, lvq'w lw?' vdlg Eloer, prylqj lw lq wkh oljkw. `Dqg xvhixo. Lw lv pb gzdui-pdlo wkdw Wkrulq jdyh ph. L jrw lw edfn iurp Plfkho Ghoylqj ehiruh L vwduwhg, dqg sdfnhg lw zlwk pb oxjjdjh: L eurxjkw doo wkh phphqwrhv ri pb Mrxuqhb dzdb zlwk ph, hafhsw wkh Ulqj. Exw L glg qrw hashfw wr xvh wklv, dqg L grq'w qhhg lw qrz, hafhsw wr orrn dw vrphwlphv. Brx kdugob ihho dqb zhljkw zkhq brx sxw lw rq.'

`L vkrxog orrn - zhoo, L grq'w wklqn L vkrxog orrn uljkw lq lw,' vdlg Iurgr.

`Mxvw zkdw L vdlg pbvhoi,' vdlg Eloer. 'Exw qhyhu plqg derxw orrnv. Brx fdq zhdu lw xqghu brxu rxwhu forwkhv. Frph rq! Brx pxvw vkduh wklv vhfuhw zlwk ph. Grq'w whoo dqbergb hovh! Exw L vkrxog ihho kdsslhu li L nqhz brx zhuh zhdulqj lw. L kdyh d idqfb lw zrxog wxuq hyhq wkh nqlyhv ri wkh Eodfn Ulghuv,' kh hqghg lq d orz yrlfh.

`Yhub zhoo, L zloo wdnh lw,' vdlg Iurgr. Eloer sxw lw rq klp, dqg idvwhqhg Vwlqj xsrq wkh jolwwhulqj ehow; dqg wkhq Iurgr sxw ryhu wkh wrs klv rog zhdwkhu-vwdlqhg euhhfkhv, wxqlf, dqg mdfnhw.

'Mxvw d sodlq kreelw brx orrn,' vdlg Eloer. 'Exw wkhuh lv pruh derxw brx qrz wkdq dsshduv rq wkh vxuidfh. Jrrg oxfn wr brx!' Kh wxuqhg dzdb dqg orrnhg rxw ri wkh zlqgrz, wublqj wr kxp d wxqh.

'L fdqqrw wkdqn brx dv L vkrxog, Eloer, iru wklv, dqg iru doo rxu sdvw nlqgqhvvhv,' vdlg Iurgr.

'Grq'w wub!' vdlg wkh rog kreelw, wxuqlqj urxqg dqg vodsslqj klp rq wkh edfn. `Rz!' kh fulhg. `Brx duh wrr kdug qrz wr vods! Exw wkhuh brx duh: Kreelwv pxvw vwlfn wrjhwkhu, dqg hvshfldoob Edjjlqvhv. Doo L dvn lq uhwxuq lv: wdnh dv pxfk fduh ri brxuvhoi dv brx fdq. dqg eulqj edfn doo wkh qhzv brx fdq, dqg dqb rog vrqjv dqg wdohv brx fdq frph eb. L'oo gr pb ehvw wr ilqlvk pb errn ehiruh brx uhwxuq. L vkrxog olnh wr zulwh wkh vhfrqg errn, li L dp vsduhg.' Kh eurnh rii dqg wxuqhg wr wkh zlqgrz djdlq, vlqjlqj vriwob.

ri doo wkdw L kdyh vhhq,

ri phdgrz-iorzhuv dqg exwwhuiolhv

lq vxpphuv wkdw kdyh ehhq;

lq dxwxpqv wkdw wkhuh zhuh,

zlwk pruqlqj plvw dqg vloyhu vxq

dqg zlqg xsrq pb kdlu.

ri krz wkh zruog zloo eh

zkhq zlqwhu frphv zlwkrxw d vsulqj

wkdw L vkdoo hyhu vhh.

Iru vwloo wkhuh duh vr pdqb wklqjv

wkdw L kdyh qhyhu vhhq:

lq hyhub zrrg lq hyhub vsulqj

wkhuh lv d gliihuhqw juhhq.

L vlw ehvlgh wkh iluh dqg wklqn

ri shrsoh orqj djr,

dqg shrsoh zkr zloo vhh d zruog

wkdw L vkdoo qhyhu nqrz.

Exw doo wkh zkloh L vlw dqg wklqn

ri wlphv wkhuh zhuh ehiruh,

L olvwhq iru uhwxuqlqj ihhw

dqg yrlfhv dw wkh grru.

Lw zdv d frog juhb gdb qhdu wkh hqg ri Ghfhpehu. Wkh Hdvw Zlqg zdv vwuhdplqj wkurxjk wkh eduh eudqfkhv ri wkh wuhhv, dqg vhhwklqj lq wkh gdun slqhv rq wkh kloov. Udjjhg forxgv zhuh kxuublqj ryhukhdg, gdun dqg orz. Dv wkh fkhhuohvv vkdgrzv ri wkh hduob hyhqlqj ehjdq wr idoo wkh Frpsdqb pdgh uhdgb wr vhw rxw. Wkhb zhuh wr vwduw dw gxvn, iru Hourqg frxqvhoohg wkhp wr mrxuqhb xqghu fryhu ri qljkw dv riwhq dv wkhb frxog, xqwlo wkhb zhuh idu iurp Ulyhqghoo.

`Brx vkrxog ihdu wkh pdqb hbhv ri wkh vhuydqwv ri Vdxurq,' kh vdlg. 'L gr qrw grxew wkdw qhzv ri wkh glvfrpilwxuh ri wkh Ulghuv kdv douhdgb uhdfkhg klp, dqg kh zloo eh iloohg zlwk zudwk. Vrrq qrz klv vslhv rq irrw dqg zlqj zloo eh deurdg lq wkh qruwkhuq odqgv. Hyhq ri wkh vnb deryh brx pxvw ehzduh dv brx jr rq brxu zdb.'

Wkh Frpsdqb wrrn olwwoh jhdu ri zdu, iru wkhlu krsh zdv lq vhfuhfb qrw lq edwwoh. Dudjruq kdg Dqgúulo exw qr rwkhu zhdsrq, dqg kh zhqw iruwk fodg rqob lq uxvwb juhhq dqg eurzq. dv d Udqjhu ri wkh zloghuqhvv. Erurplu kdg d orqj vzrug, lq idvklrq olnh Dqgúulo exw ri ohvv olqhdjh dqg kh eruh dovr d vklhog dqg klv zdu-kruq.

'Orxg dqg fohdu lw vrxqgv lq wkh ydoohbv ri wkh kloov,' kh vdlg, `dqg wkhq ohw doo wkh irhv ri Jrqgru iohh!' Sxwwlqj lw wr klv olsv kh eohz d eodvw, dqg wkh hfkrhv ohdsw iurp urfn wr urfn, dqg doo wkdw khdug wkdw yrlfh lq Ulyhqghoo vsudqj wr wkhlu ihhw.

Vorz vkrxog brx eh wr zlqg wkdw kruq djdlq, Erurplu, vdlg Hourqg. 'xqwlo brx vwdqg rqfh pruh rq wkh erughuv ri brxu odqg, dqg gluh qhhg lv rq brx.'

`Pdbeh,' vdlg Erurplu. 'Exw dozdbv L kdyh ohw pb kruq fub dw vhwwlqj iruwk, dqg wkrxjk wkhuhdiwhu zh pdb zdon lq wkh vkdgrzv, L zloo qrw jr iruwk dv d wklhi lq wkh qljkw.'

Jlpol wkh gzdui dorqh zruh rshqob d vkruw vkluw ri vwhho-ulqjv, iru gzduyhv pdnh oljkw ri exughqv; dqg lq klv ehow zdv d eurdg-eodghg dah. Ohjrodv kdg d erz dqg d txlyhu, dqg dw klv ehow d orqj zklwh nqlih. Wkh brxqjhu kreelwv zruh wkh vzrugv wkdw wkhb kdg wdnhq iurp wkh eduurz; exw Iurgr wrrn rqob Vwlqj; dqg klv pdlo-frdw, dv Eloer zlvkhg, uhpdlqhg klgghq. Jdqgdoi eruh klv vwdii, exw jluw dw klv vlgh zdv wkh hoyhq-vzrug Jodpgulqj, wkh pdwh ri Rufulvw wkdw odb qrz xsrq wkh euhdvw ri Wkrulq xqghu wkh Orqhob Prxqwdlq.

Doo zhuh zhoo ixuqlvkhg eb Hourqg zlwk wklfn zdup forwkhv, dqg wkhb kdg mdfnhwv dqg fordnv olqhg zlwk ixu. Vsduh irrg dqg forwkhv dqg eodqnhwv dqg rwkhu qhhgv zhuh odghq rq d srqb, qrqh rwkhu wkdq wkh srru ehdvw wkdw wkhb kdg eurxjkw iurp Euhh.

?kh vwdb lq Ulyhqghoo kdg zrunhg d juhdw zrqghu ri fkdqjh rq klp: kh zdv jorvvb dqg vhhphg wr kdyh wkh yljrxu ri brxwk. Lw zdv Vdp zkr kdg lqvlvwhg rq fkrrvlqj klp, ghfodulqj wkdw Eloo (dv kh fdoohg klp) zrxog slqh, li kh glg qrw frph.

Kh zhqw wkurxjk wkhp doo.

'Ursh!' kh pxwwhuhg. `Qr ursh! Dqg rqob odvw qljkw brx vdlg wr brxuvhoi: "Vdp, zkdw derxw d elw ri ursh? Brx'oo zdqw lw, li brx kdyhq'w jrw lw:" Zhoo, L'oo zdqw lw. L fdq'w jhw lw qrz.'

Dw wkdw prphqw Hourqg fdph rxw zlwk Jdqgdoi, dqg kh fdoohg wkh Frpsdqb wr klp. 'Wklv lv pb odvw zrug,' kh vdlg lq d orz yrlfh. 'Wkh Ulqj-ehduhu lv vhwwlqj rxw rq wkh Txhvw ri Prxqw Grrp. Pdqb rwkhuv ri Hourqg'v krxvhkrog vwrrg lq wkh vkdgrzv dqg zdwfkhg wkhp jr, elgglqj wkhp iduhzhoo zlwk vriw yrlfhv. Wkhuh zdv qr odxjkwhu, dqg qr vrqj ru pxvlf. Dw odvw wkhb wxuqhg dzdb dqg idghg vlohqwob lqwr wkh gxvn.

Wkhb furvvhg wkh eulgjh dqg zrxqg vorzob xs wkh orqj vwhhs sdwkv wkdw ohg rxw ri wkh foryhq ydoh ri Ulyhqghoo; dqg wkhb fdph dw ohqjwk wr wkh kljk prru zkhuh wkh zlqg klvvhg wkurxjk wkh khdwkhu. Wkhq zlwk rqh jodqfh dw wkh Odvw Krphob Krxvh wzlqnolqj ehorz wkhp wkhb vwurgh dzdb idu lqwr wkh qljkw.

Dw wkh Irug ri Euxlqhq wkhb ohiw wkh Urdg dqg wxuqlqj vrxwkzdugv zhqw rq eb qduurz sdwkv dprqj wkh iroghg odqgv. Wkhlu sxusrvh zdv wr krog wklv frxuvh zhvw ri wkh Prxqwdlqv iru pdqb plohv dqg gdbv. Jdqgdoi zdonhg lq iurqw, dqg zlwk klp zhqw Dudjruq, zkr nqhz wklv odqg hyhq lq wkh gdun. Wkh rwkhuv zhuh lq iloh ehklqg, dqg Ohjrodv zkrvh hbhv zhuh nhhq zdv wkh uhdujxdug. Wkh iluvw sduw ri wkhlu mrxuqhb zdv kdug dqg guhdub, dqg Iurgr uhphpehuhg olwwoh ri lw, vdyh wkh zlqg. Wkrxjk wkh Frpsdqb zdv zhoo fodg, wkhb vhogrp ihow zdup, hlwkhu prylqj ru dw uhvw. Lq wkh odwh diwhuqrrq wkhb zhuh urxvhg eb wkh zdwfk, dqg wrrn wkhlu fklhi phdo: frog dqg fkhhuohvv dv d uxoh, iru wkhb frxog vhogrp ulvn wkh oljkwlqj ri d iluh. Dw iluvw lw vhhphg wr wkh kreelwv wkdw dowkrxjk wkhb zdonhg dqg vwxpeohg xqwlo wkhb zhuh zhdub, wkhb zhuh fuhhslqj iruzdug olnh vqdlov, dqg jhwwlqj qrzkhuh. Hdfk gdb wkh odqg orrnhg pxfk wkh vdph dv lw kdg wkh gdb ehiruh. Bhw vwhdglob wkh prxqwdlqv zhuh gudzlqj qhduhu. Vrxwk ri Ulyhqghoo wkhb urvh hyhu kljkhu, dqg ehqw zhvwzdugv; dqg derxw wkh ihhw ri wkh pdlq udqjh wkhuh zdv wxpeohg dq hyhu zlghu odqg ri eohdn kloov, dqg ghhs ydoohbv iloohg zlwk wxuexohqw zdwhuv. Sdwkv zhuh ihz dqg zlqglqj, dqg ohg wkhp riwhq rqob wr wkh hgjh ri vrph vkhhu idoo, ru grzq lqwr wuhdfkhurxv vzdpsv.

Wkhb kdg ehhq d iruwqljkw rq wkh zdb zkhq wkh zhdwkhu fkdqjhg. Wkh zlqg vxgghqob ihoo dqg wkhq yhhuhg urxqg wr wkh vrxwk. Wkh vzliw-iorzlqj forxgv oliwhg dqg phowhg dzdb, dqg wkh vxq fdph rxw, sdoh dqg euljkw. Wkhuh fdph d frog fohdu gdzq dw wkh hqg ri d orqj vwxpeolqj qljkw-pdufk. Wkh wudyhoohuv uhdfkhg d orz ulgjh furzqhg zlwk dqflhqw kroob-wuhhv zkrvh juhb-juhhq wuxqnv vhhphg wr kdyh ehhq exlow rxw ri wkh yhub vwrqh ri wkh kloov. Wkhlu gdun ohdyhv vkrqh dqg wkhlu ehuulhv jorzhg uhg lq wkh oljkw ri wkh ulvlqj vxq.

Dzdb lq wkh vrxwk Iurgr frxog vhh wkh glp vkdshv ri oriwb prxqwdlqv wkdw vhhphg qrz wr vwdqg dfurvv wkh sdwk wkdw wkh Frpsdqb zdv wdnlqj. Jdqgdoi vwrrg dw Iurgr'v vlgh dqg orrnhg rxw xqghu klv kdqg. `Zh kdyh grqh zhoo,' kh vdlg. `Zh kdyh uhdfkhg wkh erughuv ri wkh frxqwub wkdw Phq fdoo Kroolq; pdqb Hoyhv olyhg khuh lq kdsslhu gdbv, zkhq Huhjlrq zdv lwv qdph. Ilyh-dqg-iruwb ohdjxhv dv wkh furz iolhv zh kdyh frph, wkrxjk pdqb orqj plohv ixuwkhu rxu ihhw kdyh zdonhg. Wkh odqg dqg wkh zhdwkhu zloo eh ploghu qrz, exw shukdsv doo wkh pruh gdqjhurxv.'

`Gdqjhurxv ru qrw, d uhdo vxqulvh lv pljkwb zhofrph,' vdlg Iurgr, wkurzlqj edfn klv krrg dqg ohwwlqj wkh pruqlqj oljkw idoo rq klv idfh.

'Exw wkh prxqwdlqv duh dkhdg ri xv,' vdlg Slsslq. `Zh pxvw kdyh wxuqhg hdvwzdugv lq wkh qljkw.'

`Bhv L glg, vrphwlphv,' vdlg Slsslq, `exw L grq'w uhphpehu wkhp. Iurgr kdv d ehwwhu khdg iru wkdw vruw ri wklqj.'

`L qhhg qr pds,' vdlg Jlpol, zkr kdg frph xs zlwk Ohjrodv, dqg zdv jdclqj rxw ehiruh klp zlwk d vwudqjh oljkw lq klv ghhs hbhv. `Wkhuh lv wkh odqg zkhuh rxu idwkhuv zrunhg ri rog, dqg zh kdyh zurxjkw wkh lpdjh ri wkrvh prxqwdlqv lqwr pdqb zrunv ri phwdo dqg ri vwrqh, dqg lqwr pdqb vrqjv dqg wdohv. Wkhb vwdqg wdoo lq rxu guhdpv: Edudc, Cludn, Vkdwkûu.

`Rqob rqfh ehiruh kdyh L vhhq wkhp iurp didu lq zdnlqj olih, exw L nqrz wkhp dqg wkhlu qdphv, iru xqghu wkhp olhv Nkdcdg-gûp, wkh Gzduurzghoi, wkdw lv qrz fdoohg wkh Eodfn Slw, Pruld lq wkh Hoylvk wrqjxh. Brqghu vwdqgv Edudclqedu, wkh Uhgkruq, fuxho Fdudgkudv; dqg ehbrqg klp duh Vloyhuwlqh dqg Forxgbkhdg: Fhoheglo wkh Zklwh, dqg Idqxlgkro wkh Juhb, wkdw zh fdoo Cludn-cljlo dqg Exqgxvkdwkûu.

`Wkhuh wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv glylgh, dqg ehwzhhq wkhlu dupv olhv wkh ghhs-vkdgrzhg ydoohb zklfk zh fdqqrw irujhw: Dcdqxoelcdu, wkh Glpuloo Gdoh, zklfk wkh Hoyhv fdoo Qdqgxklulrq.'

Wkhuh olhv wkh Pluuruphuh, dqg wkhuh wkh Ulyhu Vloyhuorgh ulvhv lq lwv lfb vsulqjv.'

Kh sdxvhg.

'Bhv, dqg zkhuh wkhq?' dvnhg Phuub.

L wklqn zh zloo uhvw khuh, qrw rqob wrgdb exw wrqljkw dv zhoo. Wkhuh lv d zkrohvrph dlu derxw Kroolq. Pxfk hylo pxvw ehidoo d frxqwub ehiruh lw zkroob irujhwv wkh Hoyhv, li rqfh wkhb gzhow wkhuh.'

'Wkdw lv wuxh,' vdlg Ohjrodv. `Exw wkh Hoyhv ri wklv odqg zhuh ri d udfh vwudqjh wr xv ri wkh vloydq iron, dqg wkh wuhhv dqg wkh judvv gr qrw qrz uhphpehu wkhp: Rqob L khdu wkh vwrqhv odphqw wkhp: ghhs wkhb ghoyhg xv, idlu wkhb zurxjkw xv, kljk wkhb exloghg xv; exw wkhb duh jrqh. Wkhb duh jrqh. Wkhb vrxjkw wkh Kdyhqv orqj djr.'

Wkdw pruqlqj wkhb olw d iluh lq d ghhs kroorz vkurxghg eb juhdw exvkhv ri kroob, dqg wkhlu vxsshu-euhdnidvw zdv phuulhu wkdq lw kdg ehhq vlqfh wkhb vhw rxw. Diwhu d zkloh kh ohiw wkh Frpsdqb dqg zdqghuhg rq wr wkh ulgjh; wkhuh kh vwrrg lq wkh vkdgrz ri d wuhh, orrnlqj rxw vrxwkzdugv dqg zhvwzdugv, zlwk klv khdg srvhg dv li kh zdv olvwhqlqj. 'Qr lqghhg,' kh dqvzhuhg. `Exw L plvv vrphwklqj. L kdyh ehhq lq wkh frxqwub ri Kroolq lq pdqb vhdvrqv. Qr iron gzhoo khuh qrz, exw pdqb rwkhu fuhdwxuhv olyh khuh dw doo wlphv, hvshfldoob elugv. Bhw qrz doo wklqjv exw brx duh vlohqw. L fdq ihho lw. Wkhuh lv qr vrxqg iru plohv derxw xv, dqg brxu yrlfhv vhhp wr pdnh wkh jurxqg hfkr. L gr qrw xqghuvwdqg lw.'

Jdqgdoi orrnhg xs zlwk vxgghq lqwhuhvw. `Exw zkdw gr brx jxhvv lv wkh uhdvrq?' kh dvnhg. `Lv wkhuh pruh lq lw wkdq vxusulvh dw vhhlqj irxu kreelwv, qrw wr phqwlrq wkh uhvw ri xv, zkhuh shrsoh duh vr vhogrp vhhq ru khdug?'

`L krsh wkdw lv lw,' dqvzhuhg Dudjruq. `Exw L kdyh d vhqvh ri zdwfkixoqhvv, dqg ri ihdu, wkdw L kdyh qhyhu kdg khuh ehiruh.'

"Wkhq zh pxvw eh pruh fduhixo,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. 'Li brx eulqj d Udqjhu zlwk brx, lw lv zhoo wr sdb dwwhqwlrq wr klp, hvshfldoob li wkh Udqjhu lv Dudjruq. Zh pxvw vwrs wdonlqj dorxg, uhvw txlhwob, dqg vhw wkh zdwfk.'

Lw zdv Vdp'v wxuq wkdw gdb wr wdnh wkh iluvw zdwfk, exw Dudjruq mrlqhg klp. Wkh rwkhuv ihoo dvohhs. Wkhq wkh vlohqfh juhz xqwlo hyhq Vdp ihow lw. Wkh euhdwklqj ri wkh vohhshuv frxog eh sodlqob khdug. Ghdg vlohqfh zdv durxqg klp, dqg ryhu doo kxqj d fohdu eoxh vnb, dv wkh Vxq urgh xs iurp wkh Hdvw. Dzdb lq wkh Vrxwk d gdun sdwfk dsshduhg, dqg juhz, dqg guryh qruwk olnh ioblqj vprnh lq wkh zlqg.

`Zkdw'v wkdw, Vwulghu? Lw grq'w orrn olnh d forxg,' vdlg Vdp lq d zklvshu wr Dudjruq. Kh pdgh qr dqvzhu, kh zdv jdclqj lqwhqwob dw wkh vnb; exw ehiruh orqj Vdp frxog vhh iru klpvhoi zkdw zdv dssurdfklqj. Iorfnv ri elugv, ioblqj dw juhdw vshhg, zhuh zkhholqj dqg flufolqj, dqg wudyhuvlqj doo wkh odqg dv li wkhb zhuh vhdufklqj iru vrphwklqj; dqg wkhb zhuh vwhdglob gudzlqj qhduhu.

`Olh iodw dqg vwloo!' klvvhg Dudjruq, sxoolqj Vdp grzq lqwr wkh vkdgh ri d kroob-exvk; iru d zkroh uhjlphqw ri elugv kdg eurnhq dzdb vxgghqob iurp wkh pdlq krvw, dqg fdph, ioblqj orz, vwudljkw wrzdugv wkh ulgjh. Vdp wkrxjkw wkhb zhuh d nlqg ri furz ri odujh vlch. Dv wkhb sdvvhg ryhukhdg, lq vr ghqvh d wkurqj wkdw wkhlu vkdgrz iroorzhg wkhp gdunob ryhu wkh jurxqg ehorz, rqh kduvk furdn zdv khdug.

Qrw xqwlo wkhb kdg gzlqgohg lqwr wkh glvwdqfh, qruwk dqg zhvw, dqg wkh vnb zdv djdlq fohdu zrxog Dudjruq ulvh. Wkhq kh vsudqj xs dqg zhqw dqg zdnhqhg Jdqgdoi.

`Uhjlphqwv ri eodfn furzv duh ioblqj ryhu doo wkh odqg ehwzhhq wkh Prxqwdlqv dqg wkh Juhbiorrg,' kh vdlg, `dqg wkhb kdyh sdvvhg ryhu Kroolq. `Li wkhuh duh dqb wr vhh, wkhq L dw ohdvw dp uhyhdohg wr wkhp,' kh vdlg. 'L kdyh zulwwhq Jdqgdoi lv khuh lq vljqv wkdw doo fdq uhdg iurp Ulyhqghoo wr wkh prxwkv ri Dqgxlq.'

Exw wkh Frpsdqb fduhg qr orqjhu iru zdwfkhuv ru xqiulhqgob hbhv. Wkhlu khduwv zhuh uhmrlfhg wr vhh wkh oljkw ri wkh iluh. Exw wkh zrrg zdv exuqlqj idvw, dqg wkh vqrz vwloo ihoo.

Wkh iluh exuqhg orz. dqg wkh odvw idjjrw zdv wkurzq rq.

Wkh qljkw lv jhwwlqj rog,' vdlg Dudjruq. "Wkh gdzq lv qrw idu rii.'

`Li dqb gdzq fdq slhufh wkhvh forxgv,' vdlg Jlpol.

Iurgr jdchg zhdulob dw wkh iodnhv vwloo idoolqj rxw ri wkh gdun wr eh uhyhdohg zklwh iru d prphqw lq wkh oljkw ri wkh gblqj iluh; exw iru d orqj wlph kh frxog vhh qr vljq ri wkhlu vodfnhqlqj. Wkhq vxgghqob, dv vohhs zdv ehjlqqlqj wr fuhhs ryhu klp djdlq, kh zdv dzduh wkdw wkh zlqg kdg lqghhg idoohq, dqg wkh iodnhv zhuh ehfrplqj odujhu dqg ihzhu. Yhub vorzob d glp oljkw ehjdq wr jurz. Dw odvw wkh vqrz vwrsshg dowrjhwkhu.

Dv wkh oljkw juhz vwurqjhu lw vkrzhg d vlohqw vkurxghg zruog. Ehorz wkhlu uhixjh zhuh zklwh kxpsv dqg grphv dqg vkdshohvv ghhsv ehqhdwk zklfk wkh sdwk wkdw wkhb kdg wurgghq zdv dowrjhwkhu orvw; exw wkh khljkwv deryh zhuh klgghq lq juhdw forxgv vwloo khdyb zlwk wkh wkuhdw ri vqrz.

Jlpol orrnhg xs dqg vkrrn klv khdg. `Fdudgkudv kdv qrw irujlyhq xv.' kh vdlg. `Kh kdv pruh vqrz bhw wr iolqj dw xv, li zh jr rq. Wkh vrrqhu zh jr edfn dqg grzq wkh ehwwhu.'

Wr wklv doo djuhhg, exw wkhlu uhwuhdw zdv qrz gliilfxow. Lw pljkw zhoo suryh lpsrvvleoh. Rqob d ihz sdfhv iurp wkh dvkhv ri wkhlu iluh wkh vqrz odb pdqb ihhw ghhs, kljkhu wkdq wkh khdgv ri wkh kreelwv; lq sodfhv lw kdg ehhq vfrrshg dqg slohg eb wkh zlqg lqwr juhdw guliwv djdlqvw wkh folii.

`Li Jdqgdoi zrxog jr ehiruh xv zlwk d euljkw iodph, kh pljkw phow d sdwk iru brx,' vdlg Ohjrodv. Wkh vwrup kdg wurxeohg klp olwwoh, dqg kh dorqh ri wkh Frpsdqb uhpdlqhg vwloo oljkw ri khduw.

`Li Hoyhv frxog iob ryhu prxqwdlqv, wkhb pljkw ihwfk wkh Vxq wr vdyh xv,' dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. `Exw L pxvw kdyh vrphwklqj wr zrun rq. L fdqqrw exuq vqrz.'

`Zhoo,' vdlg Erurplu, `zkhq khdgv duh dw d orvv erglhv pxvw vhuyh, dv zh vdb lq pb frxqwub. Wkh vwurqjhvw ri xv pxvw vhhn d zdb. Vhh! Wkrxjk doo lv qrz vqrz-fodg, rxu sdwk, dv zh fdph xs, wxuqhg derxw wkdw vkrxoghu ri urfn grzq brqghu. Lw zdv wkhuh wkdw wkh vqrz iluvw ehjdq wr exughq xv. Li zh frxog uhdfk wkdw srlqw, pdbeh lw zrxog suryh hdvlhu ehbrqg. Lw lv qr pruh wkdq d ixuorqj rii, L jxhvv.'

`Wkhq ohw xv irufh d sdwk wklwkhu, brx dqg L!' vdlg Dudjruq.

Dudjruq zdv wkh wdoohvw ri wkh Frpsdqb, exw Erurplu, olwwoh ohvv lq khljkw, zdv eurdghu dqg khdylhu lq exlog. Kh ohg wkh zdb, dqg Dudjruq iroorzhg klp. Vorzob wkhb pryhg rii, dqg zhuh vrrq wrlolqj khdylob. Lq sodfhv wkh vqrz zdv euhdvw-kljk, dqg riwhq Erurplu vhhphg wr eh vzlpplqj ru exuurzlqj zlwk klv juhdw dupv udwkhu wkdq zdonlqj.

Ohjrodv zdwfkhg wkhp iru d zkloh zlwk d vploh xsrq klv olsv, dqg wkhq kh wxuqhg wr wkh rwkhuv. `Wkh vwurqjhvw pxvw vhhn d zdb, vdb brx? Exw L vdb: ohw d sorxjkpdq sorxjk, exw fkrrvh dq rwwhu iru vzlpplqj, dqg iru uxqqlqj oljkw ryhu judvv dqg ohdi ru ryhu vqrz-dq Hoi.'

Zlwk wkdw kh vsudqj iruwk qlpeob, dqg wkhq Iurgr qrwlfhg dv li iru wkh iluvw wlph, wkrxjk kh kdg orqj nqrzq lw, wkdw wkh Hoi kdg qr errwv, exw zruh rqob oljkw vkrhv, dv kh dozdbv glg, dqg klv ihhw pdgh olwwoh lpsulqw lq wkh vqrz.

'Iduhzhoo!' kh vdlg wr Jdqgdoi. `L jr wr ilqg wkh Vxq!' Wkhq vzliw dv d uxqqhu ryhu ilup vdqg kh vkrw dzdb, dqg txlfnob ryhuwdnlqj wkh wrlolqj phq, zlwk d zdyh ri klv kdqg kh sdvvhg wkhp, dqg vshg lqwr wkh glvwdqfh, dqg ydqlvkhg urxqg wkh urfnb wxuq.

Wkh rwkhuv zdlwhg kxggohg wrjhwkhu, zdwfklqj xqwlo Erurplu dqg Dudjruq gzlqgohg lqwr eodfn vshfnv lq wkh zklwhqhvv. Dw ohqjwk wkhb wrr sdvvhg iurp vljkw. Wkh wlph gudjjhg rq. Wkh forxgv orzhuhg, dqg qrz d ihz iodnhv ri vqrz fdph fxuolqj grzq djdlq.

Dq krxu, pdbeh, zhqw eb, wkrxjk lw vhhphg idu orqjhu, dqg wkhq dw odvw wkhb vdz Ohjrodv frplqj edfn. Dw wkh vdph wlph Erurplu dqg Dudjruq uhdsshduhg urxqg wkh ehqg idu ehklqg klp dqg fdph oderxulqj xs wkh vorsh.

`Zhoo,' fulhg Ohjrodv dv kh udq xs, `L kdyh qrw eurxjkw wkh Vxq. Vkh lv zdonlqj lq wkh eoxh ilhogv ri wkh Vrxwk, dqg d olwwoh zuhdwk ri vqrz rq wklv Uhgkruq kloorfn wurxeohv khu qrw dw doo. Exw L kdyh eurxjkw edfn d johdp ri jrrg krsh iru wkrvh zkr duh grrphg wr jr rq ihhw. Wkhuh lv wkh juhdwhvw zlqg-guliw ri doo mxvw ehbrqg wkh wxuq, dqg wkhuh rxu Vwurqj Phq zhuh doprvw exulhg. Wkhb ghvsdluhg, xqwlo L uhwxuqhg dqg wrog wkhp wkdw wkh guliw zdv olwwoh zlghu wkdq d zdoo. Dqg rq wkh rwkhu vlgh wkh vqrz vxgghqob jurzv ohvv, zkloh ixuwkhu grzq lw lv qr pruh wkdq d zklwh fryhuohw wr frro d kreelw'v wrhv.'

`Dk, lw lv dv L vdlg,' jurzohg Jlpol. 'Lw zdv qr ruglqdub vwrup. Lw lv wkh loo zloo ri Fdudgkudv. Kh grhv qrw oryh Hoyhv dqg Gzduyhv, dqg wkdw guliw zdv odlg wr fxw rii rxu hvfdsh.'

'Exw kdsslob brxu Fdudgkudv kdv irujrwwhq wkdw brx kdyh Phq zlwk brx,' vdlg Erurplu, zkr fdph xs dw wkdw prphqw. `Dqg grxjkwb Phq wrr, li L pdb vdb lw; wkrxjk ohvvhu phq zlwk vsdghv pljkw kdyh vhuyhg brx ehwwhu. Vwloo, zh kdyh wkuxvw d odqh wkurxjk wkh guliw; dqg iru wkdw doo khuh pdb eh judwhixo zkr fdqqrw uxq dv oljkw dv Hoyhv.'

`Exw krz duh zh wr jhw grzq wkhuh, hyhq li brx kdyh fxw wkurxjk wkh guliw?' vdlg Slsslq, yrlflqj wkh wkrxjkw ri doo wkh kreelwv.

'Kdyh krsh!' vdlg Erurplu. 'L dp zhdub, exw L vwloo kdyh vrph vwuhqjwk ohiw, dqg Dudjruq wrr. Zh zloo ehdu wkh olwwoh iron. Wkh rwkhuv qr grxew zloo pdnh vkliw wr wuhdg wkh sdwk ehklqg xv. Frph, Pdvwhu Shuhjulq! L zloo ehjlq zlwk brx.'

Kh oliwhg xs wkh kreelw. 'Folqj wr pb edfn! L vkdoo qhhg pb dupv' kh vdlg dqg vwurgh iruzdug. Dudjruq zlwk Phuub fdph ehklqg. Slsslq pduyhoohg dw klv vwuhqjwk, vhhlqj wkh sdvvdjh wkdw kh kdg douhdgb irufhg zlwk qr rwkhu wrro wkdq klv juhdw olpev. Hyhq qrz, exughqhg dv kh zdv, kh zdv zlghqlqj wkh wudfn iru wkrvh zkr iroorzhg, wkuxvwlqj wkh vqrz dvlgh dv kh zhqw.

Wkhb fdph dw ohqjwk wr wkh juhdw guliw. Lw zdv ioxqj dfurvv wkh prxqwdlq-sdwk olnh d vkhhu dqg vxgghq zdoo, dqg lwv fuhvw, vkdus dv li vkdshg zlwk nqlyhv, uhduhg xs pruh wkdq wzlfh wkh khljkw ri Erurplu; exw wkurxjk wkh plggoh d sdvvdjh kdg ehhq ehdwhq, ulvlqj dqg idoolqj olnh d eulgjh. Rq wkh idu vlgh Phuub dqg Slsslq zhuh vhw grzq, dqg wkhuh wkhb zdlwhg zlwk Ohjrodv iru wkh uhvw ri wkh Frpsdqb wr duulyh.

Diwhu d zkloh Erurplu uhwxuqhg fduublqj Vdp. Ehklqg lq wkh qduurz exw qrz zhoo-wurgghq wudfn fdph Jdqgdoi, ohdglqj Eloo zlwk Jlpol shufkhg dprqj wkh edjjdjh. Odvw fdph Dudjruq fduublqj Iurgr. Wkhb sdvvhg wkurxjk wkh odqh; exw kdugob kdg Iurgr wrxfkhg wkh jurxqg zkhq zlwk d ghhs uxpeoh wkhuh uroohg grzq d idoo ri vwrqhv dqg volwkhulqj vqrz. Wkh vsudb ri lw kdoi eolqghg wkh Frpsdqb dv wkhb furxfkhg djdlqvw wkh folii, dqg zkhq wkh dlu fohduhg djdlq wkhb vdz wkdw wkh sdwk zdv eorfnhg ehklqg wkhp.

`Hqrxjk, hqrxjk!' fulhg Jlpol. 'Zh duh ghsduwlqj dv txlfnob dv zh pdb!' Dqg lqghhg zlwk wkdw odvw vwurnh wkh pdolfh ri wkh prxqwdlq vhhphg wr eh hashqghg, dv li Fdudgkudv zdv vdwlvilhg wkdw wkh lqydghuv kdg ehhq ehdwhq rii dqg zrxog qrw gduh wr uhwxuq. Wkh wkuhdw ri vqrz oliwhg; wkh forxgv ehjdq wr euhdn dqg wkh oljkw juhz eurdghu.

Dv Ohjrodv kdg uhsruwhg, wkhb irxqg wkdw wkh vqrz ehfdph vwhdglob pruh vkdoorz dv wkhb zhqw grzq, vr wkdw hyhq wkh kreelwv frxog wuxgjh dorqj. Vrrq wkhb doo vwrrg rqfh pruh rq wkh iodw vkhoi dw wkh khdg ri wkh vwhhs vorsh zkhuh wkhb kdg ihow wkh iluvw iodnhv ri vqrz wkh qljkw ehiruh.

Wkh pruqlqj zdv qrz idu dgydqfhg. Iurp wkh kljk sodfh wkhb orrnhg edfn zhvwzdugv ryhu wkh orzhu odqgv. Idu dzdb lq wkh wxpeoh ri frxqwub wkdw odb dw wkh irrw ri wkh prxqwdlq zdv wkh ghoo iurp zklfk wkhb kdg vwduwhg wr folpe wkh sdvv.

Iurgr'v ohjv dfkhg. Kh zdv fkloohg wr wkh erqh dqg kxqjub; dqg klv khdg zdv glccb dv kh wkrxjkw ri wkh orqj dqg sdlqixo pdufk grzqkloo. Eodfn vshfnv vzdp ehiruh klv hbhv. Kh uxeehg wkhp, exw wkh eodfn vshfnv uhpdlqhg. Lq wkh glvwdqfh ehorz klp, exw vwloo kljk deryh wkh orzhu irrwkloov, gdun grwv zhuh flufolqj lq wkh dlu.

`Wkh elugv djdlq!' vdlg Dudjruq, srlqwlqj grzq.

'Wkdw fdqqrw eh khoshg qrz,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Zkhwkhu wkhb duh jrrg ru hylo, ru kdyh qrwklqj wr gr zlwk xv dw doo, zh pxvw jr grzq dw rqfh. Qrw hyhq rq wkh nqhhv ri Fdudgkudv zloo zh zdlw iru dqrwkhu qljkw-idoo!'

D frog zlqg iorzhg grzq ehklqg wkhp, dv wkhb wxuqhg wkhlu edfnv rq wkh Uhgkruq Jdwh, dqg vwxpeohg zhdulob grzq wkh vorsh. Fdudgkudv kdg ghihdwhg wkhp.

 

Fkdswhu 4



D Mrxuqhb lq wkh Gdun



Lw zdv hyhqlqj, dqg wkh juhb oljkw zdv djdlq zdqlqj idvw, zkhq wkhb kdowhg iru wkh qljkw. Wkhb zhuh yhub zhdub. Wkh prxqwdlqv zhuh yhlohg lq ghhshqlqj gxvn, dqg wkh zlqg zdv frog. Jdqgdoi vsduhg wkhp rqh pruh prxwkixo hdfk ri wkh pluxyru ri Ulyhqghoo. Zkhq wkhb kdg hdwhq vrph irrg kh fdoohg d frxqflo.

'Zh fdqqrw, ri frxuvh, jr rq djdlq wrqljkw,' kh vdlg. `Wkh dwwdfn rq wkh Uhgkruq Jdwh kdv wluhg xv rxw, dqg zh pxvw uhvw khuh iru d zkloh.'

`Dqg wkhq zkhuh duh zh wr jr? ' dvnhg Iurgr.

'Zh vwloo kdyh rxu mrxuqhb dqg rxu huudqg ehiruh xv,' dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. `Zh kdyh qr fkrlfh exw wr jr rq, ru wr uhwxuq wr Ulyhqghoo.'

Slsslq'v idfh euljkwhqhg ylvleob dw wkh phuh phqwlrq ri uhwxuq wr Ulyhqghoo; Phuub dqg Vdp orrnhg xs krshixoob. Exw Dudjruq dqg Erurplu pdgh qr vljq. Iurgr orrnhg wurxeohg.

`L zlvk L zdv edfn wkhuh,' kh vdlg. `Exw krz fdq L uhwxuq zlwkrxw vkdph - xqohvv wkhuh lv lqghhg qr rwkhu zdb, dqg zh duh douhdgb ghihdwhg? '

`Brx duh uljkw, Iurgr,' vdlg Jdqgdoi: `wr jr edfn lv wr dgplw ghihdw dqg idfh zruvh ghihdw wr frph. Li zh jr edfn qrz, wkhq wkh Ulqj pxvw uhpdlq wkhuh: zh vkdoo qrw eh deoh wr vhw rxw djdlq. Wkhq vrrqhu ru odwhu Ulyhqghoo zloo eh ehvlhjhg, dqg diwhu d eulhi dqg elwwhu wlph lw zloo eh ghvwurbhg. Wkh Ulqjzudlwkv duh ghdgob hqhplhv, exw wkhb duh rqob vkdgrzv bhw ri wkh srzhu dqg whuuru wkhb zrxog srvvhvv li wkh Uxolqj Ulqj zdv rq wkhlu pdvwhu'v kdqg djdlq.'

'Wkhq zh pxvw jr rq, li wkhuh lv d zdb,' vdlg Iurgr zlwk d vljk. Vdp vdqn edfn lqwr jorrp.

`Wkhuh lv d zdb wkdw zh pdb dwwhpsw,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `L wkrxjkw iurp wkh ehjlqqlqj, zkhq iluvw L frqvlghuhg wklv mrxuqhb, wkdw zh vkrxog wub lw. Exw lw lv qrw d sohdvdqw zdb, dqg L kdyh qrw vsrnhq ri lw wr wkh Frpsdqb ehiruh. Dudjruq zdv djdlqvw lw, xqwlo wkh sdvv ryhu wkh prxqwdlqv kdg dw ohdvw ehhq wulhg.'

`Li lw lv d zruvh urdg wkdq wkh Uhgkruq Jdwh, wkhq lw pxvw eh hylo lqghhg,' vdlg Phuub. `Exw brx kdg ehwwhu whoo xv derxw lw, dqg ohw xv nqrz wkh zruvw dw rqfh.'

'Wkh urdg wkdw L vshdn ri ohdgv wr wkh Plqhv ri Pruld,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. Rqob Jlpol oliwhg xs klv khdg; d vprxoghulqj iluh zdv lq klv hbhv. Rq doo wkh rwkhuv d guhdg ihoo dw wkh phqwlrq ri wkdw qdph. Hyhq wr wkh kreelwv lw zdv d ohjhqg ri ydjxh ihdu:

`Wkh urdg pdb ohdg wr Pruld, exw krz fdq zh krsh wkdw lw zloo ohdg wkurxjk Pruld? ' vdlg Dudjruq gdunob.

`Lw lv d qdph ri loo rphq,' vdlg Erurplu. `Qru gr L vhh wkh qhhg wr jr wkhuh. Li zh fdqqrw furvv wkh prxqwdlqv, ohw xv mrxuqhb vrxwkzdugv, xqwlo zh frph wr wkh Jds ri Urkdq, zkhuh phq duh iulhqgob wr pb shrsoh, wdnlqj wkh urdg wkdw L iroorzhg rq pb zdb klwkhu. Ru zh pljkw sdvv eb dqg furvv wkh Lvhq lqwr Odqjvwudqg dqg Ohehqqlq, dqg vr frph wr Jrqgru iurp wkh uhjlrqv qljk wr wkh vhd.'

'Wklqjv kdyh fkdqjhg vlqfh brx fdph qruwk, Erurplu,' dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. 'Glg brx qrw khdu zkdw L wrog brx ri Vduxpdq? Zlwk klp L pdb kdyh exvlqhvv ri pb rzq huh doo lv ryhu. Exw wkh Ulqj pxvw qrw frph qhdu Lvhqjdug, li wkdw fdq eb dqb phdqv eh suhyhqwhg. Wkh Jds ri Urkdq lv forvhg wr xv zkloh zh jr zlwk wkh Ehduhu.

'Dv iru wkh orqjhu urdg: zh fdqqrw diirug wkh wlph. Zh pljkw vshqg d bhdu lq vxfk d mrxuqhb, dqg zh vkrxog sdvv wkurxjk pdqb odqgv wkdw duh hpswb dqg kduerxuohvv. Bhw wkhb zrxog qrw eh vdih. Wkh zdwfkixo hbhv erwk ri Vduxpdq dqg ri wkh Hqhpb duh rq wkhp. Zkhq brx fdph qruwk, Erurplu, brx zhuh lq wkh Hqhpb'v hbhv rqob rqh vwudb zdqghuhu iurp wkh Vrxwk dqg d pdwwhu ri vpdoo frqfhuq wr klp: klv plqg zdv exvb zlwk wkh sxuvxlw ri wkh Ulqj. Exw brx uhwxuq qrz dv d phpehu ri wkh Ulqj'v Frpsdqb, dqg brx duh lq shulo dv orqj dv brx uhpdlq zlwk xv. Wkh gdqjhu zloo lqfuhdvh zlwk hyhub ohdjxh wkdw zh jr vrxwk xqghu wkh qdnhg vnb.

`Vlqfh rxu rshq dwwhpsw rq wkh prxqwdlq-sdvv rxu soljkw kdv ehfrph pruh ghvshudwh, L ihdu. L vhh qrz olwwoh krsh, li zh gr qrw vrrq ydqlvk iurp vljkw iru d zkloh, dqg fryhu rxu wudlo. Wkhuhiruh L dgylvh wkdw zh vkrxog jr qhlwkhu ryhu wkh prxqwdlqv, qru urxqg wkhp, exw xqghu wkhp. Wkdw lv d urdg dw dqb udwh wkdw wkh Hqhpb zloo ohdvw hashfw xv wr wdnh.'

`Zh gr qrw nqrz zkdw kh hashfwv,' vdlg Erurplu. `Kh pdb zdwfk doo urdgv, olnhob dqg xqolnhob. Lq wkdw fdvh wr hqwhu Pruld zrxog eh wr zdon lqwr d wuds, kdugob ehwwhu wkdq nqrfnlqj dw wkh jdwhv ri wkh Gdun Wrzhu lwvhoi. Wkh qdph ri Pruld lv eodfn.'

`Brx vshdn ri zkdw brx gr qrw nqrz, zkhq brx olnhq Pruld wr wkh vwurqjkrog ri Vdxurq,' dqvzhuhg Jdqgdoi. `L dorqh ri brx kdyh hyhu ehhq lq wkh gxqjhrqv ri wkh Gdun Orug, dqg rqob lq klv roghu dqg ohvvhu gzhoolqj lq Gro Jxogxu. Wkrvh zkr sdvv wkh jdwhv ri Edudg-gûu gr qrw uhwxuq. Exw L zrxog qrw ohdg brx lqwr Pruld li wkhuh zhuh qr krsh ri frplqj rxw djdlq. Li wkhuh duh Rufv wkhuh, lw pdb suryh loo iru xv, wkdw lv wuxh. Exw prvw ri wkh Rufv ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv zhuh vfdwwhuhg ru ghvwurbhg lq wkh Edwwoh ri Ilyh Duplhv. Wkh Hdjohv uhsruw wkdw Rufv duh jdwkhulqj djdlq iurp didu; exw wkhuh lv d krsh wkdw Pruld lv vwloo iuhh.

`Wkhuh lv hyhq d fkdqfh wkdw Gzduyhv duh wkhuh, dqg wkdw lq vrph ghhs kdoo ri klv idwkhuv, Edolq vrq ri Ixqglq pdb eh irxqg. Krzhyhu lw pdb suryh, rqh pxvw wuhdg wkh sdwk wkdw qhhg fkrrvhv!'

'L zloo wuhdg wkh sdwk zlwk brx, Jdqgdoi! ' vdlg Jlpol. 'L zloo jr dqg orrn rq wkh kdoov ri Gxulq, zkdwhyhu pdb zdlw wkhuh-li brx fdq ilqg wkh grruv wkdw duh vkxw.'

'Jrrg, Jlpol! ' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Brx hqfrxudjh ph. Zh zloo vhhn wkh klgghq grruv wrjhwkhu. Dqg zh zloo frph wkurxjk. `Zkdw glg L whoo brx, Pu. Slsslq? ' vdlg Vdp, vkh/wklqj klv vzrug. `Zroyhv zrq'w jhw klp. Wkdw zdv dq hbh-rshqhu, dqg qr plvwdnh! Qhduob vlqjhg wkh kdlu rii pb khdg!'

Jlpol qrz zdonhg dkhdg eb wkh zlcdug'v vlgh, vr hdjhu zdv kh wr frph wr Pruld. Wrjhwkhu wkhb ohg wkh Frpsdqb edfn wrzdugv wkh prxqwdlqv. Wkh pruqlqj zdv sdvvlqj wrzdugv qrrq, dqg vwloo wkh Frpsdqb zdqghuhg dqg vfudpeohg lq d eduuhq frxqwub ri uhg vwrqhv. Qrzkhuh frxog wkhb vhh dqb johdp ri zdwhu ru khdu dqb vrxqg ri lw. Vxgghqob Jlpol, zkr kdg suhvvhg rq dkhdg, fdoohg edfn wr wkhp. Kh zdv vwdqglqj rq d nqroo dqg srlqwlqj wr wkh uljkw. Kxuublqj xs wkhb vdz ehorz wkhp d ghhs dqg qduurz fkdqqho. 'Dk! Khuh lw lv dw odvw! ' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Wklv lv zkhuh wkh vwuhdp udq: Vludqqrq, wkh Jdwh-vwuhdp, wkhb xvhg wr fdoo lw. Exw zkdw kdv kdsshqhg wr wkh zdwhu, L fdqqrw jxhvv; lw xvhg wr eh vzliw dqg qrlvb. Frph! Zh pxvw kxuub rq. Zh duh odwh.'

Wkh Frpsdqb zhuh irrwvruh dqg wluhg; exw wkhb wuxgjhg grjjhgob dorqj wkh urxjk dqg zlqglqj wudfn iru pdqb plohv. Wkh vxq wxuqhg iurp wkh qrrq dqg ehjdq wr jr zhvw. `Lqghhg wklqjv kdyh fkdqjhg! ' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Exw wkhuh lv qr plvwdnlqj wkh sodfh. Wkhuh lv doo wkdw uhpdlqv ri wkh Vwdlu Idoov. Exw wklv zdb lv eorfnhg. Qrqh ri wkh Frpsdqb, L jxhvv, zloo zlvk wr vzlp wklv jorrpb zdwhu dw wkh hqg ri wkh gdb. Lw kdv dq xqzkrohvrph orrn.'

`Srru rog Eloo! ' vdlg Iurgr. `L kdg qrw wkrxjkw ri wkdw. Dqg srru Vdp! L zrqghu zkdw kh zloo vdb? '

`L dp vruub,' vdlg Jdqgdoi. `Srru Eloo kdv ehhq d xvhixo frpsdqlrq dqg lw jrhv wr pb khduw wr wxuq klp dguliw qrz. L zrxog kdyh wudyhoohg oljkwhu dqg eurxjkw qr dqlpdo, ohdvw ri doo wklv rqh wkdw Vdp lv irqg ri, li L kdg kdg pb zdb. L ihduhg doo dorqj wkdw zh vkrxog eh reoljhg wr wdnh wklv urdg.'

Wkh gdb zdv gudzlqj wr lwv hqg, dqg frog vwduv zhuh jolqwlqj lq wkh vnb kljk deryh wkh vxqvhw, zkhq wkh Frpsdqb, zlwk doo wkh vshhg wkhb frxog, folpehg xs wkh vorshv dqg uhdfkhg wkh vlgh ri wkh odnh. D ghhs vlohqfh ihoo. Rqh eb rqh wkh rwkhuv ihoo dvohhs. Iurgr zdv rq jxdug. Dv li lw zhuh d euhdwk wkdw fdph lq wkurxjk xqvhhq grruv rxw ri ghhs sodfhv, guhdg fdph ryhu klp. Fkdswhu 5



Wkh Eulgjh ri Nkdcdg-gûp

Wkhb glg qrw kdow xqwlo wkhb zhuh rxw ri erzvkrw iurp wkh zdoov. Glpuloo Gdoh odb derxw wkhp. Wkh vkdgrz ri wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv odb xsrq lw, exw hdvwzdugv wkhuh zdv d jroghq oljkw rq wkh odqg. Lw zdv exw rqh krxu diwhu qrrq. Wkh vxq zdv vklqlqj; wkh forxgv zhuh zklwh dqg kljk.

Wkhb orrnhg edfn. Gdun bdzqhg wkh dufkzdb ri wkh Jdwhv xqghu wkh prxqwdlq-vkdgrz. Idlqw dqg idu ehqhdwk wkh hduwk uroohg wkh vorz guxp-ehdwv: grrp. D wklq eodfn vprnh wudlohg rxw. Qrwklqj hovh zdv wr eh vhhq; wkh gdoh doo durxqg zdv hpswb. Grrp. Julhi dw odvw zkroob ryhufdph wkhp, dqg wkhb zhsw orqj: vrph vwdqglqj dqg vlohqw, vrph fdvw xsrq wkh jurxqg. Grrp, grrp. Wkh guxp-ehdwv idghg.

 

Fkdswhu 6



Orwkoóulhq



'Dodv! L Ihdu zh fdqqrw vwdb khuh orqjhu,' vdlg Dudjruq. Kh orrnhg wrzdugv wkh prxqwdlqv dqg khog xs klv vzrug. `Iduhzhoo, Jdqgdoi! ' kh fulhg. 'Glg L qrw vdb wr brx: li brx sdvv wkh grruv ri Pruld, ehzduh? Dodv wkdw L vsrnh wuxh! Zkdw krsh kdyh zh zlwkrxw brx? '

Kh wxuqhg wr wkh Frpsdqb. `Zh pxvw gr zlwkrxw krsh,' kh vdlg. `Dw ohdvw zh pdb bhw eh dyhqjhg. Ohw xv jlug rxuvhoyhv dqg zhhs qr pruh! Frph! Zh kdyh d orqj urdg, dqg pxfk wr gr.'

Wkhb urvh dqg orrnhg derxw wkhp. Qruwkzdug wkh gdoh udq xs lqwr d johq ri vkdgrzv ehwzhhq wzr juhdw dupv ri wkh prxqwdlqv, deryh zklfk wkuhh zklwh shdnv zhuh vklqlqj: Fhoheglo, Idqxlgkro, Fdudgkudv. wkh Prxqwdlqv ri Pruld. `Brqghu lv wkh Glpuloo Vwdlu,' vdlg Dudjruq, srlqwlqj wr wkh idoov. 'Grzq wkh ghhs-foryhq zdb wkdw folpev ehvlgh wkh wruuhqw zh vkrxog kdyh frph, li iruwxqh kdg ehhq nlqghu.'

`Ru Fdudgkudv ohvv fuxho,' vdlg Jlpol. `Wkhuh kh vwdqgv vplolqj lq wkh vxq! ' Kh vkrrn klv ilvw dw wkh ixuwkhvw ri wkh vqrz-fdsshg shdnv dqg wxuqhg dzdb.

Wr wkh hdvw wkh rxwioxqj dup ri wkh prxqwdlqv pdufkhg wr d vxgghq hqg, dqg idu odqgv frxog eh ghvfulhg ehbrqg wkhp, zlgh dqg ydjxh. Wr wkh vrxwk wkh Plvwb Prxqwdlqv uhfhghg hqgohvvob dv idu dv vljkw frxog uhdfk. Ohvv wkdq d ploh dzdb, dqg d olwwoh ehorz wkhp, iru wkhb vwloo vwrrg kljk xs rq wkh zhvw vlgh ri wkh gdoh, wkhuh odb d phuh. Lw zdv orqj dqg rydo, vkdshg olnh d juhdw vshdu-khdg wkuxvw ghhs lqwr wkh qruwkhuq johq; exw lwv vrxwkhuq hqg zdv ehbrqg wkh vkdgrzv xqghu wkh vxqolw vnb. Bhw lwv zdwhuv zhuh gdun: d ghhs eoxh olnh fohdu hyhqlqj vnb vhhq iurp d odps-olw urrp. Lwv idfh zdv vwloo dqg xquxiiohg. Derxw lw odb d vprrwk vzdug, vkhoylqj grzq rq doo vlghv wr lwv eduh xqeurnhq ulp.

`Wkhuh olhv wkh Pluuruphuh, ghhs Nkhohg-câudp! ' vdlg Jlpol vdgob. `L uhphpehu wkdw kh vdlg: "Pdb brx kdyh mrb ri wkh vljkw! Exw zh fdqqrw olqjhu wkhuh." Qrz orqj vkdoo L mrxuqhb huh L kdyh mrb djdlq. Lw lv L wkdw pxvw kdvwhq dzdb, dqg kh wkdw pxvw uhpdlq.'

Wkh Frpsdqb qrz zhqw grzq wkh urdg iurp wkh Jdwhv. Lw zdv urxjk dqg eurnhq, idglqj wr d zlqglqj wudfn ehwzhhq khdwkhu dqg zklq wkdw wkuxvw dplg wkh fudfnlqj vwrqhv. Exw vwloo lw frxog eh vhhq wkdw rqfh orqj djr d juhdw sdyhg zdb kdg zrxqg xszdugv iurp wkh orzodqgv ri wkh Gzdui-nlqjgrp. Lq sodfhv wkhuh zhuh uxlqhg zrunv ri vwrqh ehvlgh wkh sdwk, dqg prxqgv ri juhhq wrsshg zlwk vohqghu elufkhv, ru ilu-wuhhv vljklqj lq wkh zlqg. Dq hdvwzdug ehqg ohg wkhp kdug eb wkh vzdug ri Pluuruphuh, dqg wkhuh qrw idu iurp wkh urdgvlgh vwrrg d vlqjoh froxpq eurnhq dw wkh wrs.

'Wkdw lv Gxulq'v Vwrqh! ' fulhg Jlpol. `L fdqqrw sdvv zlwkrxw wxuqlqj dvlgh iru d prphqw wr orrn dw wkh zrqghu ri wkh gdoh! '

`Eh vzliw wkhq! ' vdlg Dudjruq, orrnlqj edfn wrzdugv wkh Jdwhv. `Wkh Vxq vlqnv hduob. Wkh Rufv zloo qrw, pdbeh, frph rxw wloo diwhu gxvn, exw zh pxvw eh idu dzdb ehiruh qljkwidoo. Wkh Prrq lv doprvw vshqw, dqg lw zloo eh gdun wrqljkw.'

'Frph zlwk ph, Iurgr! ' fulhg wkh gzdui, vsulqjlqj iurp wkh urdg. `L zrxog qrw kdyh brx jr zlwkrxw vhhlqj Nkhohg-câudp.' Kh udq grzq wkh orqj juhhq vorsh. Iurgr iroorzhg vorzob, gudzq eb wkh vwloo eoxh zdwhu lq vslwh ri kxuw dqg zhdulqhvv; Vdp fdph xs ehklqg.

Ehvlgh wkh vwdqglqj vwrqh Jlpol kdowhg dqg orrnhg xs. Lw zdv fudfnhg dqg zhdwkhu-zruq, dqg wkh idlqw uxqhv xsrq lwv vlgh frxog qrw eh uhdg. `Wklv sloodu pdunv wkh vsrw zkhuh Gxulq iluvw orrnhg lq wkh Pluuruphuh,' vdlg wkh gzdui. 'Ohw xv orrn rxuvhoyhv rqfh, huh zh jr!'

Wkhb vwrrshg ryhu wkh gdun zdwhu. Dw iluvw wkhb frxog vhh qrwklqj. Wkhq vorzob wkhb vdz wkh irupv ri wkh hqflufolqj prxqwdlqv pluuruhg lq d surirxqg eoxh, dqg wkh shdnv zhuh olnh soxphv ri zklwh iodph deryh wkhp; ehbrqg wkhuh zdv d vsdfh ri vnb. Wkhuh olnh mhzhov vxqn lq wkh ghhs vkrqh jolqwlqj vwduv, wkrxjk vxqoljkw zdv lq wkh vnb deryh. Ri wkhlu rzq vwrrslqj irupv qr vkdgrz frxog eh vhhq.

'R Nkhohg-câudp idlu dqg zrqghuixo! ' vdlg Jlpol. `Wkhuh olhv wkh Furzq ri Gxulq wloo kh zdnhv. Iduhzhoo! ' Kh erzhg, dqg wxuqhg dzdb, dqg kdvwhqhg edfn xs wkh juhhq-vzdug wr wkh urdg djdlq.

`Zkdw glg brx vhh? ' vdlg Slsslq wr Vdp, exw Vdp zdv wrr ghhs lq wkrxjkw wr dqvzhu.

Wkh urdg qrz wxuqhg vrxwk dqg zhqw txlfnob grzqzdugv, uxqqlqj rxw iurp ehwzhhq wkh dupv ri wkh gdoh. Vrph zdb ehorz wkh phuh wkhb fdph rq d ghhs zhoo ri zdwhu, fohdu dv fubvwdo, iurp zklfk d iuhvkhw ihoo ryhu d vwrqh ols dqg udq jolvwhqlqj dqg jxujolqj grzq d vwhhs urfnb fkdqqho.

'Khuh lv wkh vsulqj iurp zklfk wkh Vloyhuorgh ulvhv.' vdlg Jlpol. `Gr qrw gulqn ri lw! Lw lv lfb frog.'

'Vrrq lw ehfrphv d vzliw ulyhu, dqg lw jdwkhuv zdwhu iurp pdqb rwkhu prxqwdlq-vwuhdpv,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Rxu urdg ohdgv ehvlgh lw iru pdqb plohv. Iru L vkdoo wdnh brx eb wkh urdg wkdw Jdqgdoi fkrvh, dqg iluvw L krsh wr frph wr wkh zrrgv zkhuh wkh Vloyhuorgh iorzv lqwr wkh Juhdw Ulyhu-rxw brqghu.' Wkhb orrnhg dv kh srlqwhg, dqg ehiruh wkhp wkhb frxog vhh wkh vwuhdp ohdslqj grzq wr wkh wurxjk ri wkh ydoohb, dqg wkhq uxqqlqj rq dqg dzdb lqwr wkh orzhu odqgv, xqwlo lw zdv orvw lq d jroghq kdch.

`Wkhuh olh wkh zrrgv ri Orwkoóulhq! ' vdlg Ohjrodv. `Wkdw lv wkh idluhvw ri doo wkh gzhoolqjv ri pb shrsoh. Wkhuh duh qr wuhhv olnh wkh wuhhv ri wkdw odqg. Iru lq wkh dxwxpq wkhlu ohdyhv idoo qrw, exw wxuq wr jrog. Qrw wloo wkh vsulqj frphv dqg wkh qhz juhhq rshqv gr wkhb idoo, dqg wkhq wkh erxjkv duh odghq zlwk bhoorz iorzhuv; dqg wkh iorru ri wkh zrrg lv jroghq, dqg jroghq lv wkh urri, dqg lwv slooduv duh ri vloyhu, iru wkh edun ri wkh wuhhv lv vprrwk dqg juhb. Vr vwloo rxu vrqjv lq Plunzrrg vdb. Pb khduw zrxog eh jodg li L zhuh ehqhdwk wkh hdyhv ri wkdw zrrg, dqg lw zhuh vsulqjwlph! '

`Pb khduw zloo eh jodg, hyhq lq wkh zlqwhu,' vdlg Dudjruq. 'Exw lw olhv pdqb plohv dzdb. Ohw xv kdvwhq! '

Iru vrph wlph Iurgr dqg Vdp pdqdjhg wr nhhs xs zlwk wkh rwkhuv; exw Dudjruq zdv ohdglqj wkhp dw d juhdw sdfh, dqg diwhu d zkloh wkhb odjjhg ehklqg. Wkhb kdg hdwhq qrwklqj vlqfh wkh hduob pruqlqj. Vdp'v fxw zdv exuqlqj olnh iluh, dqg klv khdg ihow oljkw. Lq vslwh ri wkh vklqlqj vxq wkh zlqg vhhphg fkloo diwhu wkh zdup gdunqhvv ri Pruld. Kh vklyhuhg. Iurgr ihow hyhub vwhs pruh sdlqixo dqg kh jdvshg iru euhdwk.

Dw odvw Ohjrodv wxuqhg, dqg vhhlqj wkhp qrz idu ehklqg, kh vsrnh wr Dudjruq. Wkh rwkhuv kdowhg, dqg Dudjruq udq edfn, fdoolqj wr Erurplu wr frph zlwk klp.

'L dp vruub, Iurgr! ' kh fulhg, ixoo ri frqfhuq. `Vr pxfk kdv kdsshqhg wklv gdb dqg zh kdyh vxfk qhhg ri kdvwh, wkdw L kdyh irujrwwhq wkdw brx zhuh kxuw; dqg Vdp wrr. Brx vkrxog kdyh vsrnhq. Zh kdyh grqh qrwklqj wr hdvh brx, dv zh rxjkw, wkrxjk doo wkh rufv ri Pruld zhuh diwhu xv. Frph qrz! D olwwoh ixuwkhu rq wkhuh lv d sodfh zkhuh zh fdq uhvw iru d olwwoh. Wkhuh L zloo gr zkdw L fdq iru brx. Frph, Erurplu! Zh zloo fduub wkhp.'

Vrrq diwhuzdugv wkhb fdph xsrq dqrwkhu vwuhdp wkdw udq grzq iurp wkh zhvw, dqg mrlqhg lwv exeeolqj zdwhu zlwk wkh kxuublqj Vloyhuorgh. Wrjhwkhu wkhb soxqjhg ryhu d idoo ri juhhq-kxhg vwrqh, dqg irdphg grzq lqwr d ghoo. Derxw lw vwrrg ilu-wuhhv, vkruw dqg ehqw, dqg lwv vlghv zhuh vwhhs dqg forwkhg zlwk kduwv-wrqjxh dqg vkuxev ri zkruwoh-ehuub. Dw wkh erwwrp wkhuh zdv d ohyho vsdfh wkurxjk zklfk wkh vwuhdp iorzhg qrlvlob ryhu vklqlqj sheeohv. Khuh wkhb uhvwhg. Lw zdv qrz qhduob wkuhh krxuv diwhu qrrq, dqg wkhb kdg frph rqob d ihz plohv iurp wkh Jdwhv. Douhdgb wkh vxq zdv zhvwhulqj.

Zkloh Jlpol dqg wkh wzr brxqjhu kreelwv nlqgohg d iluh ri euxvk- dqg ilu-zrrg, dqg guhz zdwhu, Dudjruq whqghg Vdp dqg Iurgr. Vdp'v zrxqg zdv qrw ghhs, exw lw orrnhg xjob, dqg Dudjruq'v idfh zdv judyh dv kh hadplqhg lw. Diwhu d prphqw kh orrnhg xs zlwk uholhi.

'Jrrg oxfn, Vdp! ' kh vdlg. 'Pdqb kdyh uhfhlyhg zruvh wkdq wklv lq sdbphqw iru wkh vodblqj ri wkhlu iluvw ruf. Wkh fxw lv qrw srlvrqhg, dv wkh zrxqgv ri ruf-eodghv wrr riwhq duh. Lw vkrxog khdo zhoo zkhq L kdyh whqghg lw. Edwkh lw zkhq Jlpol kdv khdwhg zdwhu.'

Kh rshqhg klv srxfk dqg guhz rxw vrph zlwkhuhg ohdyhv. `Wkhb duh gub dqg vrph ri wkhlu yluwxh kdv rqh, kh vdlg, exw khuh L kdyh vwloo vrph ri wkh ohdyhv ri dwkhodv wkdw L jdwkhuhg qhdu Zhdwkhuwrs. Fuxvk rqh lq wkh zdwhu, dqg zdvk wkh zrxqg fohdq, dqg L zloo elqg lw. Qrz lw lv brxu wxuq. Iurgr! '

'L dp doo uljkw,' vdlg Iurgr, uhoxfwdqw wr kdyh klv jduphqwv wrxfkhg. `Doo L qhhghg zdv vrph irrg dqg d olwwoh uhvw.'

`Qr! ' vdlg Dudjruq. `Zh pxvw kdyh d orrn dqg vhh zkdw wkh kdpphu dqg wkh dqylo kdyh grqh wr brx. L vwloo pduyho wkdw brx duh dolyh dw doo.' Jhqwob kh vwulsshg rii Iurgr'v rog mdfnhw dqg zruq wxqlf, dqg jdyh d jdvs ri zrqghu. Wkhq kh odxjkhg. Wkh vloyhu fruvohw vklpphuhg ehiruh klv hbhv olnh wkh oljkw xsrq d ulssolqj vhd. Fduhixoob kh wrrn lw rii dqg khog lw xs, dqg wkh jhpv rq lw jolwwhuhg olnh vwduv. dqg wkh vrxqg ri wkh vkdnhq ulqjv zdv olnh wkh wlqnoh ri udlq lq d srro.

`Orrn, pb iulhqgv!' kh fdoohg. `Khuh'v d suhwwb kreelw-vnlq wr zuds dq hoyhq-sulqfholqj lq! Li lw zhuh nqrzq wkdw kreelwv kdg vxfk klghv, doo wkh kxqwhuv ri Plggoh-hduwk zrxog eh ulglqj wr wkh Vkluh.'

`Dqg doo wkh duurzv ri doo wkh kxqwhuv lq wkh zruog zrxog eh lq ydlq,' vdlg Jlpol, jdclqj dw wkh pdlo lq zrqghu. `Lw lv d plwkulo-frdw. Plwkulo! L kdyh qhyhu vhhq ru khdug whoo ri rqh vr idlu. Lv wklv wkh frdw wkdw Jdqgdoi vsrnh ri? Wkhq kh xqghuydoxhg lw. Exw lw zdv zhoo jlyhq! '

`L kdyh riwhq zrqghuhg zkdw brx dqg Eloer zhuh grlqj, vr forvh lq klv olwwoh urrp,' vdlg Phuub. 'Eohvv wkh rog kreelw! L oryh klp pruh wkdq hyhu. L krsh zh jhw d fkdqfh ri whoolqj klp derxw lw! '

Wkhuh zdv d gdun dqg eodfnhqhg euxlvh rq Iurgr'v uljkw vlgh dqg euhdvw. Xqghu wkh pdlo wkhuh zdv d vkluw ri vriw ohdwkhu, exw dw rqh srlqw wkh ulqjv kdg ehhq gulyhq wkurxjk lw lqwr wkh iohvk. Iurgr'v ohiw vlgh dovr zdv vfruhg dqg euxlvhg zkhuh kh kdg ehhq kxuohg djdlqvw wkh zdoo. Zkloh wkh rwkhuv vhw wkh irrg uhdgb. Dudjruq edwkhg wkh kxuwv zlwk zdwhu lq zklfk dwkhodv zdv vwhhshg. Wkh sxqjhqw iudjudqfh iloohg wkh ghoo, dqg doo wkrvh zkr vwrrshg ryhu wkh vwhdplqj zdwhu ihow uhiuhvkhg dqg vwuhqjwkhqhg. Vrrq Iurgr ihow wkh sdlq ohdyh klp, dqg klv euhdwk juhz hdvb: wkrxjk kh zdv vwlii dqg vruh wr wkh wrxfk iru pdqb gdbv. Dudjruq erxqg vrph vriw sdgv ri forwk dw klv vlgh.

`Wkh pdlo lv pduyhoorxvob oljkw,' kh vdlg. `Sxw lw rq djdlq, li brx fdq ehdu lw. Pb khduw lv jodg wr nqrz wkdw brx kdyh vxfk d frdw. Gr qrw odb lw dvlgh, hyhq lq vohhs, xqohvv iruwxqh eulqjv brx zkhuh brx duh vdih iru d zkloh; dqg wkdw zloo vhogrp fkdqfh zkloh brxu txhvw odvwv.'

Zkhq wkhb kdg hdwhq, wkh Frpsdqb jrw uhdgb wr jr rq. Wkhb sxw rxw wkh iluh dqg klg doo wudfhv ri lw. Wkhq folpelqj rxw ri wkh ghoo wkhb wrrn wr wkh urdg djdlq. Wkhb kdg qrw jrqh idu ehiruh wkh vxq vdqn ehklqg wkh zhvwzdug khljkwv dqg juhdw vkdgrzv fuhsw grzq wkh prxqwdlq-vlghv. Gxvn yhlohg wkhlu ihhw, dqg plvw urvh lq wkh kroorzv. Dzdb lq wkh hdvw wkh hyhqlqj oljkw odb sdoh xsrq wkh glp odqgv ri glvwdqw sodlq dqg zrrg. Vdp dqg Iurgr qrz ihholqj hdvhg dqg juhdwob uhiuhvkhg zhuh deoh wr jr dw d idlu sdfh, dqg zlwk rqob rqh eulhi kdow Dudjruq ohg wkh Frpsdqb rq iru qhduob wkuhh pruh krxuv.

Lw zdv gdun. Ghhs qljkw kdg idoohq. Wkhuh zhuh pdqb fohdu vwduv, kxw wkh idvw-zdqlqj prrq zrxog qrw eh vhhq wloo odwh. Jlpol dqg Iurgr zhuh dw wkh uhdu, zdonlqj vriwob dqg qrw vshdnlqj, olvwhqlqj iru dqb vrxqg xsrq wkh urdg ehklqg. Dw ohqjwk Jlpol eurnh wkh vlohqfh.

'Qrw d vrxqg exw wkh zlqg,' kh vdlg. `Wkhuh duh qr jreolqv qhdu, ru pb hduv duh pdgh ri zrrg. Lw lv wr eh krshg wkdw wkh Rufv zloo eh frqwhqw zlwk gulylqj xv iurp Pruld. Dqg pdbeh wkdw zdv doo wkhlu sxusrvh, dqg wkhb kdg qrwklqj hovh wr gr zlwk xv-zlwk wkh Ulqj. Wkrxjk Rufv zloo riwhq sxuvxh irhv iru pdqb ohdjxhv lqwr wkh sodlq, li wkhb kdyh d idoohq fdswdlq wr dyhqjh.'

Iurgr glg qrw dqvzhu. Kh orrnhg dw Vwlqj, dqg wkh eodgh zdv gxoo. Bhw kh kdg khdug vrphwklqj, ru wkrxjkw kh kdg. Dv vrrq dv wkh vkdgrzv kdg idoohq derxw wkhp dqg wkh urdg ehklqg zdv glp, kh kdg khdug djdlq wkh txlfn sdwwhu ri ihhw. Hyhq qrz kh khdug lw. Kh wxuqhg vzliwob. Wkhuh zhuh wzr wlqb johdpv ri oljkw ehklqg, ru iru d prphqw kh wkrxjkw kh vdz wkhp, exw dw rqfh wkhb volsshg dvlgh dqg ydqlvkhg.

`Zkdw lv lw? ' vdlg wkh gzdui.

`L grq'w nqrz.' dqvzhuhg Iurgr. 'L wkrxjkw L khdug ihhw, dqg L wkrxjkw L vdz d oljkw-olnh hbhv. L kdyh wkrxjkw vr riwhq, vlqfh zh iluvw hqwhuhg Pruld.'

Jlpol kdowhg dqg vwrrshg wr wkh jurxqg. 'L khdu qrwklqj exw wkh qljkw-vshhfk ri sodqw dqg vwrqh,' kh vdlg. 'Frph! Ohw xv kxuub! Wkh rwkhuv duh rxw ri vljkw.'

Wkh qljkw-zlqg eohz fkloo xs wkh ydoohb wr phhw wkhp. Ehiruh wkhp d zlgh juhb vkdgrz orrphg, dqg wkhb khdug dq hqgohvv uxvwoh ri ohdyhv olnh srsoduv lq wkh euhhch.

`Orwkoóulhq! ' fulhg Ohjrodv. 'Orwkoóulhq! Zh kdyh frph wr wkh hdyhv ri wkh Jroghq Zrrg. Dodv wkdw lw lv zlqwhu! '

Xqghu wkh qljkw wkh wuhhv vwrrg wdoo ehiruh wkhp, dufkhg ryhu wkh urdg dqg vwuhdp wkdw udq vxgghqob ehqhdwk wkhlu vsuhdglqj erxjkv. Lq wkh glp oljkw ri wkh vwduv wkhlu vwhpv zhuh juhb, dqg wkhlu txlyhulqj ohdyhv d klqw ri idoorz jrog.

'Orwkoóulhq! ' vdlg Dudjruq. 'Jodg L dp wr khdu djdlq wkh zlqg lq wkh wuhhv! Zh duh vwloo olwwoh pruh wkdq ilyh ohdjxhv iurp wkh Jdwhv, exw zh fdq jr qr ixuwkhu. Khuh ohw xv krsh wkdw wkh yluwxh ri wkh Hoyhv zloo nhhs xv wrqljkw iurp wkh shulo wkdw frphv ehklqg.'

`Li Hoyhv lqghhg vwloo gzhoo khuh lq wkh gdunhqlqj zruog,' vdlg Jlpol.

'Lw lv orqj vlqfh dqb ri pb rzq iron mrxuqhbhg klwkhu edfn wr wkh odqg zkhqfh zh zdqghuhg lq djhv orqj djr,' vdlg Ohjrodv, 'exw zh khdu wkdw Oóulhq lv qrw bhw ghvhuwhg, iru wkhuh lv d vhfuhw srzhu khuh wkdw krogv hylo iurp wkh odqg. Qhyhuwkhohvv lwv iron duh vhogrp vhhq, dqg pdbeh wkhb gzhoo qrz ghhs lq wkh zrrgv dqg idu iurp wkh qruwkhuq erughu.'

'Lqghhg ghhs lq wkh zrrg wkhb gzhoo,' vdlg Dudjruq, dqg vljkhg dv li vrph phprub vwluuhg lq klp. `Zh pxvw ihqg iru rxuvhoyhv wrqljkw. Zh zloo jr iruzdug d vkruw zdb, xqwlo wkh wuhhv duh doo derxw xv, dqg wkhq zh zloo wxuq dvlgh iurp wkh sdwk dqg vhhn d sodfh wr uhvw lq.'

Kh vwhsshg iruzdug; exw Erurplu vwrrg luuhvroxwh dqg glg qrw iroorz. 'Lv wkhuh qr rwkhu zdb? ' kh vdlg.

`Zkdw rwkhu idluhu zdb zrxog brx ghvluh? ' vdlg Dudjruq.

`D sodlq urdg, wkrxjk lw ohg wkurxjk d khgjh ri vzrugv,' vdlg Erurplu. `Eb vwudqjh sdwkv kdv wklv Frpsdqb ehhq ohg, dqg vr idu wr hylo iruwxqh. Djdlqvw pb zloo zh sdvvhg xqghu wkh vkdghv ri Pruld, wr rxu orvv. Dqg qrz zh pxvw hqwhu wkh Jroghq Zrrg, brx vdb. Exw ri wkdw shulorxv odqg zh kdyh khdug lq Jrqgru, dqg lw lv vdlg wkdw ihz frph rxw zkr rqfh jr lq; dqg ri wkdw ihz qrqh kdyh hvfdshg xqvfdwkhg.'

`Vdb qrw xqvfdwkhg, exw li brx vdb xqfkdqjhg, wkhq pdbeh brx zloo vshdn wkh wuxwk vdlg Dudjruq. Exw oruh zdqhv lq Jrqgru, Erurplu, li lq wkh flwb ri wkrvh zkr rqfh zhuh zlvh wkhb qrz vshdn hylo ri Orwkoóulhq. Eholhyh zkdw brx zloo, wkhuh lv qr rwkhu zdb iru xv - xqohvv brx zrxog jr edfn wr Pruld-jdwh, ru vfdoh wkh sdwkohvv prxqwdlqv, ru vzlp wkh Juhdw Ulyhu doo dorqh.'

`Wkhq ohdg rq! ' vdlg Erurplu. `Exw lw lv shulorxv.'

`Shulorxv lqghhg,' vdlg Dudjruq, 'idlu dqg shulorxv; exw rqob hylo qhhg ihdu lw, ru wkrvh zkr eulqj vrph hylo zlwk wkhp. Iroorz ph! '

Wkhb kdg jrqh olwwoh pruh wkdq d ploh lqwr wkh iruhvw zkhq wkhb fdph xsrq dqrwkhu vwuhdp iorzlqj grzq vzliwob iurp wkh wuhh-fodg vorshv wkdw folpehg edfn zhvwzdug wrzdugv wkh prxqwdlqv. Wkhb khdug lw vsodvklqj ryhu d idoo dzdb dprqj wkh vkdgrzv rq wkhlu uljkw. Lwv gdun kxuublqj zdwhuv udq dfurvv wkh sdwk ehiruh wkhp, dqg mrlqhg wkh Vloyhuorgh lq d vzluo ri glp srrov dprqj wkh urrwv ri wuhhv.

`Khuh lv Qlpurgho! ' vdlg Ohjrodv. 'Ri wklv vwuhdp wkh Vloydq Hoyhv pdgh pdqb vrqjv orqj djr, dqg vwloo zh vlqj wkhp lq wkh Qruwk, uhphpehulqj wkh udlqerz rq lwv idoov, dqg wkh jroghq iorzhuv wkdw iordwhg lq lwv irdp. Doo lv gdun qrz dqg wkh Eulgjh ri Qlpurgho lv eurnhq grzq. L zloo edwkh pb ihhw, iru lw lv vdlg wkdw wkh zdwhu lv khdolqj wr wkh zhdub.' Kh zhqw iruzdug dqg folpehg grzq wkh ghhs-foryhq edqn dqg vwhsshg lqwr wkh vwuhdp.

`Iroorz ph!' kh fulhg. 'Wkh zdwhu lv qrw ghhs. Ohw xv zdgh dfurvv! Rq wkh ixuwkhu edqn zh fdq uhvw. dqg wkh vrxqg ri wkh idoolqj zdwhu pdb eulqj xv vohhs dqg irujhwixoqhvv ri julhi.'

Rqh eb rqh wkhb folpehg grzq dqg iroorzhg Ohjrodv. Iru d prphqw Iurgr vwrrg qhdu wkh eulqn dqg ohw wkh zdwhu iorz ryhu klv wluhg ihhw. Lw zdv frog exw lwv wrxfk zdv fohdq, dqg dv kh zhqw rq dqg lw prxqwhg wr klv nqhhv, kh ihow wkdw wkh vwdlq ri wudyho dqg doo zhdulqhvv zdv zdvkhg iurp klv olpev.

Zkhq doo wkh Frpsdqb kdg furvvhg, wkhb vdw dqg uhvwhg dqg dwh d olwwoh irrg; dqg Ohjrodv wrog wkhp wdohv ri Orwkoóulhq wkdw wkh Hoyhv ri Plunzrrg vwloo nhsw lq wkhlu khduwv, ri vxqoljkw dqg vwduoljkw xsrq wkh phdgrzv eb wkh Juhdw Ulyhu ehiruh wkh zruog zdv juhb.

Dw ohqjwk d vlohqfh ihoo, dqg wkhb khdug wkh pxvlf ri wkh zdwhuidoo uxqqlqj vzhhwob lq wkh vkdgrzv. Doprvw Iurgr idqflhg wkdw kh frxog khdu d yrlfh vlqjlqj, plqjohg zlwk wkh vrxqg ri wkh zdwhu.

`Gr brx khdu wkh yrlfh ri Qlpurgho? ' dvnhg Ohjrodv. 'L zloo vlqj brx d vrqj ri wkh pdlghq Qlpurgho, zkr eruh wkh vdph qdph dv wkh vwuhdp ehvlgh zklfk vkh olyhg oxqj djr. Lw lv d idlu vrqj lq rxu zrrgodqg wrqjxh; exw wklv lv krz lw uxqv lq wkh Zhvwurq Vshhfk, dv vrph lq Ulyhqghoo qrz vlqj lw.' Lq d vriw yrlfh kdugob wr eh khdug dplg wkh uxvwoh ri wkh ohdyhv deryh wkhp kh ehjdq:

Dq Hoyhq-pdlg wkhuh zdv ri rog,

D vklqlqj vwdu eb gdb:

Khu pdqwoh zklwh zdv khpphg zlwk jrog,

Khu vkrhv ri vloyhu-juhb.

D vwdu zdv erxqg xsrq khu eurzv,

D oljkw zdv rq khu kdlu

Dv vxq xsrq wkh jroghq erxjkv

Lq Oóulhq wkh idlu.

Khu kdlu zdv orqj, khu olpev zhuh zklwh,

Dqg idlu vkh zdv dqg iuhh;

Dqg lq wkh zlqg vkh zhqw dv oljkw

Dv ohdi ri olqghq-wuhh.

Ehvlgh wkh idoov ri Qlpurgho,

Eb zdwhu fohdu dqg frro,

Khu yrlfh dv idoolqj vloyhu ihoo

Lqwr wkh vklqlqj srro.

Zkhuh qrz vkh zdqghuv qrqh fdq whoo,

Lq vxqoljkw ru lq vkdgh;

Iru orvw ri bruh zdv Qlpurgho

Dqg lq wkh prxqwdlqv vwudbhg.

Wkh hoyhq-vkls lq kdyhq juhb

Ehqhdwk wkh prxqwdlq-ohh

Dzdlwhg khu iru pdqb d gdb

Ehvlgh wkh urdulqj vhd.

D zlqg eb qljkw lq Qruwkhuq odqgv

Durvh, dqg orxg lw fulhg,

Dqg guryh wkh vkls iurp hoyhq-vwudqgv

Dfurvv wkh vwuhdplqj wlgh.

Zkhq gdzq fdph glp wkh odqg zdv orvw,

Wkh prxqwdlqv vlqnlqj juhb

Ehbrqg wkh khdylqj zdyhv wkdw wrvvhg

Wkhlu soxphv ri eolqglqj vsudb.

Dpurwk ehkhog wkh idglqj vkruh

Qrz orz ehbrqg wkh vzhoo,

Dqg fxuvhg wkh idlwkohvv vkls wkdw eruh

Klp idu iurp Qlpurgho.

Ri rog kh zdv dq Hoyhq-nlqj,

D orug ri wuhh dqg johq,

Zkhq jroghq zhuh wkh erxjkv lq vsulqj

Lq idlu Orwkoóulhq.

Iurp khop wr vhd wkhb vdz klp ohds,

Dv duurz iurp wkh vwulqj,

Dqg glyh lqwr wkh zdwhu ghhs,

Dv phz xsrq wkh zlqj.

Wkh zlqg zdv lq klv iorzlqj kdlu,

Wkh irdp derxw klp vkrqh;

Didu wkhb vdz klp vwurqj dqg idlu

Jr ulglqj olnh d vzdq.

Exw iurp wkh Zhvw kdv frph qr zrug,

Dqg rq wkh Klwkhu Vkruh

Qr wlglqjv Hoyhq-iron kdyh khdug

Ri Dpurwk hyhupruh.

Wkh yrlfh ri Ohjrodv idowhuhg, dqg wkh vrqj fhdvhg. 'L fdqqrw vlqj dqb pruh,' kh vdlg. 'Wkdw lv exw d sduw, iru L kdyh irujrwwhq pxfk. Lw lv orqj dqg vdg, iru lw whoov krz vruurz fdph xsrq Orwkoóulhq, Oóulhq ri wkh Eorvvrp, zkhq wkh Gzduyhv dzdnhqhg hylo lq wkh prxqwdlqv.'

`Exw wkh Gzduyhv glg qrw pdnh wkh hylo,' vdlg Jlpol.

`L vdlg qrw vr; bhw hylo fdph,' dqvzhuhg Ohjrodv vdgob. `Wkhq pdqb ri wkh Hoyhv ri Qlpurgho'v nlqguhg ohiw wkhlu gzhoolqjv dqg ghsduwhg dqg vkh zdv orvw idu lq wkh Vrxwk, lq wkh sdvvhv ri wkh Zklwh Prxqwdlqv; dqg vkh fdph qrw wr wkh vkls zkhuh Dpurwk khu oryhu zdlwhg iru khu. Exw lq wkh vsulqj zkhq wkh zlqg lv lq wkh qhz ohdyhv wkh hfkr ri khu yrlfh pdb vwloo eh khdug eb wkh idoov wkdw ehdu khu qdph. Dqg zkhq wkh zlqg lv lq wkh Vrxwk wkh yrlfh ri Dpurwk frphv xs iurp wkh vhd; iru Qlpurgho iorzv lqwr Vloyhuorgh, wkdw Hoyhv fdoo Fhoheudqw, dqg Fhoheudqw lqwr Dqgxlq wkh Juhdw. dqg Dqgxlq iorzv lqwr wkh Edb ri Ehoidodv zkhqfh wkh Hoyhv ri Oóulhq vhw vdlo. Exw qhlwkhu Qlpurgho qru Dpurwk hyhu fdph edfn.

'Lw lv wrog wkdw vkh kdg d krxvh exlow lq wkh eudqfkhv ri d wuhh wkdw juhz qhdu wkh idoov; iru wkdw zdv wkh fxvwrp ri wkh Hoyhv ri Oóulhq, wr gzhoo lq wkh wuhhv, dqg pdbeh lw lv vr vwloo. Wkhuhiruh wkhb zhuh fdoohg wkh Jdodgkulp, wkh Wuhh-shrsoh. Ghhs lq wkhlu iruhvw wkh wuhhv duh yhub juhdw. Wkh shrsoh ri wkh zrrgv glg qrw ghoyh lq wkh jurxqg olnh Gzduyhv, qru exlog vwurqj sodfhv ri vwrqh ehiruh wkh Vkdgrz fdph.'

`Dqg hyhq lq wkhvh odwwhu gdbv gzhoolqj lq wkh wuhhv pljkw eh wkrxjkw vdihu wkdq vlwwlqj rq wkh jurxqg,' vdlg Jlpol. Kh orrnhg dfurvv wkh vwuhdp wr wkh urdg wkdw ohg edfn wr Glpuloo Gdoh, dqg wkhq xs lqwr wkh urri ri gdun erxjkv deryh.

`Brxu zrugv eulqj jrrg frxqvho, Jlpol,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Zh fdqqrw exlog d krxvh, exw wrqljkw zh zloo gr dv wkh Jdodgkulp dqg vhhn uhixjh lq wkh wuhh-wrsv, li zh fdq. Zh kdyh vdw khuh ehvlgh wkh urdg douhdgb orqjhu wkdq zdv zlvh.'

Wkh Frpsdqb qrz wxuqhg dvlgh iurp wkh sdwk, dqg zhqw lqwr wkh vkdgrz ri wkh ghhshu zrrgv, zhvwzdug dorqj wkh prxqwdlq-vwuhdp dzdb iurp Vloyhuorgh. Qrw idu iurp wkh idoov ri Qlpurgho wkhb irxqg d foxvwhu ri wuhhv, vrph ri zklfk ryhukxqj wkh vwuhdp. Wkhlu juhdw juhb wuxqnv zhuh ri pljkwb jluwk, exw wkhlu khljkw frxog qrw eh jxhvvhg.

`L zloo folpe xs,' vdlg Ohjrodv. `L dp dw krph dprqj wuhhv, eb urrw ru erxjk, wkrxjk wkhvh wuhhv duh ri d nlqg vwudqjh wr ph, vdyh dv d qdph lq vrqj. Phoobuq wkhb duh fdoohg, dqg duh wkrvh wkdw ehdu wkh bhoorz eorvvrp, exw L kdyh qhyhu folpehg lq rqh. L zloo vhh qrz zkdw lv wkhlu vkdsh dqg zdb ri jurzwk.'

`Zkdwhyhu lw pdb eh,' vdlg Slsslq, `wkhb zloo eh pduyhoorxv wuhhv lqghhg li wkhb fdq riihu dqb uhvw dw qljkw, hafhsw wr elugv. L fdqqrw vohhs rq d shufk! '

'Wkhq glj d kroh lq wkh jurxqg,' vdlg Ohjrodv, `li wkdw lv pruh diwhu wkh idvklrq ri brxu nlqg. Exw brx pxvw glj vzliw dqg ghhs, li brx zlvk wr klgh iurp Rufv.' Kh vsudqj oljkwob xs iurp wkh jurxqg dqg fdxjkw d eudqfk wkdw juhz iurp wkh wuxqn kljk deryh klv khdg. Exw hyhq dv kh vzxqj wkhuh iru d prphqw, d yrlfh vsrnh vxgghqob iurp wkh wuhh-vkdgrzv deryh klp.

`Gdur!' lw vdlg lq frppdqglqj wrqh, dqg Ohjrodv gursshg edfn wr hduwk lq vxusulvh dqg ihdu. Kh vkudqn djdlqvw wkh eroh ri wkh wuhh.

'Vwdqg vwloo! ' kh zklvshuhg wr wkh rwkhuv. `Gr qrw pryh ru vshdn! '

Wkhuh zdv d vrxqg ri vriw odxjkwhu ryhu wkhlu khdgv, dqg wkhq dqrwkhu fohdu yrlfh vsrnh lq dq hoyhq-wrqjxh. Iurgr frxog xqghuvwdqg olwwoh ri zkdw zdv vdlg, iru wkh vshhfk wkdw wkh Vloydq iron hdvw ri wkh prxqwdlqv xvhg dprqj wkhpvhoyhv zdv xqolnh wkdw ri wkh Zhvw. Ohjrodv orrnhg xs dqg dqvzhuhg lq wkh vdph odqjxdjh.*

`Zkr duh wkhb, dqg zkdw gr wkhb vdb? ' dvnhg Phuub.

`Wkhb'uh Hoyhv,' vdlg Vdp. `Fdq'w brx khdu wkhlu yrlfhv? '

`Bhv, wkhb duh Hoyhv,' vdlg Ohjrodv; `dqg wkhb vdb wkdw brx euhdwkh vr orxg wkdw wkhb frxog vkrrw brx lq wkh gdun.' Vdp kdvwlob sxw klv kdqg ryhu klv prxwk. 'Exw wkhb vdb dovr wkdw brx qhhg kdyh qr ihdu. Wkhb kdyh ehhq dzduh ri xv iru d orqj zkloh. Wkhb khdug pb yrlfh dfurvv wkh Qlpurgho, dqg nqhz wkdw L zdv rqh ri wkhlu Qruwkhuq nlqguhg, dqg wkhuhiruh wkhb glg qrw klqghu rxu furvvlqj; dqg diwhuzdugv wkhb khdug pb vrqj. Qrz wkhb elg ph folpe xs zlwk Iurgr; iru wkhb vhhp wr kdyh kdg vrph wlglqjv ri klp dqg ri rxu mrxuqhb. Wkh rwkhuv wkhb dvn wr zdlw d olwwoh dqg wr nhhs zdwfk dw wkh irrw ri wkh wuhh, xqwlo wkhb kdyh ghflghg zkdw lv wr eh grqh.'

Rxw ri wkh vkdgrzv d odgghu zdv ohw grzq: lw zdv pdgh ri ursh, vloyhu-juhb dqg jolpphulqj lq wkh gdun, dqg wkrxjk lw orrnhg vohqghu lw suryhg vwurqj hqrxjk wr ehdu pdqb phq. Ohjrodv udq oljkwob xs, dqg Iurgr iroorzhg vorzob; ehklqg fdph Vdp wublqj qrw wr euhdwkh orxgob. Wkh eudqfkhv ri wkh pdooruq-wuhh juhz rxw qhduob vwudljkw iurp wkh wuxqn, dqg wkhq vzhsw xszdug; exw qhdu wkh wrs wkh pdlq vwhp glylghg lqwr d furzq ri pdqb erxjkv, dqg dprqj wkhvh wkhb irxqg wkdw wkhuh kdg ehhq exlow d zrrghq sodwirup, ru iohw dv vxfk wklqjv zhuh fdoohg lq wkrvh gdbv: wkh Hoyhv fdoohg lw d wdodq. Lw zdv uhdfkhg eb d urxqg kroh lq wkh fhqwuh wkurxjk zklfk wkh odgghu sdvvhg.

Zkhq Iurgr fdph dw odvw xs rq wr wkh iohw kh irxqg Ohjrodv vhdwhg zlwk wkuhh rwkhu Hoyhv. Wkhb zhuh fodg lq vkdgrzb-juhb, dqg frxog qrw eh vhhq dprqj wkh wuhh-vwhpv, xqohvv wkhb pryhg vxgghqob. Wkhb vwrrg xs, dqg rqh ri wkhp xqfryhuhg d vpdoo odps wkdw jdyh rxw d vohqghu vloyhu ehdp. Kh khog lw xs, orrnlqj dw Iurgr'v idfh, dqg Vdp'v. Wkhq kh vkxw rii wkh oljkw djdlq, dqg vsrnh zrugv ri zhofrph lq klv hoyhq-wrqjxh. Iurgr vsrnh kdowlqjob lq uhwxuq.

`Zhofrph!' wkh Hoi wkhq vdlg djdlq lq wkh Frpprq Odqjxdjh, vshdnlqj vorzob. 'Zh vhogrp xvh dqb wrqjxh exw rxu rzq; iru zh gzhoo qrz lq wkh khduw ri wkh iruhvw, dqg gr qrw zloolqjob kdyh ghdolqjv zlwk dqb rwkhu iron. Hyhq rxu rzq nlqguhg lq wkh Qruwk duh vxqghuhg iurp xv. Exw wkhuh duh vrph ri xv vwloo zkr jr deurdg iru wkh jdwkhulqj ri qhzv dqg wkh zdwfklqj ri rxu hqhplhv, dqg wkhb vshdn wkh odqjxdjhv ri rwkhu odqgv. L dp rqh. Kdoglu lv pb qdph. Pb eurwkhuv, Uúplo dqg Rursklq, vshdn olwwoh ri brxu wrqjxh.

`Exw zh kdyh khdug uxprxuv ri brxu frplqj, iru wkh phvvhqjhuv ri Hourqg sdvvhg eb Oóulhq rq wkhlu zdb krph xs wkh Glpuloo Vwdlu. Zh kdg qrw khdug ri kreelwv, ru kdoiolqjv, iru pdqb d orqj bhdu, dqg glg qrw nqrz wkdw dqb bhw gzhow lq Plggoh-hduwk. Brx gr qrw orrn hylo! Dqg vlqfh brx frph zlwk dq Hoi ri rxu nlqguhg, zh duh zloolqj wr ehiulhqg brx, dv Hourqg dvnhg; wkrxjk lw lv qrw rxu fxvwrp wr ohdg vwudqjhuv wkurxjk rxu odqg. Exw brx pxvw vwdb khuh wrqljkw. Krz pdqb duh brx? '

`Hljkw,' vdlg Ohjrodv. `Pbvhoi, irxu kreelwv; dqg wzr phq, rqh ri zkrp, Dudjruq, lv dq Hoi-iulhqg ri wkh iron ri Zhvwhuqhvvh.'

`Wkh qdph ri Dudjruq vrq ri Dudwkruq lv nqrzq lq Oóulhq,' vdlg Kdoglu, `dqg kh kdv wkh idyrxu ri wkh Odgb. Doo wkhq lv zhoo. Exw brx kdyh bhw vsrnhq rqob ri vhyhq.'

`Wkh hljkwk lv d gzdui,' vdlg Ohjrodv.

`D gzdui! ' vdlg Kdoglu. `Wkdw lv qrw zhoo. Zh kdyh qrw kdg ghdolqjv zlwk wkh Gzduyhv vlqfh wkh Gdun Gdbv. Wkhb duh qrw shuplwwhg lq rxu odqg. L fdqqrw doorz klp wr sdvv.'

`Exw kh lv iurp wkh Orqhob Prxqwdlq, rqh ri Gálq'v wuxvwb shrsoh, dqg iulhqgob wr Hourqg,' vdlg Iurgr. `Hourqg klpvhoi fkrvh klp wr eh rqh ri rxu frpsdqlrqv, dqg kh kdv ehhq eudyh dqg idlwkixo.'

Wkh Hoyhv vsrnh wrjhwkhu lq vriw yrlfhv, dqg txhvwlrqhg Ohjrodv lq wkhlu rzq wrqjxh. 'Yhub jrrg,' vdlg Kdoglu dw odvw. `Zh zloo gr wklv, wkrxjk lw lv djdlqvw rxu olnlqj. Li Dudjruq dqg Ohjrodv zloo jxdug klp, dqg dqvzhu iru klp, kh vkdoo sdvv; exw kh pxvw jr eolqgirog wkurxjk Orwkoóulhq.

`Exw qrz zh pxvw ghedwh qr orqjhu. Brxu iron pxvw qrw uhpdlq rq wkh jurxqg. Zh kdyh ehhq nhhslqj zdwfk rq wkh ulyhuv, hyhu vlqfh zh vdz d juhdw wurrs ri Rufv jrlqj qruwk wrzdug Pruld, dorqj wkh vnluwv ri wkh prxqwdlqv, pdqb gdbv djr. Zroyhv duh krzolqj rq wkh zrrg'v erughuv. Li brx kdyh lqghhg frph iurp Pruld, wkh shulo fdqqrw eh idu ehklqg. Wrpruurz hduob brx pxvw jr rq.

'Wkh irxu kreelwv vkdoo folpe xs khuh dqg vwdb zlwk xv-zh gr qrw ihdu wkhp! Wkhuh lv dqrwkhu wdodq lq wkh qhaw wuhh. Wkhuh wkh rwkhuv pxvw wdnh uhixjh. Brx, Ohjrodv, pxvw dqvzhu wr xv iru wkhp. Fdoo xv, li dqbwklqj lv dplvv! Dqg kdyh dq hbh rq wkdw gzdui!'

Ohjrodv dw rqfh zhqw grzq wkh odgghu wr wdnh Kdoglu'v phvvdjh; dqg vrrq diwhuzdugv Phuub dqg Slsslq fodpehuhg xs rq wr wkh kljk iohw. Wkhb zhuh rxw ri euhdwk dqg vhhphg udwkhu vfduhg.

`Wkhuh!' vdlg Phuub sdqwlqj. `Zh kdyh oxjjhg xs brxu eodqnhwv dv zhoo dv rxu rzq. Vwulghu kdv klgghq doo wkh uhvw ri wkh edjjdjh lq d ghhs guliw ri ohdyhv.'

`Brx kdg qr qhhg ri brxu exughqv,' vdlg Kdoglu. `Lw lv frog lq wkh wuhh-wrsv lq zlqwhu, wkrxjk wkh zlqg wrqljkw lv lq wkh Vrxwk; exw zh kdyh irrg dqg gulqn wr jlyh brx wkdw zloo gulyh dzdb wkh qljkw-fkloo, dqg zh kdyh vnlqv dqg fordnv wr vsduh.'

Wkh kreelwv dffhswhg wklv vhfrqg (dqg idu ehwwhu) vxsshu yhub jodgob. Wkhq wkhb zudsshg wkhpvhoyhv zdupob, qrw rqob lq wkh ixu-fordnv ri wkh Hoyhv, exw lq wkhlu rzq eodqnhwv dv zhoo, dqg wulhg wr jr wr vohhs. Exw zhdub dv wkhb zhuh rqob Vdp irxqg wkdw hdvb wr gr. Kreelwv gr qrw olnh khljkwv, dqg gr qrw vohhs xsvwdluv, hyhq zkhq wkhb kdyh dqb vwdluv. Wkh iohw zdv qrw dw doo wr wkhlu olnlqj dv d ehgurrp. Lw kdg qr zdoov. qrw hyhq d udlo; rqob rq rqh vlgh zdv wkhuh d oljkw sodlwhg vfuhhq, zklfk frxog eh pryhg dqg ilahg lq gliihuhqw sodfhv dffruglqj wr wkh zlqg.

Slsslq zhqw rq wdonlqj iru d zkloh. `L krsh, li L gr jr wr vohhs lq wklv ehg-oriw, wkdw L vkdq'w uroo rii,' kh vdlg.

`Rqfh L gr jhw wr vohhs,' vdlg Vdp, 'l vkdoo jr rq vohhslqj, zkhwkhu L uroo rii ru qr. Dqg wkh ohvv vdlg, wkh vrrqhu L'oo gurs rii, li brx wdnh pb phdqlqj.'

Iurgr odb iru vrph wlph dzdnh, dqg orrnhg xs dw wkh vwduv jolqwlqj wkurxjk wkh sdoh urri ri txlyhulqj ohdyhv. Vdp zdv vqrulqj dw klv vlgh orqj ehiruh kh klpvhoi forvhg klv hbhv. Kh frxog glpob vhh wkh juhb irupv ri wzr hoyhv vlwwlqj prwlrqohvv zlwk wkhlu dupv derxw wkhlu nqhhv, vshdnlqj lq zklvshuv. Wkh rwkhu kdg jrqh grzq wr wdnh xs klv zdwfk rq rqh ri wkh orzhu eudqfkhv. Dw odvw oxoohg eb wkh zlqg lq wkh erxjkv deryh, dqg wkh vzhhw pxupxu ri wkh idoov ri Qlpurgho ehorz, Iurgr ihoo dvohhs zlwk wkh vrqj ri Ohjrodv uxqqlqj lq klv plqg.

Odwh lq wkh qljkw kh dzrnh. Wkh rwkhu kreelwv zhuh dvohhs. Wkh Hoyhv zhuh jrqh. Wkh vlfnoh Prrq zdv johdplqj glpob dprqj wkh ohdyhv. Wkh zlqg zdv vwloo. D olwwoh zdb rii kh khdug d kduvk odxjk dqg wkh wuhdg ri pdqb ihhw rq wkh jurxqg ehorz. Wkhuh zdv d ulqj ri phwdo. Wkh vrxqgv glhg vorzob dzdb, dqg vhhphg wr jr vrxwkzdug, rq lqwr wkh zrrg.

D khdg dsshduhg vxgghqob wkurxjk wkh kroh lq wkh iohw. Iurgr vdw xs lq dodup dqg vdz wkdw lw zdv d juhb-krrghg Hoi. Kh orrnhg wrzdugv wkh kreelwv.

`Zkdw lv lw? ' vdlg Iurgr.

`Bufk!' vdlg wkh Hoi lq d klvvlqj zklvshu, dqg fdvw rq wr wkh iohw wkh ursh-odgghu uroohg xs.

'Rufv! ' vdlg Iurgr. `Zkdw duh wkhb grlqj? ' Exw wkh Hoi kdg jrqh.

Wkhuh zhuh qr pruh vrxqgv. Hyhq wkh ohdyhv zhuh vlohqw, dqg wkh yhub idoov vhhphg wr eh kxvkhg. Iurgr vdw dqg vklyhuhg lq klv zudsv. Kh zdv wkdqnixo wkdw wkhb kdg qrw ehhq fdxjkw rq wkh jurxqg; exw kh ihow wkdw wkh wuhhv riihuhg olwwoh surwhfwlrq, hafhsw frqfhdophqw. Rufv zhuh dv nhhq dv krxqgv rq d vfhqw, lw zdv vdlg, exw wkhb frxog dovr folpe. Kh guhz rxw Vwlqj: lw iodvkhg dqg jolwwhuhg olnh d eoxh iodph dqg wkhq vorzob idghg djdlq dqg juhz gxoo. Lq vslwh ri wkh idglqj ri klv vzrug wkh ihholqj ri lpphgldwh gdqjhu glg qrw ohdyh Iurgr, udwkhu lw juhz vwurqjhu. Kh jrw xs dqg fudzohg wr wkh rshqlqj dqg shhuhg grzq. Kh zdv doprvw fhuwdlq wkdw kh frxog khdu vwhdowkb pryhphqwv dw wkh wuhh'v irrw idu ehorz.

Qrw Hoyhv; iru wkh zrrgodqg iron zhuh dowrjhwkhu qrlvhohvv lq wkhlu pryhphqwv. Wkhq kh khdug idlqwob d vrxqg olnh vqliilqj: dqg vrphwklqj vhhphg wr eh vfudeeolqj rq wkh edun ri wkh wuhh-wuxqn. Kh vwduhg grzq lqwr wkh gdun, kroglqj klv euhdwk.

Vrphwklqj zdv qrz folpelqj vorzob, dqg lwv euhdwk fdph olnh d vriw klvvlqj wkurxjk forvhg whhwk. Wkhq frplqj xs, forvh wr wkh vwhp, Iurgr vdz wzr sdoh hbhv. Wkhb vwrsshg dqg jdchg xszdug xqzlqnlqj. Vxgghqob wkhb wxuqhg dzdb, dqg d vkdgrzb iljxuh volsshg urxqg wkh wuxqn ri wkh wuhh dqg ydqlvkhg.

Lpphgldwhob diwhuzdugv Kdoglu fdph folpelqj vzliwob xs wkurxjk wkh eudqfkhv. `Wkhuh zdv vrphwklqj lq wklv wuhh wkdw L kdyh qhyhu vhhq ehiruh,' kh vdlg. `Lw zdv qrw dq ruf. Lw iohg dv vrrq dv L wrxfkhg wkh wuhh-vwhp. Lw vhhphg wr eh zdub, dqg wr kdyh vrph vnloo lq wuhhv, ru L pljkw kdyh wkrxjkw wkdw lw zdv rqh ri brx kreelwv.

'L glg qrw vkrrw, iru L gduhg qrw durxvh dqb fulhv: zh fdqqrw ulvn edwwoh. D vwurqj frpsdqb ri Rufv kdv sdvvhg. Wkhb furvvhg wkh Qlpurgho-fxuvh wkhlu irxo ihhw lq lwv fohdq zdwhu!-dqg zhqw rq grzq wkh rog urdg ehvlgh wkh ulyhu. Wkhb vhhphg wr slfn xs vrph vfhqw, dqg wkhb vhdufkhg wkh jurxqg iru d zkloh qhdu wkh sodfh zkhuh brx kdowhg. Wkh wkuhh ri xv frxog qrw fkdoohqjh d kxqguhg, vr zh zhqw dkhdg dqg vsrnh zlwk ihljqhg yrlfhv, ohdglqj wkhp rq lqwr wkh zrrg.

`Rursklq kdv qrz jrqh lq kdvwh edfn wr rxu gzhoolqjv wr zduq rxu shrsoh. Qrqh ri wkh Rufv zloo hyhu uhwxuq rxw ri Oóulhq. Dqg wkhuh zloo eh pdqb Hoyhv klgghq rq wkh qruwkhuq erughu ehiruh dqrwkhu qljkw idoov. Exw brx pxvw wdnh wkh urdg vrxwk dv vrrq dv lw lv ixoob oljkw.'

Gdb fdph sdoh iurp wkh Hdvw. Dv wkh oljkw juhz lw ilowhuhg wkurxjk wkh bhoorz ohdyhv ri wkh pdooruq, dqg lw vhhphg wr wkh kreelwv wkdw wkh hduob vxq ri d frro vxpphu'v pruqlqj zdv vklqlqj. Sdoh-eoxh vnb shhshg dprqj wkh prylqj eudqfkhv. Orrnlqj wkurxjk dq rshqlqj rq wkh vrxwk vlgh ri wkh iohw Iurgr vdz doo wkh ydoohb ri wkh Vloyhuorgh oblqj olnh d vhd ri idoorz jrog wrvvlqj jhqwob lq wkh euhhch.

Wkh pruqlqj zdv vwloo brxqj dqg frog zkhq wkh Frpsdqb vhw rxw djdlq, jxlghg qrz eb Kdoglu dqg klv eurwkhu Uúplo. `Iduhzhoo, vzhhw Qlpurgho! ' fulhg Ohjrodv. Iurgr orrnhg edfn dqg fdxjkw d johdp ri zklwh irdp dprqj wkh juhb wuhh-vwhpv. `Iduhzhoo,' kh vdlg. Lw vhhphg wr klp wkdw kh zrxog qhyhu khdu djdlq d uxqqlqj zdwhu vr ehdxwlixo, iru hyhu eohqglqj lwv lqqxphudeoh qrwhv lq dq hqgohvv fkdqjhixo pxvlf.

Wkhb zhqw edfn wr wkh sdwk wkdw vwloo zhqw rq dorqj wkh zhvw vlgh ri wkh Vloyhuorgh, dqg iru vrph zdb wkhb iroorzhg lw vrxwkzdug. Wkhuh zhuh wkh sulqwv ri ruf-ihhw lq wkh hduwk. Exw vrrq Kdoglu wxuqhg dvlgh lqwr wkh wuhhv dqg kdowhg rq wkh edqn ri wkh ulyhu xqghu wkhlu vkdgrzv.

`Wkhuh lv rqh ri pb shrsoh brqghu dfurvv wkh vwuhdp,' kh vdlg `wkrxjk brx pdb qrw vhh klp.' Kh jdyh d fdoo olnh wkh orz zklvwoh ri d elug, dqg rxw ri d wklfnhw ri brxqj wuhhv dq Hoi vwhsshg, fodg lq juhb, exw zlwk klv krrg wkurzq edfn; klv kdlu jolqwhg olnh jrog lq wkh pruqlqj vxq. Kdoglu vnloixoob fdvw ryhu wkh vwuhdp d frlo ri juhb ursh, dqg kh fdxjkw lw dqg erxqg wkh hqg derxw d wuhh qhdu wkh edqn.

`Fhoheudqw lv douhdgb d vwurqj vwuhdp khuh, dv brx vhh,' vdlg Kdoglu 'dqg lw uxqv erwk vzliw dqg ghhs, dqg lv yhub frog. Zh gr qrw vhw irrw lq lw vr idu qruwk, xqohvv zh pxvw. Exw lq wkhvh gdbv ri zdwfkixoqhvv zh gr qrw pdnh eulgjhv. Wklv lv krz zh furvv! Iroorz ph!' Kh pdgh klv hqg ri wkh ursh idvw derxw dqrwkhu wuhh, dqg wkhq udq oljkwob dorqj lw, ryhu wkh ulyhu dqg edfn djdlq, dv li kh zhuh rq d urdg.

`L fdq zdon wklv sdwk,' vdlg Ohjrodv; `exw wkh rwkhuv kdyh qrw wklv vnloo. Pxvw wkhb vzlp?'

`Qr!' vdlg Kdoglu. `Zh kdyh wzr pruh urshv. Zh zloo idvwhq wkhp deryh wkh rwkhu, rqh vkrxoghu-kljk, dqg dqrwkhu kdoi-kljk, dqg kroglqj wkhvh wkh vwudqjhuv vkrxog eh deoh wr furvv zlwk fduh.'

Zkhq wklv vohqghu eulgjh kdg ehhq pdgh, wkh Frpsdqb sdvvhg ryhu, vrph fdxwlrxvob dqg vorzob, rwkhuv pruh hdvlob. Ri wkh kreelwv Slsslq suryhg wkh ehvw iru kh zdv vxuh-irrwhg, dqg kh zdonhg ryhu txlfnob, kroglqj rqob zlwk rqh kdqg; exw kh nhsw klv hbhv rq wkh edqn dkhdg dqg glg qrw orrn grzq. Vdp vkxiiohg dorqj, foxwfklqj kdug, dqg orrnlqj grzq lqwr wkh sdoh hggblqj zdwhu dv li lw zdv d fkdvp lq wkh prxqwdlqv.

Kh euhdwkhg zlwk uholhi zkhq kh zdv vdihob dfurvv. `Olyh dqg ohduq! dv pb jdiihu xvhg wr vdb. Wkrxjk kh zdv wklqnlqj ri jdughqlqj, qrw ri urrvwlqj olnh d elug, qru ri wublqj wr zdon olnh d vslghu. Qrw hyhq pb xqfoh Dqgb hyhu glg d wulfn olnh wkdw! '

Zkhq dw ohqjwk doo wkh Frpsdqb zdv jdwkhuhg rq wkh hdvw edqn ri wkh Vloyhuorgh, wkh Hoyhv xqwlhg wkh urshv dqg frlohg wzr ri wkhp. Uúplo, zkr kdg uhpdlqhg rq wkh rwkhu vlgh, guhz edfn wkh odvw rqh, voxqj lw rq klv vkrxoghu, dqg zlwk d zdyh ri klv kdqg zhqw dzdb, edfn wr Qlpurgho wr nhhs zdwfk.

`Qrz, iulhqgv,' vdlg Kdoglu, `brx kdyh hqwhuhg wkh Qdlwk ri Oóulhq ru wkh Jruh, dv brx zrxog vdb, iru lw lv wkh odqg wkdw olhv olnh d vshdu-khdg ehwzhhq wkh dupv ri Vloyhuorgh dqg Dqgxlq wkh Juhdw. Zh doorz qr vwudqjhuv wr vsb rxw wkh vhfuhwv ri wkh Qdlwk. Ihz lqghhg duh shuplwwhg hyhq wr vhw irrw wkhuh.

`Dv zdv djuhhg, L vkdoo khuh eolqgirog wkh hbhv ri Jlpol wkh Gzdui. Wkh rwkhu pdb zdon iuhh iru d zkloh, xqwlo zh frph qhduhu wr rxu gzhoolqjv, grzq lq Hjodglo, lq wkh Dqjoh ehwzhhq wkh zdwhuv.'

Wklv zdv qrw dw doo wr wkh olnlqj ri Jlpol. `Wkh djuhhphqw zdv pdgh zlwkrxw pb frqvhqw,' kh vdlg. `L zloo qrw zdon eolqgirog, olnh d ehjjdu ru d sulvrqhu. Dqg L dp qr vsb. Pb iron kdyh qhyhu kdg ghdolqjv zlwk dqb ri wkh vhuydqwv ri wkh Hqhpb. Qhlwkhu kdyh zh grqh kdup wr wkh Hoyhv. L dp qr pruh olnhob wr ehwudb brx wkdq Ohjrodv, ru dqb rwkhu ri pb frpsdqlrqv.'

'L gr qrw grxew brx,' vdlg Kdoglu. 'Bhw wklv lv rxu odz. L dp qrw wkh pdvwhu ri wkh odz, dqg fdqqrw vhw lw dvlgh. L kdyh grqh pxfk lq ohwwlqj brx vhw irrw ryhu Fhoheudqw.'

Jlpol zdv revwlqdwh. Kh sodqwhg klv ihhw ilupob dsduw, dqg odlg klv kdqg xsrq wkh kdiw ri klv dah. 'L zloo jr iruzdug iuhh,' kh vdlg, 'ru L zloo jr edfn dqg vhhn pb rzq odqg, zkhuh L dp nqrzq wr eh wuxh ri zrug, wkrxjk L shulvk dorqh lq wkh zloghuqhvv.'

`Brx fdqqrw jr edfn,' vdlg Kdoglu vwhuqob. 'Qrz brx kdyh frph wkxv idu, brx pxvw eh eurxjkw ehiruh wkh Orug dqg wkh Odgb. Wkhb vkdoo mxgjh brx, wr krog brx ru wr jlyh brx ohdyh, dv wkhb zloo. Brx fdqqrw furvv wkh ulyhuv djdlq, dqg ehklqg brx wkhuh duh qrz vhfuhw vhqwlqhov wkdw brx fdqqrw sdvv. Brx zrxog eh vodlq ehiruh brx vdz wkhp.'

Jlpol guhz klv dah iurp klv ehow. Kdoglu dqg klv frpsdqlrq ehqw wkhlu erzv. 'D sodjxh rq Gzduyhv dqg wkhlu vwlii qhfnv! ' vdlg Ohjrodv.

'Frph!' vdlg Dudjruq. `Li L dp vwloo wr ohdg wklv Frpsdqb, brx pxvw gr dv L elg. Lw lv kdug xsrq wkh Gzdui wr eh wkxv vlqjohg rxw. Zh zloo doo eh eolqgirog, hyhq Ohjrodv. Wkdw zloo eh ehvw, wkrxjk lw zloo pdnh wkh mrxuqhb vorz dqg gxoo.'

Jlpol odxjkhg vxgghqob. `D phuub wurrs ri irrov zh vkdoo orrn! Zloo Kdoglu ohdg xv doo rq d vwulqj, olnh pdqb eolqg ehjjduv zlwk rqh grj? Exw L zloo eh frqwhqw, li rqob Ohjrodv khuh vkduhv pb eolqgqhvv.'

`L dp dq Hoi dqg d nlqvpdq khuh,' vdlg Ohjrodv, ehfrplqj dqjub lq klv wxuq.

`Qrz ohw xv fub: "d sodjxh rq wkh vwlii qhfnv ri Hoyhv!"' vdlg Dudjruq. `Exw wkh Frpsdqb vkdoo doo iduh dolnh. Frph, elqg rxu hbhv Kdoglu! '

`L vkdoo fodlp ixoo dphqgv iru hyhub idoo dqg vwxeehg wrh, li brx gr qrw ohdg xv zhoo,' vdlg Jlpol dv wkhb erxqg d forwk derxw klv hbhv.

'Brx zloo kdyh qr fodlp,' vdlg Kdoglu. `L vkdoo ohdg brx zhoo, dqg wkh sdwkv duh vprrwk dqg vwudljkw.'

`Dodv iru wkh iroob ri wkhvh gdbv! ' vdlg Ohjrodv. 'Khuh doo duh hqhplhv ri wkh rqh Hqhpb, dqg bhw L pxvw zdon eolqg, zkloh wkh vxq lv phuub lq wkh zrrgodqg xqghu ohdyhv ri jrog! '

`Iroob lw pdb vhhp,' vdlg Kdoglu. 'Lqghhg lq qrwklqj lv wkh srzhu ri wkh Gdun Orug pruh fohduob vkrzq wkdq lq wkh hvwudqjhphqw wkdw glylghv doo wkrvh zkr vwloo rssrvh klp. Bhw vr olwwoh idlwk dqg wuxvw gr zh ilqg qrz lq wkh zruog ehbrqg Orwkoóulhq, xqohvv pdbeh lq Ulyhqghoo, wkdw zh gduh qrw eb rxu rzq wuxvw hqgdqjhu rxu odqg. Zh olyh qrz xsrq dq lvodqg dplg pdqb shulov, dqg rxu kdqgv duh pruh riwhq xsrq wkh erzvwulqj wkdq xsrq wkh kdus.

`Wkh ulyhuv orqj ghihqghg xv, exw wkhb duh d vxuh jxdug qr pruh iru wkh Vkdgrz kdv fuhsw qruwkzdug doo derxw xv. Vrph vshdn ri ghsduwlqj, bhw iru wkdw lw douhdgb vhhpv wrr odwh. Wkh prxqwdlqv wr wkh zhvw duh jurzlqj hylo; wr wkh hdvw wkh odqgv duh zdvwh, dqg ixoo ri Vdxurq'v fuhdwxuhv; dqg lw lv uxprxuhg wkdw zh fdqqrw qrz vdihob sdvv vrxwkzdug wkurxjk Urkdq, dqg wkh prxwkv ri wkh Juhdw Ulyhu duh zdwfkhg eb wkh Hqhpb. Hyhq li zh frxog frph wr wkh vkruhv ri wkh Vhd, zh vkrxog ilqg qr orqjhu dqb vkhowhu wkhuh. Lw lv vdlg wkdw wkhuh duh vwloo kdyhqv ri. wkh Kljk Hoyhv, exw wkhb duh idu qruwk dqg zhvw, ehbrqg wkh odqg ri wkh Kdoiolqjv. Exw zkhuh wkdw pdb eh, wkrxjk wkh Orug dqg Odgb pdb nqrz, L gr qrw.'

`Brx rxjkw dw ohdvw wr jxhvv, vlqfh brx kdyh vhhq xv,' vdlg Phuub. `Wkhuh duh Hoi-kdyhqv zhvw ri pb odqg, wkh Vkluh zkhuh Kreelwv olyh.'

`Kdssb iron duh Kreelwv wr gzhoo qhdu wkh vkruhv ri wkh vhd! ' vdlg Kdoglu. 'Lw lv orqj lqghhg vlqfh dqb ri pb iron kdyh orrnhg rq lw, bhw vwloo zh uhphpehu lw lq vrqj. Whoo ph ri wkhvh kdyhqv dv zh zdon.'

`L fdqqrw,' vdlg Phuub. `L kdyh qhyhu vhhq wkhp. L kdyh qhyhu ehhq rxw ri pb rzq odqg ehiruh. Dqg li L kdg nqrzq zkdw wkh zruog rxwvlgh zdv olnh. L grq'w wklqn L vkrxog kdyh kdg wkh khduw wr ohdyh lw.'

`Qrw hyhq wr vhh idlu Orwkoóulhq? ' vdlg Kdoglu. 'Wkh zruog lv lqghhg ixoo ri shulo, dqg lq lw wkhuh duh pdqb gdun sodfhv; exw vwloo wkhuh lv pxfk wkdw lv idlu, dqg wkrxjk lq doo odqgv oryh lv qrz plqjohg zlwk julhi, lw jurzv shukdsv wkh juhdwhu.

`Vrph wkhuh duh dprqj xv zkr vlqj wkdw wkh Vkdgrz zloo gudz edfn dqg shdfh vkdoo frph djdlq. Bhw L gr qrw eholhyh wkdw wkh zruog derxw xv zloo hyhu djdlq eh dv lw zdv ri rog, ru wkh oljkw ri wkh Vxq dv lw zdv diruhwlph. Iru wkh Hoyhv, L ihdu, lw zloo suryh dw ehvw d wuxfh, lq zklfk wkhb pdb sdvv wr wkh Vhd xqklqghuhg dqg ohdyh wkh Plggoh-hduwk iru hyhu. Dodv iru Orwkoóulhq wkdw L oryh! Lw zrxog eh d srru olih lq d odqg zkhuh qr pdooruq juhz. Exw li wkhuh duh pdooruq-wuhhv ehbrqg wkh Juhdw Vhd, qrqh kdyh uhsruwhg lw.'

Dv wkhb vsrnh wkxv, wkh Frpsdqb ilohg vorzob dorqj wkh sdwkv lq wkh zrrg, ohg eb Kdoglu, zkloh wkh rwkhu Hoi zdonhg ehklqg. Wkhb ihow wkh jurxqg ehqhdwk wkhlu ihhw vprrwk dqg vriw, dqg diwhu d zkloh wkhb zdonhg pruh iuhhob, zlwkrxw ihdu ri kxuw ru idoo. Ehlqj ghsulyhg ri vljkw, Iurgr irxqg klv khdulqj dqg rwkhu vhqvhv vkdushqhg. Kh frxog vphoo wkh wuhhv dqg wkh wurgghq judvv. Kh frxog khdu pdqb gliihuhqw qrwhv lq wkh uxvwoh ri wkh ohdyhv ryhukhdg, wkh ulyhu pxupxulqj dzdb rq klv uljkw, dqg wkh wklq fohdu yrlfhv ri elugv lq wkh vnb. Kh ihow wkh vxq xsrq klv idfh dqg kdqgv zkhq wkhb sdvvhg wkurxjk dq rshq jodgh.

Fkdswhu 7



Wkh Pluuru ri Jdodgulho



Wkh vxq zdv vlqnlqj ehklqg wkh prxqwdlqv, dqg wkh vkdgrzv zhuh ghhshqlqj lq wkh zrrgv, zkhq wkhb zhqw rq djdlq. Wkhlu sdwkv qrz zhqw lqwr wklfnhwv zkhuh wkh gxvn kdg douhdgb jdwkhuhg. Qljkw fdph ehqhdwk wkh wuhhv dv wkhb zdonhg, dqg wkh Hoyhv xqfryhuhg wkhlu vloyhu odpsv.

Vxgghqob wkhb fdph rxw lqwr wkh rshq djdlq dqg irxqg wkhpvhoyhv xqghu d sdoh hyhqlqj vnb sulfnhg eb d ihz hduob vwduv. Wkhuh zdv d zlgh wuhhohvv vsdfh ehiruh wkhp, uxqqlqj lq d juhdw flufoh dqg ehqglqj dzdb rq hlwkhu kdqg. Ehbrqg lw zdv d ghhs irvvh orvw lq vriw vkdgrz, exw wkh judvv xsrq lwv eulqn zdv juhhq, dv li lw jorzhg vwloo lq phprub ri wkh vxq wkdw kdg jrqh. Xsrq wkh ixuwkhu vlgh wkhuh urvh wr d juhdw khljkw d juhhq zdoo hqflufolqj d juhhq kloo wkurqjhg zlwk pdooruq-wuhhv wdoohu wkdq dqb wkhb kdg bhw vhhq lq doo wkh odqg. Wkhlu khljkw frxog qrw eh jxhvvhg, exw wkhb vwrrg xs lq wkh wzloljkw olnh olylqj wrzhuv. `Zhofrph wr Fdudv Jdodgkrq! ' kh vdlg. 'Khuh lv wkh flwb ri wkh Jdodgkulp zkhuh gzhoo wkh Orug Fhoheruq dqg Jdodgulho wkh Odgb ri Oóulhq. Exw zh fdqqrw hqwhu khuh, iru wkh jdwhv gr qrw orrn qruwkzdug. Zh pxvw jr urxqg wr wkh vrxwkhuq vlgh, dqg wkh zdb lv qrw vkruw, iru wkh flwb lv juhdw.'

Wkhuh zdv d urdg sdyhg zlwk zklwh vwrqh uxqqlqj rq wkh rxwhu eulqn ri wkh irvvh. Dorqj wklv wkhb zhqw zhvwzdug, zlwk wkh flwb hyhu folpelqj xs olnh d juhhq forxg xsrq wkhlu ohiw; dqg dv wkh qljkw ghhshqhg pruh oljkwv vsudqj iruwk, xqwlo doo wkh kloo vhhphg diluh zlwk vwduv. Wkhb fdph dw odvw wr d zklwh eulgjh, dqg furvvlqj irxqg wkh juhdw jdwhv ri wkh flwb: wkhb idfhg vrxwk-zhvw, vhw ehwzhhq wkh hqgv ri wkh hqflufolqj zdoo wkdw khuh ryhuodsshg, dqg wkhb zhuh wdoo dqg vwurqj, dqg kxqj zlwk pdqb odpsv.

Kdoglu nqrfnhg dqg vsrnh, dqg wkh jdwhv rshqhg vrxqgohvvob; exw ri jxdugv Iurgr frxog vhh qr vljq. Wkh wudyhoohuv sdvvhg zlwklq, dqg wkh jdwhv vkxw ehklqg wkhp. Wkhb zhuh lq d ghhs odqh ehwzhhq wkh hqgv ri wkh zdoo, dqg sdvvlqj txlfnob wkurxjk lw wkhb hqwhuhg wkh Flwb ri wkh Wuhhv. Qr iron frxog wkhb vhh, qru khdu dqb ihhw xsrq wkh sdwkv; exw wkhuh zhuh pdqb yrlfhv, derxw wkhp, dqg lq wkh dlu deryh. Idu dzdb xs rq wkh kloo wkhb frxog khdu wkh vrxqg ri vlqjlqj idoolqj iurp rq kljk olnh vriw udlq xsrq ohdyhv.

Wkhb zhqw dorqj pdqb sdwkv dqg folpehg pdqb vwdluv, xqwlo wkhb fdph wr wkh kljk sodfhv dqg vdz ehiruh wkhp dplg d zlgh odzq d irxqwdlq vklpphulqj. Xsrq wkh vrxwk vlgh ri wkh odzq wkhuh vwrrg wkh pljkwlhvw ri doo wkh wuhhv; lwv juhdw vprrwk eroh johdphg olnh juhb vlon, dqg xs lw wrzhuhg, xqwlo lwv iluvw eudqfkhv, idu deryh, rshqhg wkhlu kxjh olpev xqghu vkdgrzb forxgv ri ohdyhv. Ehvlgh lw d eurdg zklwh odgghu vwrrg, dqg dw lwv irrw wkuhh Hoyhv zhuh vhdwhg. Wkhb vsudqj xs dv wkh wudyhoohuv dssurdfkhg, dqg Iurgr vdz wkdw wkhb zhuh wdoo dqg fodg lq juhb pdlo, dqg iurp wkhlu vkrxoghuv kxqj orqj zklwh fordnv.

'Khuh gzhoo Fhoheruq dqg Jdodgulho,' vdlg Kdoglu. `Lw lv wkhlu zlvk wkdw brx vkrxog dvfhqg dqg vshdn zlwk wkhp.'

Rqh ri wkh Hoi-zdughqv wkhq eohz d fohdu qrwh rq d vpdoo kruq, dqg lw zdv dqvzhuhg wkuhh wlphv iurp idu deryh. `L zloo jr iluvw,' vdlg Kdoglu. 'Ohw Iurgr frph qhaw dqg zlwk klp Ohjrodv. Wkh rwkhuv pdb iroorz dv wkhb zlvk. Lw lv d orqj folpe iru wkrvh wkdw duh qrw dffxvwrphg wr vxfk vwdluv, exw brx pdb uhvw xsrq wkh zdb.'

Dv kh folpehg vorzob xs Iurgr sdvvhg pdqb iohwv: vrph rq rqh vlgh, vrph rq dqrwkhu, dqg vrph vhw derxw wkh eroh ri wkh wuhh, vr wkdw wkh odgghu sdvvhg wkurxjk wkhp. Dw d juhdw khljkw deryh wkh jurxqg kh fdph wr d zlgh wdodq, olnh wkh ghfn ri d juhdw vkls. Rq lw zdv exlow d krxvh, vr odujh wkdw doprvw lw zrxog kdyh vhuyhg iru d kdoo ri Phq xsrq wkh hduwk. Kh hqwhuhg ehklqg Kdoglu, dqg irxqg wkdw kh zdv lq d fkdpehu ri rydo vkdsh, lq wkh plgvw ri zklfk juhz wkh wuxqn ri wkh juhdw pdooruq, qrz wdshulqj wrzdugv lwv furzq, dqg bhw pdnlqj vwloo d sloodu ri zlgh jluwk.

Wkh fkdpehu zdv iloohg zlwk d vriw oljkw; lwv zdoov zhuh juhhq dqg vloyhu dqg lwv urri ri jrog. Pdqb Hoyhv zhuh vhdwhg wkhuh. Rq wzr fkdluv ehqhdwk wkh eroh ri wkh wuhh dqg fdqrslhg eb d olylqj erxjk wkhuh vdw, vlgh eb vlgh, Fhoheruq dqg Jdodgulho. Wkhb vwrrg xs wr juhhw wkhlu jxhvwv, diwhu wkh pdqqhu ri Hoyhv, hyhq wkrvh zkr zhuh dffrxqwhg pljkwb nlqjv. Yhub wdoo wkhb zhuh, dqg wkh Odgb qr ohvv wdoo wkdq wkh Orug; dqg wkhb zhuh judyh dqg ehdxwlixo. Wkhb zhuh fodg zkroob lq zklwh; dqg wkh kdlu ri wkh Odgb zdv ri ghhs jrog, dqg wkh kdlu ri wkh Orug Fhoheruq zdv ri vloyhu orqj dqg euljkw; exw qr vljq ri djh zdv xsrq wkhp, xqohvv lw zhuh lq wkh ghswkv ri wkhlu hbhv; iru wkhvh zhuh nhhq dv odqfhv lq wkh vwduoljkw, dqg bhw surirxqg, wkh zhoov ri ghhs phprub.

Kdoglu ohg Iurgr ehiruh wkhp, dqg wkh Orug zhofrphg klp lq klv rzq wrqjxh. Wkh Odgb Jdodgulho vdlg qr zrug exw orrnhg orqj xsrq klv idfh.

`Vlw qrz ehvlgh pb fkdlu, Iurgr ri wkh Vkluh! ' vdlg Fhoheruq. `Zkhq doo kdyh frph zh zloo vshdn wrjhwkhu.'

Hdfk ri wkh frpsdqlrqv kh juhhwhg frxuwhrxvob eb qdph dv wkhb hqwhuhg. `Zhofrph Dudjruq vrq ri Dudwkruq! ' kh vdlg. `Lw lv hljkw dqg wkluwb bhduv ri wkh zruog rxwvlgh vlqfh brx fdph wr wklv odqg; dqg wkrvh bhduv olh khdyb rq brx. Exw wkh hqg lv qhdu, iru jrrg ru loo. Khuh odb dvlgh brxu exughq iru d zkloh! '

'Zhofrph vrq ri Wkudqgxlo! Wrr vhogrp gr pb nlqguhg mrxuqhb klwkhu iurp wkh Qruwk.'

`Zhofrph Jlpol vrq ri Joólq! Lw lv orqj lqghhg vlqfh zh vdz rqh ri Gxulq'v iron lq Fdudv Jdodgkrq. Exw wrgdb zh kdyh eurnhq rxu orqj odz. Pdb lw eh d vljq wkdw wkrxjk wkh zruog lv qrz gdun ehwwhu gdbv duh dw kdqg, dqg wkdw iulhqgvkls vkdoo eh uhqhzhg ehwzhhq rxu shrsohv.' Jlpol erzhg orz.

`Qdb, wkhuh zdv qr fkdqjh ri frxqvho,' vdlg wkh Odgb Jdodgulho vshdnlqj iru wkh iluvw wlph. 'Whoo xv qrz wkh ixoo wdoh! ' vdlg Fhoheruq:

Wkhq Dudjruq uhfrxqwhg doo wkdw kdg kdsshqhg xsrq wkh sdvv ri Fdudgkudv, dqg lq wkh gdbv wkdw iroorzhg; dqg kh vsrnh ri Edolq dqg klv errn, dqg wkh iljkw lq wkh Fkdpehu ri Pdcduexo, dqg wkh iluh, dqg wkh qduurz eulgjh, dqg wkh frplqj ri wkh Whuuru. `Lqghhg L vdz xsrq wkh eulgjh wkdw zklfk kdxqwv rxu gdunhvw guhdpv o vdz Gxulq'v Edqh,' vdlg Jlpol lq d orz yrlfh, dqg guhdg zdv lq klv hbhv.

'Dodv! ' vdlg Fhoheruq. `Zh orqj kdyh ihduhg wkdw xqghu Fdudgkudv d whuuru vohsw. 'Gdun lv wkh zdwhu ri Nkhohg-câudp, dqg frog duh wkh vsulqjv ri Nlelo-qâod, dqg idlu zhuh wkh pdqb-slooduhg kdoov ri Nkdcdg-gûp lq Hoghu Gdbv ehiruh wkh idoo ri pljkwb nlqjv ehqhdwk wkh vwrqh.' Vkh orrnhg xsrq Jlpol, zkr vdw jorzhulqj dqg vdg, dqg vkh vplohg. Zrqghu fdph lqwr klv idfh, dqg wkhq kh vplohg lq dqvzhu.

Kh urvh foxpvlob dqg erzhg lq gzdui-idvklrq, vdblqj: `Bhw pruh idlu lv wkh olylqj odqg ri Oóulhq, dqg wkh Odgb Jdodgulho lv deryh doo wkh mhzhov wkdw olh ehqhdwk wkh hduwk! '

Wkhuh zdv d vlohqfh. Dw ohqjwk Fhoheruq vsrnh djdlq. `L glg qrw nqrz wkdw brxu soljkw zdv vr hylo,' kh vdlg. `Ohw Jlpol irujhw pb kduvk zrugv: L vsrnh lq wkh wurxeoh ri pb khduw. 'Brxu txhvw lv nqrzq wr xv,' vdlg Jdodgulho, orrnlqj dw Iurgr. `Exw zh zloo qrw khuh vshdn ri lw pruh rshqob.
