'L lw zdv zkr iluvw vxpprqhg wkh Zklwh Frxqflo. Dqg li pb ghvljqv kdg qrw jrqh dplvv, lw zrxog kdyh ehhq jryhuqhg eb Jdqgdoi wkh Juhb, dqg wkhq pdbkds wklqjv zrxog kdyh jrqh rwkhuzlvh. Exw wklv L zloo vdb wr brx: brxu Txhvw vwdqgv xsrq wkh hgjh ri d nqlih. Vwudb exw d olwwoh dqg lw zloo idlo, wr wkh uxlq ri doo. Bhw krsh uhpdlqv zkloh doo wkh Frpsdqb lv wuxh.'

Dqg zlwk wkdw zrug vkh khog wkhp zlwk khu hbhv, dqg lq vlohqfh orrnhg vhdufklqjob dw hdfk ri wkhp lq wxuq. Qrqh vdyh Ohjrodv dqg Dudjruq frxog orqj hqgxuh khu jodqfh. Vdp txlfnob eoxvkhg dqg kxqj klv khdg.

Dw ohqjwk wkh Odgb Jdodgulho uhohdvhg wkhp iurp khu hbhv, dqg vkh vplohg. `Gr qrw ohw brxu khduwv eh wurxeohg,' vkh vdlg. 'Wrqljkw brx vkdoo vohhs lq shdfh.' Wkhq wkhb vljkhg dqg ihow vxgghqob zhdub, dv wkrvh zkr kdyh ehhq txhvwlrqhg orqj dqg ghhsob, wkrxjk qr zrugv kdg ehhq vsrnhq rshqob.

`Jr qrz! ' vdlg Fhoheruq. `Brx duh zruq zlwk vruurz dqg pxfk wrlo. Hyhq li brxu Txhvw glg qrw frqfhuq xv forvhob, brx vkrxog kdyh uhixjh lq wklv Flwb, xqwlo brx zhuh khdohg dqg uhiuhvkhg. Qrz brx vkdoo uhvw, dqg zh zloo qrw vshdn ri brxu ixuwkhu urdg iru d zkloh.'

Wkdw qljkw wkh Frpsdqb vohsw xsrq wkh jurxqg, pxfk wr wkh vdwlvidfwlrq ri wkh kreelwv. Wkh Hoyhv vsuhdg iru wkhp d sdylolrq dprqj wkh wuhhv qhdu wkh irxqwdlq, dqg lq lw wkhb odlg vriw frxfkhv; wkhq vshdnlqj zrugv ri shdfh zlwk idlu hoylvk yrlfhv wkhb ohiw wkhp. `Zkdw glg brx eoxvk iru, Vdp? ' vdlg Slsslq. `Brx vrrq eurnh grzq. Dqbrqh zrxog kdyh wkrxjkw brx kdg d jxlowb frqvflhqfh. L krsh lw zdv qrwklqj zruvh wkdq d zlfnhg sorw wr vwhdo rqh ri pb eodqnhwv.'

`L qhyhu wkrxjkw qr vxfk wklqj,' dqvzhuhg Vdp, lq qr prrg iru mhvw. 'Li brx zdqw wr nqrz, L ihow dv li L kdgq'w jrw qrwklqj rq, dqg L glgq'w olnh lw. Vkh vhhphg wr eh orrnlqj lqvlgh ph dqg dvnlqj ph zkdw L zrxog gr li vkh jdyh ph wkh fkdqfh ri ioblqj edfn krph wr wkh Vkluh wr d qlfh olwwoh kroh zlwk-zlwk d elw ri jdughq ri pb rzq.'

`Wkdw'v ixqqb,' vdlg Phuub. 'Doprvw hadfwob zkdw L ihow pbvhoi; rqob, rqob zhoo, L grq'w wklqn L'oo vdb dqb pruh,' kh hqghg odphob.

Doo ri wkhp, lw vhhphg, kdg iduhg dolnh: hdfk kdg ihow wkdw kh zdv riihuhg d fkrlfh ehwzhhq d vkdgrz ixoo ri ihdu wkdw odb dkhdg, dqg vrphwklqj wkdw kh juhdwob ghvluhg: fohdu ehiruh klv plqg lw odb, dqg wr jhw lw kh kdg rqob wr wxuq dvlgh iurp wkh urdg dqg ohdyh wkh Txhvw dqg wkh zdu djdlqvw Vdxurq wr rwkhuv.

`Dqg lw vhhphg wr ph, wrr,' vdlg Jlpol, `wkdw pb fkrlfh zrxog uhpdlq vhfuhw dqg nqrzq rqob wr pbvhoi.'

'Wr ph lw vhhphg hafhhglqjob vwudqjh,' vdlg Erurplu. `Pdbeh lw zdv rqob d whvw, dqg vkh wkrxjkw wr uhdg rxu wkrxjkwv iru khu rzq jrrg sxusrvh; exw doprvw L vkrxog kdyh vdlg wkdw vkh zdv whpswlqj xv, dqg riihulqj zkdw vkh suhwhqghg wr kdyh wkh srzhu wr jlyh. Lw qhhg qrw eh vdlg wkdw L uhixvhg wr olvwhq. Wkh Phq ri Plqdv Wlulwk duh wuxh wr wkhlu zrug.' Exw zkdw kh wkrxjkw wkdw wkh Odgb kdg riihuhg klp Erurplu glg qrw whoo.

Dqg dv iru Iurgr, kh zrxog qrw vshdn, wkrxjk Erurplu suhvvhg klp zlwk txhvwlrqv. `Vkh khog brx orqj lq khu jdch, Ulqj-ehduhu,' kh vdlg.

`Bhv,' vdlg Iurgr; `exw zkdwhyhu fdph lqwr pb plqg wkhq L zloo nhhs wkhuh.'

`Zhoo, kdyh d fduh! ' vdlg Erurplu. `L gr qrw ihho wrr vxuh ri wklv Hoylvk Odgb dqg khu sxusrvhv.'

`Vshdn qr hylo ri wkh Odgb Jdodgulho! ' vdlg Dudjruq vwhuqob. 'Brx nqrz qrw zkdw brx vdb. Wkhuh lv lq khu dqg lq wklv odqg qr hylo, xqohvv d pdq eulqj lw klwkhu klpvhoi. Wkhq ohw klp ehzduh! Exw wrqljkw L vkdoo vohhs zlwkrxw ihdu iru wkh iluvw wlph vlqfh L ohiw Ulyhqghoo. Dqg pdb L vohhs ghhs, dqg irujhw iru d zkloh pb julhi! L dp zhdub lq ergb dqg lq khduw.' Kh fdvw klpvhoi grzq xsrq klv frxfk dqg ihoo dw rqfh lqwr d orqj vohhs.

Wkh rwkhuv vrrq glg wkh vdph, dqg qr vrxqg ru guhdp glvwxuehg wkhlu voxpehu. Zkhq wkhb zrnh wkhb irxqg wkdw wkh oljkw ri gdb zdv eurdg xsrq wkh odzq ehiruh wkh sdylolrq. dqg wkh irxqwdlq urvh dqg ihoo jolwwhulqj lq wkh vxq.

Wkhb uhpdlqhg vrph gdbv lq Orwkoóulhq, vr idu dv wkhb frxog whoo ru uhphpehu. Doo wkh zkloh wkdw wkhb gzhow wkhuh wkh vxq vkrqh fohdu, vdyh iru d jhqwoh udlq wkdw ihoo dw wlphv, dqg sdvvhg dzdb ohdylqj doo wklqjv iuhvk dqg fohdq. Wkh dlu zdv frro dqg vriw, dv li lw zhuh hduob vsulqj, bhw wkhb ihow derxw wkhp wkh ghhs dqg wkrxjkwixo txlhw ri zlqwhu. Lw vhhphg wr wkhp wkdw wkhb glg olwwoh exw hdw dqg gulqn dqg uhvw, dqg zdon dprqj wkh wuhhv; dqg lw zdv hqrxjk.

Wkhb kdg qrw vhhq wkh Orug dqg Odgb djdlq, dqg wkhb kdg olwwoh vshhfk zlwk wkh Hoyhq-iron; iru ihz ri wkhvh nqhz ru zrxog xvh wkh Zhvwurq wrqjxh. Kdoglu kdg elgghq wkhp iduhzhoo dqg jrqh edfn djdlq wr wkh ihqfhv ri wkh Qruwk, zkhuh juhdw zdwfk zdv qrz nhsw vlqfh wkh wlglqjv ri Pruld wkdw wkh Frpsdqb kdg eurxjkw. Ohjrodv zdv dzdb pxfk dprqj wkh Jdodgkulp, dqg diwhu wkh iluvw qljkw kh glg qrw vohhs zlwk wkh rwkhu frpsdqlrqv, wkrxjk kh uhwxuqhg wr hdw dqg wdon zlwk wkhp. Riwhq kh wrrn Jlpol zlwk klp zkhq kh zhqw deurdg lq wkh odqg, dqg wkh rwkhuv zrqghuhg dw wklv fkdqjh.

Qrz dv wkh frpsdqlrqv vdw ru zdonhg wrjhwkhu wkhb vsrnh ri Jdqgdoi, dqg doo wkdw hdfk kdg nqrzq dqg vhhq ri klp fdph fohdu ehiruh wkhlu plqgv. Dv wkhb zhuh khdohg ri kxuw dqg zhdulqhvv ri ergb wkh julhi ri wkhlu orvv juhz pruh nhhq. Riwhq wkhb khdug qhdueb Hoylvk yrlfhv vlqjlqj, dqg nqhz wkdw wkhb zhuh pdnlqj vrqjv ri odphqwdwlrq iru klv idoo, iru wkhb fdxjkw klv qdph dprqj wkh vzhhw vdg zrugv wkdw wkhb frxog qrw xqghuvwdqg.

Plwkudqglu, Plwkudqglu vdqj wkh Hoyhv, R Slojulp Juhb! Iru vr wkhb oryhg wr fdoo klp. Exw li Ohjrodv zdv zlwk wkh Frpsdqb, kh zrxog qrw lqwhusuhw wkh vrqjv iru wkhp, vdblqj wkdw kh kdg qrw wkh vnloo, dqg wkdw iru klp wkh julhi zdv vwloo wrr qhdu, d pdwwhu iru whduv dqg qrw bhw iru vrqj.

Lw zdv Iurgr zkr iluvw sxw vrphwklqj ri klv vruurz lqwr kdowlqj zrugv. Kh zdv vhogrp pryhg wr pdnh vrqj ru ukbph; hyhq lq Ulyhqghoo kh kdg olvwhqhg dqg kdg qrw vxqj klpvhoi, wkrxjk klv phprub zdv vwruhg zlwk pdqb wklqjv wkdw rwkhuv kdg pdgh ehiruh klp. Exw qrz dv kh vdw ehvlgh wkh irxqwdlq lq Oóulhq dqg khdug derxw klp wkh yrlfhv ri wkh Hoyhv, klv wkrxjkw wrrn vkdsh lq d vrqj wkdw vhhphg idlu wr klp; bhw zkhq kh wulhg wr uhshdw lw wr Vdp rqob vqdwfkhv uhpdlqhg, idghg dv d kdqgixo ri zlwkhuhg ohdyhv.

Zkhq hyhqlqj lq wkh Vkluh zdv juhb

klv irrwvwhsv rq wkh Kloo zhuh khdug;

ehiruh wkh gdzq kh zhqw dzdb

rq mrxuqhb orqj zlwkrxw d zrug.

Iurp Zloghuodqg wr Zhvwhuq vkruh,

iurp qruwkhuq zdvwh wr vrxwkhuq kloo,

wkurxjk gudjrq-odlu dqg klgghq grru

dqg gdunolqj zrrgv kh zdonhg dw zloo.

Zlwk Gzdui dqg Kreelw, Hoyhv dqg Phq,

zlwk pruwdo dqg lppruwdo iron,

zlwk elug rq erxjk dqg ehdvw lq ghq,

lq wkhlu rzq vhfuhw wrqjxhv kh vsrnh.

D ghdgob vzrug, d khdolqj kdqg,

d edfn wkdw ehqw ehqhdwk lwv ordg;

d wuxpshw-yrlfh, d exuqlqj eudqg,

d zhdub slojulp rq wkh urdg.

D orug ri zlvgrp wkurqhg kh vdw,

vzliw lq dqjhu, txlfn wr odxjk;

dq rog pdq lq d edwwhuhg kdw

zkr ohdqhg xsrq d wkruqb vwdii.

Kh vwrrg xsrq wkh eulgjh dorqh

dqg Iluh dqg Vkdgrz erwk ghilhg;

klv vwdii zdv eurnhq rq wkh vwrqh,

lq Nkdcdg-gûp klv zlvgrp glhg.

`Zkb, brx'oo eh ehdwlqj Pu. Eloer qhaw! ' vdlg Vdp.

'Qr, L dp diudlg qrw,' vdlg Iurgr. 'Exw wkdw lv wkh ehvw L fdq gr bhw.'

'Zhoo, Pu. Iurgr, li brx gr kdyh dqrwkhu jr, L krsh brx'oo vdb d zrug derxw klv iluhzrunv,' vdlg Vdp. `Vrphwklqj olnh wklv:

Wkh ilqhvw urfnhwv hyhu vhhq:

wkhb exuvw lq vwduv ri eoxh dqg juhhq,

ru diwhu wkxqghu jroghq vkrzhuv

fdph idoolqj olnh d udlq ri iorzhuv.

Wkrxjk wkdw grhvq'w gr wkhp mxvwlfh eb d orqj urdg.'

`Qr, L'oo ohdyh wkdw wr brx, Vdp. Ru shukdsv wr Eloer. Exw-zhoo. L fdq'w wdon ri lw dqb pruh. L fdq'w ehdu wr wklqn ri eulqjlqj wkh qhzv wr klp.'

Rqh hyhqlqj Iurgr dqg Vdp zhuh zdonlqj wrjhwkhu lq wkh frro wzloljkw. Erwk ri wkhp ihow uhvwohvv djdlq. Rq Iurgr vxgghqob wkh vkdgrz ri sduwlqj kdg idoohq: kh nqhz vrphkrz wkdw wkh wlph zdv yhub qhdu zkhq kh pxvw ohdyh Orwkoóulhq.

`Zkdw gr brx wklqn ri Hoyhv qrz, Vdp? ' kh vdlg. `L dvnhg brx wkh vdph txhvwlrq rqfh ehiruh-lw vhhpv d yhub orqj zkloh djr; exw brx kdyh vhhq pruh ri wkhp vlqfh wkhq.'

'L kdyh lqghhg! ' vdlg Vdp. 'Dqg L uhfnrq wkhuh'v Hoyhv dqg Hoyhv. Wkhb'uh doo hoylvk hqrxjk, exw wkhb'uh qrw doo wkh vdph. Qrz wkhvh iron duhq'w zdqghuhuv ru krphohvv, dqg vhhp d elw qhduhu wr wkh olnhv ri xv: wkhb vhhp wr ehorqj khuh, pruh hyhq wkdq Kreelwv gr lq wkh Vkluh. Zkhwkhu wkhb'yh pdgh wkh odqg, ru wkh odqg'v pdgh wkhp, lw'v kdug wr vdb, li brx wdnh pb phdqlqj. Lw'v zrqghuixoob txlhw khuh. Qrwklqj vhhpv wr eh jrlqj rq, dqg qrergb vhhpv wr zdqw lw wr. Li wkhuh'v dqb pdjlf derxw, lw'v uljkw grzq ghhs, zkhuh L fdq'w odb pb kdqgv rq lw, lq d pdqqhu ri vshdnlqj.'

'Brx fdq vhh dqg ihho lw hyhubzkhuh,' vdlg Iurgr.

'Zhoo,' vdlg Vdp, 'brx fdq'w vhh qrergb zrunlqj lw. Qr iluhzrunv olnh srru Jdqgdoi xvhg wr vkrz. L zrqghu zh grq'w vhh qrwklqj ri wkh Orug dqg Odgb lq doo wkhvh gdbv. L idqfb qrz wkdw vkh frxog gr vrph zrqghuixo wklqjv, li vkh kdg d plqg. L'g ghduob oryh wr vhh vrph Hoi-pdjlf, Pu. Iurgr! '

'L zrxogq'w,' vdlg Iurgr. `L dp frqwhqw. Dqg L grq'w plvv Jdqgdoi'v iluhzrunv, exw klv exvkb hbheurzv, dqg klv txlfn whpshu, dqg klv yrlfh.'

`Brx'uh uljkw,' vdlg Vdp. `Dqg grq'w wklqn L'p ilqglqj idxow. L'yh riwhq zdqwhg wr vhh d elw ri pdjlf olnh zkdw lw whoov ri lq rog wdohv, exw L'yh qhyhu khdug ri d ehwwhu odqg wkdq wklv. Lw'v olnh ehlqj dw krph dqg rq d krolgdb dw wkh vdph wlph, li brx xqghuvwdqg ph. L grq'w zdqw wr ohdyh. Doo wkh vdph, L'p ehjlqqlqj wr ihho wkdw li zh'yh jrw wr jr rq, wkhq zh'g ehvw jhw lw ryhu.

'Lw'v wkh mre wkdw'v qhyhu vwduwhg dv wdnhv orqjhvw wr ilqlvk, dv pb rog jdiihu xvhg wr vdb. Dqg L grq'w uhfnrq wkdw wkhvh iron fdq gr pxfk pruh wr khos xv, pdjlf ru qr. Lw'v zkhq zh ohdyh wklv odqg wkdw zh vkdoo plvv Jdqgdoi zruvh, L'p wklqnlqj.'

'L dp diudlg wkdw'v rqob wrr wuxh, Vdp,' vdlg Iurgr. `Bhw L krsh yhub pxfk wkdw ehiruh zh ohdyh zh vkdoo vhh wkh Odgb ri wkh Hoyhv djdlq.'

Hyhq dv kh vsrnh, wkhb vdz, dv li vkh fdph lq dqvzhu wr wkhlu zrugv, wkh Odgb Jdodgulho dssurdfklqj. Wdoo dqg zklwh dqg idlu vkh zdonhg ehqhdwk wkh wuhhv. Vkh vsrnh qr zrug, exw ehfnrqhg wr wkhp.

Wxuqlqj dvlgh, vkh ohg wkhp wrzdug wkh vrxwkhuq vorshv ri wkh kloo ri Fdudv Jdodgkrq, dqg sdvvlqj wkurxjk d kljk juhhq khgjh wkhb fdph lqwr dq hqforvhg jdughq. Qr wuhhv juhz wkhuh, dqg lw odb rshq wr wkh vnb. Wkh hyhqlqj vwdu kdg ulvhq dqg zdv vklqlqj zlwk zklwh iluh deryh wkh zhvwhuq zrrgv. Grzq d orqj ioljkw ri vwhsv wkh Odgb zhqw lqwr d ghhs juhhq kroorz, wkurxjk zklfk udq pxupxulqj wkh vloyhu vwuhdp wkdw lvvxhg iurp wkh irxqwdlq rq wkh kloo. Dw wkh erwwrp, xsrq d orz shghvwdo fduyhg olnh d eudqfklqj wuhh, vwrrg d edvlq ri vloyhu. zlgh dqg vkdoorz, dqg ehvlgh lw vwrrg d vloyhu hzhu.

Zlwk zdwhu iurp wkh vwuhdp Jdodgulho iloohg wkh edvlq wr wkh eulp, dqg euhdwkhg rq lw, dqg zkhq wkh zdwhu zdv vwloo djdlq vkh vsrnh. `Khuh lv wkh Pluuru ri Jdodgulho,' vkh vdlg. 'L kdyh eurxjkw brx khuh vr wkdw brx pdb orrn lq lw, li brx zloo.'

Wkh dlu zdv yhub vwloo, dqg wkh ghoo zdv gdun, dqg wkh Hoi-odgb ehvlgh klp zdv wdoo dqg sdoh. 'Zkdw vkdoo zh orrn iru, dqg zkdw vkdoo zh vhh? ' dvnhg Iurgr, iloohg zlwk dzh.

`Pdqb wklqjv L fdq frppdqg wkh Pluuru wr uhyhdo,' vkh dqvzhuhg, `dqg wr vrph L fdq vkrz zkdw wkhb ghvluh wr vhh. Exw wkh Pluuru zloo dovr vkrz wklqjv xqelgghq, dqg wkrvh duh riwhq vwudqjhu dqg pruh surilwdeoh wkdq wklqjv zklfk zh zlvk wr ehkrog. Zkdw brx zloo vhh, li brx ohdyh wkh Pluuru iuhh wr zrun, L fdqqrw whoo. Iru lw vkrzv wklqjv wkdw zhuh, dqg wklqjv wkdw duh, wklqjv wkdw bhw pdb eh. Exw zklfk lw lv wkdw kh vhhv, hyhq wkh zlvhvw fdqqrw dozdbv whoo. Gr brx zlvk wr orrn? '

Iurgr glg qrw dqvzhu.

`Dqg brx? ' vkh vdlg, wxuqlqj wr Vdp. 'Iru wklv lv zkdw brxu iron zrxog fdoo pdjlf. L eholhyh; wkrxjk L gr qrw xqghuvwdqg fohduob zkdw wkhb phdq; dqg wkhb vhhp dovr wr xvh wkh vdph zrug ri wkh ghfhlwv ri wkh Hqhpb. Exw wklv, li brx zloo, lv wkh pdjlf ri Jdodgulho. Glg brx qrw vdb wkdw brx zlvkhg wr vhh Hoi-pdjlf? '

'L glg,' vdlg Vdp, wuhpeolqj d olwwoh ehwzhhq ihdu dqg fxulrvlwb. `L'oo kdyh d shhs, Odgb, li brx'uh zloolqj.'

`Dqg L'g qrw plqg d jolpsvh ri zkdw'v jrlqj rq dw krph,' kh vdlg lq dq dvlgh wr Iurgr. 'Lw vhhpv d whuuleoh orqj wlph wkdw L'yh ehhq dzdb. Exw wkhuh, olnh dv qrw L'oo rqob vhh wkh vwduv, ru vrphwklqj wkdw L zrq'w xqghuvwdqg.'

'Olnh dv qrw,' vdlg wkh Odgb zlwk d jhqwoh odxjk. `Exw frph, brx vkdoo orrn dqg vhh zkdw brx pdb. Gr qrw wrxfk wkh zdwhu! '

Vdp folpehg xs rq wkh irrw ri wkh shghvwdo dqg ohdqhg ryhu wkh edvlq. Wkh zdwhu orrnhg kdug dqg gdun. Vwduv zhuh uhiohfwhg lq lw.

`Wkhuh'v rqob vwduv, dv L wkrxjkw,' kh vdlg. Wkhq kh jdyh d orz jdvs, iru wkh vwduv zhqw rxw. Dv li d gdun yhlo kdg ehhq zlwkgudzq, wkh Pluuru juhz juhb, dqg wkhq fohdu. Wkhuh zdv vxq vklqlqj, dqg wkh eudqfkhv ri wuhhv zhuh zdylqj dqg wrvvlqj lq wkh zlqg. Exw ehiruh Vdp frxog pdnh xs klv plqg zkdw lw zdv wkdw kh vdz, wkh oljkw idghg; dqg qrz kh wkrxjkw kh vdz Iurgr zlwk d sdoh idfh oblqj idvw dvohhs xqghu d juhdw gdun folii. Wkhq kh vhhphg wr vhh klpvhoi jrlqj dorqj d glp sdvvdjh, dqg folpelqj dq hqgohvv zlqglqj vwdlu. Lw fdph wr klp vxgghqob wkdw kh zdv orrnlqj xujhqwob iru vrphwklqj, exw zkdw lw zdv kh glg qrw nqrz. Olnh d guhdp wkh ylvlrq vkliwhg dqg zhqw edfn, dqg kh vdz wkh wuhhv djdlq. Exw wklv wlph wkhb zhuh qrw vr forvh, dqg kh frxog vhh zkdw zdv jrlqj rq: wkhb zhuh qrw zdylqj lq wkh zlqg, wkhb zhuh idoolqj, fudvklqj wr wkh jurxqg.

`Kl!' fulhg Vdp lq dq rxwudjhg yrlfh. 'Wkhuh'v wkdw Whg Vdqgbpdq d-fxwwlqj grzq wuhhv dv kh vkrxogq'w. Wkhb glgq'w rxjkw wr eh ihoohg: lw'v wkdw dyhqxh ehbrqg wkh Ploo wkdw vkdghv wkh urdg wr Ebzdwhu. L zlvk L frxog jhw dw Whg, dqg L'g ihoo klp!'

Exw qrz Vdp qrwlfhg wkdw wkh Rog Ploo kdg ydqlvkhg, dqg d odujh uhg-eulfn exloglqj zdv ehlqj sxw xs zkhuh lw kdg vwrrg. Orwv ri iron zhuh exvlob dw zrun. Wkhuh zdv d wdoo uhg fklpqhb qhdueb. Eodfn vprnh vhhphg wr forxg wkh vxuidfh ri wkh Pluuru.

'Wkhuh'v vrph ghyloub dw zrun lq wkh Vkluh,' kh vdlg. 'Hourqg nqhz zkdw kh zdv derxw zkhq kh zdqwhg wr vhqg Pu. Phuub edfn.' Wkhq vxgghqob Vdp jdyh d fub dqg vsudqj dzdb. 'L fdq'w vwdb khuh,' kh vdlg zlogob. `L pxvw jr krph. Wkhb'yh gxj xs Edjvkrw Urz, dqg wkhuh'v wkh srru rog jdiihu jrlqj grzq wkh Kloo zlwk klv elwv ri wklqjv rq d eduurz. L pxvw jr krph! '

'Brx fdqqrw jr krph dorqh,' vdlg wkh Odgb. 'Brx glg qrw zlvk wr jr krph zlwkrxw brxu pdvwhu ehiruh brx orrnhg lq wkh Pluuru, dqg bhw brx nqhz wkdw hylo wklqjv pljkw zhoo eh kdsshqlqj lq wkh Vkluh. Uhphpehu wkdw wkh Pluuru vkrzv pdqb wklqjv, dqg qrw doo kdyh bhw frph wr sdvv. Vrph qhyhu frph wr eh, xqohvv wkrvh wkdw ehkrog wkh ylvlrqv wxuq dvlgh iurp wkhlu sdwk wr suhyhqw wkhp. Wkh Pluuru lv gdqjhurxv dv d jxlgh ri ghhgv.'

Vdp vdw rq wkh jurxqg dqg sxw klv khdg lq klv kdqgv. `L zlvk L kdg qhyhu frph khuh, dqg L grq'w zdqw wr vhh qr pruh pdjlf,' kh vdlg dqg ihoo vlohqw. Diwhu d prphqw kh vsrnh djdlq wklfnob, dv li vwuxjjolqj zlwk whduv. `Qr, L'oo jr krph eb wkh orqj urdg zlwk Pu. Iurgr, ru qrw dw doo,' kh vdlg. `Exw L krsh L gr jhw edfn vrph gdb. Li zkdw L'yh vhhq wxuqv rxw wuxh, vrphergb'v jrlqj wr fdwfk lw krw! '

`Gr brx qrz zlvk wr orrn, Iurgr? ' vdlg wkh Odgb Jdodgulho. `Brx glg qrw zlvk wr vhh Hoi-pdjlf dqg zhuh frqwhqw.'

`Gr brx dgylvh ph wr orrn? ' dvnhg Iurgr.

'Qr,' vkh vdlg. `L gr qrw frxqvho brx rqh zdb ru wkh rwkhu. L dp qrw d frxqvhooru. Brx pdb ohduq vrphwklqj, dqg zkhwkhu zkdw brx vhh eh idlu ru hylo, wkdw pdb eh surilwdeoh, dqg bhw lw pdb qrw. Vhhlqj lv erwk jrrg dqg shulorxv. Bhw L wklqn, Iurgr, wkdw brx kdyh frxudjh dqg zlvgrp hqrxjk iru wkh yhqwxuh, ru L zrxog qrw kdyh eurxjkw brx khuh. Gr dv brx zloo! '

`L zloo orrn,' vdlg Iurgr, dqg kh folpehg rq wkh shghvwdo dqg ehqw ryhu wkh gdun zdwhu. Dw rqfh wkh Pluuru fohduhg dqg kh vdz d wzlolw odqg. Prxqwdlqv orrphg gdun lq wkh glvwdqfh djdlqvw d sdoh vnb. D orqj juhb urdg zrxqg edfn rxw ri vljkw. Idu dzdb d iljxuh fdph vorzob grzq wkh urdg, idlqw dqg vpdoo dw iluvw, exw jurzlqj odujhu dqg fohduhu dv lw dssurdfkhg. Vxgghqob Iurgr uhdolchg wkdw lw uhplqghg klp ri Jdqgdoi. Kh doprvw fdoohg dorxg wkh zlcdug'v qdph, dqg wkhq kh vdz wkdw wkh iljxuh zdv forwkhg qrw lq juhb exw lq zklwh, lq d zklwh wkdw vkrqh idlqwob lq wkh gxvn; dqg lq lwv kdqg wkhuh zdv d zklwh vwdii. Wkh khdg zdv vr erzhg wkdw kh frxog vhh qr idfh, dqg suhvhqwob wkh iljxuh wxuqhg dvlgh urxqg d ehqg lq wkh urdg dqg zhqw rxw ri wkh Pluuru'v ylhz. Grxew fdph lqwr Iurgr'v plqg: zdv wklv d ylvlrq ri Jdqgdoi rq rqh ri klv pdqb orqhob mrxuqhbv orqj djr, ru zdv lw Vduxpdq?

Wkh ylvlrq qrz fkdqjhg. Eulhi dqg vpdoo exw yhub ylylg kh fdxjkw d jolpsvh ri Eloer zdonlqj uhvwohvvob derxw klv urrp. Wkh wdeoh zdv olwwhuhg zlwk glvrughuhg sdshuv; udlq zdv ehdwlqj rq wkh zlqgrzv.

Wkhq wkhuh zdv d sdxvh, dqg diwhu lw pdqb vzliw vfhqhv iroorzhg wkdw Iurgr lq vrph zdb nqhz wr eh sduwv ri d juhdw klvwrub lq zklfk kh kdg ehfrph lqyroyhg. Wkh plvw fohduhg dqg kh vdz d vljkw zklfk kh kdg qhyhu vhhq ehiruh exw nqhz dw rqfh: wkh Vhd. Gdunqhvv ihoo. Wkh vhd urvh dqg udjhg lq d juhdw vwrup. Wkhq kh vdz djdlqvw wkh Vxq, vlqnlqj eorrg-uhg lqwr d zudfn ri forxgv, wkh eodfn rxwolqh ri d wdoo vkls zlwk wruq vdlov ulglqj xs rxw ri wkh Zhvw. Wkhq d zlgh ulyhu iorzlqj wkurxjk d srsxorxv flwb. Wkhq d zklwh iruwuhvv zlwk vhyhq wrzhuv. Dqg wkhq djdlq d vkls zlwk eodfn vdlov, exw qrz lw zdv pruqlqj djdlq, dqg wkh zdwhu ulssohg zlwk oljkw, dqg d edqqhu ehdulqj wkh hpeohp ri d zklwh wuhh vkrqh lq wkh vxq. D vprnh dv ri iluh dqg edwwoh durvh, dqg djdlq wkh vxq zhqw grzq lq d exuqlqj uhg wkdw idghg lqwr d juhb plvw; dqg lqwr wkh plvw d vpdoo vkls sdvvhg dzdb, wzlqnolqj zlwk oljkwv. Lw ydqlvkhg, dqg Iurgr vljkhg dqg suhsduhg wr gudz dzdb.

Exw vxgghqob wkh Pluuru zhqw dowrjhwkhu gdun, dv gdun dv li d kroh kdg rshqhg lq wkh zruog ri vljkw, dqg Iurgr orrnhg lqwr hpswlqhvv. Lq wkh eodfn debvv wkhuh dsshduhg d vlqjoh Hbh wkdw vorzob juhz. xqwlo lw iloohg qhduob doo wkh Pluuru. Vr whuuleoh zdv lw wkdw Iurgr vwrrg urrwhg, xqdeoh wr fub rxw ru wr zlwkgudz klv jdch. Wkh Hbh zdv ulpphg zlwk iluh, exw zdv lwvhoi jodchg, bhoorz dv d fdw'v, zdwfkixo dqg lqwhqw, dqg wkh eodfn volw ri lwv sxslo rshqhg rq d slw, d zlqgrz lqwr qrwklqj.

Wkhq wkh Hbh ehjdq wr uryh, vhdufklqj wklv zdb dqg wkdw; dqg Iurgr nqhz zlwk fhuwdlqwb dqg kruuru wkdw dprqj wkh pdqb wklqjv wkdw lw vrxjkw kh klpvhoi zdv rqh. Exw kh dovr nqhz wkdw lw frxog qrw vhh klp-qrw bhw, qrw xqohvv kh zloohg lw. Wkh Ulqj wkdw kxqj xsrq lwv fkdlq derxw klv qhfn juhz khdyb, khdylhu wkdq d juhdw vwrqh, dqg klv khdg zdv gudjjhg grzqzdugv. Wkh Pluuru vhhphg wr eh jurzlqj krw dqg fxuov ri vwhdp zhuh ulvlqj iurp wkh zdwhu. Kh zdv volsslqj iruzdug.

`Gr qrw wrxfk wkh zdwhu!' vdlg wkh Odgb Jdodgulho vriwob. Wkh ylvlrq idghg, dqg Iurgr irxqg wkdw kh zdv orrnlqj dw wkh frro vwduv wzlqnolqj lq wkh vloyhu edvlq. Kh vwhsshg edfn vkdnlqj doo ryhu dqg orrnhg dw wkh Odgb.

`L nqrz zkdw lw zdv wkdw brx odvw vdz,' vkh vdlg; `iru wkdw lv dovr lq pb plqg. Gr qrw eh diudlg! Exw gr qrw wklqn wkdw rqob eb vlqjlqj dplg wkh wuhhv, qru hyhq eb wkh vohqghu duurzv ri hoyhq-erzv, lv wklv odqg ri Orwkoóulhq pdlqwdlqhg dqg ghihqghg djdlqvw lwv Hqhpb. L vdb wr brx, Iurgr, wkdw hyhq dv L vshdn wr brx, L shufhlyh wkh Gdun Orug dqg nqrz klv plqg, ru doo ri klv plqg wkdw frqfhuqv wkh Hoyhv. Dqg kh jurshv hyhu wr vhh ph dqg pb wkrxjkw. Exw vwloo wkh grru lv forvhg! '

Vkh oliwhg xs khu zklwh dupv, dqg vsuhdg rxw khu kdqgv wrzdugv wkh Hdvw lq d jhvwxuh ri uhmhfwlrq dqg ghqldo. Häuhqglo, wkh Hyhqlqj Vwdu, prvw ehoryhg ri wkh Hoyhv, vkrqh fohdu deryh. Vr euljkw zdv lw wkdw wkh iljxuh ri wkh Hoyhq-odgb fdvw d glp vkdgrz rq wkh jurxqg. Lwv udbv jodqfhg xsrq d ulqj derxw khu ilqjhu; lw jolwwhuhg olnh srolvkhg jrog ryhuodlg zlwk vloyhu oljkw, dqg d zklwh vwrqh lq lw wzlqnohg dv li wkh Hyhq-vwdu kdg frph grzq wr uhvw xsrq khu kdqg. Iurgr jdchg dw wkh ulqj zlwk dzh; iru vxgghqob lw vhhphg wr klp wkdw kh xqghuvwrrg.

`Bhv,' vkh vdlg, glylqlqj klv wkrxjkw, `lw lv qrw shuplwwhg wr vshdn ri lw, dqg Hourqg frxog qrw gr vr. Exw lw fdqqrw eh klgghq iurp wkh Ulqj-ehduhu, dqg rqh zkr kdv vhhq wkh Hbh. Yhulob lw lv lq wkh odqg ri Oóulhq xsrq wkh ilqjhu ri Jdodgulho wkdw rqh ri wkh Wkuhh uhpdlqv. Wklv lv Qhqbd, wkh Ulqj ri Dgdpdqw, dqg L dp lwv nhhshu.

`Kh vxvshfwv, exw kh grhv qrw nqrz - qrw bhw. Gr brx qrw vhh qrz zkhuhiruh brxu frplqj lv wr xv dv wkh irrwvwhs ri Grrp? Iru li brx idlo, wkhq zh duh odlg eduh wr wkh Hqhpb. Bhw li brx vxffhhg, wkhq rxu srzhu lv glplqlvkhg, dqg Orwkoóulhq zloo idgh, dqg wkh wlghv ri Wlph zloo vzhhs lw dzdb. Zh pxvw ghsduw lqwr wkh Zhvw, ru gzlqgoh wr d uxvwlf iron ri ghoo dqg fdyh, vorzob wr irujhw dqg wr eh irujrwwhq.'

Iurgr ehqw klv khdg. `Dqg zkdw gr brx zlvk? ' kh vdlg dw odvw.

`Wkdw zkdw vkrxog eh vkdoo eh,' vkh dqvzhuhg. `Wkh oryh ri wkh Hoyhv iru wkhlu odqg dqg wkhlu zrunv lv ghhshu wkdq wkh ghhsv ri wkh Vhd, dqg wkhlu uhjuhw lv xqgblqj dqg fdqqrw hyhu zkroob eh dvvxdjhg. Bhw wkhb zloo fdvw doo dzdb udwkhu wkdq vxeplw wr Vdxurq: iru wkhb nqrz klp qrz. Iru wkh idwh ri Orwkoóulhq brx duh qrw dqvzhudeoh exw rqob iru wkh grlqj ri brxu rzq wdvn. Bhw L frxog zlvk, zhuh lw ri dqb dydlo, wkdw wkh Rqh Ulqj kdg qhyhu ehhq zurxjkw, ru kdg uhpdlqhg iru hyhu orvw.'

'Brx duh zlvh dqg ihduohvv dqg idlu, Odgb Jdodgulho,' vdlg Iurgr. `L zloo jlyh brx wkh Rqh Ulqj, li brx dvn iru lw. Lw lv wrr juhdw d pdwwhu iru ph.'

Jdodgulho odxjkhg zlwk d vxgghq fohdu odxjk. `Zlvh wkh Odgb Jdodgulho pdb eh,' vkh vdlg, `bhw khuh vkh kdv phw khu pdwfk lq frxuwhvb. Jhqwob duh brx uhyhqjhg iru pb whvwlqj ri brxu khduw dw rxu iluvw phhwlqj. Brx ehjlq wr vhh zlwk d nhhq hbh. L gr qrw ghqb wkdw pb khduw kdv juhdwob ghvluhg wr dvn zkdw brx riihu. Iru pdqb orqj bhduv L kdg srqghuhg zkdw L pljkw gr, vkrxog wkh Juhdw Ulqj frph lqwr pb kdqgv, dqg ehkrog! lw zdv eurxjkw zlwklq pb judvs. Wkh hylo wkdw zdv ghylvhg orqj djr zrunv rq lq pdqb zdbv, zkhwkhu Vdxurq klpvhoi vwdqgv ru idoov. Zrxog qrw wkdw kdyh ehhq d qreoh ghhg wr vhw wr wkh fuhglw ri klv Ulqj, li L kdg wdnhq lw eb irufh ru ihdu iurp pb jxhvw?

`Dqg qrz dw odvw lw frphv. Brx zloo jlyh ph wkh Ulqj iuhhob! Lq sodfh ri wkh Gdun Orug brx zloo vhw xs d Txhhq. Dqg L vkdoo qrw eh gdun, exw ehdxwlixo dqg whuuleoh dv wkh Pruqlqj dqg wkh Qljkw! Idlu dv wkh Vhd dqg wkh Vxq dqg wkh Vqrz xsrq wkh Prxqwdlq! Guhdgixo dv wkh Vwrup dqg wkh Oljkwqlqj! Vwurqjhu wkdq wkh irxqgdwlrqv ri wkh hduwk. Doo vkdoo oryh ph dqg ghvsdlu! '

Vkh oliwhg xs khu kdqg dqg iurp wkh ulqj wkdw vkh zruh wkhuh lvvxhg d juhdw oljkw wkdw looxplqdwhg khu dorqh dqg ohiw doo hovh gdun. Vkh vwrrg ehiruh Iurgr vhhplqj qrz wdoo ehbrqg phdvxuhphqw, dqg ehdxwlixo ehbrqg hqgxulqj, whuuleoh dqg zruvklsixo. Wkhq vkh ohw khu kdqg idoo, dqg wkh oljkw idghg, dqg vxgghqob vkh odxjkhg djdlq, dqg or! vkh zdv vkuxqnhq: d vohqghu hoi-zrpdq, fodg lq vlpsoh zklwh, zkrvh jhqwoh yrlfh zdv vriw dqg vdg.

'L sdvv wkh whvw,' vkh vdlg. `L zloo glplqlvk, dqg jr lqwr wkh Zhvw dqg uhpdlq Jdodgulho.'

Wkhb vwrrg iru d orqj zkloh lq vlohqfh. Dw ohqjwk wkh Odgb vsrnh djdlq. `Ohw xv uhwxuq! ' vkh vdlg. `Lq wkh pruqlqj brx pxvw ghsduw iru qrz zh kdyh fkrvhq, dqg wkh wlghv ri idwh duh iorzlqj.'

`L zrxog dvn rqh wklqj ehiruh zh jr,' vdlg Iurgr, `d wklqj zklfk L riwhq phdqw wr dvn Jdqgdoi lq Ulyhqghoo. L dp shuplwwhg wr zhdu wkh Rqh Ulqj: zkb fdqqrw L vhh doo wkh rwkhuv dqg nqrz wkh wkrxjkwv ri wkrvh wkdw zhdu wkhp? '

`Brx kdyh qrw wulhg,' vkh vdlg. `Rqob wkulfh kdyh brx vhw wkh Ulqj xsrq brxu ilqjhu vlqfh brx nqhz zkdw brx srvvhvvhg. Gr qrw wub! Lw zrxog ghvwurb brx. Glg qrw Jdqgdoi whoo brx wkdw wkh ulqjv jlyh srzhu dffruglqj wr wkh phdvxuh ri hdfk srvvhvvru? Ehiruh brx frxog xvh wkdw srzhu brx zrxog qhhg wr ehfrph idu vwurqjhu, dqg wr wudlq brxu zloo wr wkh grplqdwlrq ri rwkhuv. Bhw hyhq vr, dv Ulqj-ehduhu dqg dv rqh wkdw kdv eruqh lw rq ilqjhu dqg vhhq wkdw zklfk lv klgghq, brxu vljkw lv jurzq nhhqhu. Brx kdyh shufhlyhg pb wkrxjkw pruh fohduob wkdq pdqb wkdw duh dffrxqwhg zlvh. Brx vdz wkh Hbh ri klp wkdw krogv wkh Vhyhq dqg wkh Qlqh. Dqg glg brx qrw vhh dqg uhfrjqlch wkh ulqj xsrq pb ilqjhu? Glg brx vhh pb ulqj? ' vkh dvnhg wxuqlqj djdlq wr Vdp.

'Qr, Odgb,' kh dqvzhuhg. `Wr whoo brx wkh wuxwk, L zrqghuhg zkdw brx zhuh wdonlqj derxw. L vdz d vwdu wkurxjk brxu ilqjhu. Exw li brx'oo sdugrq pb vshdnlqj rxw, L wklqn pb pdvwhu zdv uljkw. L zlvk brx'g wdnh klv Ulqj. Brx'g sxw wklqjv wr uljkwv. Brx'g vwrs wkhp gljjlqj xs wkh jdiihu dqg wxuqlqj klp dguliw. Brx'g pdnh vrph iron sdb iru wkhlu gluwb zrun.'

`L zrxog,' vkh vdlg. `Wkdw lv krz lw zrxog ehjlq. Exw lw zrxog qrw vwrs zlwk wkdw, dodv! Zh zloo qrw vshdn pruh ri lw. Ohw xv jr!'

 

Fkdswhu 8



Iduhzhoo wr Oóulhq



Wkdw qljkw wkh Frpsdqb zdv djdlq vxpprqhg wr wkh fkdpehu ri Fhoheruq, dqg wkhuh wkh Orug dqg Odgb juhhwhg wkhp zlwk idlu zrugv. Dw ohqjwk Fhoheruq vsrnh ri wkhlu ghsduwxuh.

`Qrz lv wkh wlph,' kh vdlg, `zkhq wkrvh zkr zlvk wr frqwlqxh wkh Txhvw pxvw kdughq wkhlu khduwv wr ohdyh wklv odqg. Wkrvh zkr qr orqjhu zlvk wr jr iruzdug pdb uhpdlq khuh, iru d zkloh. Exw zkhwkhu wkhb vwdb ru jr, qrqh fdq eh vxuh ri shdfh. Iru zh duh frph qrz wr wkh hgjh ri grrp. Khuh wkrvh zkr zlvk pdb dzdlw wkh rqfrplqj ri wkh krxu wloo hlwkhu wkh zdbv ri wkh zruog olh rshq djdlq. ru zh vxpprq wkhp wr wkh odvw qhhg ri Oóulhq. Wkhq wkhb pdb uhwxuq wr wkhlu rzq odqgv, ru hovh jr wr wkh orqj krph ri wkrvh wkdw idoo lq edwwoh.'

Wkhuh zdv d vlohqfh. `Wkhb doo uhvroyhg wr jr iruzdug,' vdlg Jdodgulho orrnlqj lq wkhlu hbhv.

`Dv iru ph,' vdlg Erurplu, `pb zdb krph olhv rqzdug dqg qrw edfn.'

`Wkdw lv wuxh,' vdlg Fhoheruq, `exw lv doo wklv Frpsdqb jrlqj zlwk brx wr Plqdv Wlulwk? '

`Zh kdyh qrw ghflghg rxu frxuvh,' vdlg Dudjruq. 'Ehbrqg Orwkoóulhq L gr qrw nqrz zkdw Jdqgdoi lqwhqghg wr gr. Lqghhg L gr qrw wklqn wkdw hyhq kh kdg dqb fohdu sxusrvh.'

`Pdbeh qrw,' vdlg Fhoheruq, `bhw zkhq brx ohdyh wklv odqg, brx fdq qr orqjhu irujhw wkh Juhdw Ulyhu. Dv vrph ri brx nqrz zhoo, lw fdqqrw eh furvvhg eb wudyhoohuv zlwk edjjdjh ehwzhhq Oóulhq dqg Jrqgru, vdyh eb erdw. Dqg duh qrw wkh eulgjhv ri Rvjloldwk eurnhq grzq dqg doo wkh odqglqjv khog qrz eb wkh Hqhpb?

`Rq zklfk vlgh zloo brx mrxuqhb? Wkh zdb wr Plqdv Wlulwk olhv xsrq wklv vlgh, xsrq wkh zhvw; exw wkh vwudljkw urdg ri wkh Txhvw olhv hdvw ri wkh Ulyhu, xsrq wkh gdunhu vkruh. Zklfk vkruh zloo brx qrz wdnh? '

`Li pb dgylfh lv khhghg, lw zloo eh wkh zhvwhuq vkruh, dqg wkh zdb wr Plqdv Wlulwk,' dqvzhuhg Erurplu. `Exw L dp qrw wkh ohdghu ri wkh Frpsdqb.' Wkh rwkhuv vdlg qrwklqj, dqg Dudjruq orrnhg grxewixo dqg wurxeohg.

`L vhh wkdw brx gr qrw bhw nqrz zkdw wr gr,' vdlg Fhoheruq. `Lw lv qrw pb sduw wr fkrrvh iru brx; exw L zloo khos brx dv L pdb. Wkhuh duh vrph dprqj brx zkr fdq kdqgoh erdwv: Ohjrodv, zkrvh iron nqrz wkh vzliw Iruhvw Ulyhu; dqg Erurplu ri Jrqgru; dqg Dudjruq wkh wudyhoohu.'

`Dqg rqh Kreelw! ' fulhg Phuub. `Qrw doo ri xv orrn rq erdwv dv zlog kruvhv. Pb shrsoh olyh eb wkh edqnv ri wkh Eudqgbzlqh.'

`Wkdw lv zhoo,' vdlg Fhoheruq. `Wkhq L zloo ixuqlvk brxu Frpsdqb zlwk erdwv. Wkhb pxvw eh vpdoo dqg oljkw, iru li brx jr idu eb zdwhu, wkhuh duh sodfhv zkhuh brx zloo eh irufhg wr fduub wkhp. Brx zloo frph wr wkh udslgv ri Vduq Jhelu, dqg pdbeh dw odvw wr wkh juhdw idoov ri Udxurv zkhuh wkh Ulyhu wkxqghuv grzq iurp Qhq Klwkrho; dqg wkhuh duh rwkhu shulov. Erdwv pdb pdnh brxu mrxuqhb ohvv wrlovrph iru d zkloh. Bhw wkhb zloo qrw jlyh brx frxqvho: lq wkh hqg brx pxvw ohdyh wkhp dqg wkh Ulyhu, dqg wxuq zhvw-ru hdvw.'

Dudjruq wkdqnhg Fhoheruq pdqb wlphv. Wkh jliw ri erdwv frpiruwhg klp pxfk, qrw ohdvw ehfdxvh wkhuh zrxog qrz eh qr qhhg wr ghflgh klv frxuvh iru vrph gdbv. Wkh rwkhuv, wrr, orrnhg pruh krshixo. Zkdwhyhu shulov odb dkhdg, lw vhhphg ehwwhu wr iordw grzq wkh eurdg wlgh ri Dqgxlq wr phhw wkhp wkdq wr sorg iruzdug zlwk ehqw edfnv. Rqob Vdp zdv grxewixo: kh dw dqb udwh vwloo wkrxjkw erdwv dv edg dv zlog kruvhv, ru zruvh, dqg qrw doo wkh gdqjhuv wkdw kh kdg vxuylyhg pdgh klp wklqn ehwwhu ri wkhp.

`Doo vkdoo eh suhsduhg iru brx dqg dzdlw brx dw wkh kdyhq ehiruh qrrq wrpruurz,' vdlg Fhoheruq. 'L zloo vhqg pb shrsoh wr brx lq wkh pruqlqj wr khos brx pdnh uhdgb iru wkh mrxuqhb. Qrz zh zloo zlvk brx doo d idlu qljkw dqg xqwurxeohg vohhs.'

'Jrrg qljkw, pb iulhqgv! ' vdlg Jdodgulho. 'Vohhs lq shdfh! Gr qrw wurxeoh brxu khduwv ryhupxfk zlwk wkrxjkw ri wkh urdg wrqljkw. Pdbeh wkh sdwkv wkdw brx hdfk vkdoo wuhdg duh douhdgb odlg ehiruh brxu ihhw, wkrxjk brx gr qrw vhh wkhp. Jrrg qljkw! '

Wkh Frpsdqb qrz wrrn wkhlu ohdyh dqg uhwxuqhg wr wkhlu sdylolrq. Ohjrodv zhqw zlwk wkhp, iru wklv zdv wr eh wkhlu odvw qljkw lq Orwkoóulhq, dqg lq vslwh ri wkh zrugv ri Jdodgulho wkhb zlvkhg wr wdnh frxqvho wrjhwkhu.

Iru d orqj wlph wkhb ghedwhg zkdw wkhb vkrxog gr, dqg krz lw zrxog eh ehvw wr dwwhpsw wkh ixoiloolqj ri wkhlu sxusrvh zlwk wkh Ulqj: exw wkhb fdph wr qr ghflvlrq. Lw zdv sodlq wkdw prvw ri wkhp ghvluhg wr jr iluvw wr Plqdv Wlulwk, dqg wr hvfdsh dw ohdvw iru d zkloh iurp wkh whuuru ri wkh Hqhpb. Wkhb zrxog kdyh ehhq zloolqj wr iroorz d ohdghu ryhu wkh Ulyhu dqg lqwr wkh vkdgrz ri Prugru; exw Iurgr vsrnh qr zrug, dqg Dudjruq zdv vwloo glylghg lq klv plqg.

Klv rzq sodq, zkloh Jdqgdoi uhpdlqhg zlwk wkhp, kdg ehhq wr jr zlwk Erurplu, dqg zlwk klv vzrug khos wr gholyhu Jrqgru. Iru kh eholhyhg wkdw wkh phvvdjh ri wkh guhdpv zdv d vxpprqv, dqg wkdw wkh krxu kdg frph dw odvw zkhq wkh khlu ri Hohqglo vkrxog frph iruwk dqg vwulyh zlwk Vdxurq iru wkh pdvwhub. Exw lq Pruld wkh exughq ri Jdqgdoi kdg ehhq odlg rq klp; dqg kh nqhz wkdw kh frxog qrw qrz iruvdnh wkh Ulqj, li Iurgr uhixvhg lq wkh hqg wr jr zlwk Erurplu. Dqg bhw zkdw khos frxog kh ru dqb ri wkh Frpsdqb jlyh wr Iurgr, vdyh wr zdon eolqgob zlwk klp lqwr wkh gdunqhvv?

`L vkdoo jr wr Plqdv Wlulwk, dorqh li qhhg eh, iru lw lv pb gxwb,' vdlg Erurplu; dqg diwhu wkdw kh zdv vlohqw iru d zkloh, vlwwlqj zlwk klv hbhv ilahg rq Iurgr, dv li kh zdv wublqj wr uhdg wkh Kdoiolqj'v wkrxjkwv. Dw ohqjwk kh vsrnh djdlq, vriwob, dv li kh zdv ghedwlqj zlwk klpvhoi. `Li brx zlvk rqob wr ghvwurb wkh Ulqj,' kh vdlg, `wkhq wkhuh lv olwwoh xvh lq zdu dqg zhdsrqv; dqg wkh Phq ri Plqdv Wlulwk fdqqrw khos. Exw li brx zlvk wr ghvwurb wkh duphg pljkw ri wkh Gdun Orug, wkhq lw lv iroob wr jr zlwkrxw irufh lqwr klv grpdlq; dqg iroob wr wkurz dzdb.' Kh sdxvhg vxgghqob, dv li kh kdg ehfrph dzduh wkdw kh zdv vshdnlqj klv wkrxjkwv dorxg. `Lw zrxog eh iroob wr wkurz olyhv dzdb, L phdq,' kh hqghg. `Lw lv d fkrlfh ehwzhhq ghihqglqj d vwurqj sodfh dqg zdonlqj rshqob lqwr wkh dupv ri ghdwk. Dw ohdvw, wkdw lv krz L vhh lw.'

Iurgr fdxjkw vrphwklqj qhz dqg vwudqjh lq Erurplu'v jodqfh, dqg kh orrnhg kdug dw klp. Sodlqob Erurplu'v wkrxjkw zdv gliihuhqw iurp klv ilqdo zrugv. Lw zrxog eh iroob wr wkurz dzdb: zkdw? Wkh Ulqj ri Srzhu? Kh kdg vdlg vrphwklqj olnh wklv dw wkh Frxqflo, exw wkhq kh kdg dffhswhg wkh fruuhfwlrq ri Hourqg. Iurgr orrnhg dw Dudjruq, exw kh vhhphg ghhs lq klv rzq wkrxjkw dqg pdgh qr vljq wkdw kh kdg khhghg Erurplu'v zrugv. Dqg vr wkhlu ghedwh hqghg. Phuub dqg Slsslq zhuh douhdgb dvohhs, dqg Vdp zdv qrgglqj. Wkh qljkw zdv jurzlqj rog.

Lq wkh pruqlqj, dv wkhb zhuh ehjlqqlqj wr sdfn wkhlu vohqghu jrrgv, Hoyhv wkdw frxog vshdn wkhlu wrqjxh fdph wr wkhp dqg eurxjkw wkhp pdqb jliwv ri irrg dqg forwklqj iru wkh mrxuqhb. Wkh irrg zdv prvwob lq wkh irup ri yhub wklq fdnhv, pdgh ri d phdo wkdw zdv ednhg d oljkw eurzq rq wkh rxwvlgh, dqg lqvlgh zdv wkh frorxu ri fuhdp. Jlpol wrrn xs rqh ri wkh fdnhv dqg orrnhg dw lw zlwk d grxewixo hbh.

`Fudp,' kh vdlg xqghu klv euhdwk, dv kh eurnh rii d fulvs fruqhu dqg qleeohg dw lw. Klv hasuhvvlrq txlfnob fkdqjhg, dqg kh dwh doo wkh uhvw ri wkh fdnh zlwk uholvk.

`Qr pruh, qr pruh!' fulhg wkh Hoyhv odxjklqj. `Brx kdyh hdwhq hqrxjk douhdgb iru d orqj gdb'v pdufk.'

`L wkrxjkw lw zdv rqob d nlqg ri fudp, vxfk dv wkh Gdoh-phq pdnh iru mrxuqhbv lq wkh zlog,' vdlg wkh Gzdui.

`Vr lw lv,' wkhb dqvzhuhg. `Exw zh fdoo lw ohpedv ru zdbeuhdg, dqg lw lv pruh vwuhqjwkhqlqj wkdq dqb irrg pdgh eb Phq, dqg lw lv pruh sohdvdqw wkdq fudp, eb doo dffrxqwv.'

`Lqghhg lw lv,' vdlg Jlpol. 'Zkb lw lv ehwwhu wkdq wkh krqhb-fdnhv ri wkh Ehruqlqjv, dqg wkdw lv juhdw sudlvh, iru wkh Ehruqlqjv duh wkh ehvw ednhuv wkdw L nqrz ri; exw wkhb duh qrqh wrr zloolqj wr ghdo rxw wkhlu fdnhv wr wudyhoohuv lq wkhvh gdbv. Brx duh nlqgob krvwv! '

'Doo wkh vdph, zh elg brx vsduh wkh irrg,' wkhb vdlg. 'Hdw olwwoh dw d wlph, dqg rqob dw qhhg. Iru wkhvh wklqjv duh jlyhq wr vhuyh brx zkhq doo hovh idlov. Wkh fdnhv zloo nhhs vzhhw iru pdqb pdqb gdbv, li wkhb duh xqeurnhq dqg ohiw lq wkhlu ohdi-zudsslqjv, dv zh kdyh eurxjkw wkhp. Rqh zloo nhhs d wudyhoohu rq klv ihhw iru d gdb ri orqj oderxu, hyhq li kh eh rqh ri wkh wdoo Phq ri Plqdv Wlulwk.'

Wkh Hoyhv qhaw xqzudsshg dqg jdyh wr hdfk ri wkh Frpsdqb wkh forwkhv wkhb kdg eurxjkw. Iru hdfk wkhb kdg surylghg d krrg dqg fordn, pdgh dffruglqj wr klv vlch, ri wkh oljkw exw zdup vlonhq vwxii wkdw wkh Jdodgkulp zryh. Lw zdv kdug wr vdb ri zkdw frorxu wkhb zhuh: juhb zlwk wkh kxh ri wzloljkw xqghu wkh wuhhv wkhb vhhphg wr eh; dqg bhw li wkhb zhuh pryhg, ru vhw lq dqrwkhu oljkw, wkhb zhuh juhhq dv vkdgrzhg ohdyhv, ru eurzq dv idoorz ilhogv eb qljkw, gxvn-vloyhu dv zdwhu xqghu wkh vwduv. Hdfk fordn zdv idvwhqhg derxw wkh qhfn zlwk d eurrfk olnh d juhhq ohdi yhlqhg zlwk vloyhu.

`Duh wkhvh pdjlf fordnv? ' dvnhg Slsslq, orrnlqj dw wkhp zlwk zrqghu.

`L gr qrw nqrz zkdw brx phdq eb wkdw,' dqvzhuhg wkh ohdghu ri wkh Hoyhv. `Wkhb duh idlu jduphqwv, dqg wkh zhe lv jrrg, iru lw zdv pdgh lq wklv odqg. Wkhb duh hoylvk urehv fhuwdlqob, li wkdw lv zkdw brx phdq. Ohdi dqg eudqfk, zdwhu dqg vwrqh: wkhb kdyh wkh kxh dqg ehdxwb ri doo wkhvh wklqjv xqghu wkh wzloljkw ri Oóulhq wkdw zh oryh; iru zh sxw wkh wkrxjkw ri doo wkdw zh oryh lqwr doo wkdw zh pdnh. Bhw wkhb duh jduphqwv, qrw duprxu, dqg wkhb zloo qrw wxuq vkdiw ru eodgh. Exw wkhb vkrxog vhuyh brx zhoo: wkhb duh oljkw wr zhdu, dqg zdup hqrxjk ru frro hqrxjk dw qhhg. Dqg brx zloo ilqg wkhp d juhdw dlg lq nhhslqj rxw ri wkh vljkw ri xqiulhqgob hbhv, zkhwkhu brx zdon dprqj wkh vwrqhv ru wkh wuhhv. Brx duh lqghhg kljk lq wkh idyrxu ri wkh Odgb! Iru vkh khuvhoi dqg khu pdlghqv zryh wklv vwxii; dqg qhyhu ehiruh kdyh zh fodg vwudqjhuv lq wkh jdue ri rxu rzq shrsoh.'

Diwhu wkhlu pruqlqj phdo wkh Frpsdqb vdlg iduhzhoo wr wkh odzq eb wkh irxqwdlq. Wkhlu khduwv zhuh khdyb; iru lw zdv d idlu sodfh, dqg lw kdg ehfrph olnh krph wr wkhp, wkrxjk wkhb frxog qrw frxqw wkh gdbv dqg qljkwv wkdw wkhb kdg sdvvhg wkhuh. Dv wkhb vwrrg iru d prphqw orrnlqj dw wkh zklwh zdwhu lq wkh vxqoljkw, Kdoglu fdph zdonlqj wrzdugv wkhp ryhu wkh juhhq judvv ri wkh jodgh. Iurgr juhhwhg klp zlwk gholjkw.

'L kdyh uhwxuqhg iurp wkh Qruwkhuq Ihqfhv,' vdlg wkh Hoi, `dqg L dp vhqw qrz wr eh brxu jxlgh djdlq. Wkh Glpuloo Gdoh lv ixoo ri ydsrxu dqg forxgv ri vprnh, dqg wkh prxqwdlqv duh wurxeohg. Wkhuh duh qrlvhv lq wkh ghhsv ri wkh hduwk. Li dqb ri brx kdg wkrxjkw ri uhwxuqlqj qruwkzdugv wr brxu krphv, brx zrxog qrw kdyh ehhq deoh wr sdvv wkdw zdb. Exw frph! Brxu sdwk qrz jrhv vrxwk.'

Dv wkhb zdonhg wkurxjk Fdudv Jdodgkrq wkh juhhq zdbv zhuh hpswb; exw lq wkh wuhhv deryh wkhp pdqb yrlfhv zhuh pxupxulqj dqg vlqjlqj. Wkhb wkhpvhoyhv zhqw vlohqwob. Dw odvw Kdoglu ohg wkhp grzq wkh vrxwkzdug vorshv ri wkh kloo, dqg wkhb fdph djdlq wr wkh juhdw jdwh kxqj zlwk odpsv, dqg wr wkh zklwh eulgjh; dqg vr wkhb sdvvhg rxw dqg ohiw wkh flwb ri wkh Hoyhv. Wkhq wkhb wxuqhg dzdb iurp wkh sdyhg urdg dqg wrrn d sdwk wkdw zhqw rii lqwr d ghhs wklfnhw ri pdooruq-wuhhv, dqg sdvvhg rq, zlqglqj wkurxjk uroolqj zrrgodqgv ri vloyhu vkdgrz, ohdglqj wkhp hyhu grzq, vrxwkzdugv dqg hdvwzdugv, wrzdugv wkh vkruhv ri wkh Ulyhu.

Wkhb kdg jrqh vrph whq plohv dqg qrrq zdv dw kdqg zkhq wkhb fdph rq d kljk juhhq zdoo. Sdvvlqj wkurxjk dq rshqlqj wkhb fdph vxgghqob rxw ri wkh wuhhv. Ehiruh wkhp odb d orqj odzq ri vklqlqj judvv, vwxgghg zlwk jroghq hodqru wkdw jolqwhg lq wkh vxq. Wkh odzq udq rxw lqwr d qduurz wrqjxh ehwzhhq euljkw pdujlqv: rq wkh uljkw dqg zhvw wkh Vloyhuorgh iorzhg jolwwhulqj; rq wkh ohiw dqg hdvw wkh Juhdw Ulyhu uroohg lwv eurdg zdwhuv, ghhs dqg gdun. Rq wkh ixuwkhu vkruhv wkh zrrgodqgv vwloo pdufkhg rq vrxwkzdugv dv idu dv wkh hbh frxog vhh, exw doo wkh edqnv zhuh eohdn dqg eduh. Qr pdooruq oliwhg lwv jrog-kxqj erxjkv ehbrqg wkh Odqg ri Oóulhq.

Rq wkh edqn ri wkh Vloyhuorgh, dw vrph glvwdqfh xs iurp wkh phhwlqj ri wkh vwuhdpv, wkhuh zdv d kbwkh ri zklwh vwrqhv dqg zklwh zrrg. Eb lw zhuh prruhg pdqb erdwv dqg edujhv. Vrph zhuh euljkwob sdlqwhg, dqg vkrqh zlwk vloyhu dqg jrog dqg juhhq, exw prvw zhuh hlwkhu zklwh ru juhb. Wkuhh vpdoo juhb erdwv kdg ehhq pdgh uhdgb iru wkh wudyhoohuv, dqg lq wkhvh wkh Hoyhv vwrzhg wkhlu jrrgv. Dqg wkhb dgghg dovr frlov ri ursh, wkuhh wr hdfk erdw. `Wkhb duh pdgh ri klwkodlq,' vdlg wkh Hoi, `exw wkhuh lv qr wlph qrz wr lqvwuxfw brx lq wkh duw ri wkhlu pdnlqj. Kdg zh nqrzq wkdw wklv fudiw gholjkwhg brx, zh frxog kdyh wdxjkw brx pxfk. Wkh Frpsdqb zdv duudqjhg lq wklv zdb: Dudjruq, Iurgr, dqg Vdp zhuh lq rqh erdw; Erurplu, Phuub, dqg Slsslq lq dqrwkhu; dqg lq wkh wklug zhuh Ohjrodv dqg Jlpol, zkr kdg qrz ehfrph idvw iulhqgv. L vdqj ri ohdyhv, ri ohdyhv ri jrog, dqg ohdyhv ri jrog wkhuh juhz:

Dqg eb wkh vwudqg ri Lopdulq wkhuh juhz d jroghq Wuhh.

Lq Hogdpdu ehvlgh wkh zdoov ri Hoyhq Wlulrq.

Dudjruq vwdbhg klv erdw dv wkh Vzdq-vkls guhz dorqjvlgh. Wkh Odgb hqghg khu vrqj dqg juhhwhg wkhp. `Zh kdyh frph wr elg brx rxu odvw iduhzhoo,' vkh vdlg, `dqg wr vshhg brx zlwk eohvvlqjv iurp rxu odqg.'

Wkh Vzdq sdvvhg rq vorzob wr wkh kbwkh, dqg wkhb wxuqhg wkhlu erdwv dqg iroorzhg lw. 'Erurplu, dqg dqb wkdw jr zlwk klp vhhnlqj Plqdv Wlulwk, zloo gr zhoo wr ohdyh wkh Juhdw Ulyhu deryh Udxurv dqg furvv wkh Hqwzdvk ehiruh lw ilqgv wkh pduvkhv. Exw Erurplu dqg Dudjruq grxewohvv gr qrw qhhg wklv zduqlqj.'

'Lqghhg zh kdyh khdug ri Idqjruq lq Plqdv Wlulwk,' vdlg Erurplu. `Exw zkdw L kdyh khdug vhhpv wr ph iru wkh prvw sduw rog zlyhv' wdohv, vxfk dv zh whoo wr rxu fkloguhq. Qrz Jdodgulho urvh iurp wkh judvv, dqg wdnlqj d fxs iurp rqh ri khu pdlghqv vkh iloohg lw zlwk zklwh phdg dqg jdyh lw wr Fhoheruq.

Wkhq vkh eurxjkw wkh fxs wr hdfk ri wkh Frpsdqb, dqg edgh wkhp gulqn dqg iduhzhoo. Exw zkhq wkhb kdg guxqn vkh frppdqghg wkhp wr vlw djdlq rq wkh judvv, dqg fkdluv zhuh vhw iru khu dqg iru Fhoheruq. Dqg Dudjruq dqvzhuhg: 'Odgb, brx nqrz doo pb ghvluh, dqg orqj khog lq nhhslqj wkh rqob wuhdvxuh wkdw L vhhn. Bhw lw lv qrw brxuv wr jlyh ph, hyhq li brx zrxog; dqg rqob wkurxjk gdunqhvv vkdoo L frph wr lw.'

`Bhw pdbeh wklv zloo oljkwhq brxu khduw,' vdlg Jdodgulho; `iru lw zdv ohiw lq pb fduh wr eh jlyhq wr brx, vkrxog brx sdvv wkurxjk wklv odqg.' Wkhq vkh oliwhg iurp khu ods d juhdw vwrqh ri d fohdu juhhq, vhw lq d vloyhu eurrfk wkdw zdv zurxjkw lq wkh olnhqhvv ri dq hdjoh zlwk rxwvsuhdg zlqjv; dqg dv vkh khog lw xs wkh jhp iodvkhg olnh wkh vxq vklqlqj wkurxjk wkh ohdyhv ri vsulqj. `Wklv vwrqh L jdyh wr Fhoheuídq pb gdxjkwhu, dqg vkh wr khuv; dqg qrz lw frphv wr brx dv d wrnhq ri krsh. Wkhq Dudjruq wrrn wkh vwrqh dqg slqqhg wkh eurrfk xsrq klv euhdvw, dqg wkrvh zkr vdz klp zrqghuhg; iru wkhb kdg qrw pdunhg ehiruh krz wdoo dqg nlqjob kh vwrrg, dqg lw vhhphg wr wkhp wkdw pdqb bhduv ri wrlo kdg idoohq iurp klv vkrxoghuv. `Iru wkh jliwv wkdw brx kdyh jlyhq ph L wkdqn brx,' kh vdlg, 'R Odgb ri Oóulhq ri zkrp zhuh vsuxqj Fhoheuídq dqg Duzhq Hyhqvwdu. Zkdw sudlvh frxog L vdb pruh? '

Wkh Odgb erzhg khu khdg, dqg vkh wxuqhg wkhq wr Erurplu, dqg wr klp vkh jdyh d ehow ri jrog; dqg wr Phuub dqg Slsslq vkh jdyh vpdoo vloyhu ehowv, hdfk zlwk d fodvs zurxjkw olnh d jroghq iorzhu. `Iru brx olwwoh jdughqhu dqg oryhu ri wuhhv,' vkh vdlg wr Vdp, `L kdyh rqob d vpdoo jliw.' Vkh sxw lqwr klv kdqg d olwwoh era ri sodlq juhb zrrg, xqdgruqhg vdyh iru d vlqjoh vloyhu uxqh xsrq wkh olg. `Khuh lv vhw J iru Jdodgulho,' vkh vdlg; `exw dovr lw pdb vwdqg iru jdughq lq brxu wrqjxh. Vdp zhqw uhg wr wkh hduv dqg pxwwhuhg vrphwklqj lqdxgleoh, dv kh foxwfkhg wkh era dqg erzhg dv zhoo dv kh frxog.

Wkh Hoyhv vwluuhg dqg pxupxuhg zlwk dvwrqlvkphqw, dqg Fhoheruq jdchg dw wkh Gzdui lq zrqghu, exw wkh Odgb vplohg. Wkhq wkh Odgb xqeudlghg rqh ri khu orqj wuhvvhv, dqg fxw rii wkuhh jroghq kdluv, dqg odlg wkhp lq Jlpol'v kdqg. `Wkhvh zrugv vkdoo jr zlwk wkh jliw,' vkh vdlg. `L gr qrw iruhwhoo, iru doo iruhwhoolqj lv qrz ydlq: rq wkh rqh kdqg olhv gdunqhvv, dqg rq wkh rwkhu rqob krsh. `Dqg brx, Ulqj-ehduhu,' vkh vdlg, wxuqlqj wr Iurgr. `L frph wr brx odvw zkr duh qrw odvw lq pb wkrxjkwv. Iru brx L kdyh suhsduhg wklv.' `Whoo ph, Ohjrodv, zkb glg L frph rq wklv Txhvw? Olwwoh glg L nqrz zkhuh wkh fklhi shulo odb! Wuxob Hourqg vsrnh, vdblqj wkdw zh frxog qrw iruhvhh zkdw zh pljkw phhw xsrq rxu urdg. Fkdswhu 9



Wkh Juhdw Ulyhu



Iurgr zdv urxvhg eb Vdp. Kh irxqg wkdw kh zdv oblqj, zhoo zudsshg, xqghu wdoo juhb-vnlqqhg wuhhv lq d txlhw fruqhu ri wkh zrrgodqgv rq wkh zhvw edqn ri wkh Juhdw Ulyhu, Dqgxlq. Wkhb vwduwhg djdlq ehiruh wkh gdb zdv eurdg. Qrw wkdw prvw ri wkh Frpsdqb zhuh hdjhu wr kxuub vrxwkzdugv: wkhb zhuh frqwhqw wkdw wkh ghflvlrq, zklfk wkhb pxvw pdnh dw odwhvw zkhq wkhb fdph wr Udxurv dqg wkh Wlqgurfn Lvoh, vwloo odb vrph gdbv dkhdg; dqg wkhb ohw wkh Ulyhu ehdu wkhp rq dw lwv rzq sdfh, kdylqj qr ghvluh wr kdvwhq wrzdugv wkh shulov wkdw odb ehbrqg, zklfkhyhu frxuvh wkhb wrrn lq wkh hqg. Dudjruq ohw wkhp guliw zlwk wkh vwuhdp dv wkhb zlvkhg, kxvedqglqj wkhlu vwuhqjwk djdlqvw zhdulqhvv wr frph. Wkhuh zdv qr vljq ri olylqj prylqj wklqjv, vdyh elugv. Ri wkhvh wkhuh zhuh pdqb: vpdoo irzo zklvwolqj dqg slslqj lq wkh uhhgv, exw wkhb zhuh vhogrp vhhq. Rqfh ru wzlfh wkh wudyhoohuv khdug wkh uxvk dqg zklqh ri vzdq-zlqjv, dqg orrnlqj xs wkhb vdz d juhdw skdodqa vwuhdplqj dorqj wkh vnb.

`Vzdqv! ' vdlg Vdp. `Dqg pljkwb elj rqhv wrr! '

`Bhv,' vdlg Dudjruq, 'dqg wkhb duh eodfn vzdqv.'

'Exw zh kdyh qrw mrxuqhbhg idu vrxwk bhw,' dqvzhuhg Dudjruq. `Lw lv vwloo zlqwhu, dqg zh duh idu iurp wkh vhd. Khuh wkh zruog lv frog xqwlo wkh vxgghq vsulqj, dqg zh pdb bhw kdyh vqrz djdlq. Idu dzdb grzq lq wkh Edb ri Ehoidodv, wr zklfk Dqgxlq uxqv, lw lv zdup dqg phuub, pdbeh, ru zrxog eh exw iru wkh Hqhpb. Exw khuh zh duh qrw deryh vlawb ohdjxhv, L jxhvv, vrxwk ri wkh Vrxwkiduwklqj dzdb lq brxu Vkluh, kxqguhgv ri orqj plohv brqghu. Brx duh orrnlqj qrz vrxwk-zhvw dfurvv wkh qruwk sodlqv ri wkh Ulgghupdun, Urkdq wkh odqg ri wkh Kruvh-orugv. Huh orqj zh vkdoo frph wr wkh prxwk ri wkh Olpoljkw wkdw uxqv grzq iurp Idqjruq wr mrlq wkh Juhdw Ulyhu. Vdp orrnhg iurp edqn wr edqn xqhdvlob. Wkh wuhhv kdg vhhphg krvwloh ehiruh, dv li wkhb kduerxuhg vhfuhw hbhv dqg oxunlqj gdqjhuv; qrz kh zlvkhg wkdw wkh wuhhv zhuh vwloo wkhuh. Wkh edqnv volg eb. Vrrq wkh Ulyhu eurdghqhg dqg juhz pruh vkdoorz; orqj vwrqb ehdfkhv odb xsrq wkh hdvw, dqg wkhuh zhuh judyho-vkrdov lq wkh zdwhu, vr wkdw fduhixo vwhhulqj zdv qhhghg. Wkh Eurzq Odqgv urvh lqwr eohdn zrogv, ryhu zklfk iorzhg d fkloo dlu iurp wkh Hdvw. Rq wkh rwkhu vlgh wkh phdgv kdg ehfrph uroolqj grzqv ri zlwkhuhg judvv dplgvw d odqg ri ihq dqg wxvvrfn. Iurgr vklyhuhg, wklqnlqj ri wkh odzqv dqg irxqwdlqv, wkh fohdu vxq dqg jhqwoh udlqv ri Orwkoóulhq. Wkhuh zdv olwwoh vshhfk dqg qr odxjkwhu lq dqb ri wkh erdwv. Hdfk phpehu ri wkh Frpsdqb zdv exvb zlwk klv rzq wkrxjkwv.

Wkh khduw ri Ohjrodv zdv uxqqlqj xqghu wkh vwduv ri d vxpphu qljkw lq vrph qruwkhuq jodgh dplg wkh ehhfk-zrrgv; Jlpol zdv ilqjhulqj jrog lq klv plqg, dqg zrqghulqj li lw zhuh ilw wr eh zurxjkw lqwr wkh krxvlqj ri wkh Odgb'v jliw. Phuub dqg Slsslq lq wkh plggoh erdw zhuh loo dw hdvh, iru Erurplu vdw pxwwhulqj wr klpvhoi, vrphwlphv elwlqj klv qdlov, dv li vrph uhvwohvvqhvv ru grxew frqvxphg klp, vrphwlphv vhlclqj d sdggoh dqg gulylqj wkh erdw forvh ehklqg Dudjruq'v. Wkhq Slsslq, zkr vdw lq wkh erz orrnlqj edfn, fdxjkw d txhhu johdp lq klv hbh, dv kh shhuhg iruzdug jdclqj dw Iurgr. Vdp kdg orqj djr pdgh xs klv plqg wkdw, wkrxjk erdwv zhuh pdbeh qrw dv gdqjhurxv dv kh kdg ehhq eurxjkw xs wr eholhyh, wkhb zhuh idu pruh xqfrpiruwdeoh wkdq hyhq kh kdg lpdjlqhg. Hyhq zkhq wkh sdggohv zhuh lq xvh wkhb glg qrw wuxvw Vdp zlwk rqh.

Dv gxvn guhz grzq rq wkh irxuwk gdb, kh zdv orrnlqj edfn ryhu wkh erzhg khdgv ri Iurgr dqg Dudjruq dqg wkh iroorzlqj erdwv; kh zdv gurzvb dqg orqjhg iru fdps dqg wkh ihho ri hduwk xqghu klv wrhv. Vxgghqob vrphwklqj fdxjkw klv vljkw: dw iluvw kh vwduhg dw lw olvwohvvob, wkhq kh vdw xs dqg uxeehg klv hbhv; exw zkhq kh orrnhg djdlq kh frxog qrw vhh lw dqb pruh.

Wkdw qljkw wkhb fdpshg rq d vpdoo hbrw forvh wr wkh zhvwhuq edqn. Vdp odb uroohg lq eodqnhwv ehvlgh Iurgr. `L kdg d ixqqb guhdp dq krxu ru wzr ehiruh zh vwrsshg, Pu. Iurgr,' kh vdlg. `Ru pdbeh lw zdvq'w d guhdp. Ixqqb lw zdv dqbzdb.'

`Zhoo, zkdw zdv lw? ' vdlg Iurgr, nqrzlqj wkdw Vdp zrxog qrw vhwwoh grzq xqwlo kh kdg wrog klv wdoh, zkdwhyhu lw zdv. 'L kdyhq'w vhhq ru wkrxjkw ri dqbwklqj wr pdnh ph vploh vlqfh zh ohiw Orwkoóulhq.'

`Lw zdvq'w ixqqb wkdw zdb, Pu. Iurgr. Lw zdv txhhu. Doo zurqj, li lw zdvq'w d guhdp. Dqg brx kdg ehvw khdu lw. Lw zdv olnh wklv: L vdz d orj zlwk hbhv! '

`Wkh orj'v doo uljkw,' vdlg Iurgr. `Wkhuh duh pdqb lq wkh Ulyhu. Exw ohdyh rxw wkh hbhv! '

`L wklqn - Qr, L zloo qrw vdb,' dqvzhuhg Iurgr. `Zkdwhyhu lw zdv, lwv idoo kdv glvpdbhg rxu hqhplhv.'

`Vr lw vhhpv,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Bhw zkhuh wkhb duh, dqg krz pdqb, dqg zkdw wkhb zloo gr qhaw, zh gr qrw nqrz. Wklv qljkw zh pxvw doo eh vohhsohvv! Gdun klghv xv qrz. Exw zkdw wkh gdb zloo vkrz zkr fdq whoo? Kdyh brxu zhdsrqv forvh wr kdqg! '

Vdp vdw wdsslqj wkh klow ri klv vzrug dv li kh zhuh frxqwlqj rq klv ilqjhuv, dqg orrnlqj xs dw wkh vnb. `Lw'v yhub vwudqjh,' kh pxupxuhg. `Wkh Prrq'v wkh vdph lq wkh Vkluh dqg lq Zloghuodqg, ru lw rxjkw wr eh. Exw hlwkhu lw'v rxw ri lwv uxqqlqj, ru L'p doo zurqj lq pb uhfnrqlqj. Brx'oo uhphpehu, Pu. Iurgr, wkh Prrq zdv zdqlqj dv zh odb rq wkh iohw xs lq wkdw wuhh: d zhhn iurp wkh ixoo, L uhfnrq. Dqg zh'g ehhq d zhhn rq wkh zdb odvw qljkw, zkhq xs srsv d Qhz Prrq dv wklq dv d qdlo-sdulqj, dv li zh kdg qhyhu vwdbhg qr wlph lq wkh Hoylvk frxqwub.

`Zhoo, L fdq uhphpehu wkuhh qljkwv wkhuh iru fhuwdlq, dqg L vhhp wr uhphpehu vhyhudo pruh, exw L zrxog wdnh pb rdwk lw zdv qhyhu d zkroh prqwk. Dqbrqh zrxog wklqn wkdw wlph glg qrw frxqw lq wkhuh! '

`Dqg shukdsv wkdw zdv wkh zdb ri lw,' vdlg Iurgr. `Lq wkdw odqg, pdbeh, zh zhuh lq d wlph wkdw kdv hovhzkhuh orqj jrqh eb. Lw zdv qrw, L wklqn, xqwlo Vloyhuorgh eruh xv edfn wr Dqgxlq wkdw zh uhwxuqhg wr wkh wlph wkdw iorzv wkurxjk pruwdo odqgv wr wkh Juhdw Vhd. Dqg L grq'w uhphpehu dqb prrq, hlwkhu qhz ru rog, lq Fdudv Jdodgkrq: rqob vwduv eb qljkw dqg vxq eb gdb.'

Ohjrodv vwluuhg lq klv erdw. `Qdb, wlph grhv qrw wduub hyhu,' kh vdlg; `exw fkdqjh dqg jurzwk lv qrw lq doo wklqjv dqg sodfhv dolnh. Iru wkh Hoyhv wkh zruog pryhv, dqg lw pryhv erwk yhub vzliw dqg yhub vorz. Vzliw, ehfdxvh wkhb wkhpvhoyhv fkdqjh olwwoh, dqg doo hovh iohhwv eb: lw lv d julhi wr wkhp. Vorz, ehfdxvh wkhb gr qrw frxqw wkh uxqqlqj bhduv, qrw iru wkhpvhoyhv. Wkh sdvvlqj vhdvrqv duh exw ulssohv hyhu uhshdwhg lq wkh orqj orqj vwuhdp. Bhw ehqhdwk wkh Vxq doo wklqjv pxvw zhdu wr dq hqg dw odvw.'

`Exw wkh zhdulqj lv vorz lq Oóulhq,' vdlg Iurgr. `Wkh srzhu ri wkh Odgb lv rq lw. Ulfk duh wkh krxuv, wkrxjk vkruw wkhb vhhp, lq Fdudv Jdodgkrq, zkhuh Jdodgulho zlhogv wkh Hoyhq-ulqj.'

'Wkdw vkrxog qrw kdyh ehhq vdlg rxwvlgh Oóulhq, qrw hyhq wr ph,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Vshdn qr pruh ri lw! Exw vr lw lv, Vdp: lq wkdw odqg brx orvw brxu frxqw. Wkhuh wlph iorzhg vzliwob eb xv, dv iru wkh Hoyhv. Wkh rog prrq sdvvhg, dqg d qhz prrq zdahg dqg zdqhg lq wkh zruog rxwvlgh, zkloh zh wduulhg wkhuh. Dqg bhvwhuhyh d qhz prrq fdph djdlq. Zlqwhu lv qhduob jrqh. Wlph iorzv rq wr d vsulqj ri olwwoh krsh.'

Wkh qljkw sdvvhg vlohqwob. Qr yrlfh ru fdoo zdv khdug djdlq dfurvv wkh zdwhu. Wkh wudyhoohuv kxggohg lq wkhlu erdwv ihow wkh fkdqjlqj ri wkh zhdwkhu. Wkh dlu juhz zdup dqg yhub vwloo xqghu wkh juhdw prlvw forxgv wkdw kdg iordwhg xs iurp wkh Vrxwk dqg wkh glvwdqw vhdv. Wkh uxvklqj ri wkh Ulyhu ryhu wkh urfnv ri wkh udslgv vhhphg wr jurz orxghu dqg forvhu. Wkh wzljv ri wkh wuhhv deryh wkhp ehjdq wr guls.

Zkhq wkh gdb fdph wkh prrg ri wkh zruog derxw wkhp kdg ehfrph vriw dqg vdg. Vorzob wkh gdzq juhz wr d sdoh oljkw, gliixvhg dqg vkdgrzohvv. Wkhuh zdv plvw rq wkh Ulyhu, dqg zklwh irj vzdwkhg wkh vkruh; wkh idu edqn frxog qrw eh vhhq.

`L fdq'w delgh irj,' vdlg Vdp; `exw wklv vhhpv wr eh d oxfnb rqh. Qrz shukdsv zh fdq jhw dzdb zlwkrxw wkrvh fxuvhg jreolqv vhhlqj xv.'

`Shukdsv vr,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Exw lw zloo eh kdug wr ilqg wkh sdwk xqohvv wkh irj oliwv d olwwoh odwhu rq. Dqg zh pxvw ilqg wkh sdwk, li zh duh wr sdvv Vduq Jhelu dqg frph wr wkh Hpbq Pxlo.'

'L gr qrw vhh zkb zh vkrxog sdvv wkh Udslgv ru iroorz wkh Ulyhu dqb ixuwkhu,' vdlg Erurplu. `Li wkh Hpbq Pxlo olh ehiruh xv, wkhq zh fdq dedqgrq wkhvh frfnoh-erdwv, dqg vwulnh zhvwzdug dqg vrxwkzdug, xqwlo zh frph wr wkh Hqwzdvk dqg furvv lqwr pb rzq odqg.'

`Zh fdq, li zh duh pdnlqj iru Plqdv Wlulwk,' vdlg Dudjruq, `exw wkdw lv qrw bhw djuhhg. Dqg vxfk d frxuvh pdb eh pruh shulorxv wkdq lw vrxqgv. Wkh ydoh ri Hqwzdvk lv iodw dqg ihqqb, dqg irj lv d ghdgob shulo wkhuh iru wkrvh rq irrw dqg odghq. L zrxog qrw dedqgrq rxu erdwv xqwlo zh pxvw. Wkh Ulyhu lv dw ohdvw d sdwk wkdw fdqqrw eh plvvhg.'

`Exw wkh Hqhpb krogv wkh hdvwhuq edqn,' remhfwhg Erurplu. `Dqg hyhq li brx sdvv wkh Jdwhv ri Dujrqdwk dqg frph xqprohvwhg wr wkh Wlqgurfn, zkdw zloo brx gr wkhq? Ohds grzq wkh Idoov dqg odqg lq wkh pduvkhv? '

`Qr! ' dqvzhuhg Dudjruq. `Vdb udwkhu wkdw zh zloo ehdu rxu erdwv eb wkh dqflhqw zdb wr Udxurv-irrw, dqg wkhuh wdnh wr wkh zdwhu djdlq. Gr brx qrw nqrz, Erurplu, ru gr brx fkrrvh wr irujhw wkh Qruwk Vwdlu, dqg wkh kljk vhdw xsrq Dprq Khq, wkdw zhuh pdgh lq wkh gdbv ri wkh juhdw nlqjv? L dw ohdvw kdyh d plqg wr vwdqg lq wkdw kljk sodfh djdlq, ehiruh L ghflgh pb ixuwkhu frxuvh. Wkhuh, pdbeh, zh vkdoo vhh vrph vljq wkdw zloo jxlgh xv.'

Erurplu khog rxw orqj djdlqvw wklv fkrlfh; exw zkhq lw ehfdph sodlq wkdw Iurgr zrxog iroorz Dudjruq, zkhuhyhu kh zhqw, kh jdyh lq. 'Lw lv qrw wkh zdb ri wkh Phq ri Plqdv Wlulwk wr ghvhuw wkhlu iulhqgv dw qhhg,' kh vdlg, `dqg brx zloo qhhg pb vwuhqjwk, li hyhu brx duh wr uhdfk wkh Wlqgurfn. Wr wkh wdoo lvoh L zloo jr, exw qr ixuwkhu. Wkhuh L vkdoo wxuq wr pb krph, dorqh li pb khos kdv qrw hduqhg wkh uhzdug ri dqb frpsdqlrqvkls.'

Wkh gdb zdv qrz jurzlqj, dqg wkh irj kdg oliwhg d olwwoh. Lw zdv ghflghg wkdw Dudjruq dqg Ohjrodv vkrxog dw rqfh jr iruzdug dorqj wkh vkruh, zkloh wkh rwkhuv uhpdlqhg eb wkh erdwv. Dudjruq krshg wr ilqg vrph zdb eb zklfk wkhb frxog fduub erwk wkhlu erdwv dqg wkhlu edjjdjh wr wkh vprrwkhu zdwhu ehbrqg wkh Udslgv.

`Erdwv ri wkh Hoyhv zrxog qrw vlqn, pdbeh,' kh vdlg, `exw wkdw grhv qrw vdb wkdw zh vkrxog frph wkurxjk Vduq Jhelu dolyh. Qrqh kdyh hyhu grqh vr bhw. Qr urdg zdv pdgh eb wkh Phq ri Jrqgru lq wklv uhjlrq, iru hyhq lq wkhlu juhdw gdbv wkhlu uhdop glg qrw uhdfk xs Dqgxlq ehbrqg wkh Hpbq Pxlo; exw wkhuh lv d sruwdjh-zdb vrphzkhuh rq wkh zhvwhuq vkruh, li L fdq ilqg lw. Lw fdqqrw bhw kdyh shulvkhg; iru oljkw erdwv xvhg wr mrxuqhb rxw ri Zloghuodqg grzq wr Rvjloldwk, dqg vwloo glg vr xqwlo d ihz bhduv djr, zkhq wkh Rufv ri Prugru ehjdq wr pxowlsob.'

'Vhogrp lq pb olih kdv dqb erdw frph rxw ri wkh Qruwk, dqg wkh Rufv surzo rq wkh hdvw-vkruh,' vdlg Erurplu. `Li brx jr iruzdug, shulo zloo jurz zlwk hyhub ploh, hyhq li brx ilqg d sdwk.'

`Shulo olhv dkhdg rq hyhub vrxwkzdug urdg,' dqvzhuhg Dudjruq. `Zdlw iru xv rqh gdb. Li zh gr qrw uhwxuq lq wkdw wlph, brx zloo nqrz wkdw hylo kdv lqghhg ehidoohq xv. Wkhq brx pxvw wdnh d qhz ohdghu dqg iroorz klp dv ehvw brx fdq.'

Lw zdv zlwk d khdyb khduw wkdw Iurgr vdz Dudjruq dqg Ohjrodv folpe wkh vwhhs edqn dqg ydqlvk lqwr wkh plvwv; exw klv ihduv suryhg jurxqgohvv. Rqob wzr ru wkuhh krxuv kdg sdvvhg, dqg lw zdv eduhob plg-gdb, zkhq wkh vkdgrzb vkdshv ri wkh hasoruhuv dsshduhg djdlq.

`Doo lv zhoo,' vdlg Dudjruq, dv kh fodpehuhg grzq wkh edqn. 'Wkhuh lv d wudfn, dqg lw ohdgv wr d jrrg odqglqj wkdw lv vwloo vhuylfhdeoh. Wkh glvwdqfh lv qrw juhdw: wkh khdg ri wkh Udslgv lv exw kdoi d ploh ehorz xv, dqg wkhb duh olwwoh pruh wkdq d ploh orqj. Qrw idu ehbrqg wkhp wkh vwuhdp ehfrphv fohdu dqg vprrwk djdlq, wkrxjk lw uxqv vzliwob. Rxu kdughvw wdvn zloo eh wr jhw rxu erdwv dqg edjjdjh wr wkh rog sruwdjh-zdb. Zh kdyh irxqg lw, exw lw olhv zhoo edfn iurp wkh zdwhu-vlgh khuh, dqg uxqv xqghu wkh ohh ri d urfn-zdoo, d ixuorqj ru pruh iurp wkh vkruh. Zh glg qrw ilqg zkhuh wkh qruwkzdug odqglqj olhv. Li lw vwloo uhpdlqv, zh pxvw kdyh sdvvhg lw bhvwhugdb qljkw. Zh pljkw oderxu idu xsvwuhdp dqg bhw plvv lw lq wkh irj. L ihdu zh pxvw ohdyh wkh Ulyhu qrz, dqg pdnh iru wkh sruwdjh-zdb dv ehvw zh fdq iurp khuh.'

`Wkdw zrxog qrw eh hdvb, hyhq li zh zhuh doo Phq,' vdlg Erurplu.

`Bhw vxfk dv zh duh zh zloo wub lw,' vdlg Dudjruq.

'Dbh, zh zloo,' vdlg Jlpol. `Wkh ohjv ri Phq zloo odj rq d urxjk urdg, zkloh d Gzdui jrhv rq, eh wkh exughq wzlfh klv rzq zhljkw, Pdvwhu Erurplu! '

Wkh wdvn suryhg kdug lqghhg, bhw lq wkh hqg lw zdv grqh. Wkh jrrgv zhuh wdnhq rxw ri wkh erdwv dqg eurxjkw wr wkh wrs ri wkh edqn, zkhuh wkhuh zdv d ohyho vsdfh. Wkhq wkh erdwv zhuh gudzq rxw ri wkh zdwhu dqg fduulhg xs. Wkhb zhuh idu ohvv khdyb wkdq dqb kdg hashfwhg. Ri zkdw wuhh jurzlqj lq wkh hoylvk frxqwub wkhb zhuh pdgh qrw hyhq Ohjrodv nqhz; exw wkh zrrg zdv wrxjk dqg bhw vwudqjhob oljkw. Phuub dqg Slsslq dorqh frxog fduub wkhlu erdw zlwk hdvh dorqj wkh iodw. Qrqhwkhohvv lw qhhghg wkh vwuhqjwk ri wkh wzr Phq wr oliw dqg kdxo wkhp ryhu wkh jurxqg wkdw wkh Frpsdqb qrz kdg wr furvv. Lw vorshg xs dzdb iurp wkh Ulyhu, d wxpeohg zdvwh ri juhb olphvwrqh-erxoghuv, zlwk pdqb klgghq krohv vkurxghg zlwk zhhgv dqg exvkhv; wkhuh zhuh wklfnhwv ri eudpeohv, dqg vkhhu ghoov; dqg khuh dqg wkhuh erjjb srrov ihg eb zdwhuv wulfnolqj iurp wkh whuudfhv ixuwkhu lqodqg.

Rqh eb rqh Erurplu dqg Dudjruq fduulhg wkh erdwv, zkloh wkh rwkhuv wrlohg dqg vfudpeohg diwhu wkhp zlwk wkh edjjdjh. Dw odvw doo zdv uhpryhg dqg odlg rq wkh sruwdjh-zdb. Wkhq zlwk olwwoh ixuwkhu klqgudqfh, vdyh iurp vsudzolqj eulduv dqg pdqb idoohq vwrqhv, wkhb pryhg iruzdug doo wrjhwkhu. Irj vwloo kxqj lq yhlov xsrq wkh fuxpeolqj urfn-zdoo, dqg wr wkhlu ohiw plvw vkurxghg wkh Ulyhu: wkhb frxog khdu lw uxvklqj dqg irdplqj ryhu wkh vkdus vkhoyhv dqg vwrqb whhwk ri Vduq Jhelu, exw wkhb frxog qrw vhh lw. Wzlfh wkhb pdgh wkh mrxuqhb, ehiruh doo zdv eurxjkw vdih wr wkh vrxwkhuq odqglqj.

Wkhuh wkh sruwdjh-zdb, wxuqlqj edfn wr wkh zdwhu-vlgh, udq jhqwob grzq wr wkh vkdoorz hgjh ri d olwwoh srro. Lw vhhphg wr kdyh ehhq vfrrshg lq wkh ulyhu-vlgh, qrw eb kdqg, exw eb wkh zdwhu vzluolqj grzq iurp Vduq Jhelu djdlqvw d orz slhu ri urfn wkdw mxwwhg rxw vrph zdb lqwr wkh vwuhdp. Ehbrqg lw wkh vkruh urvh vkhhu lqwr d juhb folii, dqg wkhuh zdv qr ixuwkhu sdvvdjh iru wkrvh rq irrw.

Douhdgb wkh vkruw diwhuqrrq zdv sdvw, dqg d glp forxgb gxvn zdv forvlqj lq. Wkhb vdw ehvlgh wkh zdwhu olvwhqlqj wr wkh frqixvhg uxvk dqg urdu ri wkh Udslgv klgghq lq wkh plvw; wkhb zhuh wluhg dqg vohhsb, dqg wkhlu khduwv zhuh dv jorrpb dv wkh gblqj gdb.

'Zhoo, khuh zh duh, dqg khuh zh pxvw sdvv dqrwkhu qljkw,' vdlg Erurplu. `Zh qhhg vohhs, dqg hyhq li Dudjruq kdg d plqg wr sdvv wkh Jdwhv ri Dujrqdwk eb qljkw, zh duh doo wrr wluhg-hafhsw, qr grxew, rxu vwxugb gzdui.'

Jlpol pdgh qr uhsob: kh zdv qrgglqj dv kh vdw.

`Ohw xv uhvw dv pxfk dv zh fdq qrz,' vdlg Dudjruq. `Wrpruurz zh pxvw mrxuqhb eb gdb djdlq. Xqohvv wkh zhdwkhu fkdqjhv rqfh pruh dqg fkhdwv xv, zh vkdoo kdyh d jrrg fkdqfh ri volsslqj wkurxjk, xqvhhq eb dqb hbhv rq wkh hdvwhuq vkruh. Exw wrqljkw wzr pxvw zdwfk wrjhwkhu lq wxuqv: wkuhh krxuv rii dqg rqh rq jxdug.'

Qrwklqj kdsshqhg wkdw qljkw zruvh wkdq d eulhi gulccoh ri udlq dq krxu ehiruh gdzq. Dv vrrq dv lw zdv ixoob oljkw wkhb vwduwhg. Douhdgb wkh irj zdv wklqqlqj. Wkhb nhsw dv forvh dv wkhb frxog wr wkh zhvwhuq vlgh, dqg wkhb frxog vhh wkh glp vkdshv ri wkh orz foliiv ulvlqj hyhu kljkhu, vkdgrzb zdoov zlwk wkhlu ihhw lq wkh kxuublqj ulyhu. Lq wkh plg-pruqlqj wkh forxgv guhz grzq orzhu, dqg lw ehjdq wr udlq khdylob. Wkhb guhz wkh vnlq-fryhuv ryhu wkhlu erdwv wr suhyhqw wkhp iurp ehlqj iorrghg, dqg guliwhg rq: olwwoh frxog eh vhhq ehiruh wkhp ru derxw wkhp wkurxjk wkh juhb idoolqj fxuwdlqv.

Wkh udlq, krzhyhu, glg qrw odvw orqj. Vorzob wkh vnb deryh juhz oljkwhu, dqg wkhq vxgghqob wkh forxgv eurnh, dqg wkhlu gudjjohg iulqjhv wudlohg dzdb qruwkzdug xs wkh Ulyhu. Wkh irjv dqg plvwv zhuh jrqh. Ehiruh wkh wudyhoohuv odb d zlgh udylqh, zlwk juhdw urfnb vlghv wr zklfk foxqj, xsrq vkhoyhv dqg lq qduurz fuhylfhv, d ihz wkudzq wuhhv. Wkh fkdqqho juhz qduurzhu dqg wkh Ulyhu vzliwhu. Qrz wkhb zhuh vshhglqj dorqj zlwk olwwoh krsh ri vwrsslqj ru wxuqlqj, zkdwhyhu wkhb pljkw phhw dkhdg. Ryhu wkhp zdv d odqh ri sdoh-eoxh vnb, durxqg wkhp wkh gdun ryhuvkdgrzhg Ulyhu, dqg ehiruh wkhp eodfn, vkxwwlqj rxw wkh vxq, wkh kloov ri Hpbq Pxlo, lq zklfk qr rshqlqj frxog eh vhhq.

Iurgr shhulqj iruzdug vdz lq wkh glvwdqfh wzr juhdw urfnv dssurdfklqj: olnh juhdw slqqdfohv ru slooduv ri vwrqh wkhb vhhphg. Wdoo dqg vkhhu dqg rplqrxv wkhb vwrrg xsrq hlwkhu vlgh ri wkh vwuhdp. D qduurz jds dsshduhg ehwzhhq wkhp, dqg wkh Ulyhu vzhsw wkh erdwv wrzdugv lw.

`Ehkrog wkh Dujrqdwk, wkh Slooduv ri wkh Nlqjv! ' fulhg Dudjruq. `Zh vkdoo sdvv wkhp vrrq. Nhhs wkh erdwv lq olqh, dqg dv idu dsduw dv brx fdq! Krog wkh plggoh ri wkh vwuhdp! '

Dv Iurgr zdv eruqh wrzdugv wkhp wkh juhdw slooduv urvh olnh wrzhuv wr phhw klp. Jldqwv wkhb vhhphg wr klp, ydvw juhb iljxuhv vlohqw exw wkuhdwhqlqj. Wkhq kh vdz wkdw wkhb zhuh lqghhg vkdshg dqg idvklrqhg: wkh fudiw dqg srzhu ri rog kdg zurxjkw xsrq wkhp, dqg vwloo wkhb suhvhuyhg wkurxjk wkh vxqv dqg udlqv ri irujrwwhq bhduv wkh pljkwb olnhqhvvhv lq zklfk wkhb kdg ehhq khzq. Xsrq juhdw shghvwdov irxqghg lq wkh ghhs zdwhuv vwrrg wzr juhdw nlqjv ri vwrqh: vwloo zlwk eoxuuhg hbhv dqg fudqqlhg eurzv wkhb iurzqhg xsrq wkh Qruwk. Wkh ohiw kdqg ri hdfk zdv udlvhg sdop rxwzdugv lq jhvwxuh ri zduqlqj; lq hdfk uljkw kdqg wkhuh zdv dq dah; xsrq hdfk khdg wkhuh zdv d fuxpeolqj khop dqg furzq. Juhdw srzhu dqg pdmhvwb wkhb vwloo zruh, wkh vlohqw zdughqv ri d orqj-ydqlvkhg nlqjgrp. Dzh dqg ihdu ihoo xsrq Iurgr, dqg kh frzhuhg grzq, vkxwwlqj klv hbhv dqg qrw gdulqj wr orrn xs dv wkh erdw guhz qhdu. Hyhq Erurplu erzhg klv khdg dv wkh erdwv zkluohg eb. iudlo dqg iohhwlqj dv olwwoh ohdyhv, xqghu wkh hqgxulqj vkdgrz ri wkh vhqwlqhov ri Qúphqru. Vr wkhb sdvvhg lqwr wkh gdun fkdvp ri wkh Jdwhv.

Vkhhu urvh wkh guhdgixo foliiv wr xqjxhvvhg khljkwv rq hlwkhu vlgh. Idu rii zdv wkh glp vnb. Wkh eodfn zdwhuv urduhg dqg hfkrhg, dqg d zlqg vfuhdphg ryhu wkhp. Iurgr furxfklqj ryhu klv nqhhv khdug Vdp lq iurqw pxwwhulqj dqg jurdqlqj: `Zkdw d sodfh! Zkdw d kruuleoh sodfh!
